LS 1.1 (AndrewBright)
B3.3.1.1.
Saint Andrew: Cassidy and Ringler 1971, 205-19.



 1. SANCTE ANDREAE Her segð þæt æfter þam þe Drihten
Hælend Crist to heofonum astah þæt þa apostolas wæron ætsomne,
and hie sendon hlot him betweonum, hwider hyra gehwylc faran scolde to
læranne.
 3. Segþ þæt se eadiga Matheus gehleat to Marmadonia
þære ceastre.
 4. Segð þonne þæt þa men þe on þære ceastre
wæron þæt hie hlaf ne æton ne wæter ne drvncon, ac æton manna
lichaman and heora blod druncon.
 6. And æghwylc man þe on þære ceastre com ælþeodisc,
segð þæt hie hine sona genamon and his eagan ut astungan, and hie him
sealdon attor drincan þæt mid myclen lybcræfte wæs geblanden: and
mid þy þe hie þone drenc druncon, hraþe heora heorta wæs tolesed and
heora mod onwended.
 10. Se eadiga Matheus þa in eode on þa ceastre, and hraðe hie
hine genamon and his eagan ut astungan.
 11. And hie him sealdon attor drinccan and hine sendon on
carcerne.
 12. And hie hine heton þæt attor etan and he hit etan nolde,
forþon þe his heorte næs tolesed ne his mod onwended.
 13. Ac he wæs simle to Drihtne biddende mid myclum wope and
cwæþ to him: Min Drihten Hælend Crist,for þon we ealle forleton ure
cneorisse and wæron þe fylgende and þu eart ure ealra fultum, þa þe
on þe gelyfað, beheald nu and geseoh hu þas men þinum þeowe doð.
 17. And ic þe bidde, Drihten, þæt þu me forgife minra
eagna leoht þæt ic geseo þa þe me onginnað don on þisse ceastre
þa weorstan tintrego; and ne forlæt me, min Drihten Hælende Crist, ne
me ne sele on þone bitterestan deaþ.
 21. Mid þy þe he þis gebed se eadiga Matheus gecweden
hæfde, mycel leoht and beorht onleohte þæt carcern and Drihtnes stefn
wæs on þæm leohte cweþende: Matheus min se leofa, beheald on me.
 23. Matheus þa lociende, he geseah Drihten Crist, and eft
Drihtnes stefn wæs cweþende: Matheus, wes þu gestrangod and ne ne
ondræd þu þe, for þon ne forlæte ic þe æfre, ac ic þe
gefreolsige of ealra frecennesse, and nalæs þæt an, ac simle ealle
þine breþere and ealle þa þe on me gelyfað on eallum tidum oþ
ecnesse.
 27. Ac onbid her <foreign>XXVII</foreign> nihta, and æfter þan ic sende to þe
Andreas þinne broþor and he þe ut alædeþ of þissum carcerne and
ealle þa þe mid þe syndon.
 29. Mid þy þe þis gecweden wæs, Drihten him eft to
cwæþ; Sib si mid þe.
 31. Matheus þa þurhwuniende mid gebedum and Drihtnes lof
singende on þam carcerne.
 32. And þa unrihtan men in eodon in þæt carcern þæt hie
þa men ut lædan woldon and him to mete don.
 33. Se eadiga Matheus þa betynde his eagan þy læs þa
cwelleras gesawan þæt his eagan geopenede wæron, and he cwædon him
betwynum: <foreign>III</foreign> dagas nu to lafe syndon þæt we hine willað acwellan and
us to mete gedon.
 37. Se eadiga Matheus, se gefelde <foreign>XX</foreign> daga ða Drihten
Hælende/ Crist cwæþ to Andreae his apostole, mid þi þe he wæs
in Achaia þam lande and þær lærde his discipuli.
 39. He cwæþ: Gang on Marmadonia ceastre and alæd þanon
Matheus, for þon <foreign>iii</foreign> dagas to lafe syndon þæt hie hine willað
acwellan and him to mete gedon.
 42. Se haliga Andreas him andswarode and he cwæþ: Min Drihten
Hælende/ Crist, hu mæg ic hit on þrim dagum gefaran?
 43. Ac ma wen is þæt þu onsende þinne engel, se hit mæg
hrædlicor gefaran, for þon, min Drihten, þu wast þæt ic eam
flæsclic man, and ic hit ne mæg hrædlice gefaran for þon se
siðfæt is þider to lang and ic þone weg ne can.
 47. Drihten him to cwæþ: Andreas, geher me, for þon þe ic
þe geworhte and ic þinne sið gestaþelode and getrymede.
 48. Gang nu to þæs sæs waroðe mid þinum discipulum, and
þu þær gemetest scip on þam waroðe: astig on þæt mid þinum
discipulum.
 51. Se haliga Andreas þa aras on mergen and he eode to þære
sæ mid his discipulum and he geseah scip on þam waroðe and <foreign>iii</foreign> weras
on þam sittende.
 53. And he wæs gefeonde mid micle gefean and him to cwæþ:
Broðor, hwider willað ge faran mid þis medmiclum scipe?
 55. Drihten Hælend wæs on þam scipe swa se steorreðra,
and his twegen englas mid him, þa wæron gehwyrfede on manna onsyne.
 56. Drihten Crist him to cwæþ: On Marmadonia ceastre.
 58. Se haliga Andreas him andswarode and he cwæþ: Broþor,
onfoh us mid eow on þæt scip and gelædað us on þa ceastre.
 60. Drihten him to cwæþ: Ealle men fleoð of þære
ceastre.
 60. To hwæm willað ge þider feran?
 62. Se haliga Andreas him andswarode.
 62. He cwæþ: Nedmycel ærende we þider habbað and us is
þearf þæt we hit gefyllon.
 64. Drihten Hælend him to cwæþ, Astigað on þis scip to
us and sellað us eowerne færsceat.
 66. Se haliga Andreas him andswarode: Gehyrað ge, broþor,
nabbað we færsceat.
 67. Ac we syndon discipuli Drihtnes Hælendes Cristes, þa he
geceas, and þis bebod he us sealde and he cwæþ: þonne ge faren godspel
to lærenne, þonne nabbe ge mid eow hlaf ne feoh ne twifeald hrægl.
 69. Gif þu þonne wille mildheortnesse us don, saga us þæt
hrætlice; gif þu þonne nelle, gecyð us þone weg.
 71. Drihten Hælend him to cwæþ: Gif þis gebod eow wære
geseald fram eowrum Drihtene, astigað hider mid gefean on min scip.
 72. Se halga Andreas astah on þæt scip and he gesæt beforan
þam steorreþran þæt wæs Drihten Hælend Crist.
 75. Drihten Hælend him to cwæþ: Ic geseo for þon þe
þas broðor synt geswencede of þisse sæwe hreohnesse.
 76. Acsa hie hwæþer hi woldon to lande astigan and þin
þær onbidan oþ þæt þu gefylle þine þenunge, to þære þu
eart sended; and þu eft hwyrfest to him.
 79. Se halga Andreas him to cwæþ: Mine bearn, wille ge to
lande faran and min þær onbidan?
 81. His discipuli him andswarodon and hie cwædon: Gif we
gewitað fram þe, þonne beo we fram eallum þam godum þe þu us
gearwodest.
 82. Ac we beoð mid þe swa hwær swa þu færest.
 84. Drihten Hælend him to cwæþ, to þam halgan Andrea: Gif
þu sy soðlice his discipul se is cweden Crist, spec to þinum discipulum
be þam mægenum þe þin læreow dyde, þæt sie gebletsod hiere
heorte and hie ofergieton þisse sæwe ege.
 88. Se haliga Andreas cwæþ to his discipulum: Sumre tide, mid
þi þe we wæron mid urum Drihtne, we astigon mid him on scip.
 89. He ætywde us swa he slæpende wære to costianne and
dyde swiþe hreoge þa sæ: fram þam winde wæs geworden swa þæt
þa selfan yþa wæron ahafene ofer þæt scip.
 91. We us þa swiðe andrædon and cigdon to him, Drihtne
Hælendum Criste, and he þa aras and bebead þam winde þæt he
gestilde, and wæs geworden mycel smyltnes on þære sæ; hie ondredon,
ealle þa þe his weorc gesawon.
 94. Nu þonne, mine bearn, ne ondrædaþ ge eow, for þon þe
ure God us ne forlæteð.
 96. And þus cweþende se halga Andreas, he sette his heafod ofer
ænne his discipul and slep.
 97. Drihten Hælend þa wiste for þon þe se halga Andreas
þa slep.
 98. He cwæþ to his englum: Genimað Andreas and his discipuli
and asettað hie beforan Marmadonia ceastre, and mid þi þe ge hie þær
asetton, hrowað eft to me.
 100. And þa englas dydon swa heom beboden wæs, and he astah on
heofonas.
 102. Þa se mergen geworden wæs, þa se haliga Andreas
licgende wæs beforan Marmadonia ceastre and his discipulos þær
slæpende wæron mid him.
 103. And he hie aweahte and cwæþ: Arisað, mine bearn, and
ongitað Godes mildheortnesse sio is nu mid us geworden; we witon þæt ure
Drihten mid us wæs on þam scipe and we hine ne ongeaton.
 106. He hine geeadmedde swa steorreþra and he hine æteowde swa
man us to costienne.
 108. Se halga Andreas þa locode to heofonum and he cwæþ: Min
Drihten Hælend Crist, ic wat þæt þu ne eart feor fram þinum
þeowum.
 109. And ic þe beheold on þam scype and ic wæs to þe
sprecende swa to men.
 110. Nu þonne, Drihten, ic þe bidde þæt þu me þe onywe
on þisse stowe.
 112. Þa þis gecweden wæs, þa Drihten him ætywde his
onsyne on fægeres cildes hiwe and him to cwæþ: Andreas, geseoh mid
þinum discipulum.
 114. Se halga Andreas þa hine gebæd and cwæþ: Forgif me,
min Drihten, þæt ic to þe sprecende wæs swa to men.
 115. And wen is þæt ic gefirnode, for þon ic þe ne
ongeat.
 118. Drihten him þa to cwæþ: Andreas, nænigwuht þu
gefirnodest, ac for þon ic swa dyde, for þon þu swa cwæde þæt
þu hit ne meahtes on <foreign>iii</foreign> dagum þider geferan.
 120. For þon ic þe swa æteowe, for þon ic eom mihtig swa
eall to done and anra gehwilcum to æteowenne swa swa me licað.
 120. Nu þonne aris, and ga on þa ceastre to Matheum þinum
breþer, and læt þonne hine of þære ceastre and ealle þa þe mid
him syndon.
 122. Ana ic þe gecyþe, Andreas, for þon þe manega tintrega
hie þe on bringað, and þinne lichaman geond þisse ceastre lonan hi
tostencaþ swa þæt þin blod flowð ofer eorðan swa wæter.
 124. To deaþe hie þe willaþ gelædan, ac hi ne magon; ac
manega/ earfoðnessa hie þe magon on gebringan.
 126. Ac þonne hwæþere arefna þu þa ealle, Andreas, and
ne do þu æfter heora ungeleafulnesse.
 127. Gemune hu manega earfoðnesse fram Iudeum ic wæs
þrowiende, þa hie me swungon and hie me spætton on mine onsyne; ac eall
ic hit aræfnede þæt ic eow æteowe hwylce gemete ge sculon
aræfnan.
 129. Gehiere me, Andreas, and aræfna þas tintrego, for þon
manige synt on þisse ceastre þa sculon geleofan on minne naman.
 131. Mid þi he þis cwæð, Drihten Hælend Crist, he astah
on heofonas.
 133. Se haliga Andreas þa in eode on þa ceastre mid his
discipulum, and nænig man hine ne mihte geseon.
 134. Mid þi þe hie comon to þæs carcernes duru, hie
þær gemetton seofon hyrdas standan.
 135. Se haliga Andreas þa gebæd on his heortan and raðe hio
wæron deade.
 136. Se halga Andreas þa eode to þæs carcernes duru and he
worhte Cristes rodetacen, and raþe þa dura wæron ontynede.
 137. And he in eode on þæt carcern mid his discipulum and he
geseah þone eadigan Matheus ænne sitton singende.
 140. Se eadiga Matheus þa and se haliga Andreas hie wæron
cyssende him betweonon.
 141. Se halga Andreas him to cwæþ: Hwæt is þæt,
broþor.
 141. Hu eart þu her gemet?
 142. Nu þry dagas to hlafe syndon þæt hie þe willaþ
acwellan and him to mete gedon.
 144. Se halga Matheus him andswarode and he cwæþ: Broþor
Andreas, ac ne gehyrdest þu Drihten cweþende for þon þe ic eow sende
swa swa sceapon middum wulfum?
 146. Þanon wæs geworden, mid þy þe hie me sendon on þis
carcern, ic bæd urne Drihten þæt he hine æteowde, and hraþe he me
hine æteowde and he me to cwæþ: Onbid her <foreign>XXVII</foreign> daga and æfter
þon ic sende to þe Andreas þinne broðor, and he þe ut alæt of
þissum carcern and ealle þa mid þe syndon.
 150. Swa me Drihten to cwæþ, ic gesie.
 150. Broðor, hwæt sculon we nu don?
 152. Se halga Andreas þa and se halga Matheus gebædon to
Drihtne.
 152. And æfter þon gebede se haliga Andreas sette his hand
ofer þara wera eagan þa þær on lande wæron, and gesihþe hie
onfengon.
 154. And eft he sette his hand ofer hiora heortan, and heora
andgiet/ him eft to hwirfde.
 155. Se haliga Andreas him to cwæþ: Gangað on þas
niþeran dælas þisse ceastre and ge þær gemetað mycel fictreow:
sittað under him and etað of his wæstmum oð þæt ic eow to cyme.
 158. Hi cwædon to þam halgan Andrea: Cum nu mid us, for þon
þe þu eart ure wealdend, þy læs wen is þæt hi us eft genimon and
on þa wyrstan tintregu hie us on gebringan.
 161. Se haliga Andreas him to cwæþ: Farað þider, for þon
þe eow nænig wiht ne derað ne ne swenceþ.
 162. And hraðe hie þa ealle ferdon, swa him se halga Andreas
bebead.
 163. And þær wæron on þæm carcerne twa hund and eahta
and feowertig wera and nigon and feowertig wifa, ða se haliga Andreas þanon
onsende.
 165. And þone eadigan Matheum he gedyde gangan to þam
eastdæle mid his discipulum.
 166. And se haliga Andreas and asetton on þa dune þær se
eadiga Petrus se apostol wæs, and he þær wunode mid him.
 168. Se haliga Andreas þa ut eode of þæm carcerne and he
ongan gangan ut þurh midde þa ceastre.
 169. And he com to sumre stowe and he þær geseah swer standan,
and ofer þone swer ærne onlicnesse.
 170. And he gesæt be þam swere anbidende hwæt him gelimpan
scolde.
 172. Ða unrihte men þa eodon þæt hie þa men ut
gelædan/ woldon and him to mete gedon, and hie gemetton þæs carcernes
duru opene and þa seofon hyrdas deade licgan.
 174. Mid þy þe hie þæt gesawon, hie eft hwirfdon to hiora
ealdormannum and hie cwædon: þin carcern open we gemetton, and in gangende
nænige we þær gemetton.
 177. Mid þi þe hie gehyrdon þara sacerda ealdormen and hie
cwædon him betweonon Hwæt wile þis wesan?
 178. Wen is þæt hwilc wundor in eode on þæt carcern and
þa hyrdas acwælde and somnunga alysde þa þe þær betynede
wæron.
 181. Æfter þiossum him æteowde deofol on cnihtes onlicnysse
and him to cwæþ: Gehyrað me, and secað her sumne ælþeodigne man
þæs nama is Andreas and acwellað hine.
 183. He þæt is se þa gebundenan of þissum carcerne ut
alædde and he is nu on þisse ceastre.
 184. Ge hine nu witon: efstað, mine bearn, and acwellað hine.
 186. Se haliga Andreas þa þa cwæþ to þam deofle: Ana
þu heardeste stræl to æghwilcre unrihtnesse, þu þe simle fihtest
wið manna cyn: min Drihten Hælende Crist þe gehnæde in helle.
 189. Þæt deofol, þa he þis gehyrde, he him to cwæþ:
þine stefne ic gehiere, ac ic ne wat hwær þu eart.
 191. Se haliga Andreas him to cwæþ: For þon þe þu eart
blind, þu ne gesihst ænigne of Godes þam halgum.
 193. Þæt deofol þa cwæþ to þam folce: Behealdað eow
and geseoð hine, for þon þe he þæt is se þe wið me spræc.
 195. Ða burhleode þa urnon and hi betyndon þære ceastre
gatu and hie sohton þæne halgan Andreas þæt hie hine genamon.
 196. Drihten Hælend hine þa æteowde þam haligan Andrea
and him to cwæþ: Andreas aris and gecyð him, þæt hie ongieton min
mægen on þe wesan.
 199. Se haliga Andreas þa aras on þæs folces gesihþe and
he cwæþ: Ic eom se Andreas þe ge secaþ.
 201. Þæt folc þa arn and hi hine genamon and cwædon: For
þon þu us þus dydest, we hit þe forgyldað.
 202. And hie þohton hu hie hine acwellan meahton.
 203. Þa wæs se deofol in gangende and cwæþ to þam
folce: Gif eow swa licige.
 204. Uton sendon rap on his swyran and hine teon þurh þisse
ceastre lanan, and þis uton we don oþ þæt he swelte.
 205. And mid þi þe he dead sie, uton we dælan his lichaman
urum burhleodum.
 207. And þa eall þæt folc þæt gehierde, hit him licode,
and hraðe hie sendon rap on his sweoran and hie hine tugon geond þære
ceastre lanan.
 208. Mid þi þe se eadiga Andreas wæs togen, his lichama
wæs gemengeð mid þære eorðan swa þæt blod fleow ofer eorðan
swa wæter.
 211. Ða æfen geworden wæs, hi hine sendon on þæt
carcern and hie gebunden his handa behindan and hie hine forleton, and eall his
lichama gelysed.
 213. Swilce oþre dæge þæt ilce hie dydon.
 213. Se haliga Andreas þa weop and he cwæþ: Min Drihten
Hælend Crist, cum and geseoh þæt hie me doð, þinum þeowe: and
eall ic hit aræfnie for þinum gebode þe þu me sealdest.
 215. And þu cwæde: Ne do æfter hiora ungeleafulnesse.
 216. Beheald, Drihten, and geseoh hu hie me doð.
 218. Mid þi he þus cwæþ, þæt deofol cwæþ to
þam folce: Swingað hine on his muð, þæt he þus ne sprece.
 220. Ða geworden wæs þæt hie hine eft betyndon on þam
carcerne.
 220. Ðæt deofol þa genam mid him oþre seofon deoflo, þa
þe haliga Andreas þanon afliemde, and in gangende on þæt carcern hie
gestodon on gesihþe þæs eadigan Andreas and hine bismriende mid myclere
bismre and hie cwædon: Hwæt is þæt þu her gemetest?
 224. Hwilc gefreolseð þe nu of urum gewealde?
 224. Hwær is þinn gilp and þi hiht?
 226. Þæt deofol þa cwæþ to þam oðrum deoflum: Mine
bearn, acwellað hine, for þon he us gescende and ure weorc.
 228. Þa deofla þa blæstan hie ofer þone halgan Andreas,
and hie gesawon Cristes rodetacen on his onsiene: hi ne dorston hine
genealæcan ac hraðe hie onweg flugon.
 230. Þæt deofol him to cwæþ: Mine bearn, for hwon ne
acwealdon ge hine?
 231. Hie him andswarodon and hie cwædon: We ne mihton, for þon
þe Cristes rodetanc on his onsiene we gesawon and we us ondrædon.
 232. We witon hine, for þon þe, ær he on þæs
earfoðnesse com he ure wæs wealdend.
 233. Gif þu mæge, acwel hine.
 234. We þe on þissum ne hersumiað, þy læs wen sie
þæt hine God gefreolsige and us sende on wyrsan tintrego.
 236. Se haliga Andreas him to cwæþ: þeah þe ge me
acwellan, ne do ic eowerne willan, ac ic do willan mines Drihtnes Hælendes
Cristes.
 237. And þus hi geherdon and onweg flugon.
 239. On mergen þa geworden wæs, eft hie tugon þone halgan
Andreas.
 239. And he cigde mid mycle wope to Drihtne and cwæþ: Min
Drihten Hælende Crist, me genihtsumiað þas tintrega, for þon ic eom
geteorod.
 241. Min Drihten Hælende Crist, ane tid on rode þu
þrowodest, and þu cwæde: Fæder, for hwon forlete þu me?
 243. Nu <foreign>iii</foreign> dagas syndon syððan ic wæs getogen þurh
þisse ceastre lanum.
 243. Þu wast, Drihten, þa menniscan tyddernysse.
 244. Hat onfon minne gast.
 244. Hwær syndon þine word, Drihten, on þam þu us
gestrangodest and þu cwæde: Gif ge me gehyrað and ge me beoð fylgende,
ne an locc of eowrum heafde forwyrð.
 246. Beheald, Drihten, and geseoh, for þi min lichama, and
loccas mines heafdes mid þisse eorðan synd gemengde.
 248. Ane, <foreign>iii</foreign> dagas syndon syððan ic wæs getogen to
þæm wyrstan tintregum, and þu me ne æteowdest.
 249. Min Drihten Hælend Crist, gestranga mine heortan.
 251. Ðus gebiddende þam halgan Andrea, Drihtenes stefn wæs
geworden on Ebreisc cweþende: Min Andreas, heofon and eorðe mæg gewitan,
min word næfre ne gewitaþ.
 253. Beheald æfter þe and geseoh þinne lichaman and loccas
þines heafdes, hwæt hie syndon gewordene.
 255. Se haliga Andreas þa lociende, he geseah geblowen treow
wæstm berende and he cwæþ: Nu ic wat, Drihten, for þon þæt þu
ne forlete me.
 257. On æfenne þa geworden, hie hine betyndon on þam
carcerne and hio cwædon him betwynum for þon þe þisse nihte he swelt.
 259. Him æteowde Drihten Hælend Crist on þæm carcerne,
and he æþenede his hand and genam, and he cwæþ: Andreas, aris.
 261. Mid þi þe he þæt gehyrde, hraþe he þa aras gesund
and he hine gebæd and he cwæþ: þancas ic þe do, min Drihten
Hælend Crist.
 262. Se haliga Andreas þa lociende, he geseah on middum þæm
carcerne swer standan, and ofer þone swer stænenne anlicnesse.
 264. And he aþenede his handa and hiere to cwæþ: Ondræd
þe Drihten and his rodetanc, beforan þæm forhtigað heofon and
eorþe.
 265. Nu þonne, anlicnes, do þæt ic bidde on naman mines
Drihtnes Hælendes Cristes: sænd mycel wæter þurh þinne muþ swa
þæt sien gewemmede ealle þa on þisse ceastre syndon.
 269. Mid þi he þus cwæþ, se eadiga Andreas, hraþe sio
stænene/ onlicnes sendde mycel wæter þurh hiora muþ swa sealt, and
hit/ æt manna lichaman.
 271. And hit acwealde heora bearn and hyra nytenu, and hie ealle
woldon fleon of þære ceastre.
 272. Se haliga Andreas þa cwæþ: Min Drihten Hælend Crist
ne forlæt me, ac send me þinne engel of heofonum on fyrenum wolcne,
þæt þa embgange ealle þas ceastre þæt ne magen genesan for
þæm fyre.
 274. And þus cweþende, fyren wolc astah of heofonum and hit
ymbsealde ealle þa ceastre.
 276. Mid þy þæt ongeat se eadiga Andreas, he bletsode
Drihten.
 277. Þæt wæter weox oþ mannes swuran and swiþe hit
æt hyra lichaman, and hie ealle cigdon and cwædon: Wa us, for þon þe
þas ealle up coman for þissum ælþeodigum þe we on þissum carcerne
betyned hæbbað.
 279. Hwæt beo we donde?
 280. Sume hie cwædon: Gif eow swalice þuhte, utan gangan on
þissum carcerne and hine ut forlætan, þy læs wen sie þæt we
yfele forweorþon; and uton we ealle cigean and cweþan for þon þe we
geleofað on Drihten þyses ælþeodigan mannes: þonne afyrseþ he
þas earfoðnesse fram us.
 284. Mid þi se eadiga Andreas ongeat þæt hie to Drihtene
wæron gehwyrfede, he cwæþ to þære stæenan anlicnesse: Ara nu
þurh mægen ures Drihtenes, and ma wæter of þinum muþe þu ne
send.
 286. And þa gecweden, þæt wæter oflan, and ma of heora
muþe hit ne eode.
 288. Se haliga Andreas þa ut eode of þam carcerne, and þæt
selfe wæter þegnunge gearwode beforan his fotum.
 289. And þa þær to hlafe wæron, hie comon to þæs
carcernes duru and hie cwædon: Gemiltsa us, God, and ne do us swaswa we
dydon on þisne ælþeodigan.
 292. Se haliga Andreas þa gebæd on þæs folces gesihþe,
and seo eorþe hie ontynde and hio forswealh þæt wæter mid þam
mannum.
 293. Þa weras þa þæt gesawon hie him swiþe ondrædon
and hie cwædon: Wa us, for þon þe þes deað fram Gode is.
 295. And he us wile acwellan for þissum earfoðnessum þe we
þissum mannan dydon.
 296. Soðlice fram Gode he is send, and he is Godes þeowa.
 297. Se halga Andreas him to cwæþ: Mine bearn, ne
ondrædaþ ge eow, for þon þe þas þe on þis wætere syndon, eft
he libbað.
 298. Ac þis is for þon þus geworden, þæt ge geleofon on
minum Drihtne Hælendum Criste.
 300. Se haliga Andreas þa gebæd to Drihtne and cwæþ: Min
Drihten Hælende Crist, send þinne þone Halgan Gast þæt awecce
ealle þa þe on þisse wætere syndon, þæt hie geliefon on þinne
naman.
 302. Drihten þa het ealle arisan þe on þam wætere
wæron.
 304. And æfter þissum se haliga Andreas het cyrican getimbrian
on þære stowe þær se swer stod, and he him sealde bebodu Drihtnes
Hælendes/ Cristes.
 305. And lufiað hine for þon mycel is his mægen.
 306. And ænne of heora aldormannum to bisceope he him gesette,
and he hi gefullode and cwæþ: Nu þonne ic eom gearo þæt ic gange to
minum discipulum.
 309. Hie ealle hine bædon and hie cwædon: Medmycel fæc nu
gyt wuna mid us, þæt þu us gedefran gedo, for þon þe we niwe syndon
to þissum geleafan gedon.
 312. Se halga Andreas hie þa nolde gehieran, ac he hie grette and
hie swa forlet.
 313. Him fylgede mycel manigo þæs folces wepende and
hrymende.
 313. And þa ascan leoht ofer hieora heafod.
 315. Mid þi se halga Andreas þanon wæs farende, him
ætiwde Drihten Hælende Crist on þam wege on ansine fægeres cildes
and him to cwæþ: Andreas, for hwan gæst þu swa, buton wæstme
þines gewinnes?
 317. And þu forlete þa þe þe bædon and þu nære
miltsiend ofer heora cild, þa þe wæron fyliende and wepende, þara cirm
and wop to me astah on heofonas.
 319. Nu þonne hwyrfe eft on þa ceastre and beo þær seofon
dagas, oþ þæt þu gestrangie hera mod on minne geleafan.
 321. Gang þonne to þære ceastre mid þinum discipulum, and
ge on minne geleafan geleofon.
 322. Mid þi he þis cwæþ, Drihten Hælende Crist, he
astah on heofonas.
 324. Se eadiga Andreas þa wæs eft hwyrfende on Marmadonia
ceastre and he cwæþ: Ic þe bletsige, min Drihten Hælend Crist, þu
þe gehwyrfest ealle saula, for þon þu me ne forlete ut gangan mid minre
hatheortan of þisse ceastre.
 327. Hio wæron gefeonde mycle gefean.
 327. And he þær wunode mid him seofon dagas, lærende and
strangende hira heortan on geleafan ures Drihtnes Hælendes Cristes.
 329. Mid þi þe þa wæron gefyllede seofon dagas, swa swa
him Drihten bebead, he ferde of Marmadonia ceastre, efstende to his
discipulum.
 330. And eall þæt folc hine lædde mid gefean and hie
cwædon: An is Drihten God, se is Hælende Crist and se Halga Gast, þam
is wuldor and geweald on þære Halgan þrynnysse þurh ealra worulda
woruld soðlice a butan ende.
 333. Amen.

LS 1.2 (AndrewMor)
B3.3.1.2.
Saint Andrew: Morris 1874-80, 229-37.



 14. Sendon on carcern, & hie hine heton þæt attor etan;
& he hit etan nolde.
 16. Forðon þe his heorte næs tolysedu, ne his mod næs
onwended.
 17. Ah he wæs simle hine to Drihtne gebiddende mid myclum wope,
& cwæð to him, Min Drihten Hælend Crist, forðon we ealle forleton
ure cneorisne & wæron þe fylgende, & þu eart ure ealra fultum,
ða þe on þe gelyfað, beheald nu & geseoh hu þas men þinum
ðeowe doþ.
 21. & ic þe bidde, Dryhten, þæt þu me forgife minra
eagena leoht, þæt ic geseo þa me onginnað don on þisse ceastre ða
werrestan tintrega; & ne forlæt me, min Drihten Hælende Crist, ne
þu me ne syle on þone biterestan deað.
 24. & mid þy þe he þis gebed se eadiga Matheus gecweden
hæfde, mycel leoht & frea beorht onlyhte þæt carcern; &
Drihtnes stefn wæs geworden to him on þæm leohte cweþende, Matheus,
min se leofa, beheald on me.
 28. Se eadiga Matheus þa lociende geseah Drihten Crist; & eft
Drihten wæs cweþende, Matheus, wes þu gestrangod & ne ondræd þu
þe, forþon ne forlæte ic þe æfre; ah ic þe gefreolsige of ealre
frecennesse, & ealle þine broþor, & ealle þa þe on me gelyfað
eallum tidum on ecnesse.
 33. Ac onbid her seofon & twentig nihta; æfter þon ic
sende to þe Andreas þinne broþor, þæt he þe utalædeþ of
þyssum carcerne, & ealle þa ðe mid þe syndon.
 35. & mid þy þe þis gecweden wæs, Drihten him eft
tocwæð, Sib sy mid þe, Matheus.
 36. He þa þurhwunigende mid gebedum wæs Drihtnes lof
singende on þæm carcerne.
 38. & þa unrihtan men ineodan on þæt carcern, þæt
hie þa men utlædan woldan & him to mete don.
 39. Se eadiga Matheus þa betynde his eagan, þe læs þa
cwelleras gesawon þæt his eagan geopenode wæron, & hie cwædon
him betweonum, þry dagas nu to lafe syndon, þæt we hine willað
acwellan & us to mete gedon.
 43. Se eadiga Matheus þa gefylde <foreign>XX</foreign> daga.
 44. Þa Drihten Hælend Crist cwæð to ðæm halgan
Andrea his apostole, mid þy þe he wæs in Achaia þæm lande &
þær lærde his discipuli.
 46. He cwæð, Gang on Mermedonia ceastre, & alæde
þonon Matheum þinne broþor of þæm carcerne, forþon þe nu git
þry dagas to lafe syndon, þæt hie hine willað acwellan & him to
mete don.
 49. Se halga Andreas him andswarede, & he cwæð, Min
Drihten Hælende Crist, hu mæg ic hit on þrim dagum gefaran?
 51. Ac ma wen is þæt þu onsende þinne engel, se hit mæg
hrædlicor geferan; forðon, min Drihten, þu wast þæt ic eom
flæsclic man, & ic hit ne mæg hrædlicor þider geferan, forðon
þe, min Drihten, se siþfæt is þyder to lang, & þone weg ic ne
con.
 55. Drihten Crist him tocwæð, Andreas, gehyre me, forðon
þe ic þe geworhte, & ic þinne siþfæt gestaðelode &
getrymede.
 57. Gang nu to ðæs sæs waroðe mid þinum discipulum;
& þu þær gemetst scip on þæm waroðe; & astig on þæt
mid þinum discipulum.
 59. & mid þy þe he þis cwæð Drihten Hælend
ðagit wæs sprecende & cwæð, Sib mid þe & mid eallum þinum
discipulum.
 61. & he astag on heofenas.
 61. <foreign>Tunc Sanctus Andreas surgens mane abiit ad mare cum discipulis
suis, et uidit nauiculam in litore, et intra naue sedentes tres uiros</foreign>; Se
halga Andreas þa aras on morgen, & he eode to þære sæ mid his
discipulum; & he geseah scip on þæm warþe & þry weras on
þæm sittende.
 66. & he wæs gefeonde myclum gefean, & him to cwæþ,
Broþor, hwyder wille feran mid þys medmyclum scipe?
 67. Drihten Hælende Crist wæs on þæm scipe swa se
steorreþra, & his twegen englas mid him þa wæron gehwyrfde on manna
onsyne.
 70. Drihten Crist him þa to cwæð, On Mermedonia ceastre.
 70. Se halga Andreas him ondswerede & cwæð, Broðor,
onfoh us mid eow on þæt scip, & gelædaþ us on þa ceastre.
 72. Drihten him to cwæð, Ealle men fleoþ of þære
ceastre; to hwam wille ge þyder faran?
 74. Se halga Andreas him andswerede, he cwæþ, Medmycel
ærende we þyder habbað, & us is þearf þæt we hit þeh
gefyllon.
 76. Drihten Hælende Crist him to cwæð, Astigað on þis
scip to us, & syllaþ us eowerne fersceat.
 78. Se halga Andreas him andswerede, Gehyraþ gebroþor, ne
habbað we fersceat.
 79. Ah we syndon discipuli Drihtnes Hælendes Cristes þa he
geceas, & þis bebod he us sealde & he cwæð, þonne ge faran
godspel to lærenne, þonne næbbe ge mid eow hlaf, ne feoh, ne twyfeald
hrægl.
 82. Gif þu þonne wille mildheortnesse us don, sæge us
þæt hrædlice.
 83. Gif þu þonne nelle, gecyþe us swa þeah þone weg.
 84. Drihten him to cwæð, Gif þis gebod eow wære geseald
fram eowrum Drihtne, astigað hider mid gefean on min scip.
 86. Se halga Andreas þa astag on þæt scip mid his
discipulum, & he gesæt be þæm steorreþran þæs scipes,
þæt wæs Drihten Hælend Crist.
 89. Drihten Hælend Crist him to cwæð, Ic geseo þæt
þas broþor synd geswencede of ðisse sæwe hreonesse.
 90. Axa hie hweþer hie woldon to eorþan astigan, & þin
þær onbidan, oþþæt þu gefylle þine þegnunge to þære þe
þu sended eart, & ðu þonne eft hwyrfest to him.
 93. Se halga Andreas him to cwæð, Min bearn, willaþ ge
astigan on eorðan & min þær onbidan.
 94. His discipuli him andswaredon & cwædon, Gif we gewitaþ
fram þe, þonne beo we fremde from eallum þæm godum þe þu us
gegearwodest.
 97. Ac we beoþ mid þe swa hwyder swa þu færest.
 98. Drihten Hælend him to cwæþ to þæm, Gif þu sy
soþlice his discipul se is cweden Crist, sprec to þinum discipulum be
þæm mægenum þe þin lareow dyde, þætte sy geblissad heora
heorte, & hie syn ofergytende þisse sæwe ege.
 101. Se halga Andreas þa cwæð to his discipulum, Sumre tide
mid þy þe we wæron mid urum Drihtne, we astigon mid him on scip.
 104. & he æteowde us swa he slæpende wære to
costianne, ond dyde swiþe hreonesse ðære sæwe, fram þæm winde
wæs geworden, swa þæt þa sylfan yþa wæron ahafene ofer þæt
scip.
 106. We us þa swiþe ondredon & cegdon to him Drihtne
Hælendum Criste, & he þa aras & bebead þæm winde þæt he
gestilde; ða wæs geworden mycel smyltnes on þære sæ; & hi hine
ondredon ealle þa þe hie weorc gesawon.
 110. Nu þonne, min bearn, ne ondrædaþ ge eow, forþon þe
ure God us ne forlæteþ.
 111. Ond þus cweþende se halga Andreas asette his heafod ofer
ænne his discipula & he onslep.
 113. Drihten Hælende Crist þa wiste, forðon þe se halga
Andreas þa slep.
 114. He cwæþ to his englum, Genimaþ Andreas & his
discipuli & asettað hie beforan Mermedonia ceastre; & mid þy ðe
ge hie þær asetton, hweorfað eft to me.
 117. Þa englas þa dydon swa him beboden wæs; & he astag
on heofenas.
 118. Ða se morgen geworden wæs beforan Mermedonia ceastre,
& his discipulos ðær slæpende wæron mid him, & he hie awehte
& cwæð, Arisað ge, mine bearn, & ongytað Godes mildheortnesse,
seo is nu mid us geworden.
 121. Witon we þæt ure Drihten mid us wæs on þæm scipe,
& we hine ne ongeaton; he hine geeaðmedde swa steorreðra, & he hine
æteowde swa swa man us to costiænne.
 124. Se halga Andreas þa locodeon heofenas & he cwæð,
Min Drihten Hælend Crist, ic wat þæt þu ne eart feor fram þinum
þeowum, & ic þe beheold on þæm scipe & ic wæs to ðe
sprecende swa to men.
 127. Nu þonne, Drihten, ic þe bidde þæt þu me þe
æteowe on þisse stowe.
 128. Þa ðis gecweden wæs, Drihten him æteowde his onsyne
on fægeres cildes heowe, & him to cwæð, Andreas, gefeoh mid þinum
discipulum.
 130. Se halga Andreas þa hine gebæd & cwæð, Forgif
me, Drihten þæt ic to ðe sprecende wæs swa to men; wen is þæt ic
gefyrenode, forðon þe ic þe ne ongeat.
 133. Drihten him þa to cwæð, Andreas, ne gefyrenodest þu
nan wuht, ah forðon ðu cwæde þæt þu hit ne mihte on ðrim dagum
hider gefaran, forþon ic þe swa æteowde, forþon ic eom mihtig mid
worde swa eal to donne, & anra gehwylcum to æteowenne swa hwæt swa me
licað.
 137. Nu þonne aris & gang on ða ceastre to Matheum þinum
breþer, & alæde þonne hine of ðare ceastre & ealle þa ðe
mid him syndon.
 140. Eno ic þe gecyþe, Andreas, forþon þe manega tintrega
hie þe onbringað, & þinne lichoman geond þisse ceastre lanan hie
tostenceað, swa þætte þin blod flewþ ofer eorðan swa swa
wæter.
 142. To deaðe hie þe willaþ gelædan, ac hi ne magon; ac
manega earfoðnessa hie þe magon ongebringan, ah þonne hweþre aræfne
þu þa ealle Andreas, & ne do þu æfter heora ungeleaffulnesse.
 145. Gemune ge hu manega earfoðnesse fram Iudeum ic wæs
ðrowiende.
 146. Hie me swungon, & hi me spætlædon on minne
ondwleotan; ah eal ic hit aræfnede þæt ic eow æteowe hwylcum gemete
ge sceolan aræfnan.

LS 2 (DepAugust)
B3.3.2.
Deposition of Saint Augustine in England: Tristram 1970, 428.



 1. <foreign>In die depositionis beati augustini anglorum doctoris</foreign>.
 1. Men ða leofestan we wyllað eow sume gereccednysse cyðan
embe ðyses þurhhaligan symbeldæges mærsunge & wurðunge þe nu
andwerd ys.
 4. Aerest on frymðe us gedafenað to herigenne & to
wuldrigenne ælmihtigne scyppend þurh þæne & on þam synd ealle
gesceafta gesceapene & underðeodde.
 7. He eac swylce hys gecorenan & his haligan on heofena rices
gefean fægere gelogað.
 9. Sume synd gecwedene englas, sume heahenglas.
 10. Ðæge wæron on fruman of godes oroðe & blæde
beorhte gesceapene.
 11. We na durron embe þæt deoppur gereccan for ðon hit ys
unriht ricum ge heanum þæt hi godes diglu deoplice spyrian.
 14. Ac we wyllað embe þæt secgan & reccean þe we of
boca latæ leorniað gelome þæt he heonon geceas haligra mænigu.
 17. Sume wæron heahfæderan healice.

LS 3 (Chad)
B3.3.3.
Saint Chad: Vleeskruyer 1953, 162-84.



 1. <foreign>In natale sancti Ceadde episcopi & confessoris.</foreign>.
 2. Men þa leofestan, ic eow onginnu secgan be þam life þes
halgan weres sancte Ceaddan þes biscopes, hu he dyde in þam biscopdome
oððe er þam biscopdome.
 4. Þeah we nenge þinga magen becuman to eallum þam megenum
his weorca forþon þe in him swa swiðe nes þet he herinesse sohte fram
mannum swa swiðe swa in him wes þet he eall his megen wolde mannum
miðan.
 7. Ah þonne hweðere we eow reccað medmicle intingan of
miclum megenum toþon þet us genihtsumien þa bisne & þa segene be
þam arwyrðan feder.
 10. Se halga wer Ceadda erest wes gehadad in biscopdome fram Alwine
se wes biscop in þere lundoniscan cestre.
 11. Norðhymbra þeoda rixiendum Oswie þam kyninge in þam
selde þe his eftergengan hefdon in þam bolde þe is haten
eoferwicceaster.
 14. Ða com þeodorus se ercebiscop on breotone ealond.
 14. He wes onsended fram þam apostolican selde & mid þy he
manegu ealond geondferde & ealle þing geendebyrde.
 16. He in gelumpenlicum stowum biscopas halgede & þa þe he
unmedume gemette þes godes geleafan he þa gode gefultumiendum gerihte in
þam þingum.
 19. He eac Ceaddan þone biscop erest swiðe þreade & segde
þet he unrihtlice gehalgod were.
 20. He him Ceadda andswearede þere eadmodestan stefne &
cweð, gif þu me on wite þet ic unrihtlice þone biscopdom onfenge ic
þonne lustlice fram þere þegnunge gewitu forðon þe ic me nefre þes
wyrðne wende.
 23. Ac ic for hersumnesse intingan geneded þone had underfeng.
 24. & mid þe swa he geherde þa eadmodnisse his andsware
þa/ cweð he þet he nenge þinga þone biscopdom forletan sceolde ah he
eft edneowunga his hadunga mid þy rihtgeleaffullan rihte gefylde.
 27. Wilfrid eac swilce of breotan ealonde wes onsend & he on
galwalum wes gehadod & forðon he beforan þeodore cærde on cænt
& he þer messepreostas & diaconos hadode oðþet se ercebiscop
þider com.
 31. & þa he com to hrofeceastre þa wes Damianus se biscop
forðfered & he þer gehadode godne wer se wes mid ciriclicum
þeodscipum geseted & in lifes bilwetnisse þoncfulre þonne in
woruldæhtum þes nama wes Putta.
 34. Se ealles tylgest romanisce þeawe song in godes circan þone
song he geleornade æt þam iungrum þes eadigan Gregorius þes papan.
 36. & eft hit gelomp on þa tid þe Wulfhere wes cining fore
mærcna megðum & Germanna his biscop wes dead þa bed he æt
þeodore þam ercebiscope þet him & his ðeode were biscop sald.
 39. He him nalde neowne biscop hadian ac he bed æt Oswio þam
cininge þet him were sald Ceadda se biscop Se þa git hefde stille lif in
his mynstre þet wes gehaten in lestinga ege.
 42. & Wilferð wes þere cirican biscop in eoferwicceastre
& nohte þon les ealra norðhymbra ah eac swilce pehta swa hwider swa se
cining Oswi his rice mihte þennan.
 44. & þa wes þeaw þam ilcan arwyrþestan biscope
Ceaddan þet he godspell geond stowe bodade ma gongende þonne ridende &
he þa þeodorus heht hine þet he swa hwider swa him long weg stode &
he þa swiðe higienda mid geornfulnisse & mid lufan þes arfullan
gewinnes.
 49. Hine se ercebiscop mid his agene hond on horse ahof forðon
þe he hine swiðe haligne wer gemette & he hine nedde þet he swa
hwider on horse wegen were swa hit neodþearf were.
 52. & þa onfeng Ceadda mærcna þeode biscopdom samod on
lindesfarena efter þere bisne ealdra federa & he teolede þet he þa
þeode gehelde in micelre lifes gefremednisse.
 54. Þam biscope Wulfhere se cining gesealde landes fiftig hida in
þere stowe seo is gecweden æt bearwe & þet is in þere megðe
lindesse þer nu git todege wuniað þa gesettan swaðe his lifes.
 57. He hefde eft biscopseld in þere stowe seo is gecweden
licetfeld in þere he forðferde & bebyriged wes þer nu git todege is
þet seld efterfylgendra þere mægðæ biscopa.
 60. He warhte eac degulran eardungstowe in þere he synderlicor
mid feawum þet wes mid seofenum oððe mid ehta broðrum swa oft swa he
hine fram þam gewinne & þes wordes þegnungæ geemetgade þet he
Ceadda þer him gebed & bec redde.
 64. He eac in þere ilcan megðe on twam gearum & on halfum
gere þa wuldelicestan cirican arerde þa wes æt seo tid þam uplican
dome stihtendum be þere sprec seo ciriclice domboc, Tid is stanas to settenne
& to somnienne.
 67. Þet wes gecweden be þam cwalme his lichaman þet he
sceolde his þone halgan gast sendan of þisum eorðlican sældum to þam
heofonlican getimbrum.
 70. Mittes per monige broðore of þere gesomnunge þes
arwurðestan biscopes of lichama atogene weron þa com his tid Ceaddan þet
he sceolde faran of þysum middangearde to drihtne.
 73. Ða gelomp hit sume dege þet he Ceadda wunade in þere
foresegdan eardungstowe mid anum breþer þes gecignis wes Owine & þa
oðre broðru to cirican gewitene weron fore sumum gelumpenlicum intingan.
 76. Se ilca Owine wes munuc micelre geearnunge & clenre
ingehygde & he abad þet uplice edlean & he forlæt þisne
middangeard & he wes meodum on eallum þingum & him swutulice drihten
his digolnesse onwrah.
 80. He com mid Eþelðryden cwene of eastengla mægðæ
& he wes ældost hire þegna & ealdormon hire heordes se mid þy
waxendum þes geleafan getihhade þet he þas woruld forhogode.
 82. Ne dyde he þet naht slaulice ac he hine eallum middangeardas
ehtum ongerede & forletenum eallum þam woroldþingum þe he hefde.
 85. He hine gegerede mid anfalde gegerelan & ber acse &
eadusan him on honda & com to þam mynstre þes arwurðestan fæder
Ceaddan.
 87. Þet wes geciged læstinga æg ne com he to idelnesse to
þam mynstre swa sume men doþ ac he tacnade þet he to gewinne in þet
mynster eode þet he mid weorcum gecyðde.
 89. Cuðlice se ilca Owine mid þone biscop in þere forsegdan
eardungstowe betwih oðrum broðrum wes hefd for his megenes arwurðnesse
æste mitte se biscop Ceadda þerinne bec redde & he þerute warhte swa
hwet swa hit gesegen wes þet hit þearf wes.
 93. Se mid þy þyslices hwethugu sume dege þerute warhte &
se biscop wes ana in his gebedhuses stowe þer he bocredan & gebedum werc
sealde þa geherde he feringa þesþe he efterþon segde þa swetestan
stefne singendra & blissendra of heofonum to eorðan niðer astigan.
 98. Þa stefne he erest geherde easten & suþan þet wes
fram þes heofones heanisse & syððan sticcemelum him neolecan
oðþet he becom ofer þone hrof þes gebedhuses in þam se biscop Ceadda
wes þet he in gongende all gefylde & in ymbhwyrfte ymbsalde.
 102. & he þa ymbhydelice his mod fæstnade in þa þing
þe he þer geherde & þa geherde he feringa swaswa agongnum halfre tide
fyrst of þes ilcan gebedhuses hrofe þone ilcan blisse song upp astigan
& þy wege þe he com to heofonum beon gecerredne mid unaseggendlicræ
swetnisse.
 106. & mitte hit þa wunade on þere stowe swaswa tide fec
swilce hit þunurrad were & he þa ymbhygdie mode spyrede hwet þet
were.
 108. Ða ontynde se biscop Ceadda þet egðyrl þes gebedhuses
& hof his honda upp swaswa he foroft gewunade þet he dyde & sealde
his bletsunge & bebead gif þer hwa ute were þet he þonne in to him
eode.
 111. & þa eode he ricene in to him & þa cweð se
biscop to him, fer þu ricene to cirican & gedo þu þet heo hider cuman
þas ure seofen broðru & beo þu eac mid heom.
 114. Mittes heo þa swa comon þa manode he Ceadda heo erest
þet hi lufan & megen & sibbe him betweonum & ealle geleafnisse
heoldon mid ealre anrednesse & þet hi eac swylce þa gesettan
þeodscipas & regolþeawas þa þe hi et him geleornadon & in him
gesegen oððe in foregongendra fedora dedum oððe cwidum gemetun þet
heo þet eall efestlice heoldon & fyligdon.
 120. Syððan he him þa underþeodde & cyðde þone deg
his forðfore þe þa iu him neh stod.
 121. He cweð, se leofwynda cuma se gewunade þet he þa ure
broðra neosade he nu todeg wes geeadmodad þet he me walde of þissere
worulda gecigen.
 123. Cerrað ge forþon to cirican & secgað urum broðrum
þet heo minne endedeg drihtne mid benum ætfestun & þet hi eac swilce
gemynen þet hi heora utgong forecumen þes tid is uncuð mid godum weorcum
& mid weacenum & mid gebedum.
 127. & mittes he þas sprec & manegu þisum gelic hi þa
onfengon/ his bletsunge þa hi swiðe unrote ut eodon ða cerde se an se
þone heofonlicon song geherde & þenede hine on þa eorðan &
cweð, Feder, is me alyfed þet ic þe mote ohtes fregnan?
 131. Þa cweð he Cedda, fregn þes þe þu wille.
 131. Þa cweð he to þam biscope, Ic þe halsie þet þu me
secge hwet wes se blissendra song þe ic geherde of heofonum cuman ofer þis
gebædhus & efter tide fece he wes gecerred to heofonum.
 134. Ða answarude se biscop Ceadda him & cweð, Gif þu
songes stefne geherdest & heofonlicne þreat geherdest cuman ofer þis
gebedhus ic þe þonne bebeodu on drihtnes naman þet þu hit nenegum men
ne asecge er minre forðfore.
 138. Cuðlice ic þe secge þet hit weron engla gastas þa
comon me gecigan to þam heofonlican rice þa ic a lufade & þes
edleanes to him wilnade & heo me gehehton þet heo nu æfter seofon
dagum hider gecerde weron & me mid him geleadan wolden.
 142. Þet eallswa hit mid wordum gecweden wes swa hit wes mid
weorcum gefylled.
 143. & he þa ricene mid lichaman ece wes gehrinen & þa
þy seofoðan dege swaswa him gehaten wes efter þere onfongnisse þes
drihtenlican lichaman & his blodes seo halige sawul wes onlesedu of þam
carcerne þes lichaman & hio wes gelededu swa hit riht is to gelefenne mid
engla þreatum to þam ecan gefean.
 148. Nes þet naht wunderlic þet he þone deaþes deg swa
unforht abad forþon þe hit nes deaðes deg ac his wes tylig drihtnes
blisse deg þone he swa bliðe ymbhygdelice abad þet wes in monegum
forhæfdnisse/ & in eadmodnisse & in gebedu lare & on wilsumre
þearfednisse & in manegum megena geearnungum.
 153. & ealles swiþest he wes in eallum his weorcum godes
lufan gemyndig & his þera nehstena.
 154. Swa hit sum broðor segde þone he in gewritum lerde &
he wes in his mynstere & in his laredome gelered þes nama wes
Trumberht.
 157. He segde, gif þet gelumpe þet se biscop Ceadda his bec
redde oððe hwet swilces dyde gif þes windes bled mare aras þonne hit
gewunelic were he þonne ricene gecigde drihtnes mildheortnesse & bed
þet manncynne gemiltsade.
 160. Gif þonne strengra se wind astod he þonne betynedre þere
bec, forðleat in his anseone & geornlicor þam gebede gefalh.
 162. & gif þonne git se storm wes strengra oððe yste
þeosne middangeard bregdon & þunurrade & lægetas on eorðan
& lyftas þreadon he þonne ricene com to cirican & þer
ymbhygdelicor gebeodum & salmsongum feste mode emetgade oðþet þes
lyftes smyltnes cerde.
 166. & mittes hine fregnaden his gingran forhwon he þet dyde
ða andwyrde he him & cweð, Ac ne leornaden ge þet drihten leoðrað
of heofone & se hesta seleð his stefne he sendeð his strelas & he
hio tostenceð, he gemonigfaldað legeto & he heo gedrefeð?
 170. Drihten onstyreð lyftas & awecceð windas.
 171. He sceotað legeto & he leoðrað of heofone þet he
þa eorðlican mod awecce hine to ondredenne & þet he heora heortan
gecige in þa gemynd þes toweardan domes & þet he heora oferhygd
tostence & heora bældu gedrefe & heora gemynd gelede to þere
beofugendlican/ tide þonne he bið toweard to demene cwice & deade
heofones & eorðan beornendum & in micelre mihte & megenþrymme.
 177. Forðon us gedafenað, cweð se biscop Ceadda, þet we his
monunge/ þere heofonlican andswarien mid gedefe ege & lufan þet swa oft
swa drihten on lyfte his handa onstyrie swaswa he beotige us to slenne &
þonne hweðere þonne gyt ne slæð.
 181. Bidden we sona ymbhygdilice his mildheortnisse þet we
toslegenum ure heortena digolnessum & geclensade ure uncysta scamum þet
we geearnien þet we nefre seon slegene in þam ecan wite.
 184. Hit gelomp be þere forðfore þes foresegdan biscopes
þet com to hys gemynde onwrignesse þet word þes arwurðestan fæder
Egberhtes se geara mid þone ilcan Ceaddan iungne & hio begen ginge on
scotta ealonde syndrig munuclif hæfdon.
 187. & hi þoncfulle weron in gebecum & in forhefednisse
& in leornunge godcundra gewrita.
 189. Ac efterþon þe he wes gecerred on his æþel se oðer
elþeodig for drihtnes lufan þurhwunade oð his lifes ende.
 190. Mittes him to com of breotene ealonde æfter longe tide mid
neosunge gefe se halgesta wer & se þoncfullista þes nama wes Hygbald se
wes abbud in þere megðe lindesse & þa dydon hi swa hit halgum
gedafnade sprecon be þam life þera erran hæhfædera.
 194. & hio gefegun heora somnunge.
 195. Heo comon to þere gemyndæ þes arwurðestan biscopes
Ceaddan.
 196. Ða cweð sanctus ægberht, Ic wat enne man in þisum
ealonde mittes se halga wer Ceadda se biscop ferde of þisum middangearde
þe/ he geseh his broðor saule mid micle engla werode niðer astigan of
heofone & genam mid hine his saule & to þam heofonlican rice eft
gecerde.
 200. Ðonne hweðere us þet wunað uncuð hweðer he hit be
him seolfum segde hweðer þe be oðrum men hwylcum ac þonne hweðere
þet ne meg uncuð beon þet swa swiðe halig wer segde.
 203. Sancte Ceadde forðferda in þam dege sexta nonas martis.
 204. & he wes erest bebyrged be sancta Marian cirican ac
efterþon þer mon getimbrade cirican & gehalgode þam eadigestan þera
apostole ealdre sancte Petre.
 206. In gehweðre þera stowa gelomlico helo & wundra beoð
gewrohte to cuðnesse his megena.
 208. Hit gelomp þet sum woda se eall þet lond dwoligende
geondearn þet he on efenne þider becom swa þa nyston oððe ne gemdon
þe þere stowe heordas weron & he þer ealle niht gereste & on
margene mid gehelde andgitte ut eode.
 211. & he cudde eallum þam mannum wundrigendum hwet him þer
drihten to helo forgifen hefde.
 213. Seo stow þere byrgene wes treowene þruh & heo wes
gewarht ufan on huses gelicnesse.
 214. & þer stondeþ wigbed be þere þruh þet hafeð
þyrel on þam wage þurh þet gewuniað þa men þe þa stowe secað
& tocumað þet hio heora hand þerin sendað & del þes dustes
þanon genemað.
 217. & mittes hit mon in weter sendað & seleð untruman
horsum oððe nutenum oððe mannum to byrgenne þonne sona seo uneþnis
þere untrumnesse intingan onweg gewitað & þere helo gefea him
tocerreð.
 220. In þere stowe þeodorus gehadode Wynferð, godne wer &
gemetfestne swa his forgengan mercna megða, on middelengla, on lindesfarena,
biscophades þegnunge forewes in eallum þam þingum Wulfere þa git wes
ofer & rices anwald hæfde.
 224. Se Wynferð wes of preosthade þes biscopes þe he
æfterfylgede & he diacones þegnunge under him bræc naht fea tide.
 226. Genihtsumien us nu, men þa leofestan, þas þe us segd
earun be þam arwurðan biscope sancte Ceaddan & þeah þe us
medmicelo/ of micclum beon gesegde þonne hweðere beon we gewisse his lifes
& his drohtunge gemyndig, hu he dyde ær þes biscophades onfongnisse ge
in þam biscophade.
 230. Eale, þet wes eadig wær in þam ne wes enig inwit ne he
nenigne fordemde ne he nenigne gehende ne he nanegum men yfel for yfele gealt
ac he wið eallum earfodnissum & teonum nam geþyldu.
 233. & mittes he wes heh biscop on orleahtre & swilce
þeah þe he fram untrumum & unwisum preostum were gedered na geseah hine
mon efre forðon eorne ne mid hatheortnesse onstyredne ne nenig man hine
geseah swiðe hlahendne ne nenig man hine geseah swiðe grorniende.
 237. Ac he a an & þet ilce sume gemete heofonlice blisse ber
on his onseone.
 239. Nes nefre in his muðe nympðe crist nympðe mildheortnis.
 239. Bidden we nu men þa untodeledlican þrinnesse þet we mid
þam benum þes halgestan weres sancte Ceaddan seon gefultumade þet we
geearnian þet we magen becuman to þam geferscipe haligra biscopa &
eadigra gasta forgifendum urum drihtne helendum criste se leofað &
rixað mid þam feder & mid þam haligan gasta in eallre worulda woruld,
Amen.

LS 4 (Christoph)
B3.3.4.
Saint Christopher: Rypins 1924, 68-76.



 1. Mines dryhtnes hælendes Cristes ac þu dysig &
unsnotor þu ðe ne ondrætst dryhten se ys ealra þinga scyppend.
 3. Se cyninge þa yrre geworden wæs & het gebindan his
handa/ & hys fet tosomne & he hyne het swingan mid isernum gyrdum
& he het settan on his heafde.
 7. Þry weras þa cempan þa ðe hyne swungan gecwædon to
ðam cyninge, eadig wær ðu Dagnus gif þu næfre geboren nære þu
ðe þus wælgrimlice hetst tintregian þillicne godes cempan.
 11. Se cyningc þa yrre geworden wæs & he het þære
ylcan tide þa weras acwellan.
 13. Se halga Cristoforus cigde to þæm cynige & cwæð,
gyf þu hwylce maran witu be me geþoht hæbbe hrædlice, do ðu þa
for ðon þine tintrego me synt swettran þonne huniges beobread.
 17. Se cyningc þa het bringan isenne scamol se wæs emnheah
þæs mannes upwæstme þæt wæs twelf fæðma lang & he hyne
het asettan on middan þa ceastre & þone halgan Cristoforus he het
þær to gebindan.
 21. & he het beneoðan him þæt unmætoste fyr onælan
& myt ty þe þæs fyres lig on þære mæstan hæto wæs he
þær ofer het geotan tyn orcas fulle eles þæt he wolde þæt
þæs fyres hæto þe reðre wære & þe ablæstre on þone
halgan man.
 26. Se halga Cristoforus þa on middum þam reðestan &
þam unmætostan liges bæle he cigde to drihtne beorhtre stefne & he
cwæð to ðam cyninge, þas tintrego þe ðu on me bringan hehst to
þinre gecyndnesse & to þinre forwyrde becumað.
 31. & ic me næfre þine tintrego ne ondræde ne þin
yrre.
 32. & mit ty þe he þis cwæð se halga on middes
þæs fyres mænigo se scamull him wæs geworden eall swa geþywed
weax.
 35. Þa geseah Dagnus se cyningc þone halgan Cristoforus on
middum þam fyre standende & he geseah þæt his ansyn wæs swylce
rosan blostma.
 38. Myt ty þe he þæt geseah he wæs on miceles modes
wafunga & for þæs eges fyrhto he wæs swa abreged þæt he gefeol
on eorðan & þær læg fram þære ærestan tide þæs
dæges oð ða nigoþan tide.
 43. Þæt þa geseah se halga Cristoforus he hyne het up
arisan.
 44. & myt ty þe he up aras he him to cwæð, þu wyrresta
wilddeor, hu lange dyrstlæcest þu þæt ðu þis folc fram me tyhtest
swa þæt him nis alyfed þæt hi minum godum onsecgen?
 48. Se halga Cristoforus hin andswarode & cwæð, nu git
micel folces mænio þurh me gelyfað on minne drihten hælend Crist
& æfter þon þu selfa.
 51. Se cyningc þa him andswarode bysmerigende & him to
cwæð, is þæs wen þæt ðu me swa beswican mæge þæt ic
þone god gebidde & minum wiðsace?
 53. Wite þu þonne þæt ðys mergenlican dæge æt
þisse sylfan tide ic wrece minne teonan on þe & ic gedo þæt ðu
byst forloren & þin nama of þys gemynde & of þyssum life
adilgod.
 57. & þu scealt wesan ealra bysen þara þe ðurh þe on
ðinne god gelyfað.
 59. Oðre dæge þa se cyninge het þone halgan Cristoforus to
him gelædan & him to cwæð, ongit min word & onsaga minum godum
þæt ðu on swa manegum tintregum ne forweorðe swa ðe gegearwode
synt.
 63. Se halga him andswarode & cwæð symle, þine goda ic
laðette & him teonan do for þon þe minne geleafan ic unwemne geheold
þone þe ic on fulwihte onfeng.
 67. Se cyningc þyder þa het bringan unmætre micelnesse
treow þæt wæs efnheah þæs halgan mannes lengo & he hit het
asettan beforan þære healle & he hyne het þær on gefæstnian
& bebead þæt ðry cempan hyne scotedon mid hyra strælum oð
þæt he wære acweald.
 72. Þa cempan hyne þa scotedon fram þære ærestan tide
þæs dæges oð æfen.
 74. Se cyningc þa wende þæt ealle þa strælas on his
lichaman gefæstnode wæron ac ne furþonan his lichaman ne gehran.
 76. Ac godes mægen wæs on ðam winde hangigende æt
þæs halgan mannes swyðran healfe.
 78. & se cyningc þa æfter sunnan setlgange he sende to
ðam cempum & he bead þæt hi hyne swa gebundenne geornlice heoldon
for ðon he wende þæt þæt cristene folc hyne wolde onlysan þy
mergenlican dæge.
 83. Þa se cyningc wæs ut gangende to þam halgan Cristoforus
& him to cwæþ, hwær ys þin god for hwon ne com he & þe
gefreolsode of minum handum & of þyssum egeslican strælum?
 87. Hraðe þa myt ty þe he þas word gecwæð twa flana of
þam strælum scuton on þas cyninges eagan & he þurh þæt wæs
ablend.
 90. Þæt þa geseah se halga Cristoforus he him to cwæð,
þu wælgrimma & þu dysega, wite þu þæt ðis mergenlican
dæge æt þære eahtoðan tide þæs dæges ic onfo minne sigor
& dryhten.
 94. Sylf me wæs ætywed þæt cristene men cumað &
onfoð mines lichaman & hyne gesettaþ on þa stowe þe him fram
drihtne ætywed wæs.
 97. Cum þonne to minum lichaman & nym þære eorðan lam
þe ic on gemartyrod wæs & meng wið min blod & sete on þine
eagan.
 100. Þonne gif þu gelyfst on god of ealre heortan þære
sylfan tide þu bist gehæled fram þinra eagena blindnesse.
 102. Wite þu þæt seo tid nealæceð þæt Cristforus
godes se gecorena onfehð his gewinna mede & geliffæsted ferð to
drihtne þy mergenlican dæge ær þam þe he fram þam cempum acweald
wære.
 107. Þyssum wordum he ongan gebiddan & cweþan, drihten
ælmihtig, þu ðe me of gedwolan gehwyrfdest & godne wisdom
gelærdest þæt ic þin þeow nu on þysse tide þe bidde gearwa hyt
me þætte on swa hwylcre stowe swa mines lichaman ænig dæl sy ne sy
þær ne wædl ne fyres broga.
 113. & gif þær neah syn untrume men & hig cumon to
þinum þam halgan temple & hig þær gebiddon to þe of ealre
heortan & for þinum naman hi ciggen minne naman gehæl þu þone
drihten fran swa hwylcere untrumnesse swa hie forhæfde.
 118. & on ðære ylcan tide stefn wæs gehyredu to him
cweþendu, Cristoforus min þeow, þin gebed ys gehyred.
 121. Þeah þin lichama ne sy on þære stowe swa hwyllce
geleaffulle men swa þines naman on heora gebedum beoð gehælede fram hyra
synnum & swa hwæs swa hie rihtlice biddaþ for þinum naman & for
þinum geearningum hig hyt onfoð.
 126. Mit ty þe þeos wuldorlice spræc of heofenum wæs
gehyredu & gefylledu hraðe fram þam cempum he wæs slegen & he on
þære mæstan blisse & unasecgendlican wuldre he ferde to criste.
 130. & þæt wæs wundor þæs folces þe se halga
Cristoforus þurh his lare gode gestrynde þæt wæs eaht & feower
þusenda manna & hundteontig & fiftyne.
 134. Oþre dæge þa se cyningc cwæð to his þegnum, uton
gangan & geseon hwær þa cempan hyne gesett habbon.
 136. & mit ty þe hit becomon to þære stowe þær se
halga lichama wæs se cyningc cigde micelre stemne & cwæð,
Cristoforus, ætyw me nu þines godes soðfæstnesse & ic gelyfe on
hyne.
 140. & he genam dæl þære eorðan þær þæs
cristes martyr wæs on þrowigende & medmicel þæs blodes &
mengde tosomne & sette on his eagan.
 143. & he cwæð, on naman Cristoforus godes ic þis dem.
 144. & hraðe on ðære ylcan tide his eagan wæron
ontynde & gesihþe he onfeng & he cigde micelre stemne & he
cwæð beforan eallum þam folce, wuldorfæst ys & micel cristenra
manna god.
 148. Þæs wuldorgeworces nane mennisce searwa ofercuman ne
magon.
 150. Ic þonne nu fram þyssum dægenlican dæge ic sende
mine bebodu geond eall min rice þætte nan mon þe to mines rices anwealde
belimpe ne gedyrstlæce nan wuht do ongean þæs heofonlican godes willan
þe Cristoforus beeode.
 155. Gif þonne ænig man þurh deofles searwa to þon
beswicen sy þæt hyt gedyrstlæce on þære ylcan tide sy he mid
swyrde witnod for þon ic nu soðlice wat þæt nan eorðlic anweald ne
nan gebrosnodlic nys noht butan his anes.
 159. & swa þa wæs geworden þurh godes miht & þurh
geearnunga þæs eadigan Cristoforus þætte se cyningc gelyfde se wæs
ær deofles willan full.
 163. Þæs eadigan Cristoforus wuldorgeworc synd nu lang to
asecgane þe dryhten þurh hyne geworhte to herennesse his naman & nu
oð þyssne dæg wyrcð.
 166. For þon þe þær nu blowað & growað his þa
halgan gebedu & þær ys drihtnes hyrnes mid ealre sybbe & gefean
& þær ys gebletsod crist godes sunu lyfigendes se rixað mid
fæder & mid suna & mid þam halgan gaste a butan ende.
 172. Þyses eac bæd se halga Cristoforus of þære nihstan
tide ær he his gast onsende & cwæð, drihten min god syle gode mede
þam þe mine þrowunga awrite & þa ecean edlean þam þe hie mid
tearum/ ræde.
