LS 8 (Eust)
B3.3.8.
Saint Eustace and his Companions: Skeat 1881-1900, II, 190-218.



 1. <foreign>IIII NON NOVEMBR, PASSIO SANCTI EUSTACHII MARTYRIS SOCIORVMGUE
EIVS</foreign>.
 1. ON TRAIANES DAGVM ðæs caseres rixiendum, deofolgilda
biggenga wæs sum cempena ealdorman þæs nama wæs Placidas, æfter
worulde swiðe æþelboren, and swiþe þeonde on his weorcum, and ealle
oferhlifigende on wurðmynte.
 4. Wæs he soðlice on rihtwisnysse weorcum, and on eallum godum
weorcum, swiðe gefrætwod; ofþryhtum he gehealp, and gemundbyrde þa
ðe fordemde wæron, and eac swilce he for wel manega þe unrihtlice fram
yflum demum genyþrode wæron alyhte.
 8. Nacode he scrydde; and swa ic soðlice secge, ealle
nydbehæfnysse he wæs dælende, þam þe þæs behofodon; and eac
swilce his wif þa ylcan godan weorc beeode, ac hi swaþeah hwæðere butu
þa git hæðene wæron, forþam þe him nan man þone godcundan
geleafan ne tæhte.
 12. Hi hæfdon twægen suna þa hi tyhton þæt hi him
geefenlæhton on godum willan.
 14. Wæs he witodlice swiðe æþele on rihtwisnysse, and
strang on gefeohte, swa þæt þa hæþenan wæron fram him swiðe
gewylde.
 16. Wæs he eac wel gleaw on huntunge, and þæt singallice
ælce dæge beeode.
 17. Ac se mildheorta and se welwillenda God, þe simle
æghwær to him þa þe him wurðe beoð gecygð, ne forseah his godan
weorc, ne he nolde þæt his welwillende mod, and Gode swiðe wurðful,
buton mede sceolde beon forlætan, and mid ðam þystrum þæs
deofollican biggenges oferwrigen beon.
 21. Ac æfter þam þe hit awriten is, þæt on ælcre
þeode þe rihtwisnysse wyrcð him bið andfencge, he becom þa to þysse
welwillendan mildheortnysse, and hine mid þyllicum gemete gehælde.
 24. Hit gelamp sume dæge þæt he ferde ut on huntað mid
eallum his werode and his wuldre; þa geseah he micelne floc heorta, and he
ða gestihte his werod swa him gewunelic wæs, hu hi on þone huntað fon
sceoldon.
 27. Þa hi ealle ymb þone huntað abysgode wæron, þa
æteowde himsylfum an ormæte heort, se wæs ormætre mycelnysse ofer
ealle ða oþre, and wlitig, and þa gewende he fram þam flocce, and
ræsde into þam wudu þær he þiccost wæs.
 31. Þa þæt Placidas geseah, þa gewilnode he þæt he
hine gefenge, and him geornlice æfter ferde, mid fæwum geferum.
 33. Þa æt nixtan wurdon hi ealle geteorode, and he ana unwerig
him æfterfyligde.
 34. Witodlice þurh Godes forestihtunge, ne hors ne he sylf
gewergod wæs, ne he for ðæs weges earfoðnysse ablan, ac he lange
æfter ferde, and feor fram his geferum gewat.
 37. Se heort þa witodlice astah on anne heahne clud, and
þær gestod.
 38. Placidas ða lange stod, and beheold þone heort, and
wundrode his micelnysse, and ablan his æhtan.
 40. Him þa god geswutelode þæt he him swilcne dom ne
ondrede, ne his mægnes micelnysse ne wundrode.
 41. Witodlice betwux þæs heortes hornum glitenode gelicnys
þære halgan Cristes rode breohtre þonne sunnan leoma, and seo anlicnysse
ures Drihtnes Hælendes Cristes, and he mennisce spræce asende on þone
heort, and clypode to Placidam þus cwæþende, Eala Placida, hwi ehtest
þu min?
 46. Efne for þinum intingum ic com nu, þæt ic þurh þis
nyten þe me ætywde.
 47. Ic eom se Crist þe þu nytende wurðast, þa ælmyssan
þe þu þearfum dest, beforan me syndon, and ic com þæt ic me þe
ætywde þurh þysne heort, and for hine þe gehuntian and gefon mid þam
nettum minre mildheortnysse.
 50. Nis hit na riht þæt min se leofa þeow for his godum
weorcum þeowige unclænum deoflum, and þam unwittigum heargum; þurh
þæt ic com to eorðan on þisum hiwe swilcne þu me nu gesihst,
þæt ic mancynn gehælde.
 53. Þa ða Placidas þis gehyrde, þa wæs he afyrht mid
þam mæstan ege, and feoll of his horse to eorðan, and þær læg
sume tid dæges, and aras þa eft, and wolde gewislicor witan ymbe þa
ætywnysse þe him æteawde, and cwæð to himsylfum, Hwæt is þeos
gesihð þe me her æteawde?
 58. Drihten leof, onwreoh me hwæt ðu to me spræce, þæt
ic on þe gelyfan mæge.
 59. Þa cwæð Crist to him, Hlyst nu, Placida.
 60. Ic eom Hælende Crist, þe heofon and eorðan of nanan
þingan geworhte, and gedyde þæt leoht up asprang, and þystro
todælde, and ic eom se ðe gesette dagas and tida and gear, and ic eom se
ðe man of eorðan gehiwode.
 63. And for mancynnes hælo ic com to eorðan, and flæsc
underfeng, and ahangen wæs, and bebyrged, and þy þriddan dæge of
deaðe aras.
 65. Þa Placidas þis gehyrde þa feoll he eft sona on eorþan
and cwæð, Ic gelyfe, Drihten, þæt þu eart se ðe ealle þincg
geworhtest, and gecyrst ða dweliendan, and deade geliffestast.
 68. Þa cwæð Drihten to him, Gif ðu on me gelyfst, far to
þære byrig to Cristenra manna bisceope, and bide hine fulluhtes.
 70. Ða cwæð Placidas, Drihten leof, mot ic þis cyðan
minum wife, and minum cildum, þæt hi gelyfan on þe?
 72. Þa cwæð Drihten to him, far nu, and sege hiom þæt
hi fulwiht onfon, and ge beoð þonne geclænsode fram deofolgilda
besmitennysse, and cum hider eft, and ic þe fullicor ætywe, and þe
cyþe þa ðe toweard syndon, and onwreo þa halgan gerynu.
 75. Hwæt ða Placide on niht þanon ham ferde, and his wife
rehte eall þæt he geseah.
 77. Sona swa heo hit gehyrde þa cwæð heo, Hlaford min,
þone God þu gesawe, þe ahangen wæs, þe Cristene men wurþiað.
 78. He soðlice is ana soð God þe þurh swilce tacna
gecigeð to him þa þe on hine gelyfað, and on þissere nihte ic hine
geseah, and he cwæð to me, nu tomergen þu, and þin wer, and þine
suna cumað to me.
 82. And nu ic oncneow þæt he sylf a is Hælende Crist.
 82. Witodlice he wolde under swilcum hiwe wundorlicre wæfersyne
þurh þone heort ætywan, þæt þu þy swiþor wundrie his mihta,
and on hine gelyfe.
 85. Uton nu faran on þisse nihte, and begitan us þæt halige
fulluht Cristenra manna, þurh þæt soðlice beoð his agenne þa ðe
on hine gelyfað.
 87. Þa cwæð Placidas to hire, þæt ylce me sæde se
þe ic geseah.
 88. Þa soðlice to middre nihte hi ferdon swa heora men nyston
to Cristenra manna sacerda, and rehton him ealle þincg þe him ætywde
wæron, and þæt hi on God gelyfdon, and halsodon hine þæt he hi
gefullode.
 91. Se bisceop wæs ða mid micelre blisse gefylled, and
wuldrode God, se þe wile þæt ealle menn hale beon, and to
soðfæstnysse wege becumað.
 93. And he hi þa gecristnode, and tæhte hi þa geryna þas
halgan geleafan, and gefullode hi on naman fæder and sunu and þæs
halgan gastes, and nemde Placidam Eustachium, and his wif Theophistim, and his
anne suna Agapitum, and oþerne Theofistum.
 97. And sealde hi þæt halige geryne Cristes lichaman and
blodes, and forlet hi þus cwæþende, Drihten Hælende Crist, þæs
lifigendan Godes sunu, sy mid eow, and forgife eow þa ecan rica.
 100. Soðlice ic oncnawe þæt Godes bletsung is mid eow;
brucað ge Godes neorxnewonges and gemunað min Iohannis, ic bidde eow.
 102. Þa soþlice eft on ærnemergen genam Eustachius feawa
geferan, and ferde to ðære stowe þær he ær þa gesyhðe geseah,
and tosende his geferan swilce for huntoðes intingan.
 104. And he ana belaf and nealæhte to þære stowe, and
geseah þa ylcan gesihðe þe he ær geseah, and feol niþer on his
ansyne and cwæð, Ic halsige þe Drihten, and ic oncnawe þæt þu
eart Hælend Crist, þæs lifigendan Godes sunu.
 108. And nu ic hider com, and bidde þine untodæledlican
godcundnysse, þæt þu me geswutelige þæt þu me ær behete.
 110. Ða cwæð Hælend to him, Eadig þu eart þe onfenge
þone þweal minre gife and þe gegyredest mid undeadlicnysse.
 111. And nu þu oferswiðdest deofol and fortræde þone þe
þe beswac, and nu ðu unscryddest þe þone brosnigendlican mann, and þe
gescryddest þone unbrosnigendlican, se þurhwunað a on worulde.
 114. Nu beoð geswutelode þa weorc þines geleafan, and deofles
anda bið astyred wið þin, forðan þu hine forlæte, and efest
þæt he ælc yfel do ymbutan þe.
 117. Þe gedafenaþ soðlice fela aræfnian, þæt þu
onfo wuldorbeah.
 117. Efne þu wære nu oð þis upahafen on þisse worulde
æhtum, and hwilwendum weorcum, nu gedafnað þe þæt þu beo
geeaðmet of þire hean idelnysse, þæt þu eft beo upahafen on
gastlicum welum.
 120. Ne ateorige þin mægen, ne ðu ne beseoh to þinum
ærran wuldre.
 121. Ac eall swa þu gewilnodest þæt þu mannum gelicodest
þurh þin sigefæst gefeoht, and þam deadlican cynincge, swa þe eac
gedafenað to efstenne þæt þu me þam undeadlican cynincge þine
trywa gehealde, and on þissum tidum beon gecostnod þurh þrowunga and
geswinc, swa min se leofa ðeow Iob, and deofles oferswiðend þurh
geþyld.
 127. Warna huru þæt nan wyrgung and ceorung astige on þinum
geþohte.
 128. Soðlice þonne þu bist geeaðmodad ic cume to ðe, and
gelæde þe eft to þinum agenum wuldre and wurðscipe.
 129. Þa æfter þysse spræce, astah Crist to heofonum, and
cwæð to Eustachio, hwæðer is ðe leofre þe ðu nu onfo þa
costnunga, þe near þinum ende.
 132. Þa cwæð Eustachius, Ic halsige Drihten Hælend buton
hit unaræfnedlic sy to ofercumenne, þa þing þe us synd fram ðe
forestihtode læt us nu onfon þa costnunge, and syle us geðyld to
aræfnigenne, þylæs se awyrgeda feond astyrige þæt we ænig
þing cwæþan and geþencan ongen þinne willan.
 136. Drihten him to cwæð, Eustachi, winn ongen; soðlice min
gifu is mid eow, and gehylt eowre sawla.
 138. Eustachius gewende þa ham, and arehte his wife eall þæt
him fram Drihtne gesæd wæs, and hi bigdon heora cneowa, and bædon God
cweðende, Drihten Hælend, beo hit swa þin wylla sy.
 141. Þa gelamp hit æfter feawum dagum þæt his hired
wæs gestanden mid cwylmendre adle, and wæron deada, ægðer ge his
þeowas ge þeowena.
 143. Þa ongeat Eustachius þæt seo foresæde costnung him
ða æt wæs, and þancfullice hi underfeng, and bæd his wif þæt
heo ne ateorede, ne to sarig wære.
 145. Þa eft æfter lytlan fæce, wurdon his hors ealle, and
ælces cynnes nytena deade, and he þa costnunga lustlice underfeng, and
dihlice mid his wife, and mid his twam sunum aweg gewat.
 148. Þa þæt ongeaton yfele men, þæt hi swa bereafode
wæron, þa ferdon hi to and namon heora gold and seolfor, and eall þæt
þær wæs, and swa eall heora æhta losodon þurh deofles searwa.
 151. On þam dagum gelamp þæt eall folc wurþodon
symbelnysse mid þam casere þurh þone sige þe he on Persia ðeoda
gefeaht.
 153. Was hit eac þeaw þæt Placidas on þære symbelnysse
fyrmest beon sceolde, forðam he wæs þæra cempena lareow and
ealdorman.
 155. Þa wæs he soht, and hine nan man findan mihte.
 156. Þa wundrodon ealle men þæt on swa lytlan fæce hine
nan man findan mihte, ne nan þing þæs him to belamp; and se casere and
ealle his þægnas wæron swiðe sarie, for his færedlican
aweggewitennysse.
 159. Þa cwæð his wif to him, hu lange wunige we her?
 160. Utan niman uncre twa cild and faran heonan.
 161. Elles we beoð to hospe and edwite eallum þe us cunnon.
 161. Þa on niht genamon hy heora twægen suna.
 162. And ferdon to egypta lande.
 163. Soðlice æfter þam þe hi ferdon twegen dagas, þa
comon hi to sæ, and þær gemetton scip standan, and hi on þæt
eodon, and mid him reowan.
 165. Þa geseah þæs scypes hlaford þæt Eustachies wif
swiðe fæger wæs, þa gewilnode he hi habban, and gyrnde þæs
scyptolles; ac ða hi nan þincg næfdon to syllanne, þa gyrnde he
þæs wifes for þam tolle.
 168. Þa Eustachius þæt aget, þa nolde he hi alætan,
þa bicnode se sciphlaford to his mannum þæt hi hine ut sceoldon wurpan.
 170. Þa Eustachius ongæt heora sarwa, þa let he þæt
wif, and genam his twa cild, and eode geomrigende and cweðende, Wa me and
eow, forþam eower modor is ælfremedum were geseald.
 173. Eode þa swa heofende, oð þæt he becom to sumum flode,
and ne dorste ða for ðæs flodes mycelnysse mid þam twam cildum ingan,
ac bær þæt an cild ærest, and sette on oðre healfe þæs
staðes and eode ongean feccan þæt oþer.
 176. Þa he ða wæs tomiddes wætres, þa geseah he
þæt an leo genam þæt cild, and gewende to wuda mid.
 178. He ða wæs geortruwod þæs cildes, and gehwearf
geðyldelice hopiende þæs oðres; ac þa he ðyderweard wæs, geseah
he þæt an wulf genam þæt.
 180. Þa tær he his loccas heofende, and wolde hine sylfne
adrencan on þam wætre, ac hine seo uplice arfæstnyss gestaþelode mid
geþylde, þæt he þæt ne dyde.
 182. Seo leo soðlice heold þæt cild ungederod, æfter
Godes gestihtunge.
 183. Þa hyrdas ðæs landes geseonde þæt se leo þæt
cild swa cucu bær, æfter urnon, and hit ahreddon, and eallswa þa
yrðlingas ahreddon þæt oðer cild æt þam wulfe.
 186. Witodlice ge ða hyrdas ge ða yrðlingas wæron of anre
scire, and hi þa cild afeddan mid him.
 188. Eustachius soðlice heora fæder wende þæt hi fram
þam wildeorum abitene wæron, eode þa heofende and cwæðende, Wala
wa, hu ic nu greow swa þæt treow þe mid wæstmum bið fægre
gefrætwod, and eom nu swa þæt twig þæt bið acorfen of þam
treowe, and aworpen on micclum ystum and eghwanon gecnissed.
 192. Wala on hu micelre genihtsumnysse ic hwilum wæs, and eom nu
bereafod swa an hæftnydlincg.
 194. Iu ic wæs cempena lareow, and mid mycclum were ymbseald.
 195. Nu ic eom ana forlæten, ne furþum mine bearn ic
næbbe.
 196. Ac þu drihten, ne forlæt me, ne mine teares ne forseoh;
ic geman, leof Drihten, þæt þu cwæde þæt ic sceolde gecostnod
beon eallswa Iob, ac on sumum þingum mare ic þolige þonne he.
 199. He soðlice þeh him æhta losodon, swaþeah him wæs
his myxen forlæten, þæt he þæruppan sittan mihte; Ic soþlice on
ælþeodignesse anxsumnysse þrowige.
 201. He hæfde frynd þæt hine frefrodon, and him
efensargodon; ic soðlice on þis westene hæbbe wilde deor þe mine bearn
me benaman.
 203. He hæfde his wif mid him, þe hine arette, þeah he his
bearna þolode; ic witodlice æghwanane eom ungesælig buton westme, ne
furðum an spearca mines cynrenes nis me forlætan, ac eom gelic þam bogum
þe on westene æghwanane mid ystum slægene synt.
 207. Drihten leof, ne onscunige ðu þines þeowes
mænigfealdan word; ic sorgie soðlice þæt ic ma spræce þonne hit
gedafnað.
 209. Sete, drihten, heordrædene minum muðe, þæt min
heorte ne abuge to yflum wordum, þilæs þe ic beo aworpen fram þine
ansyne.
 211. Drihten leof, syle me nu reste mire mænigfealdan
gedrefednysse.
 212. And mid þisum wordum he eode wepende on þone tun þe
hatte Dadissus, and þær wunode, and beget him biglyfne mid his weorce.
 214. Þa æfter micelre tide, bæd he þæs tunes
hlafordas/ þæt he moste healdan heora æceras, and him mede earnian; and
he ðær drohtnode fiftyne gear.
 216. His suna þonne wæron afedde on oþran tune, and heora
naðor nyste þæt hi wæron gebroðra.
 218. Witodlice se hæþena sciphlaford se ðe genam Eustachius
wif, gelædde hi to his earde; and Godes gife hi gescylde þæt he hi ne
gewemde, þa hwile þe heo mid him wæs, ealswa heo to Gode wilnode; and
siððan he dead wæs heo wæs his yrfenuma.
 222. Æfter þissum wæs geworden micel hergung on þam lande
þe Eustachius ær on wæs, and hi fela ðæra Romaniscra landa
awestan.
 224. Þa wæs se casere þearle geancsumod for þære
hergunge, and gemunde þa Placidam, and swiþe geomrode for his færlican
awæggewitennysse.
 226. Gesomnode þa his fyrd ealle to him, and geornlice axode be
him, and bebead þæt man foran sceolde, swa wide swa his anweald wære,
and hine geornlice axian, and he eac behet þam þe hine funden, micelne
wurðscipe and fremfulnesse.
 230. Þa ferdon soðlice twegen cempan þa wæron genemde
Antiochus and Achaius, þa ær wæron under Eustachius handa, and
þurhferdon ealle þa land þe into Rome hyrdon, oððæt hi comon
þær he wunode.
 233. Eustachius þa soðlice feorran hi behealdende, be heora
gewunelican gange hi gecneow, and gedrefed on his mode.
 234. He gebæd hine and cwæð, Drihten ure God, þu ðe
generast of ælcum geswince þa þe on þe gehihtað, gefultuma me
þæt ic mote þine þeowene mine gemæccan git geseon, swa ic nu þas
gehænde geseo þe me hwilon þenedon.
 238. Witodlice ic wat þæt mine bearn for minum synnum fram
wildeorum abitene synd, forgif me Drihten, þæt ic huru on æristes
dæge hi geseon mote.
 240. Him þa ðus sprecendum com stefn ufane to him
cwæðende, Getryw Eustachi; soðlice on þisse andweardan tide þu
gehwyrfst to þinum þam ærran wurðscipe, and þu onfehst ge þin wif
ge þine cild.
 243. Witodlice on þære æriste þu gesihst micelre
mærran þincg, and þu onfehst þara ecra goda gelustfullunga, and þin
nama bið ecelice gemærsod.
 246. Eustachius þa ðis gehyrende, mid mycelre fyrhto geslegen
wæs, þæt he gestandan ne mihte ac gesæt.
 247. Aras ða eft upp and locode wið ðæs weges, and geseah
þæt þa menn wæron wið his weard; and he hi wel gecneow, ac hi ne
cneowan hine.
 249. Þa cwædon hi to him, Hal wæs ðu, broðor.
 250. He him oncwæð, Syb sy mid eow, broðra.
 251. Ða cwædon hi eft, Sæge us, la leof, hwæðer ðu
her wite ænigne ælþeodigne þe hatte Placidas mid his wife and his
twam sunum; soþlice gif ðu hine us gecyþest, we þe willað syllan gode
mede.
 254. Þa cwæð he, for hwilcum þingum sece ge hine?
 254. Hi cwædon, he wæs us swyðe leof freond; nu wolde hine
geseon, gif we hine geaxian mihton æfter swa fela gearum.
 256. Ða cwæð he, nat ic her nanne swilcne wer, soðlice ic
sylf eom ælþeodig.
 257. Eustachius þa gelædde hi into his gesthuse, and
utgangende bohte him win, and him scencte for heora micclan geswince.
 259. Þa cwæð he to þam hushlaforde, þas men synd me
cuðe, and hi forþi comon to me; gif me nu mettas and win, and ic hit þe
gilde eft of mire hyre.
 261. And he him þa glædlice tiþode, and he ða Eustachius
him þenode, and gemunde hu hi him ær þenode.
 263. And ne mihte forberan þæt he ne weope, ac eode ut and
þwoh his eagan, and com eft inn and þenode him.
 265. Hi þa geornlice hine beheoldon and hine be dæle oncneowan
and cwædon, gelic is þæs man þam menn þe wit secað, eaðe he hit
mihte beon.
 267. Ða cwæð se oðer, Ic wat þæt he hæfde ane
dolhswaðe on his hneccan þæt him gelamp iu on gefeohte.
 269. Gyman we nu hwæðer he þæt tacen þære wunde
hæbbe.
 270. Þa hi þa hine geornlice beheoldon, þa gesawon hi þa
dolhswaðe on him, and hi sona hine beclypton, and cystan, and weopen for
blisse; and axodon hine hwæðer he hit wære þe heora cempena lareow
geo wæs.
 273. He þa oðsoc þæt he hit nære.
 274. Hi þa ongen hine gecnæwne gedydon be þam tacne þe on
his hneccan wæs þæt he hit wæs, and hine axodon be his wife and his
cildan hwæt hi geferdon.
 276. He þa cwæð þæt he hit wæs, and þæt his wif
and his cild deade wæron.
 277. Ða sona wearð þis cuð eallum on þam lande, and hi
þider comon mid mycelre wundrunge, and þa menn þe him æfter ferdon,
rehton þam mannum eallum be his ærran wuldre.
 280. Þa hi þus gehyrdon, þa weopon hi ealle cwæðende,
Eala þæt swa mycel healicnys swilces weres us þeowode.
 282. Ða cempan þa cyðdon him þæs caseres bebod, and
scryddon hine mid þam betstan reafe, and læddon forð mid him, and þa
landleode hine furðor gebrohton, and he hi mid sibbe forlet.
 284. Eustachius þa on þam wege him rehte hu him Crist
ætywde, and hu he of fulwihte genemned wæs Eustachius, and eall hu him
gelamp be his wife and his cildum.
 287. Þa embe fiftyne dagas, comon hi to ðam casere and þa
cempan; hi þa arehton eall him hu hi hine fundon, and se casere eode ongen
hine, and cyste hine, and axode hwi he swa feor of his earde faran wolde.
 290. He ða him and ealle his duguðe endebyrdlice arehte ealne
his sið, and his wifes, and his cilda.
 292. Se casere þa and ealle wæron swiðe bliðe his
ongeancymes, and hine bædon þæt he eft fenge to þam anwealde þe he
ær hæfde, and he swa dyde.
 294. Het ða gegaderian fyrde; þa he þa fyrde sceawode, þa
onget he þæt ðær næs fyrd genoh ongen heora fynd.
 296. Het þa of ælcre byrig and tunum gegaderian ma cempena.
 297. Þa gelamp hit þæt man bead þam tunræde þe his
suna on afedde wæron, þæt man sceolde twegen cempan gescyrpan to
þære fyrde.
 299. Þa geceas man þa twegen cnihtas, forþam þe hi wæron
caflice and cyrtene, and ælþeodige, to þære fyrdunga.
 300. Þa wæs eall seo fyrd gegaderod beforan him, and he hi
þa getrymede, and gesette swa his þeaw wæs.
 302. Þa geseah he ongemang oþrum þa geongan cnihtas þæt
hi wæron wlitige on hiwe, and lange on wæstmum; gesette hi þa fyrmeste
on his þenunge, and wearð onæled on heora lufe.
 305. And æfter þam þe he gefadod hæfde eall his werod swa
his þeaw wæs, þa ferde he to þam gefeohte, and geeode þa land þe
ða hæðenan ætbrodon hæfdon, and hi þam casere underþeodde.
 308. Ferde ða forð ofer þæt wæter þæt wæs
genemned Idispis, in þa inran land þæra hæðenra, and hi ofercom,
and heora eard aweste; þa git he wilnode þæt he innor ferde.
 310. Þa ðurh Godes forestihtunge he becom to ðam lande
þær his wif wæs; hæfde hio hire gebogod on anan wyrtigan hamme, and
wæs hio, swa we bufan sædon, ungederod þurh Godes gescyldnysse, fram
þæs hæðenan gemanan.
 314. Þa com Eustachius mid his here to þam tune þe heo ða
on wæs.
 315. Wæs seo wunung þær swyþe wynsum on to wicenne, and
his geteld wæron gehende hire wununge geslagene.
 316. Ða gelamp hit eac þæt þa twegen cnihtas hire suna,
heom in gecuron mid hyre meder.
 318. Ne hi niston þæt heo wæs hire modor, ne heo niste
þæt hi wæron hire suna.
 319. Þa an undermæl spræcon hi betwux him þærinne embe
heora cildgeogoðe, and seo modor sæt geornlice hlystende hire tale.
 321. Þa cwæð se yldra broðor, þæt is þæt ic
gefyrnost gemunan mæg, þæt min fæder wæs cempena ealdorman, and
min modor swyðe wlitig wæs on hiwe, and hi hæfdon twegen suna, me and
oþerne gingran, and þa on niht ferdon hi ut, and genamon unc and ferdon to
sæ and ut reowan.
 325. Þa we up comon þa næs ure modor mid us, nat ic forhwi.
 326. Þa genam ure fæder unc, and bær us wepende forð on
his weg.
 327. Þa becomon we to anre ea, þa eode he in þæt wæter,
and bær mine gingran broþor, and forlet me.
 329. Þa cyrde he eft ongean, wolde feccan me, þa com an wulf
and gelæhte mine broðor, and ær he to me cuman mihte, færinga com of
ðam wuda an leo, and gegrap me, and arn to wuda.
 332. And þa hyrdas ðe þær gehende wæron, ahreddan me
and ic wæs ða afed on þam tune ealswa ðu wast, and ic nyste hwæt
min fæder geferde, and min broðor.
 334. Þa se gingra broðor þis eall gehyrde fram þam yldran
broðor, þa aras he and gelæhte hine be þam swuran, and cyste and
clypte, and sæde, þurh þone God þe Cristene wurðað, ic eom þin
broðor be þire tale, forþam me sædon þe me afeddon þæt hi me
ahreddan fram þam wulfe.
 338. Ða hiora modor þas word gehyrde, þa wæs eall hire
heorte astired, and hire innoð, and þohte hwæðer hit hire suna
wæron, forðam he cwæð þæt heora fæder wære cempena
ealdorman, and eac þæt heora modor æt ðam scype forlætan wearð.
 342. Þa ðy oþre dege gesohte heo þæra cempena ealdorman,
þus cweðende, Ic bidde þe, leof hlaford, þæt þu me gelæde to
minum earde.
 344. Ic eom soðlice Romanisc, and ic on hæftnyd hider gelæd
wæs.
 345. Þa ongemang ðyssum beheold heo hine swyðe georne, and
gecneow þa tacna þe on his hneccan wæron.
 347. And heo þa aforhtode, and ne mihte forbæran þæt heo
hit leng forhæle, ac gefeoll to his fotum and cwæð, Ic halsige þe
leof hlaford þæt þu ne beo geæbylged ongen þine þeowene.
 350. Ac for þinre arfæstnysse gehyr me, and sege me hwæt
þu sy.
 351. Ic wene, leof, þæt þu sy Placidas, cempena ealdorman,
and wære eft on fulluhte genemned Eustachius, þone eac swylce se Hælend
sylf wæs gemedemod þurh þone heort to his mildheortnysse gecigan,
þæt he on hine gelyfde.
 354. And he ða þurh mænigfealde costunga þe him on becomon
genam his wif, þæt ic eom, and his twegen suna, Agapitum and Theophistum
and ferde to egypta lande.
 357. And þa ða we reowan, þa genam se sciphlaford me neadinga
æt him, forþam he wæs hæðen, and he me gehæfte on his eðle,
and Crist me is gewita þæt he ne nan man me gewemde oþ þisne dæg.
 360. Ac Crist se lifigenda geheold mine clænnysse.
 360. Nu ic hæbbe eall þis gesæd swa hit gelamp, nu bidde ic
ðe þurh þæt miccle mægen ures Drihtnes, þæt þu me secge
hweðer þu ðis gecnawe.
 363. Þa Eustachius þis gehyrde þa beheold he hi and gecneow
hi be hyre wlite, and for micelre blisse weop and hi cyste, and Gode þancode,
se gefrefrað ealle þa þe on hine getrywað, and of ealre angsumnysse
generað.
 366. Þa cwæð heo to him, Hlaford, hwær synd uncre suna?
 367. He andswarode, wildeor hi gelæhton.
 367. And he ða arehte hire hu hi genumene wæron.
 368. Þa cwæð heo, Uton don Criste þancung, ic gelyfe
witodlice þæt eallswa God unc geuþe þæt wit unc gemetton, þæt
he ealswa forgife, þæt wit uncre bearn oncnawen.
 371. Ða cwæð Eustachius, and ne sæde ic þæt wilde
deor hi gelæhton?
 372. Ða cwæð heo, Gyrstan dæg ic sæt binnan minan
cafertune, þa gehyrde ic hu twegen geonga cnihtas spræcon him betwux be
heora cildgeogoðe.
 374. Nu wat ic to soþan, þæt hi synd uncre bearn.
 374. Ne hi sylfe nyston þæt hi wæron gebroþra, buton
þurh þa reccinge þe se yldra broþor rehte þam gingran ongit nu hu
micel is Godes mildheortnysse þe him forgeaf þæt hi hi gecnawan moston
þæt hi gebroðra synd.
 378. Ða het Eustachius hi to him clypian, and axode hwæt hi
wæron, and hi him sona arehton eallswa we herbufan sædon.
 380. And he þa gecneow þæt hi his suna wæron, and hi to
him genam, and clypte and cyste, and hi ða ealle heora cneowa gebigdon to
Criste, and mid wope and onbryrdnysse þancunge dydon, fram þære oþre
tide þæs deges oþþe sixtan tide for heora gemetinge.
 384. Þa soðlice asprang se hlisa geond ealne þone hired, and
hi ealle gegadere wundrodon, and blissodon for heora gemetinge, and miccle þe
bliðran þe hi oferwinnen hæfdon þa hæþenan.
 387. Ða þy oðran dæge dydon hi þa mæstan gebeorscype,
and Gode þancode his micclan mildheortnysse.
 388. Þa æfter þam þe hi gewyld hæfdon eall heora feonda
land, and hi mid micclum sige ham hwurfon, and læddon mid him micele
herehuþe, and manige hæftnydlingas.
 391. Þa gelamp hit þæt se casere Traianus wæs forðfaren
ær þam Eustachius of þam gefeohte come, and wæs gesæt oþer
cyning, Adrianus hatte, se wæs hæþen, and wyrsa on welhreownysse.
 394. Þa Eustachius ongen com of þam gefeohte, þa eode se
casere him ongean swa hit þeaw is mid Romanum, and mersode micele symbelnysse
for þam sige þe he geworht hæfde, and axode hine embe þæt gefeoht,
and embe his wif and his suna, hu he hi geaxode.
 398. Þa ðy oþran dæge ferde se casere to þam temple
þæra deofolgilda, and Eustachius nolde ingan mid him; ac stod
þærute.
 400. Þa clypode se casere hine, and axode hwi he nolde offrian
þam godum for his sige, and swiþost forþam þe his wif and his cild
funden hæfde.
 402. Ða cwæð he, Ic wurþige and gebidde minne Drihten
Hælendne Crist, and him unablinnendlice bena offrige, se þe gemiltsode
mire eaðmodnysse, and me geledde of hæftnyde, and min wif me forgeaf and
mine cild.
 405. Nat ic witodlice nanne oþerne god, ne na wurðige, buton
þone heofonlican God, se ðe ealle gesceafta gesceop, ge þa heofonlican ge
þa eorðlican, and fela wundra wyrcð.
 408. Þa wearð se casere mid micelre hatheortnysse gefylled, and
het hine ungyrdan, and bewæpnian, and beforan his ansyne ætstandan mid
his wife and his cildum swilce ofergægendne his hlafordes bebod.
 411. And he swaðeah na to þæs hwon fram his geleafan and
þam soðan Gode gecyrran wolde.
 413. Þa geseah se casere þæt he hine þurh nan ðing
awendan ne mihte fram Cristes geleafan.
 414. Het ða hine gelædan mid his wife and his cildum into anum
eorðhuse, and het ane strange leo lætan into him, þæt hio hi abitan
sceolde.
 416. Þa arn seo leo, and gestod wið þone eadigan wer
Eustachium, and aleat mid þam heafde, and feoll to his fotum, and
geeaðmedde hi to him, and aras eft and eode of þam huse.
 419. Eornostlice se casere geseah þas wundorlican wæfersyne,
þæt se leo heora ne oðhran.
 420. Þa het he gefeccan ænne ærenne oxan, and þone
onælan, and þa halgan ðæron don.
 422. Þa com þider unrim folces, Cristenra and hæðenra, to
þisse wæfersyne, þæt hi woldon geseon hu þa halgan þrowodon.
 424. Þa bæd Eustachius þæt hi him fyrst leton þæt hi
him to Gode gebædon, hi þa aþenedon up heora handa to Gode cweðende,
Drihten God eallra gesceafta scyppend, gesewenlicra and ungesewenlicra, þu
þe eallum eart ungesewenlic, on þinum mægenþrymme.
 428. Fram us soðlice þu wære gesewen swa þin willa
wæs.
 429. Gehyr us nu, leof Drihten, to þe gebiddende.
 429. Efne nu ure gewilnung is gefylled þæt we togædere
cuman moston, and geearnian to onfone þone gemannan þara haligra, swa ða
ðry cnihtas þe þurh fyr afandode wæron, and swaþeah þe ne
wiðsocon.
 432. Læt us nu, Drihten þurh þis fyr geendian.
 433. And sele ðam mede on heofenum þines wuldres mid us þam
ðe on eorðan ure gemyndig beo, and syle him genihtsumnysse ofer eorðan,
and gif hi on sæ oððe on lande gefrecnode beon, and hi ða gecigan
þurh urne naman, beon hy alysede fram ælcere frecednysse.
 437. And gif hi on synnum befeallan, and hi þe þonne halsian
þurh ure eadmodnysse, forgif him, Drihten, forgifnysse heora synne, and
eallum þe ure gemynd don and þe wuldrian, forgif him fultum and heora
gehelp.
 441. Forgif, Drihten, þæt þyses fyres hæto sy gecyrred on
wætne deaw, and læt us on þisum geendian, and gelicie þe on urum
lichaman, þæt hi ne beon totwæmede, ac læt hi beon her
ætgædere gelede.
 444. Þa hi þis sædon, þa com stefn of heofonum þus
cweþende, swa hit bið swa ge biddað, and miccle ma, forþam ge wæron
winnende on godan life, and ge wæron forþyldiende mænigfealde
costnunga/, and swaþeah næron oferswiþde.
 447. Cumað nu on sybbe, and onfoð wuldorbeah eowres siges, and
for þissum hwilwendlicum yflum, brucað þæra ecera goda on worulda
woruld.
 450. Ða þis gehyrdon þa eadigan halgan, þa sealdon hi hi
sylfe þam fyre, and þærrihte seo hæto þæs fyres acolode.
 451. And hi þa wuldrodon þa anwaldan and hergendlican
þrynysse, and sungon Godes lofsang, and heora sawla on sibbe Criste ageafon,
and þæt fyr heora ne æthran, ne furþum an hær heora heafdes.
 454. Witodlice æfter þrim dagum com se arleasa casere to
þære stowe, and het geopenian þone ærenan searecræft þæt he
gesawe to hwam þara haligra lichaman gewordene wæron.
 457. Þa geseah he hi gesunde, þa wende he þæt hi ða git
lyfdon, and het hi ða wurpan ut on ða eorðan.
 459. Þa wundrodon ealle þa þe þær wæron, þæt
þæt fyr ne æthran furðon anes hæres on him, ac heora lichaman
wæron hwittran þonne snaw.
 461. Þa wæs se casere afyrht, and þanon ferde to his
healle.
 462. And seo menio þe þær ætstod clypodon, Mycel and
mære is se God Cristenra manna, and an soð God Hælende Crist, and nis
nan oþer buton him, se gedyde þæt fyr ne fornam ne an hær heora
feaxes.
 465. And þa Cristenan namon heora lichaman diglice, and
bebyrgdon; and getimbrodon gebædhus siððan seo ehtnys gestilled wæs;
and mærsodon heora gemynd on þam dæge <foreign>kal nouembris</foreign>.
 468. Ðis is þæt lif þæra eadigra martyra, and her is
seo geendung heora wuldorfullan gewinnes.
 469. Witodlice ealle þa ðe geearniað and mærsiað heora
gemynd, and hi gecigað to fultume, hi begitað þa god þe þam halgum
behatene synd þurh ða gife ures Drihtnes Hælendes Cristes.
 472. Ðam sy wuldor and miht on worulda woruld a on ecnysse.
 473. AMEN.

LS 9 (Giles)
B3.3.9.
Saint Giles: Picard 1980, 96-129.



 1. Se eadiga egidius wæs geboren of swiðe worðfullum mannum
of greciscre æþele and seo burh þær he on geboren wæs hatte
athenis and his fæder het theodorus and his moder pelagia.
 3. Soðlice hi fandedon symle hu heo mihton healdon heom fram
synne and clæne lif habbon betweoxan heom.
 4. And eal swa hi geseawan þæt heora leofa cild ongan wel to
þeonne, þa befæsten hi hine to boclicere lare.
 6. And he wearð þa swiðe næmel þurh þæs halgan
gastes gife þæt on litle firste he oferþeah his mægster on wisdome
forþon þæt leohtfæt þære soþan lufe wærð onæled
oninnan him.
 8. And godas gife gefrefrode symle his lif and hine swiðe
þeawlice gefrætewode and geglæinde mid wurðfulnesse.
 9. Ða gelamp hit on anum dæge eal swa he eode to circe weard
þæt an seoc man læg on middan þære stræte and bæd him helpes
æt þam mannum þe þær forðferdon.
 11. Witodlice eal swa þæt halig cild egidius his stefne
geherde, þærrihtes he ateah his kyrtel of his rycge and dyde hine on þam
untrumen forþan þe he næfde nan betere þincg him to sellenne.
 13. And eal swa hraðe swa se earme man hæfde on þæs
cildes kertel swa he underfencg his lichames hæle and he þas gode
þancode and þan halgan egidium.
 15. Eornestlice þæt eadiga cild for þa to his mægstre and
ealswa he hine geseah þa axode he hine hwær his kertel wære and he
sæde þæt an uncuð man hine him hæfde benumen.
 17. Ða næs hit lang æfter þam þæt his fæder and
his moder forðferdon of þisum life and he heora forðsið wiste ær
beforen þurh þæs halgan gastes gife.
 18. Soðlice he ne gymde nan þincg of heora mycele æhte þe
his fæder and his moder him belæfdon ac betæhte hit æt sumen ceare
eal swa he eode fram circe hamward þæt an man hine gemette on swiðe
earmlice hiwe forþon þe an næddre hine hæfde swa grimlice geslagen
þæt eal his lichame wæs toswollen and swa swiðe toblawen þæt
earfoðlice he mihte þa ænig word specan.
 22. Ac se halig godes deorlincg egidius behreowsode his earme lif
swa hraðe swa he hine geseah and gebæd for hine to drihtne mid inwærdre
heorte swa lange oðþæt he hine eal swa hal gebrohte swa he ær wæs
þurh godes mildheortnesse.
 25. And he hine siððan bæd þæt he gode þancunge dyde
þe hine swa mihtiglice hæfde gehælod.
 26. Eft soðlice hit gelamp on anen sunnendæge eal swa se
eadige egidius stod on his gebedum innen sumre cyrcen þæt se awergede gast
begrap ænne mann swiðe færlice þærinne amang þæt se prest
stod on þære swimæsse.
 29. And geswæncgte hine swa swiðe þæt he nænne þyld
hæbben ne miht eac feoll niðer on þan flore and ongan to walwigenne and
to windenne hider and þider and swa hlude to hræmenne þæt ealle þa
menn þe wæron binnan þære cirece wurdon offirhte.
 31. And eal swa hraðe swa se godes þeowe egidius þæt
geherdo þærrihtes he gestreahte hine on þære eorþan eal swa his
gewune wæs and gebæd hine to his drihtne and siððan up astod fægre
gefrefrod of drihtnes mildse.
 34. He eode þa hrædlice to þam earmum men.
 34. And he gefeng hine mid fullan geleafan and þus wæs
cweðende mid hludre stefne ætforan eallum þam mannum þe wæro binnon
þære cirece, Ic bidde þe ealles mancynnes feond and ic hælsige þe
þurh urne drihten hælend crist þæt þu na læncg her ne wunige.
 37. Ac far ut rædlice of þisum men þæt þu na læncg
hine ne gedræfe.
 38. Soðlice þe awergode gast ne mihte þa forsittan þæs
halgas bebodu ac þærrihtes he forlet þæne wrecne man þe he swa
geomerlice begripan hæfde and ongan egeslice to hremenne and grislice to
þietenne and swiðe biterlice to wepenne eal swa he aweg for and se man
belaf hal and wel gesund.
 42. Ða æfter þis ne mihte se halige wer egidius na læncg
lutian ne beon forholen.
 42. Ac his nama asprancg þa ofer eall greclande and þa
manigfealde wundre and mihte þe drihten for him dyde.
 44. Him sohton þa to swiðe feole manne æghwanen biddende
heora lichame hæle and eac heora sawle hæle and eal swa heo gehælde
wæron, þa budon hi him gold and seolfor and feola cynne gyrsumen, eac he
eall þæt forseah and forsoc.
 46. He þohte þa eac eall hrædlice to forlætenne his
æþele forþon þe he ondræd him þæt he sceolde beon mid þises
worulde wurðscipe up onhafen and his gode dæde þurh þan sceolden
wurðon gelitlode.
 49. He bæd eac swiðe geornlice his drihten þæt he hine to
þam fultumian sceolde and for þa on anre niht to þære sæ swa
stillice swa swa hit nan man nyste.
 51. And eal swa he stod þær on his gebedum, þa geseah he an
scip ut on þære sæ swa swiðe torfigende fram þan wealcendum sæs
yðum þæt ealle þa men wendon þæt heora scip tobrocen wære.
 53. Soðlice hi forgeaton þa ealle þa þincg þe hi on hande
hæfdon forþon þe hi wendon þærrihtes ealle besincan to þan
sægrunde.
 54. Hi ongunnon þa ealle swiðe sarlice to wepenne and to
gymerigenne forþon þe hi wiston þa fulgære þæt se bitere deað
heom to genealæhte.
 56. Ða eall swa seo yþigende sæ heo wærp up and niðer
þa geseagon hi onmang heora gedræfodnesse þone godes man egidium licgan
uppan þære sæstrande on his gebedum.
 58. Ða þohten hi ealle swa hit soð wæs þæt þa
sælice yðas mihton swiðe eðelice beon gestilde þurh his gebedum.
 59. Hwæt þa se ælmihtiga god stilde þana strangan sæ
þurh þæs halges bedum and gemacode hine swiðe wynsum on to wunigenne.
 61. And eal swa þa earmæ scipmen geseawon þa modian sæ
swiðe liðe and swa milde geworden, þa ongunnon hi ealle to wepenne for
fagennesse and ahofen ealle heora handa up to heofonum weard and þus wæron
cweðende, Gebletsod þu eart drihten god þu þe ne forlætst nan
þæra manne þe hihtað on þe.
 65. Soðlice þu eart gebletsod and herigendlic on worulde þu
þe mildheortlice besceawast þa næronisse þinre þeowene
ungesælignesse.
 66. We þanciað þe mildheorta drihten þæt þu us
geuþest swilcne man to geseonne þe us hæfð to þe geþingod þurh
his gebedum þæt we todæg swa mihtiglice synd gehælede.
 68. Ða æfter þis hie reowan to þam lande herigende heora
drihten and mid bliðum mode upeodon fram þære sæ to þæs godes
deorlinge/ egidium þær þær he stod on his gebedum.
 71. Witodlice eal swa hi comon ætforen him þa fyllon hio ealle
to his fotum and axoden him Hwæt manne he wære oððe for hwilcum
þingum he come to þære sæ.
 72. He andwyrde and cwæð þæt he cristen wære and
þæt he wolde faran to rome gif him god uðe.
 73. And eal swa hi þas wurd geherdon, þa feollan hi eft
niðer to his fotum and þus cwædon, Hlaford we habbað soðlice ongyton
þæt se ælmihtiga god hæfð us alesde þurh þine gebedu fram urum
micelum dræfednesse.
 76. Sy his nama gebletsod on ecnesse þæt he us geuðe swilcne
frofer of þe to begitanne.
 77. Soðlice we syndon of rome and gif þin willan sy þæt
þu mid us þider faren wille, þonne wille we þe bliðelice underfon and
we willað gearwian þe ealle þinre lichamlice neode.
 79. Ða se halga egidius þas word geherde þa þancode he
þæs drihten and gebletsode his drihtnes nama ofer ealle oþer þincg.
 80. And betæhte his sawle and ealre his geferene sawle þam
ælmihtigan gode and asteh þa into þæt scip mid godes gife afylled and
for þa mid his geferan ut on þære sæ glæde and blissigende on his
drihtenes mildheortnesse.
 83. Witodlice eal swa hi hæfdon færen feower dagas and feower
niht on þære sæ þa gelænton hi on anen eglande for þon þe heom
beþorfte stræw to heora bedræste.
 85. Hi eodon þa up on þæt land and geseowan þær anes
mannes fotswaða getredene on þan sande be þære sæstaðe.
 86. And hi eodon þa swa lange æfter þan stapan þæt hi
comen to anum þiccum scrubbe and se wæs swiðe þicce mid þornan
gegrowan and mid bræmlan and mid fela oðre cynne treowa.
 88. And eal swa hi þæron comen wel fyrr in þæt scrub,
þa geseawon hi ætforen heom an scræf and æt þæs scræfes dure
sæt an litel man and rædde on anre boc.
 90. Ða wæron þa scipmenn ealle afyrhte forþon heom
tweonode hwæðer he riht man wære.
 91. Ac se halige egidius oncneow þærrihtes þæt he wæs
gode þeowa and eode to him mid bliðe mode and him þus to cwæð,
Hlaford broðer hwæt eart þu.
 93. Se godes man him andwyrde and cwæð þæt he wære an
sunful mann toforan gode.
 94. Egidius cwæð, Hu lange hæfst þu her gewunod.
 94. Eft cwæð se eadiga egidius, Be hwylce þinge hæfst
þu her gelyfod.
 95. Se godes freond cwæð þæt he leofode be weode and be
wyrtan roten and be wæteres drence.
 96. Ða se halga egidius geherde þæt he wunede on swylce life
eal swa he self wilnode an to drohtnigenne, þa wearð he swa bliðe
þæt he cleopode þone godes man and gecyste hine mid mycelre lufe.
 98. And swa siððan betæhte her ægðer oþer þam
ælmihtigan gode mid halige bedum.
 99. Soðlice þry dagas hi wunodon togædere and geornlice
andledon godes lof betweoxan heom be dæges and be nihte.
 100. Ða æfter þriora dagana fec gegrette her ægðer
oðerne mid sibsumnesse and se egidius forlet þær þone godes man and
gewende him siððan þanon sarlice wepende and his drihten herigende.
 102. Hwæt þa se godes man asteh into þæt scip to his
geferan and sundfullice forð segledon on twam dagum and on twam nihtum and on
þam þriddan dæge becomen to þære burh massilie and þær up
gelænton æfter drihtnes willan.
 105. Witodlice binnen þære ilcan burh wunode sum hælig
biscop eusebius gehaten, se wæs swiðe wundorfull on godum weorcum and of
mycel godes gife afylled.
 106. And eal swa se eadiga egidius geherde of his halgan drohtnunge
he wilnode mid ealre gyrnfulnesse hine to geseonne þæt he mihte beon
gefrefrod mid his godcundan spræce.
 109. Soðlice eal swa he becom into þære burh Arelaten þa
underfeng hine sum rice widewa into hire huse mid glæde mode, hire nama
wæs Theochrita.
 110. Ða onmang þon þe man his þenunge gearcode þa geherde
he fyr in þæs huses hyrne sumes sices mannes granunge and wanunge and
axode sona hwæt þæt wære.
 112. Him andwerde þæs huses hlæfedig Teochrita and
cwæð mid wependre stæmne, Hlaford hit is min dohtor þe swa sarlice
onginð forþon þe heo hafað nu þreo gær hefitenlice beon
geswæint on þan gedrife and ic hæbbe geseald swiðe mycel dæl of
minre æhte for hire hæle.
 115. And þæt ic hæbbe eall forloren forþon þe heo ne
mihte næfre beon gehæld of nan þære læce þe hio gehælen
sceolde.
 116. And þeah hlaford þe ic wolde sellan godne gyrsum gif þu
cuðost hi gehælon mid læcedome.
 117. Se eadiga egidius hire andwyrde and cwæð þæt he
nawiht eorðlices læcecræftes ne cuðe ac swilcne cræft swa he
cuðe he wolde hire þæt bliðelice don.
 119. Het him þa rymen þæt hus and hi swa dydon.
 120. Ða eode se godes mann to þam mædenne and astrehte hine
toforan hire bedde mid ealre eadmodnesse biddende his drihtnes mildse.
 121. Leofa swuster ic hate þe on mines drihtnes naman þæt
þu arise up eal hal and bletse þinne hælend and þæt mæden aras
up of hire legerbedde and feol to his fotum mid wependre stefne and þus
cwæð, Sy drihtenes nama gebletsod se þe me todæg hæfð gehælod
þurh þine gebedu.
 124. Soðlice egidius genam þa þæt mæden up and
gelædde hio to hire moder and þus cwæð, Leofa wif underfeng nu
cristes gifa and do þancunge þine drihten þe hire swa mihtelice hæfð
gehæled.
 127. Ðæt wif wærð þa ofwundred of swylcere sundfulnesse
and þærrihtes beot hire handan togædere for fagennesse and cwæð,
Wel me wel me hlaford þæt ic þe æfre mid minum eagum geseah for þon
þe ic becnæwe soðlice þæt þu eart godes deorling and gode word
is soð on þinum muþe.
 130. Ða asprang þis godes wulder ofer eall þa burh and eal
swa hraðe swa se bisceop eusebius hit geherde swa he sænde æfter þam
halgan egidium be his arcediacne aurelius gehaten.
 132. Eac þes ilce biscop gecneow his tocyme þurh þan halgan
gaste and eal swa se eadi egidius com ætforan him swa he underfeng hine mid
mycelre arwurðnesse.
 134. Ða æfter þon wolde se eadige wer faren þanon ac se
biscop hine wiðheold þær twa gær mid him his unþances.
 135. Ða smæde he æfre on his geþance hu he mihte þanon
fleon for þære mycclan socne þe him tosohte ac he ne mihte ær þan
þe twa gær aganne wæron.
 137. Ða gewearð hit æfter drihtnes wille þæt he raðe
deornelice þonen gewænde and for þa swa lange þæt he becom to
þære æa þe is gehaten rodanus wið þone staðe guardones and eal
swa he hæfde oferfaran þæt wæter þa eode he forð on þæt
land and gesohte him sumne scræf þæt wære gedafonlic his goodere
drohtnunge on to wunigenne and his clæne lif on to libbanne.
 141. Hwæt se godes man egidius eal swa he þæt geornlice
sohte þa becom he to anen heage monte þurh godes forsceawunge and gefand
þæt ænne pæð upwærd se wæs swa scearp mid stanum and eac swa
nære þæt earfoðlice þær mihte ænig man upcuman.
 144. Ac swa þeah se halig wer hit nolde forlætan ungesoht
forþon þe he hopode þæruppe to findenne þæt he lange stunde ær
ætforan gesoht hæfde ac for upp mid ealle geleafan and eal swa he com wel
nih þæruppe, þa fand he þær ætforan him ænne scræf se
wæs swiðe dyp innen þam clude.
 147. Ða se eadiga egidius þæt geseah þa gestreahte he hine
selfne þærrihtes and þancode his drihtne mid wependre stæmne þæt
he him swicne stede ateowed hæfde.
 149. He aras þa up and eode into þam scræfe herigende his
drihten and þa he com wel ferr in, þa geseah he ænne westensetle
þæs nama wæs ueredemius se wæs swiðe halig wer and þurh godfela
wundra wyrcendæ.
 152. Soðlice þa se godes mann egidius geseah þær þa
godcundlice drohtnunge, he eode þa hrædlice to him and befeng hine
betweoxan his earmum and hine swiðe mildelice gecyste and þærrihtes
oncneow heore ægþer oðres godnesse þurh þæs halgan gastes gife
and se eadige egidius belaf þa sume stunde mid þan arwurþan ueredemie
þæt he wurþe þurh hine getimbrod mid halgum weorcum.
 156. Ðus wynsumlice gaderode se ælmihtiga god þas twegen
scinende steorran on annesse þæt hi þurhscinen eal þone eard þe hi
onwunodon mid heora byrhta leoman.
 158. Witodlice hi onlihton ealle þa blinde þe on þam lande
wæron þurh heora gebedum and gesealdon þam deafum heora hlest and þan
dumben heora spræce and þam crypelan heora gang and þa hryfligen hi
geclænsoden and þan unwittigen hi gesealdon heora witt and swa forð hi
gehældon þa untrumen þurh heora drihtnes mildheortnesse þæt
þær ne belæfde nan ungehæled.
 162. Eac þæt land þe þær onbuton læg wæs swiðe
unwæstmebære þæt hit nolde nanes cynnes sæd forðbringan þan
folce to frofre.
 164. Ða wearð hit gecydd þan godes men egidium and he
þærrihtes gemacode þa eorðe wæstmbeære þurh his halgum
gebedum.
 165. Eft on sume dæge for se godes man ueredemius to
gehælenne þa untruman and se eadig egidius belaf æt þam scræfe.
 166. Ða wearð þær rædlice an swiðe sic man ætforan
him gebroht and þa þe hine þider brohten sworen mid mycclan aðe
þæt hi næfre nolden hine þanen gebringan ær þan þe se halga
hine gehæled hæfde.
 169. Egidius hiom andwyrde and cwæð, ðus gesceolden biddan
æt þan halgan ueredemio þe hæfð gehælod ealle þas untruman
þurh his gode geearnunge and naht æt me.
 171. Hi cleopoden þa ealle uppon þone halgan þus cweþende,
Eala þu godes man nylle we na þas word gehyran forþon we witon ful wel
hwæt þu eart.
 173. Eac we nabbað na forgeton hu þu bæde to drihtne of uran
hearde lande þe us nane wæstmes sellan nolde and drihten hit macode
þærrihtes wæstmebære þurh þine gebede eal swa þu miht nu gif
þu wilt æt gode gebiddon þæt þes man gehæled wurðe.
 176. Hwæt þa se godes deorlincg egidius wearð ofercumen mid
þæra manna bene and gestrehte hine on þære eorþan and dyde his
gebede mid gelomlicen tearan agotennesse and siððan uparas fægre
gefrefrod of þas halgan gastas gife and eode to þan untruman and
gegearcode hine mid cristes rode tacne and genam hine up be his hand and
betæhte hine þa his freonde eal hal and wel gesund.
 180. Ða wearð se halga ofdrædd for þisum tacne and eac for
þan oðrum þe he hæfde þær mænigfealdlice gedon þæt hit
þan folce wurde gecydd and he þærof herunge habban sceolde and hit
þonne/ his drihtne sum þincg mislicode and for þan þe he þohte sum
dernlic lif to beganne and forlet þa þane eadiga ueredemium and þurhfor
ealle þa westene þe þær be healfes wæron, geornlice secende hwær
he wunigunge habban mihte.
 186. Ða gelamp hit þæt he becom to sumre stowe þurh godes
forsceawunge þe is gehaten septimania seo wæs al beset mid ðifelum and
mid treowum and wæs eac swiðe hol of wildum deorum holum.
 188. Ða feand se godes deorlincg egidius on þære ilca stowa
ænne scræf and ætforan þæs scræfes dure ænne lytelne
welspryng, þanon ut arn swiðe clæne wæter and eal swa he þæt
geseah þa feol he niðer on þære eorðan and ongan to wepenne for
fægennesse and þancode his drihten mid inweardre heortan þæt he him
uðe swilcne stede to findonne.
 192. Soðlice þreo gear he wunode on þan ilcan stede and
leofede be wyrtan rotan and be wæteres drynce.
 193. Ða ofþuhte þan ælmihtigum gode his hearde lif and
gesænde him þa dæghwamlice ane hinde þe hine gefedde mid hire meolce
on gewisse tide.
 195. Ða gewearð hit æt sumre tide þæt þæs
cyninges hunten comen mid heora hundum into þam ilcan wude þe se godes
deorlincg egidius onwunode and huntoden þærinne and þærrihtes hi
arærdon up þa ilcan hinde þe fedde þone godes deorling mid hire meolce
and hire anrædlice folgedon and forleten ealle þa oðre deor for hire
anre sace.
 199. Hwæt þa seo earma hind arn hider and þider mid micclan
gedræfednesse and þa hunten hire æfre folgedon and hio fleah þa swa
lange oðþæt hio becom to þam scræfe þe hire fostercild inne
wunode.
 201. Ða stod hio æt þæs scræfes dure and ongan to
hlowenne æfter þan halgan egidium swylce hio his helpes bæde.
 202. And eal swa se halga egidius hire sarige stefne geherde, þa
wearð he swiðe ofwundrod for hwi hio bærde þa oðerlocer þonne hio
ær wæs gewunod and þærrihtes eode ut of þam scræfe and gehyrde
þa hundes and þa huntan.
 204. He beheold þa on þa hinde and geseah hu sarlice hio sicode
æfre anan and hio let hangian ut hire tunga forþon þe hio swa swiðe
fordrifen wæs.
 206. Hwæt þa se eadige egidius oncneow hu hire gelumpen wæs
and he þa mid gebygdum cneowum his drihten inweardlice bæd þæt he
geheolde þæt deor ungederod þe he him to fostermoder geunnon hæfde.
 208. Æfter þisum gebede he stod up and bebead þam hinde
þæt hio hire earmen hlowunge geswice and hio dydo swa hire fostercild hire
bebead and eode hire swiðe stillice and læg æt his fotum.
 210. Ða wearð þær mycel godes wuldor ateowod þurh
þæs halgenes bene þæt ealle þa hundes þe folgede þære hinde
wiðstoden and ne mihton cumen na nier þan halgan þonne be anes stanes
wyrpe and mid hwinsunge and mid dreorige mode hio cerdon ealle ongean to þan
hunten.
 213. Hi sændon þa æfter þæs cyninges hirdcnihten and
æfter ealle heore hunden and þær on morgen com eal þæs cyninges
hird into þan ilcan stede þær heora hundes wiðstodan þæs ærran
dæges and wolden anrædlice to þære hinde.
 216. Ac se halga hio ealle gelette and wiðheold hio þær
þæs dæges eal swa he dyde þæs ærræn dæges þurh his
drihtenes fultum and hio þa geomerunge ham gewændon and gecyddan þam
cyninge eall be endebyrdnesse hu heom belumpen wæs.
 219. Soðlice se cyning het flauius and þæt land þe he on
rixode het goutland and eal swa he gehyrde þære huntena spæce he
wearð þa swiðe ofwundrod and sænde rædlice æfter þan biscope
Nemausesi/ and gerehte him ealle þas þing.
 222. Ða rædde se biscop þan cyninge þæt eal swa hraðe
swa se dægriome upasprunge þæt hi sceolden faren begen into þam wude
and fandian hwæt soð wære.
 224. Hi dydon þa eal swa hi hæfden geræd.
 224. Foren þa on huntoð mid þan hunten and mid þan hunden
into þam ilcan wude and arærden up eft þa hind and folgoden hire swa hi
dydon þæs ærran dæges eal to þære stowe þe se eadiga egidius
onwunode.
 227. Soðlice seo hind arn eft to hire fostercilde and gelegde hio
æt his fotum and þa hundes urnen ealle buton þæs halgenes scræf
and ne mihton cumen na neor þonne hi mihton þæs ærran dæges.
 229. Ða com þær an sceotere and geseah hwær seo hind
læg æt þæs scræfes duru and þærrihtes he gebænte his boge
and wolde sceotan þa hind mid his aruwa & gemiste hire and gehitte þone
godes deorlincg egidium swa þæt he wearð swiðe sarlice gewundod and
swa þeah he wæs æfre geornlice biddende his drihten þæt he
geheolde his fostermoder ungederod.
 233. Ða onmang þis com se cyncg and se biscop mid micclan
gegæncge and spyredon swiðe geornlice æfter þære hind and gedrifen
hire fære riht to þære scræfe ac hio ne mihton þærto cuman for
þæs wudes þicnesse.
 235. Se cyning het þa forheawon þone wude ætforen him and
gearcoden him ænne pæð æfter þære hindfære forþon he wolde
soðlice/ witen hwider hie becumen wære.
 238. Ða hirdcnihtes gearwedon þone pæð ætforen þam
cyninge and he and se biscop folgedon heom þa swa lange þæt hi becomen
to þan scræfe.
 239. And fundan þær ænne ealdne mann mid muneclicum reafe
gescredd and sæt swiðe ærwurðlice æt þæs scræfes dure
forþon þe he ne mihte cneowlian na swa gelomlice swa his gewune wæs for
þon blode þe droppode stundmæle on þa eorðan of his wunde.
 242. Eac hio gesawon þa hinde licgan æt his fotan mid mycelre
ondrædednesse forþon þe þa hundes ne geswicon to hwinsianne mid
ceariendre stæmne and ne dorstan na læng beorcan forþon þe hi
wæron gebundene mid þæs halgenes mihte.
 245. Ða bead se cynincg his cnihtes and his hunten þæt hi
ealle wæron swiðe gedrioge and þæt heore nan him æfter ne folgoden
buton se biscop ane and hio dydon eal swa heom beboden wæs.
 247. Hwæt þa se cynincg and se biscop eodon on heora baran
fotum to þan godes freond egidium and hine eadmodlice gretton and he hi
ongean mid mare eadmodnesse.
 249. Hi axodon hine hwæt manna he wære and hu he þider
come.
 250. Ac þa þa hi geseawon þæt blod hu hit droppode of his
wunde on þære eorþan, þa wurðon hi swiðe sarie and axodon hine eac
hwilc ungesælig man hine swa grimlice wundian dorste.
 252. Se halige wer egidius gerehte þa þan cyninge and þan
biscope eall be ændebyrdnesse his æðele hwanen he geboren wære and
hwæt his nama wæs and for hwilce þinge he com æræst þider and
hu he gewundod wæs.
 254. Witodlice eal swa hio þas word geherdon þa feollan hi to
his fotum and bædon forgyfennesse ealra þære misdæde þe hi wið
him gedon hæfdon and behetan him þæt hi woldon hine gehælon mid
deorwurðe læcecræfte.
 257. Heom andwyrde se eadiga egidius and cwæð þæt he
nolde nanes mannes læcecræft underfangen butan his drihtenes ane, se þe
hine hæfde æfre wel gehæled and gestrehte hine þærrihtes on
þære eorþan and gebæd his drihten mid wependre stæmne þæt
heom gemildsode on heofonum eal swa he dyde on eorðan.
 261. Hwæt þa se cynincg and se biscop hine geornlice beheoldan
and geseawon on him eall þæt drihtne licwurðe wæs and hi feollan þa
eft to his fotum and his bletsunge bædon.
 262. Se godes man cwæð heom, Drihten se þe ealle þincg
gescop, gemiltsie eow and sy his bletsunge ofer eow nu and on ecnesse and
gecyste hi þa mid micelre eadmodnesse and swa mid his halige bletsunge him
fram gewændon eac se halige godas þeowa egidius gesiclode of þære
wunde þe him on wæs ac beþohte þa word þe ure hlaford crist
cwæð to his apostolen paule, On untrumnesse wurð godes mihte fulforðod
and mid þis ilcan geþance he bæd his drihten mid inweardre heortan
þæt swa langa swa he libban moste þæt he næfre gehæled ne
wurðe.
 269. Witodlice se cynincg flauius com siððan to þam godes
deorlinge gelomlice to þan þæt he wurðe of his spæce and of his
wissunge gefrefrod and halwændlice getimbrod.
 271. He bead him eac gold and seolfer and fela cynne gersumes swa
oft swa he him to com, ac he æfre þæt wiðsoc.
 272. Ða æt læste gewissode se halige egidius þam cyninge
þæt he lete aræron sum heafodmynstre mid þam ilcan feo þe he him
sellan wolde and gegaderode þærto sume godes þeowan þe mid regolicre
steoran and mid muneclicre drohtnunge dæiges and nihtes heora drihten herian
wolden.
 275. Ða andwyrde se cynincg and cwæð, Hlaford ic wille
þæt don swiðe bliðelice gif þu wilt me behaten þæt þu heora
gastlice fæder beon wille.
 277. Se eadiga egidius cwæð þæt he swylcere wice
unwurðe wære and hine wislice gewerode mid boclicum lare and sænde
symle mid micclan gesceade þæt he hit understanden ne mihte.
 279. Se cyncg ongan þa swiðe biterlice to wepenne and
gehælsode hine þurh ures drihtnes nama and þurh ealre halgane geearnunge
þæt he þa wice underfangen scolde.
 281. Ða wearð se godes man ofercuman þurh þæs cyncges
bene and for his teara agotennesse and getyðode him þæs þe he him to
gewilnode and þa wicen underfeng swa willes swa unwilles.
 283. Ða axode he þone godes deorlincg egidium hwær he wolde
þæt se mynster wære aræred and hu mycel he wolde habban þæt
weorc and eal swa se halie wer þas word geherde þærrihtes he gewissode
þan cincge hwær he hit habban wolde forþon þe drihten hit hæfde him
ær ætforen openlice ateowed.
 287. He sæde eac þan cynge þæt he sceolde læten
þær aræron twa circan, ane on sanctes petres naman þæs halgan
apostlas and þæt oðer on sanctes prisces naman þæs halgan martyres
riht wið þan scræfe þe he inne wunode and binnan þære ilcan circe
he drohtnode ane on his sunder gebedum swa lange swa his lif wæs.
 291. Hwæt þa se cing flauius let þa rædlice aræren
þa twa circan swa swa se eadiga egidius hi gedihte and gegaderode þærto
æghwanen swylce godes þeowan þe rihtlice wolden libban heora lif
æfter þæs halgenes wissunge.
 294. Ða gelamp hit anes dæges þæt se godes man eode ut
fram his scræfe sume fif milen and se cyng flauius hine gemette and spæc
wið hine mid mycelre lufe and wearð þa swa bliðe of his tocyme þæt
he betæhte to þære muneca neode eall þæt land þe læg onbutan
þan mynstre be fif milen mærce forþon þe he wæs swa feor ut gegan
and þæt wæs soðlice þurh godes foresceawunge swilce hit for his
lichames scyrtunge wære.
 299. Æfter þisum for se cyning to þam mynstre and genam
þone biscop nemausensi and þa munecas and ealle þa wisesta menn þe on
his rice wæron and eodon þa anes dæges to þam godes deorlinge egidium
and bædon hine mid mycelre eadmodnesse þæt he sacerdhad underfenge.
 302. Se godes man heom þæs bliðelice getiðode forþon
þe drihten hit wolde habban swa idon and eal swa hie þis geherdon, þa
ongunnen hie ealle to wepenne for fægennesse and þancodan þan
ælmihtigan gode þæt he swilc wurðmynt geunnon hæfde.
 305. Ða underfeng se halga wer presthad and hit geheold mid
anrærdnesse and eadmodnessæ þe he ær onwunode.
 306. He wæs soðfæst on spæce and arwurð on þeawe,
stæðig on his gelæte and estfull on bodunge, wacol on gebedu and
glæd on gastlice dæde.
 308. Eadig wæs se wer, on him ne wunode nan yfel.
 308. He ne fordemde nænne man ne he ne forgeald yfel mid yfele.
 309. Ac he eðelice forbær manna teona mid mycele geðylde.
 310. Eale hu mildelice and hu fægerlice he gewissode þa
gebroðra þe him underþeodda wæron hu hi sceolden beren cristes rode
uppan heora hrycge, þæt is hu hie scolden forhæfdnessa hæbben and
þa soðe lufe healden.
 312. Hi æton dæghwamlice togædere on gesettum tidum and
wines drync hi ne gemdon buton to þam seocan broðran and to þærftigum
mannum and manega þær hæfdon hæren to lice and hnesce gewæde
þær wæron for leahtre getealde.
 315. Æþelborene weres þær wunedon on þam mynstre.
 316. Se eadiga egidius nolde næfre forlæten his wæccan on
niht ne his fæsten on dæg ac hit swiðe geornlice beeode and his lichama
þærmide swa swiðe geswængte þæt he þurh þan geleofode his
lif eall buton yfelum lustum and drihten þær to gestrangode mid his
godcundum mihte.
 319. Witodlice his halie lif wearð þa wide cuð and þa
manigfealde tacne þe drihten dyde þurh him, hio wurðon þa eac gecydde
fram lande to lande.
 321. And eall swa se cynincg carolus of francene rice geherde
secgan of his micclan godnesse, þa gewilnode hine to gesynne þæt he
mihte beon gefrefrod of his halwende spæce.
 323. He sænde þa rædlice his boden to þam godes men,
geornlice biddende þæt he come to him for mycelre neode gif hit his wille
wære.
 325. Ða cnihtes dydon þa eal swa heom beboden wæs, foron to
þam godes þeowa egidium and gebuden þæs kinges ærende to him mid
mycelre eadmodnesse.
 326. And eal swa se godes man þis gehyrde, þa smeade he on his
geþance hwæt him to donne wære and þohte gif he ferde to þam cincge
and hu he hine gehælen mihte þurh his drihtnes fultum þæt hit his
sawle on sumre wise fremian scolde.
 329. Se eadige wer heom andwyrde and cwæð þæt he wolde
bliðelice faran to heora cynehlaforde gif hit god swa forsceawian wolde.
 331. Hwæt þa se godes freond egidius gefrefrode his
gebroðran mid his halwændan lare and hie gyrnlice tihte to gode weard and
gesette heora bigleofa swa swa he wiste for gode þæt hit wel beon mihte.
 333. He nam eac to his fære þa þincg þe him neodbehefe
wæron and for to þam cyninge weard carolum and swa he com in to þære
burh þe is gehaten aurelia, þa underfeng he þær gestninge.
 335. Eac eal swa raðe swa he wæs geliht of his asse swa he
eode in to þam mynstre þe wæs gehalgod þære halga rode to
wurðmente þæt he hine þærinne gebæde and eal swa he hine
geornlice gebæd to his drihtne, þa ongan se awergede gast hlude to
grædenne þurh anes witleases muð þus cweðende, Walawa, walawa.
 339. Egidi grimlice pinest þu me mid þinum gebedum and feala
tintregane geþolige ic þurh þe.
 340. Geare me sume stunde and wiðheald þine gebede swa lange
þæt ic muge utfaran of þisum men.
 341. Soðlice eal swa se godes þeowe þis wunder geherde, he
aras þa up fram þære eorðe and gebletsode hine mid cristes rodetacne
and eode siððan to þam wrecce men þe se awergode gast hæfde swa
geomerlice begripen and þus wæs cweðende, Eala þu mancynnes feond ic
hate þe on mines drihtnes nama þæt þu hrædlice gewit ut of þisum
men.
 345. And he þær forlet þone earmne man þe he swa
hefigtenlice hæfde geswæint and mid grislicere þeotunge þanon
gewænde.
 347. Ða wearð þis wunder hrædlice cuð ofer eal þa burh
and æghwær þær onbuton þæt se eadige egidius þe wæs ær
þurh þa tacne icydd þe drihten þurh hine gedon hæfde.
 349. Wearð þa eac þurh þas tacne myceles þe swiðre
gewurðod.
 349. And eal swa hraðe swa he geherde þæt menn heroden hine
þurh þis tacan.
 350. He for þa swiðe hraðe ut of þære burh to þam
cynge carole and eal swa he becom to þam wel nih þær se cincg wæs,
þa wearð hit him gecydd of his tocyme.
 352. And for þa mid mycele gegæncge ongean þone godes
deorlincg edigium and hine underfencg mid mycele wurðmente.
 353. Ða undergeat se cyncg þæt hit wæs eal soð þæt
him wæs gesæd be þam godes þeowa.
 354. Hio spæcon þan gelomlice betweoxan heom of þises
middeneardes forseowennesse and of manegra mihte gewilnunga and se godes man
getihte æfre þone cyning to gode weard, hu he þurh dædbote begetan
sceolde his synne forgifennesse.
 357. Ða hæfde se cynincg gedon sume synne seo wæs swa
scandlic þe he hit ne dorsten andeaten to nanum men.
 358. Ac bæd þone halige wer þæt he for hine geþingode
to drihtene and he swa dyde be dæg and be nihte.
 360. Ða gelamp sum þincg þe wulderlic is ymbe to specenne
þæt se eadige egidius mæssode on þan nextan sunnandæge and eal swa
he wæs on þære swigmesse and geornlice bæd for þon cincge þa
ateowde him godes engel and let fallen an writ uppan þæt wifod on þan
wæs gewriten eal hu se cing gefremode þa synne.
 363. Eac hit cwæð on þam gewrite þæt ure drihten
hæfde forgifen þan cinge þa ilca synne þurh þæs halgenes gebedu
gif he æfer ma forðward fram þan synnum geswican wolde.
 365. Eac hit cwæð ætþan ænde þæt ælc þære
manna þe bið gebunden mid mycelre synne and he cleopige to þan haligan
godes deorlinge egidium.
 367. Soðlice gelæfe he þæt drihten hine aleseð fram
his synne gif æfer ma eac þæs geswican wille.
 368. Witodlice eal swa se godes mann hæfde gemæssod &
geseah þæt gewrit þus awriten, he þancode georne þus his drihtne mid
wependre stæmne and betæhte hit siððan þan cincge to rædenne and
eal swa he hit geræd hæfde, þa oncneow he on þam gewritu þa
manfulnesse þe he gedon hæfde and feol sona to þas halgan fotum biddende
þæt he for him geþingode to drihtene mid his gebedum.
 372. Hwæt þa se drihtnes deorling egidius underfeng þa on
his gebedum and bebead him eft mid þreate þæt he næfre ma eft þone
gylt ne geedneowode.
 374. Soðlice efter þis bæd se godes man þam cinge geleafe
þæt he moste faran ham to his mynstre and geneosian his gebroðra.
 375. Se cing him andwyrde and cwæð, Hlaford fæder get ic
wolde biddan þe ane bene gif hit þin wille wære þæt þu wunodest
swa lange mid me þæt ic moste hæbban full specen wið þe forþon ic
lange gewilnode þin halige lif to geseonne and þine halwændan spæce
to geheronne.
 379. Se eadige egidius þa eal swa se cyning hine gebæd.
 379. Wunode þa get mid him sume feawe dagas and siððan he
begeat ærfoðlice geleafan þæt he moste faran fram him.
 381. Se cing sænde þa swiðe fela gersumas ham to his mynstre
mid him and het hi geoffrian up to þan weofode his drihtne to lofa and þan
halgan apostole þe se mynster wæs for gehalgod and hit wearð þa swa
gedon.
 383. Soðlice þa se godes þeow sceolde faran ham to his
mynstre þa ongan se cyng sarilice to wepenne and þus cwæð mid wependre
stæmne, Eala to hwam mæg ic heonon forð cleopian oððe hwylc frofer
mæg ic onfon.
 386. Ða cwæð se halga wer to þam cinge mid wependre
stæmne, Drihten se þe alesde his halgan gehealde þe fram eallen yfele.
 387. Hwæt þa se godes freond egidius geweande þa to his
mynstres weard and eal swa he becom to anre burh þe is gehaten mausensis,
þa genam he þær herebeorge and drihten hine þær gewurþode swa
þæt he arærde anes rices mannes sune of deaðe binnen þære ilcan
burh and þærrihtes gewænde ham to his mynstre.
 391. Witodlice eal swa he hæfde þær gewunod sume stunde,
þa smeade he on his geþance þæs mynstres frigdom to begetenne æt
þan pape mid anre privilegium and bæd swiðe geornlice his drihten
þæt he hit geforðian most swa swa hit him licwurðe wære.
 394. He let þa ealle þa þincg þe him neodbehefe wæron to
hæbbenne and genam þa mid him swa feola gebroðra swa swa him þuhte
þæt hit wel beon mihte and for þa into rome mid mycele sibsumnesse and
symle tacne wyrcende þurh his drihtnes mihte.
 397. Soðlice eal swa he com into rome þa eode he mid mycelre
eadmodnessa into þære eadigra apostola mynstre petri and pauli and hine
þærinne swiðe georne gebæd and æfter þan þe he hæfde criste
geoffrod his halige bedu þa underfeng se papa hine mid mycelan wurðmente
and wearð swiðe on his tocyme.
 401. Se eadiga egidius wunode mid þan papan sume stunde and se
papa hine bæd þæt he scolde geornan to him swa hwæt swa his wille
wære þæt he habban wolde and se godes man him wæs þæs
inwardlicere heorte þanconde and bæd æt þan papan his mynstres
frigdom and se papa him þæs bliðelice getyþode and sealde him ænne
privilegium/ to swutelunge þæs fridomes.
 405. Ða on sume dæge eal swa he wæs dreolice on his gebedum
innan petres mynstre, þa geseah he þærinne twa duren þa wæron
geworhte of cypressene treowe and þæron wæron gegrauene þære
apostola anlicnesse þe he gebead eac æt þan papan to his mynstres wlite
and for wedde þæra soðan lufa and he him þæs bliðelice
getyðode.
 409. Ða nyste se godes mann hu hi scoldon cuman ham to his
mynstre ac betæhte þa lade on drihtnes gewealde and het hi gebringen into
þære tefre and hi þærinne forleton and hit wearð swa gedon.
 411. And eal swa þa romani þæt geseawon, þa þuhte heom
mycel wunder of þa deorwurþam madmas þæt se godes man hi wolde swa
lihtlice forleosan.
 413. Ac se papa undergeat and ealle þa þe þis miht cuðen
þæt he hit dyde þurh his drihtnes willan.
 414. Eac æfter þisum he begeat earfoðlice geleafan æt
þan papan þæt he moste faran ham to his mynstre forþon þe he
hæfde oncnawan on him eall þæt drihtne licwurðe wæs.
 416. Hi betæhton þa heora lif and heora sawle þam
ælmihtigum gode and sealde heom betweoxan sibbecos and swa toscyledon mid
þære soðan lufe.
 418. Ða gewænde se godes deorlincg egidius ut of rome ham to
his mynstre weard and eal swa he com to cabenomen þære burh þa gereste
he hine þær þreo dagas forþon þe he wæs swiðe werig of swa
mycelre fara and gehælde þær ænne crepel se wæs fram feala geare
eal togædere gecrocad.
 422. He gewænde þa fram þære burh mid bliðum mode and
eal swa hraðe swa he wæs gecumen ham to his mynstre, þa cydde me him
þæt þær wæron gecumen up æt þære hyðe twa duren
wunderlice fægre gegrafena þa wæron buton scipe and buton ælces
mannes lade þider geferode.
 425. Ða se eadige egidius þis geherde he wearð þa swiðe
bliðe and his drihten þæs miccla þancunge dyde þæt he þa
deorwurða madmas swa ungederode þider gesænt hæfde þeah ðe hio
gelomlice wæron fordrifene innen þære sæ and oft tosceacenne ofer
feola sandbedda and feola earfoðnesse þolodon eac þurh manega hæfene
lædunge and swa þeah hi belifen ungederode þurh drihtnes
mildheortnesse.
 430. Se godes man eode þa to þær æstaðe þær se
haligdom wæs up gelænt and let hine bringen into his mynstre mid micclan
arwurðnesse and þærinne he let hine uparæren for wlite and for
þæs mynstres neode þæt me scolde æfre ma oncnawan be þeosum
tacne þæs mynstres frydom þe he hæfde begetan æt þam papan.
 434. Drihten wolde þa geglængen his cniht mid cynehelme and
forgeldan him his micclan geswinc forþon þe he hæfde him fulfremedlice
gefandod on his þeowdome and nolde hine na læng þær geletton ac
geswutelode him þurh þone halige gast þæt he sceolde hrædlice
geændian his lif.
 438. And he hit gecydde þa sume his gastlice gebroðre
eadmodlice biddende þæt hi for hine gebædon and hi swa dydon mid
mycelre lufa.
 439. He befadode þa swiðe arwurðlice eal þæs mynstres
þincg and gewissode his gebroðra mid mycelre eadmodnesse to godes þenunge
and to haligre drohtnunge geornlice getrymode.
 441. Ða com se time þæt se eadige egidius sceolde
underfangen his mede æt criste þæt wæs on kalendas septembris.
 442. He geændode his swincfulle lif and drihten betæhte his
sawle and sancte michael and his ængla wyrd to begemanne and hi hio
geferodon mid sangum up to heofonum and hio þær geoffrodon ure drihtene se
þe leofað and rixað mid his sune and mid þan halgan gaste an god on
ealra worulda woruld a butan ænde amen.

END_TEXT

LS 10 (Guth)
B3.3.10.
Saint Guthlac: Gonser 1909, 117-34.



 4.5. Wæs þær in þam sprecenan iglande sum mycel hlæw
of eorþan geworht, þone ylcan hlæw iu geara men bræcon and dulfon for
feos þingum.
 4.10. Ða wæs þær on oðre sidan ðæs hlæwes
gedolfen swylce mycel seaþ; on þam seaþe ufan se eadiga wer Guðlac him
hus and eardungstowe getimbrode.
 4.16. Sona on fruman, þæs ðe he þæt ancersetl gesæt,
þa þohte he, þæt he nawðer þara ne wyllenes hrægles ne linenes
brucan wolde, ac on fellenum gegyrlan þæt he wolde ealle dagas his lifes
alifigean; and he hit swa forðgelæste.
 4.24. Ælce dæge wæs his ondleofenes swylc gemetegung of
þære tide, þe he þæt westen ærest eardigean began.
 4.33. Þa gelamp hit sume dæge, mid þy þe he þy
gewunelican þeowdome his sealmas sang and his gebedum ætfealh, þa se
ealda feond mancynnes gengde geond þæt græswang swa grymetende leo,
þæt he his costunga attor wide geond stregde.
 4.42. Mid þy he þa yfelnes mægen and his grimnesse attor
teldað, þæt he mid þy atre þa menniscean heortan wundað, þa
semninga swa he of bendum & of brogan wæs his costunge ða he ða
þam earhwinnendan stræle on þam mode gefæstnode þæs Cristes
cempan.
 4.51. Þa he ða se eadiga wer mid þære geætredan
stræle gewundod wæs þæs werigan gastes, þa wæs his mod þæs
eadigan weres swiðe gedrefed on him be þam onginne, þe he ongan, þæt
westen swa ana eardigan.
 4.58. He ða hine hider and þyder gelomlice on his mode cyrde,
and he gemunde þa ærran fyrena and leahteras, þe he gefremede and
geworht hæfde; he wende, þæt he hie æfre gebetan ne meahte.
 4.66. Þa wæs se eadiga wer Guðlac mid þære ormodnesse
swa gedrefed and gewundod, þæt he sylfa nyste, hwider he mid his mode
cyrran wolde.
 4.74. Þa wæs ðy ðriddan dæge þære
æfterfyllendan nihte, þæt he ðam wolberendan geþohtum fæste
wiðstod; and eft swa he witedomlice muðe sang and þus cleopode to gode
and cwæð, Min drihten, mid minre geswencendnesse ic clypige and cige, ac
gehyr ðu me and me gefultuma in minum earfeðum.
 4.88. Ða wæs sona æfter ðam, þæt his se getrywa
fultum him to com, sanctus Bartholomeus, and nalas þæt he him on slæpe
ætywde, ac he wæccende þone apostol on gelicre fægernesse geseah and
sceawode.
 4.95. And he wæs þa sona se eadiga wer swiðe feonde þæs
heofonlican cuman.
 4.103. Frefrede hine þa sanctus Bartholomeus, and hine mid
wordum trymede and strangode, and hine het, þæt him ne tweode no, ac
þæt he wære anræde; and he him on fultume beon wolde in eallum his
earfeðum.
 4.110. Ða he se haliga Guðlac þas word gehyrde his þæs
getrywan freondes, ða wæs he on gæstlicre blisse and heofoncundre gife
swiðe gefeonde, and his geleafan fæste in god sylfne getrymede and
fæstnode.
 4.117. Syððan seo tid wæs, þæt næfre þæt deoful
eft wið hine þære ormodnesse wæpnum on hine sceotode.
 5.1. Swylce eac gelamp on sumne sæl, þa he ymb ða drohtunga
smeade his lifes, hu he mihte gecwemlicost, ða coman þær semninga tu
deoflu of þære lyfte slidan, and þa mid cuðlicum wordum ðus
cwædon, We syndon gewisse þines lifes, and þines geleafan trumnesse we
witon.
 5.11. And þin geþyld eac we cunnon unoferswiðde, þær we
þin cunedon and costedon, þæt we mid manigfealdum cræfte ussa
wæpna stræla wið mec sendan.
 5.17. Wene ic þæt we ðe furðor ne wyllan leng swencan, ne
ðe mid brogan bysmrian; ac nales þæt an þæt we ðe ðær nu
nellað lætan, þær ðu geðoht hæfdest, ac we ðe eac wyllað
secgan be ðam eallum, þe iu geara westen geardodan, hu hie heora lif
lifdon.
 5.26. Moyses æst and Elias hie fæston, and swylce eac se
hælend ealles middangeardes in westene he fæste, and swylce eac ða
mæran munecas, þe mid Egiptum wæron and þa ær in westenum
eardodan, þa ðe þurh heora forhæfednesse in him eallum uncysta
ofslogon and acwealdon.
 5.36. Þonne gif ðu þæs wilnast, þæt ðu of ðe ða
ærran fremednesse yfelra leahtra ofaðwea, þonne scealt þu þinne
lichaman þurh forhæfednesse wecean.
 5.41. Forþan swiððor swa ðu þe her on worulde swecst and
wecest to forgifenesse þinra gylta, swa ðu þonne eft bist in ecnessum
getrymed fæstlicor.
 5.46. And swa micle swiðor swa ðu on þyssan andweardan life
ma earfeða dreogest, swa micle þu eft in towyrdnesse forgifest and þanne
þu bist on fæsten her on worulde astreaht, þonne byst ðu ahafen for
godes eagan.
 5.53. Forðan þin fæsten ne sceal beon þæt a twega daga
fyrst oððe þreora oððe ælce dæge, þæt ðu ðe swa on
teala micelre forhæfdnesse ahebbe; ac on seofon nihta fyrste fæsten bið
to clænsigeanne se man.
 5.60. Swa on syx dagum ærest god ealles middangeardes
fægernesse gehiwode and on þam seofoðan hine reste, swa þonne
gedafenað þane man gelice þurh syx daga fæsten þone gast
frætewigean, and þonne þy seofeðan dæge mete þycgan and his
lichoman restan.
 5.70. Ða he ða se eadiga wer þas word gehyrde, þa aras he
sona and to gode cleopode and hine gebæd and þus cwæð, Min drihten
god, syn mine fynd a onhinder gecyrred, forðan ic þe ongite and geþence,
forðan þu eart min scyppend.
 5.78. Þa sona se awyrgeda feond efne swa rec beforan his onsyne
aidlode.
 5.81. He þa sona forseah þa deofollican lare, forþan he þa
ealle idle and unnytte ongeat; ac þa feng to þære teala myclan
andleofone, þæt wæs to þam berenan hlafe, and þone geþygde and
his feorh bigferede.
 5.88. Ða þa werigan gastas þis ongeaton, þæt he
forhogode hie and heora lara, hie þæt mid wependre stefne bemurnon and
wide geond þæt land wæðdon; and he se geadiga wer swa gesigefæsted
þa bysmornesse ealle forhogode þara werigra gasta and him for naht dyde.
 5.98. Swylce eft gelamp on sumum sæle ymb unmanega dagas,
þæs þe he Guðlac þy gewunelican þeowdom wæccende þa niht in
halegum gebedum wunode, þa on þære nihte stilnesse gelamp semninga,
þæt þær com micel mænego þara werigra gasta.
 5.107. And hie eal þæt hus mid heora cyrme gefyldon; and him
on ælce healfe inguton, ufan and neoþan and æghwænon.
 5.111. Wæron hie on syne egeslice, and hæfdon heafdu, and
lange sweoran, and mænigre onsyne; wæron fulice and orfyrme on heora
bearde; and hæfdon ruge earan, and woh neb, egeslice eagan, and ondrysenlice
muðas.
 5.119. And heora teð wæron horses tuxum gelice, and him
wæron þa hracan lige afylled, and hie wæron ondrysenlice on stefne.
 5.123. And hie hæfdon wo sceancan, and micle cneowo and hindan
greate, and misscrence tan, and has hrymedon on heora cleopunge.
 5.128. And hie swa ungemetlice hrymdon and foran mid forhtlicum
egesum and ungeþwærnessum, þæt hit þuhte, þæt hit eall betweoh
heofone and eorðan hleoþrode þam egeslicum stefnum.
 5.135. Næs þa nænig ylding to þam, syððan hie in
þæt hus comon, hie ða sona þone halgan wer eallum limum gebundenum
hine tugon and læddon ut of ðære cytan.
 5.141. Ond hie hine on þæt swearte fenn læddon and hine on
þa horwihtan wæter wurpon and besencton.
 5.144. Æfter þam hie hine bæron and læddon æfter
reðum stowum þæs westenes betuh þa þiccan gewridu þara brymela,
þæt eal se lichoma wæs gewundod.
 5.150. Mid þy hie ða lange on þære þystran nihte hine
swa læddon and swencton, þa leton hie hine bidan ana and gestandan; heton
hine þa, þæt he of ðam westene gewite, oððe gif he þæt nolde,
þæt hie woldon mid maran brogan bysmrigan and wæcan.
 5.159. He ða se eadiga wer heora worda ne gymde, ac he mid
witigende muðe þus cwæð, Dryhten me is on ða swiðran healfe,
forðam ic ne beo oncyrred.
 5.165. Þa æfter ðam þa werigan gastas hine genamon and
hine swungon mid isenum swipum, and þa æfter þam hine læddon in þam
andrysenlicum fiðerum betuh þa caldan facu þære lyfte.
 5.171. Þa he ða wæs on þære heannesse þære lyfte
up gelæded, þa geseah he ealne norðdæl heofones, swylce he wære
þam sweartestum wolcnum afylled swiðra genipa.
 5.178. Þa geseah he semninga þær ða ondrysenlican fiðeru
ongen cuman þara werigra gasta, and unmæte weorod hyra þær coman
togenes, and hie sona þær tosomne geþyddon, hie ða sona þone halgan
wer gelæddon to ðam sweartum tintreges gomum helledures.
 5.191. Ða he ðær geseah þa smicendan þismas þara
byrnendra liga and þone ege þære sweartan nywylnesse, he ða sona
wæs ofergeotol ealra þæra tintegra, þe he fram þam werigum gastum
ær dreah and drefde.
 5.194. And nalas þæt an þæt he þær þa leglican
hyðe ðæs fyres upþyddan geseah and eac þa fulan receas tunge swefles
þær geseah upgeotan.
 5.200. Hie þa sona þa werigan gastas betwuh ða grimlican
ligeas inhruron and feollon, and þær þa sawla arleasra manna
manigfealdum tintregum tintregud.
 5.205. Þa he se eadiga wer Guðlac geseah þa micelnesse þara
wita, and hine for þy ege swiðlice onþræc, ða clypedon hie sona þa
werigan gastas micelre clypunge and þus cwædon, Us is miht seald þe to
scafanne on ðas witu þysse neowolnesse.
 5.214. And her þæt fyr, þæt ðu sylfa in þe
bærndest, and for þinum synnum helleduru ongen þe openað.
 5.218. Mid þy þe ða werigea gastas þyssum wordum spræcon
and him swa to beotodon, þa andswarude he him and him to cwæð, Wa eow
þystra bearnum and forwyrde tuddor ge syndon dustes acsan.
 5.224. Hwa geaf eow yrmingum þæt, ðæt ge min geweald
ahton in þas witu to sendanne?
 5.227. Hwæt, ic eom her andweard and earo, and bide mines
dryhtnes willan, for hwan mid eowrum leasum beotingum me bregean?
 5.232. Hie þa werigan gastas hine to ðam gegearwodon, swylce
hine man þær inscufan wolde.
 5.236. Ða semninga com se heofones biggenga, se haliga apostol
sanctus Bartholomeus, mid heofonlicre beorhtnesse and wuldre scinende betuh
þa dimman þystro þære sweartan helle.
 5.242. Hie ða þa werigan gastas ne meahton þære
fægernesse þæs haligan cuman þær gewunigean, ac hie sylfe in
heolstre hyddon.
 5.247. Þa he ða se eadiga wer his þone getrywan freond
geseah, ða wæs he mid gastlicre gefeannesse and on heofoncundre blisse
swiðe gefeonde.
 5.252. And þa æfter þam fleah se haliga Guðlac mid þam
apostole sancte Bartholomei to heofona rices wuldre, and hine se hælend
þær onfeng, and he þær leofað and rixað in heofona rices wuldre a
butan ende on ecnesse, <foreign>Amen fiat</foreign>.
