LS 10.1 (Guth)
B3.3.10.1.
Saint Guthlac: Gonser 1909, 100-73.



 0.1. Urum wealdende rihtgelyfendum a worulda woruld, minum þam
leofestan hlaforde ofer ealle oðre men, eorðlice kyningas, Alfwold
Eastengla kyning, mid rihte and mid gerisenum rice healdend, Felix þone
rihtan geleafan gesette eallum geleafullum godes folcum, and ecere
gesundfulnysse hælo and gretingce gesend.
 0.6. Þinum wordum and bebodum ic hyrsumode: ða boc ic gesette,
þe þu ahtest be life þæs arwurðan gemynde Guðlaces, hluttrum
wordum and tacnum.
 0.10. Ic forþan halsige and bidde þone gelæredan and þone
geleafullan, gif he her hwylc hleahterlic word onfinde, þæt he þæt us
ne wite.
 0.12. Ac gemune and geþence ælc þara tælendra and
hleahterfulra, þæt on wordum godes rice ne wunað, ac on anwylnysse
þæs halgan geleafan.
 0.14. And þa hælo middaneardes ac gemune and geþence na fram
idelum þancum geþoht, ac fram fiscerum gebodod and gesæd.
 0.17. Ac gif hwylc man ure angin and weorc tæle, swa ic menige
wat on Angelcynne mid þam fægerum stafum gegylde, fæger and glæwlice
gesette, þæt hig þas boc sylf settan mihton, ne wite he þonne us, swa
we/ neode and hæse gehyrsumodon and word gefyldon.
 0.22. Forþan la, þu leornere, gif þu mid þan þeawe
tælendra me hleahtrige, warna þe sylfne, þær þu þe hleahtres
wene, þæt þu þær semninga ne wurðe mid dymnysse þystro ablend.
 0.25. Þæt bið blindra þeaw, þonne hi on leohte beoð,
þæt hig sylfe nyton, buton hi on þeostrum dwelion.
 0.26. On halgum gewrihtum bið oft unwisdom blindnes geciged,
forþon se fruma ealles yfeles ærest þonan cymð.
 0.29. For þisum þingum þonne, þu leornere, ic þe manige,
þæt þu þa fremdan ne tæle, þelæs þu fram oþrum eft swa
fremde getæled sig.
 0.31. Ac þylæs ic lengc þone þanc hefige þara leornendra
mid gesegenum þara fremdra tælnysse, swa swa ic strange sæ and mycele
oferliðe, and nu becume to þære smyltestan hyðe Guðlaces lifes.
 0.35. Forþon þu abæde æt me, þæt ic þe write and
sæde be þære drohtnunge Guðlaces and his lifes bysene, ic þe
forþon hyrsumode, and ic forþon write, swa me þa dihteras sædon, þe
his lif geornost cuðon: ærost hwylc wære se fruma, oþþe on hwylcum
ende he hit eft gelædde.
 0.39. For þisum þingum ic þas bec sette, þæt þa, þe
his lif þæs eadigan weres cuðon, þæt him þonne þig geneahhor
his lifes to gemyndum come; and þam oðrum, þe hit ær ne cuþon, swa
swa ic him rumne weg and geradne tæhte.
 0.44. Þas þingc, þe ic her onwrite, ic geleornode fram
gesegenum þæs arwyrðan abbodes Wilfrides.
 0.45. Swilc eac manige oðre me þæt sædon, þe mid þam
eadigan were wæron and his lif hira eagum ofersawon.
 0.47. Ne tweoge ic aht þa mine dihteras, þæt hi mihton
gemunan and eall asecgan þa wundru þises eadigan weres: wæron hi swiðe
wide cuðe and mære geond Angelcynnes land.
 0.51. Ic forþon þinum bebodum hyrsumede, and þin word and
willan hæbbe gefylled, and þæt gewrit þisse andweardan hyrde, swa ic
mihte mid wisdome minra foregengena and þære yldrena, gesette; þone
fruman on þam fruman ic gesette, and þone ende in þam ende.
 1.1. On þam dagum æþelredes, þæs mæran kyninges
Myrcna, wæs sum æþela man on þære hehþeode Myrcnarice; se wæs
haten Penwald.
 1.3. He wæs þæs yldestan and þæs æþelstan cynnes,
þe Iclingas wæron genemnede.
 1.4. He wæs for worulde welig and myccle gestreon hæfde, and
þaþa he welegost wæs and mæst gestreon hæfde, ða gyrnde he him
his gemæccan to nymanne.
 1.7. He him þa ana geceas on æþre mædena heape, þe
þær fægorost wæs and æþelestan kynnes; seo wæs gehaten
Tette.
 1.10. And hi þa samod wæron oð þone fyrst, þæt god
foresceawode, þæt þæt wif mid bearne geeacnod wæs.
 1.11. Ða se tima com, þæt heo þæt bearn cennan scolde,
þa sæmninga com tacn of heofenum, and þæt tacn swytelice mid inseglum
beclysde.
 1.15. Efne, men gesawon ane hand on þam fægerestan readan hiwe
of heofonum cumende; and seo hæfde ane gyldene rode, and wæs æteowod
manegum mannum, and helde toweard toforan þæs huses duru, þær
þæt cild inne acenned wæs.
 1.19. Ða men þa ealle, þe þæt gesawon, þiderweard
efeston, þæt hig þæt tacen swutelicor geseon woldon and ongitan; seo
hand þa gewende mid þære rode up to heofonum.
 1.22. Ða men þa ealle, þe þæt tacen gesawon, hi hi þa
ealle on eorðan astrehton, and god bædon, þæt he heom geswutelian
scolde, hwæt þæt tacn and æþt forebeacn beon scolde, þe him
þær swa færlice æteowod wæs.
 1.25. Ða hi þa þæt gebed gefylled heafdon, þa com
þær sum wif mid miccle rædlicnysse yrnan of þam huse, þe þæt
cild inne acenned wæs, and cleopode and cwæð þus to þam mannum:
Beoð ge staþolfæste and gehyrte, forþan þæs toweardan wuldres man
on þisum middanearde her ys acenned.
 1.31. Ða hi þa men þæt word gehyrdon, þa spræcon hig
heom betwynan, þæt þæt wære godcundlic tacn, þe þær
ætywed wæs, forþon þe þæt bearn þær acenned wæs.
 1.33. Sume hig þonne cwædon, þæt þurh godcunde
stihtunge in þære ece eadignysse him wære seo gifu forestihtod þæs
haliges tacnes, þe him æt his acennednysse ætywod wæs.
 1.37. Wæron men swiþe wundriende be þære wisan and be
þam tacne, þe þær ætywed wæs; and efne, ær þon þe sunna
on setl eode, hit wæs ofer eall Middelengla land cuð and mære.
 2.1. Ða þæs ymbe eahta niht, þæs þe mon þæt cild
brohte to þam halgan þweale fulwihtbæþes, ða wæs him nama sceapen
of þæs cynnes gereorde and of þære þeode Guþlac, swa hit wære
of godcundlicre stihtunge gedon, þæt he swa genemned wære.
 2.5. Forþon swa þa wisan leorneras secgað on Angelcynne,
þæt se nama standeð on feawum gewritum: Guðlac se nama ys on romanisc
<foreign>belli munus</foreign>.
 2.7. Forþon þeah he mid woruldlicre geswince menige
earfoðnysse adreah, and þeah mid gecyrrednysse þa gife þære ecan
eadignysse mid sige eces lifes onfengc, and swa mid þam apostolum cweþende:
<foreign>beatus vir, qui suffert temptationem, quia cum probatus fuerit, accipiet
coronam vite, quam repromisit dominus diligentibus se</foreign>.
 2.13. Þæt ys on englisc: eadig man bið, cwæð he, se
þe her on worulde manigfealdlice geswincnysse and earfoðnysse dreogeð,
forþon mid þam þe he gecostod bið and geswenced, þonne onfehð he
ecum beage, and þæt god gehet eallum þam, þe hine lufiað.
 2.18. Æfter þon þe he wæs aþwegen mid þam þweale
þæs halgan fulluhtes, ða wæs he eft to þære fæderlican healle
gelædd and þær gefedd.
 2.20. Mid þam þe seo yld com, þæt hit sprecan mihte
æfter cnihtwisan, þonne wæs he nawiht hefig, ne unhyrsum his yldrum on
wordum ne þam, þe hine feddon, nænigum oþþe yldran oþþe
gingran.
 2.23. Ne he cnihtlice galnysse næs begangende, ne idele
spellunge folclicra manna, ne ungeliclice olæcunge, ne leaslicetunge; ne he
mistlice fugela sangas ne wurþode, swa oft swa cnihtlicu yldo begæð, ac
on his scearpnysse þæt he weox, and wearð glæd on his ansyne, and
hluttor and clæne on his mode, and bilwite on his þeawum.
 2.29. Ac on him wæs se scima gastlicre beorhtnysse swa swyðe
scinende, þæt ealle þa men, þe hine gesawon, on him geseon mihton þa
þing, þe him towearde wæron.
 2.32. Ða wæs æfter siðfate, þæt mægen on him
weox, and gestiþode on his geogoðe; þa gemunde he þa strangan dæda
þara iumanna and þara woruldfrumena.
 2.34. He þa, swa he of slæpe onwoce, wearð his mod oncyrred,
and he gesomnode miccle scole and wered his geþoftena and hys
efenhæfdlingas, and him sylf to wæpnum feng.
 2.37. Þa wræc he his æfþancas on his feondum, and heora
burh bærnde, and heora tunas oferhergode; and he wide geond eorþan
menigfeald wæl felde, and sloh, and of mannum heora æhta nam.
 2.41. Þa wæs he semninga innan manod godcundlice and læred,
þæt he þa word hete: ealle þa he swa he het þriddan dæl agifan
þam mannum, þe he hit ær ongenæmde.
 2.45. Ða wæs ymbe nigon winter þæs þe he þa ehtnysse
begangende wæs se eadiga Guthlac, and he hine sylfne betweox þises
andweardan middaneardes wealcan dwelode.
 2.48. Þa gelamp sume niht, mid þam þe he com of farendum
wege, and he hys þa werigan lima reste, and he menig þing mid his mode
þohte, ða wæs he færinga mid godes ege onbryrd, and mid gastlicre
lufan his heorte innan gefylled.
 2.51. And mid þy he geþohte þa ealdan kyningas, þe iu
wæron, he awoc þurh earmlicne deað and þurh sarlicne utgang þæs
manfullan lifes, þe þas woruld forleton.
 2.54. And þa micclan welan, þe hig ærhwilon ahton, he geseh
on hrædlicnysse ealle gewitan; and he geseah his agen lif dæghwamlice to
þam ende efstan and scyndan.
 2.58. Ða wæs he sæmninga mid þam godcundan egesan innan
swa swyþe onbryrded, þæt he andette gode, gif he him þæs
mergendæges geunnan wolde, þæt he his þeow beon wolde.
 2.61. Mid þy þære nihte þystro gewiton, and hit dæg
wæs, þa aras he and hine sylfne getacnode insegle Cristes rode.
 2.63. Ða bead he his geferum, þæt hi fundon him oðerne
ealdorman and latteow hira geferscipe; and he him andette and sæde, þæt
he wolde beon cristes þeow.
 2.66. Mid þam þe his geferan þas word gehyrdon, þa wæron
hi swiþe wundriende and swyþe forhte for þam wordum, þe hi þær
gehyrdon; þa hi ealle to him aluton and hine bædon, þæt he næfre
þa þing swa gelþste, swa he mid wordum gecwæð.
 2.70. He þa hwæþere heora worda ne gimde, ac þæt ilce,
þæt he ær geþohte, þæt he þæt forðlæstan wolde: barn
him swa swyþe innan þære godes lufan, þæt nalæs þæt an
þæt he þas woruld forseah, ac swilce hys yldrena gestreon and his eard
and þa sylfan his heafodgemacan, þæt he þæt eall forlet.
 2.75. Ða he wæs feower and twentig wintra eald, þa forlet he
ealle þas woruldglenga and eallne his hiht on Crist gesette.
 2.78. And þa æfter þon þæt he ferde to mynstre, þe ys
gecweden Hrypadun, and þær þa gerynelican sceare onfeng sancte Petres
þæs apostoles under Ælfðryðe abbodyssan; and syþþan he to
sceare and to þam munuclife feng, hwæt, he nænigre wætan onbitan
nolde, þe druncennysse þurh come.
 2.83. And þa for þan þingum hine þa broðra hatedon, þy
he swa forhæbbende wæs; and þa raðe, syþþan hi þa
hluttorlicnysse his modes and þa clænnysse his lifes ongeaton, þæt
hig ealle hine lufedon.
 2.87. Wæs he on ansine mycel and on lichaman clæne, wynsum on
his mode and wlitig on ansyne; he wæs liðe and gemetfæst on his worde,
and he wæs geþyldig and eadmod; and a seo godcunde lufu on hys heortan hat
and byrnende.
 2.92. Mid þy he þa wæs in stafas and on leornunge getogen,
þa girnde he his sealmas to leornianne; þa wæron þa wæstmberendan
breost þæs eadigan weres mid godes gife gefyllede and mid þam lareowdome
þæs hean magistres godes, þæt he wþs on godcundlican þeodscipe
getyd and gelæred.
 2.97. Mid þam þe he wæs twa gear on þære leornunge,
ða hæfde he his sealmas geleornod, and canticas and ymnas, and gebeda,
æfter cyriclicre endebyrdnysse.
 2.99. Þa ongan he wurðigan þa godan þeawas þara godra on
þam life: eadnysse and hyrsumnysse, geþyld and þolemodnysse and
forhæfednysse his lichaman; and ealra þara godra mægen he wæs
begangende.
 2.104. Ða ymbe twa winter, þæs þe he his lif swa leofode
under munuchade, þæt he þa ongan wilnian westenes and sundersetle.
 2.106. Mid þy he gehyrde secgan and he leornode be þam ancerum,
þe geara on westene and on sundorsettlum for godes naman wilnodon and heora
lif leofodon, ða wæs his heorte innan þurh godes gifu onbryrdod,
þæt he westenes gewilnode.
 2.110. Ða wæs sona ymbe unmanige dagas, þæt he him leafe
bæd æt þam þeowum, þe þær yldest wæron, þæt he feran
moste.
 3.1. Ys on Bretonelande sum fenn unmætre mycelnysse, þæt
onginneð fram Grante ea, naht feor fram þære cestre, ðy ylcan nama ys
nemned Granteceaster.
 3.3. Þær synd unmætre moras, hwilon sweart wætersteal,
and hwilon fule eariþas yrnende, and swylce eac manige ealand, and hreod, and
beorhgas, and treowgewrido, and hit mid menigfealdan bignyssum widgille and
lang þurhwunað on norðsæ.
 3.8. Mid þan se foresprecena wer and þære eadigan gemynde
Guðlac/ þæs widgillan westenes þa ungearawan stowe þær gemette,
þa wæs he mid godcundre fultume gefylst, and þa sona þan rihtestan
wege þyder togeferde.
 3.11. Þa wæs, mid þam þe he þyder com, þæt he
frægn þa bigengcan þæs landes, hwær he on þam westene him
eardungstowe findan mihte.
 3.14. Mid þy hi him menigfeald þing sædon be þære
widgilnysse þæs westenes, þa wæs Tatwine gehaten sum man, sæde
þa, þæt he wiste sum ealand synderlice digle, þæt oft menige men
eardian ongunnon, ac for menigfealdum brogum and egsum and for annysse þæs
widgillan westenes þæt hit nænig man adreogan ne mihte, ac hit ælc
forþan befluge.
 3.21. Mid þam þe se halga wer Guðlac þa word gehyrde, he
bæd sona, þæt he him þa stowe getæhte, and he þa sona swa dyde.
 3.23. Eode þa on scip, and þa ferdon begen þurh þa rugan
fennas, oþ þæt hi comon to þære stowe, þe man hateð Cruwland.
 3.26. Wæs þæt land on middan þam westene swa gerad
geseted þæs foresædan fennas, swyðe digle, and hit swyþe feawe men
wiston, buton þam anum, þe hyt him tæhte; swylc þær næfre menig
man ær eardian ne mihte,ær se eadiga wer Guðlac tocom, for þære
eardunga þara awerigedra gasta.
 3.31. And he þa se eadiga wer Guðlac forhogode sona þa
costunge þæra awerigdra gasta, and mid heofonlicum fultume gestrangod
wearð; betwyx þa fenlican gewrido þæs widgillan westenes, þæt he
ana ongan eardian.
 3.35. Ða gelamp mid þære godcundan stihtunge, þæt he on
þa tid sancte Bartholomei þæs apostoles, þæt he com to þam
ealande, forþan he on eallum þingum his fultum sohte.
 3.37. And he þa gelufode þa stowe digelnysse, and he þa
gehet, þæt he wolde ealle dagas his lifes þær on þam ealande gode
þeowian.
 3.41. Mid þy þe he þa unmanige dagas þær wæs, þa
geondsceawode he þa þing, þe to þære stowe belumpon.
 3.43. Ða þohte he, þæt he eft wolde to þam mynstre feran
and his gebroðra gretan, forþan he ær fram heom ungegret gewat.
 3.45. Ða þæs on mergen, mid þan hit dæg wæs, þa
ferde he eft to þam mynstre; þa wæs he þær hundnigantig nihta mid
þam broðrum; and þa syþþan he hig grette, he þa eft hwærf to
þære stowe þæs leofan westenes mid twam cnihtum.
 3.49. Ða wæs se eahtoða dæg þæs kalendes Septembres,
þe man on þa tid wurðað sancte Bartholomei þæs apostoles, þa se
eadiga wer Guðlac com to þære foresprecenan stowe, to Cruwlande,
forþon he his fultum on eallum þingum ærest to þam sundorsetle sohte.
 3.53. Hæfde he þa on ylde six and twentig wintra, þa he
ærest se godes cempa on þam westene mid heofenlicre gife geweorðod
gesæt.
 3.56. Þa sona wið þam scotungum þara werigra gasta,
þæt he hine mid gastlicum wþpnum gescylde: he nam þone scyld þæs
halgan gastes, geleafan; and hyne on þære byrnan gegearowode þæs
heofonlican hihtes.
 3.59. And he him dyde heolm on heafod clænere geþanca; and mid
þam strælum þæs halgan sealmsangas a singallice wið þam
awerigedum gastum sceotode and campode.
 3.63. And nu, hwæt, ys swa swiþe to wundrianne þa diglan
mihte ures drihtnes and his mildheortnysse domas; hwa mæg þa ealle
asecgan.
 3.65. Swa se æþela lareow ealra þeoda sanctus Paulus se
apostol, þone ure drihten ælmihtig god forestihtode to godspellianne his
folce: he wæs ærþon ehtere his þære halgan cyrcan, and mid þan
þe he to Damascum ferde þære byrig, þæt he wæs of þam
þystrum gedwolumabroden Judea ungeleafulnysse mid þam swege heofonlicre
stefne: swa þonne þære arwurðan gemynde Guðlac of þære
gedrefednysse þissere worulde wæs gelæded to camphade þæs ecan
lifes.
 4.1. Be þam halgan were, hu he eardode on þære stowe.
 4.2. Onginne ic nu be ðam life ðæs eadigan weres Guðlaces,
swa swa ic gehyrde secgan þa, þe his lif cuðon, Wilfrid and Cissa;
þonne secge ic swa æfter þære endebyrdnysse.
 4.5. Wæs þær on þam ealande sum hlaw mycel ofer eorðan
geworht, þone ylcan men iu geara for feos wilnunga gedulfon and bræcon.
 4.9. Þa wæs þær on oþre sidan þæs hlawas gedolfen
swylce mycel wæterseað wære; on þam seaðe ufan se eadiga wer
Guthlac him hus getimbrode.
 4.16. Sona fram fruman, þæs þe he þæt ancersetle
gesæt, þa geþohte he, þæt he naðor ne wyllenes hrægles ne
linenes brucan nolde, ac on fellenum gegyrelan þæt he wolde ealle his
dagas his lifes alifian; and he hit swa forðgelæstende wæs.
 4.24. Ælce dæge wæs his bigleofan swylc to gereorde of
þære tide, þe he þæt westen eardigan ongan, þæt he nawiht ne
onbyrigde buton berene hlaf and wæter; and þonne sunne wæs on setle,
þonne þigede he þæs andlyfene, þe he bigleofode.
 4.33. Sona þæs þe he westen eardigan ongan, þa gelamp hit
sume dæge, mid þan gewunelican þeawe his sealm sang and his gebedum
befeal, þa se ealda feond mancynnes efne swa grymetigende leo, þæt he
his costunga attor wide todæleð.
 4.43. Mid þy he þa his yfelnysse mægen and grymnysse attor
þæt he mid þan þa menniscan heortan wundode, þa semninga swa he of
gebendum bogan his costunge streale on þam mode gefæstnode þæs
Cristes cempan.
 4.51. Ða he þa se eadiga wer mid þære geættredan
streale gewundod wæs þæs awerigedan gastes, ða wæs his mod
þæs eadigan weres swiðe gedrefed on him be þam onginne, þe he ongan,
þæt westen swa ana eardigan.
 4.58. Mid þam he þa hine hider and þyder gelomlice on his
mode cyrde, and gemunde þa ærran synna and leahtras, þe he gefremede and
geworht hæfde, and þa maran and unmættra him sylfa dyde, þonne he
wende, þæt he hi æfre gebetan mihte, ða hæfde hine seo deofollice
stræl mid ormodnysse gewundodne.
 4.68. Wæs se eadiga wer Guðlac mid þære ormodnysse þri
dagas gewundod, þæt he sylfa nyste, hwider he wolde mid his mode
gecyrran.
 4.74. Ða wæs þy þryddan dæge þære
æfterfylgendan nihte, þæt he þam tweogendum geþohtum fæstlice
wiðstod; and efne swa witedomlice muþe þæt he sang and clypode to gode
and cwæð: <foreign>In tribulatione mea invocavi Dominum, et reliqua</foreign>.
 4.82. Þæt ys on englisc: Min drihten on minre geswincnysse ic
þe to clypige, ac gehyr þu me and gefultuma me on minum earfeðum.
 4.88. Ða wæs sona æfter þon, þæt his se getreowa
fultum him to com, sanctus Bartholomeus; and nalæs þæt he him on
slæpe ætywde, ac he wæccende þone apostol on engellicre
fægernysse geseah and sceawode.
 4.95. And he þa sona se eadiga wer Guðlac swiþe bliþe
wæs þæs heofonlican cuman; and him sona his heorte and his geþanc
eall wæs onlihtod.
 4.100. And he þa hrædlice þa yfelan and þa twyfealdan
geþohtas forlet, and hine se heofonlica cuma frefrode, sanctus Bartholomeus,
and hine mid wordum trymede and strangode, and hine het, þæt he ne tweode,
ac þæt hewære anræd; and þæt he him on fultume beon wolde on
eallum his earfeðum.
 4.110. Ða se halga Guðlac þas word gehyrde his þæs
getreowan freondes, þa wæs he mid gastlicre blisse gefylled, and his
geleafan fæste on god sylfne getrymede and fæstnode.
 5.1. Swylce eac gelamp on sumne sæl, mid þy he be þære
drohtnunge smeade his lifes, hu he gode gecwemlicost mihte lybban, ða comon
semninga twegen deoflu to him of þære lyfte slidan, and þa to him
cuðlice spræcon and cwædon: We syndon gewisse þines lifes, and
þines geleafan trumnesse we witon, and eac þin geþyld we cunnon
unoferswyþed; and þær we þin fandedon and costodon, þæt we mid
manigfealde cræfte ura wæpna wið þe sendon.
 5.16. We nu heononforð nellað þe leng swencan ne þe
bysmrian; nalæs þæt an þæt we þe þæs nu nellað lettan,
þæs þu ær geþoht hæfdest, ac we þe eac wyllað secgan be
þam eallum, þe iu geara westene eardedon, hu hi heora lif leofodon.
 5.25. Moyses ærest and Helias hi fæston, and swylce eac se
hælend ealles middaneardes on westene he fæste, and eac swylce þa
mæran munecas, þa mid Aegiptum wæron and þær on westenum wunedon;
þa þurh heora forhæfdnysse on heom ealle uncyste ofaslogon and
acwealdon.
 5.35. Þonne gif þu þæt wilnast, þæt þu of þe þa
ær gefremedan synna aþwean wylt, þonne scealt þu þinne lichaman
þurh forhæfdnysse wæccan.
 5.40. Forþon swa myccle swa þu þe her on worulde swyþor
swincst, swa þu eft byst on ecnysse fæstlicor getrymed; and swa myccle swa
þu on þisum andweardan life ma eorfoða drigast, swa myccle þu eft on
toweardnysse gefehst; and þonne þu on fæsten her on worulde gestihst,
þonne bist þu ahafen for godes eagum.
 5.51. Forþon þin fæsten ne sceal beon þæt an twegra
daga fyrst oþþe þreora oþþe ælce dæge, þæt þu þe on
swa tela myccle forhæfdnysse ahebbe; ac on seofon nihta fyrstes fæste ne
biþ to clænsienne þone man.
 5.59. Swa on six dagum ærest god ealles middaneardes
fægernysse gehiwode and gefrætwode, and on þam seofoþan he hine
reste, swa þonne gedafenað þam þe gelice þurh six daga fæsten
þone gast gefrætwian, and þonne þy seofoðan dæg mete þicgan and
his lichaman restan.
 5.70. Ða se eadiga wer Guðlac þas word gehyrde, þa aras he
sona and to gode clypode and hyne gebæd and þus cwæð: Syn mine fynd,
min drihten god, a onhinder gecyrde, forþon ic þe ongite and oncnawe,
forþon þe þu eart min scyppend.
 5.78. Þa sona æfter þam wordum se awyrigeda gast efne swa
smic beforan his ansyne aidlode.
 5.81. He þa forseah þa deofollican lare, forþam þe he ealle
þa ydele ongeat; ac þa feng medmycclan bigleofan, þæt wæs to þam
berenan hlafe, and þone þigede and his lif bileofode.
 5.88. Ða þa awyrigedan gastas þæt ongeaton, þæt he
hig ealle forhogode and heora lara, hig þa þæt mid wependre stefne
sorhgodon, þæt hi oferswiðde wæron; and se eadiga wer swa
gesigefæstod wearð, þæt he þa bysmornysse forhogode heora lara and
heora costunga.
 5.98. Swylce eac gelamp on sumne sæl ymb unmanige dagas,
þæt he wæccende þa niht on halgum gebedum awunode, þa on þære
nihte stilnysse gelamp semninga, þæt þær comon mycele meniu þara
awyrigedra gasta, and hi eall þæt hus mid heora cyme fyldon; and hi on
ealce healfe inguton, ufan and neoðan and eghwonen.
 5.111. Hi wæron on ansyne egslice, and hig hæfdon mycele
heafda, and langne sweoran, and manigre ansyne; hi wæron fulice and orfyrme
on heora beardum; and hi hæfdon ruge earan, and woh nebb, and reðelice
eagan, and fule muðas; and heora toþas wæron gelice horses twuxan.
 5.121. And him wæron þa þrotan mid lege gefylde, and hi
wæron ongristlice on stefne; hi hæfdon woge sceancan, and mycele cneowu
and hindan greate, and mis croccetan and has runigendum stefnum; and hi þa
swa ungemetlicre gestundum foron and swa unmetlicre ege, þæt him þuhte,
þæt hit eall betweox heofone and eorðan hleoþrode þam egeslicum
stefnum.
 5.135. Næs þa nænig yldend to þam þæt, syþþan hi
on þæt hus comon, hi þa sona þone halgan wer eallum limum gebundon,
and hi hine tugon and læddon ut of þære cytan, and hine þa læddon
on þone sweartan fenn, and hine þa on þa orwehtan wæter bewurpon and
besencton.
 5.144. Æfter þon hi hine læddon on þam reðum stowum
þæs westenes betwux þa þiccan gewrido þara bremela, þæt him
wæs eall se lichama gewundod.
 5.150. Mid þy hi þa lange on þære þystrunge hine swa
swencton, þa leton hi hine ane hwile abidan and gestandan; heton hine þa,
þæt he of þam westene gewite, oþþe gif he þæt nolde, þonne
woldon hi hine mid maran bysmerum swencan and costian.
 5.158. He þa se eadiga wer Guðlac heora worda ne gimde, ac he
mid witegiende muðe þus cwæð: Drihten me ys on þa swyþran healfe
forþon ic ne beo oncyrred fram þe.
 5.165. Ða æfter þan þa awerigedan gastas hine genamon and
hine swungon mid isenum swipum, and þa æfter þon hi hine læddon on
þam ongryrlican fiðerum betwux þa cealdan faca þære lyfte.
 5.172. Þa he þa wæs on þære heannysse þære lyfte,
þa geseah he ealne norðdæl heofones, swylce he wære þam sweartestan
wolcnum ymbseald swiðlicra þeostra.
 5.178. Ða geseah he færinga unmæta werod þæra
awerigedra gasta him ongean cuman; and hi þa sona þær tosomne
gegaderodon, and hi þa sona ealle þone halgan wer gelæddon to þam
sweartum tintrehstowum, helleduru hi hine gebrohton.
 5.186. Ða he þa þær geseah þa fulnysse þæs smyces
and þa byrnenda lega and þone ege þære sweartan deopnysse, he þa
sona wæs forgitende ealra þara tintrega and þæra wita, þe he fram
þam awyrgedum gastum ær dreah and aþolode.
 5.200. Hi þa sona þa awyrgedan gastas betwux þa grimlican
lege inhruron and feollon, and þær þara arleasra manna sawla mid
manigfealdum witum getintregodon.
 5.205. Ða se eadiga Guthlac þa micelnysse geseah þara witu,
þa wæs he for þæra egsan swyðe afyrht.
 5.209. Ða cleopodon sona þa awyrgedan gastas mid mycelre
cleopunge and þus cwædon: Us ys miht geseald þe to sceofanne on þas
witu þisse deopnysse; and her þæt fyr, þæt þu sylfa on þe
onbærndest; and for þinum synnum and gyltum helleduru þe ongean
openað.
 5.218. Mid þy þa awyrgedan gastas þisum wordum beotodon, ða
andswerode he heom þus and cwæð: Wa eow þeostra bearn and forwyrde
tuddre, ge syndon dust and acsan and ysela; hwa sealde eow earman, þæt ge
min ahton geweald on þas witu to sendanne?
 5.227. Hwæt, ic her eom andweard and gearu, and bidige mines
drihtnes willan; for hwon sceolon ge mid eowrum leasum beotingum me egsian?
 5.233. Hig þa sona þa awyrgedan gastes to þam eadigan woldon,
swylce hi hine þær insceofan woldon.
 5.236. Ða semninga com se heofones bigengca, se halga apostol
sanctus Bartholomeus, mid heofonlicre byrhtnysse and wuldre scinende betwuhx
þa dimnysse þeostru þære sweartan helle.
 5.242. Hi þa awyrgedan gastas ne mihton for þære
fægernysse þæs halgan cuman þær awunian, ac hi sylfe on þeostre
gehyddon.
 5.247. Ða se eadiga wer Guthlac his þone getreowan freond
geseah, þa wæs he mid gastlicre blisse and mid heofonlice gefean swiðe
bliþe.
 5.260. Ða æfter þam het se halga apostol sanctus
Bartholomeus and heom bebead, þæt hi him wæron underþeodde, þæt
hi hine eft gebrohton mid smyltnysse on þære ylcan stowe, þe hi hine
ær æt genamon.
 5.263. And hig þa swa dydon, and hine mid ealre smyltnysse swa
gelæddon, and on heora fiðerum bæron and feredon, þæt he ne mihte
ne on scipe fægeror gefered beon.
 5.266. Mid þy hi þa comon on middan þære lyfte heannysse,
ða comon him togeanes haligra gasta heap, and hi ealle sungon and þus
cwædon: <foreign>Ibunt de virtute in virtutem, et reliqua</foreign>.
 5.269. Ðæt ys on englisc: Halige men gangað of mægene on
mægen.
 5.270. Ða hit þa on mergen dagian wolde, þa asetton hi hine
eft, þær hi hine ær genaman.
 5.272. Ða he þa his morgengebedtida wolde gode gefyllan, þa
geseah he þær standan twegen þara awerigdra gasta weopon swyþe and
geomerian.
 5.274. Mid þy he hi ahsode, for hwan hi weopon, þa andswarodon
hi him and þus cwædon: Wit wepað, forþon þe uncer mægn eall
þurh þe ys gebrocen, and we þe nu ne moton to cuman, ne to þe nane
spræce habban; ac on eallum þingum þu unc hæfst gebysmrod, and ure
miht eall oferswyþed.
 5.279. Ða æfter þam wordum hi gewiton ða awyrgedan gastes
efne swa smic fram his ansyne.
 6.1. Hu þa deofla on brytisc spræcon.
 6.1. Ðæt gelamp on þam dagum Cenredes Mercna kyninges,
þæt Bryttaþeod, Angolcynnes feond, þæt hi mid manigum gewinnum and
mid missenlicum gefeohtum, þæt hi Angolcynne geswencton.
 6.4. Ða gelamp hit sumre nihte, þa hit wæs hancred, and se
eadiga wer Guðlac his uhtgebedum befeal, þa wæs he sæmninga mid
leohte slæpe swefed.
 6.6. Þa onbræd he Guðlac of þam slæpe, and eode þa
sona ut, and hawode and hercnode; þa gehyrde he mycel werod þara awyrgedra
gasta on bryttisc sprecende; and he oncneow and ongeat heora gereorda, forþam
he ærhwilon mid him wæs on wrace.
 6.12. Ða sona æfter þon he geseah eall his hus mid fyre
afylled, and hi hine æfter þon ealne mid spera ordum afyldon, and hi hine
on þam sperum up on þa lyft ahengon.
 6.14. Þa ongeat sona se stranga Cristes cempa, þæt þæt
wæron þa egsan and þa witu þæs awyrgedan gastes; he þa sona
unforhtlice þa stræle þara awerigdra gasta him fram asceaf, and þone
sealm sang: <foreign>Exurgat deus et dissipentur, et reliqua</foreign>.
 6.19. Sona swa he þæt fyrmeste fers sang þæs sealmes,
þa gewiton hi swa swa smic fram his ansyne.
 6.20. Mid þy se eadiga wer Guðlac swa gelomlice wið þam
awerigedum gastum wann and campode, þa ongeaton hi, þæt heora mægn
and weorc oferswyþed wæs.
 7.1. Be Beccelle þam preoste.
 7.1. Wæs sum preost, þæs nama wæs Beccel; þa com he to
þam halgan were and hine bæd, þæt he hine to him gename, and þæt
gehet, þæt he eadmodlice wolde on godes þeowdome be his larum lyfian.
 7.5. He þa se awyrgeda gast þæs ylcan preostes heortan and
geþanc mid his searwes attre geond sprengde and mengde; lærde hine se
awyrgeda gast, þæt he Guðlac ofsloge and acwealde, and þus on his
heortan gesende: Gif ic hine ofslea and acwelle, þonne mæg ic eft agan
þa ylcan stowe æfter him, and me þonne woruldmen arwurðiað, swa swa
hi hine nu doð.
 7.12. Ða gelamp hit sume dæge, þæt se ylca preost com to
þam eadigan were, þæt he hine wolde scyran, swa his gewuna wæs ymbe
twentig nihta, þæt he hine wolde þwean; þa wæs he swyðe oflysted,
þæt he þæs eadigan weres blod agute.
 7.17. He þa sona Guðlac geseah þa lare þæs awyrgedan
gastes, swa him ealle þa toweardan þing þurh godes gifu wæron gecydde,
and eac swylce þa andweardan, and he mihte þone man innan geseon and
geondsceawian swa utan, and he cwæð þus to him.
 7.21. Eala þu min Beccel, to hwan hafast þu bedigled under
þam dysigan breoste þone awyrgedan feond?
 7.23. For hwon nelt þu þæs biteran attres þa
deaþberendan wæter of þe aspiwan?
 7.24. Ic þæt geseo, þæt þu eart fram þam awyrgedan
gaste beswicen, and þa manfullan smeaunge þinre heortan; mannakynnes
costere and middaneardes feond hafað acenned on þe þa unablinnu þæs
yfelan geþohtes, ac ahwyrf þe fram þære yfelan lare þæs awyrgedan
gastes.
 7.30. Ða ongeat he sona, þæt he wæs fram þam awyrgedan
gaste beswicen, feol sona to þæs halgan weres fotum, and þa sona mid
tearum him his synne andette.
 7.32. He þa sona se halga wer Guðlac nalæs þæt an
þæt he him þa synne forgeaf, ac eac swylce he him gehet, þæt he him
wolde beon on fultume on eallum his earfeþum.
 8.1. Hu þa deofla ferdon.
 8.1. Ðæt gelamp sumere nihte, þa se halga wer Guðlac his
gebedum befeal, þa gehyrde he grymetigenda hryþera and mislicra wildeora.
 8.3. Næs þa nan hwil to þam, þæt he geseah ealra wihta
and wildeora and wurma hiw incuman to him.
 8.5. Ærest he geseah leon ansyne, and he mid his blodigum tuxum
to him beotode; swylce eac fearres gelicnysse, and beran ansyne, þonne hi
gebolgene beoð.
 8.7. Swylce eac næddrena hiw, and swynes grymetunge, and wulfa
geþeot, and hræfena cræcetung and mislice fugela hwistlunge, þæt
hi woldon mid heora hiwunge þæs halgan weres mod awendan.
 8.11. He þa se halga wer Guþlac hine gewæpnode mid þan
wæpen þære Cristes rode and mid þam scylde þæs halgan geleafan,
and forseah þa costunge þara awyrgedra gasta, and þus cwæð: Eala
þu earma wiðerwearda gast, þin mægn ys gesyne, and þin miht ys
gecyþed.
 8.15. Þu nu earma wildeora and fugela and wyrma hiw ætywes,
þu iu þe ahofe, þæt þu woldest beon gelic þam ecan gode.
 8.17. Nu þonne ic bebeode þe on þam naman þæs ecan
godes, se þe worhte and þe of heofones heannysse awearp, þæt þu fram
þisum ungeþwærnysse gestille.
 8.21. Þa sona æfter þon ealle þa ætywnysse þara
awerigdra gasta onweg gewiton.
 9.1. Hu þæt gewrit begiten wæs.
 9.1. Ðæt gelamp on sumere nihte, þæt þær com sum man
to þæs halgan weres spræce.
 9.2. Mid þy he þær dagas wunode, þa gelamp hit, þæt
he sum gewrit awrat on cartan.
 9.4. Þa he þa hæfde þæt gewrit awriten, þa eode he
ut.
 9.5. Ða com þær sum hrefen inn; sona swa he þa cartan
geseah, þa genam he hig sona and gewat mid on þæne fenn.
 9.6. Sona swa se foresæda cuma ongean com, þa geseah he þone
hrefen þa cartan beran, þa wæs he sona swyðe unbliþe.
 9.9. Ða wæs on þam ylcan timan, þæt se halga wer
Guðlac ut of his cyrcan eode; þa geseah he þone broþor sarig.
 9.10. Þa frefrode he hine and him to cwæð: Ne beo þu
broþor sarig; ac swa se hrefen þurh þa fennas upp afligeð, swa þu him
æfter row; þonne metest þu þæt gewrit.
 9.14. Næs þa nænig hwil to þan, þæt he to scipe eode
se ylca, þe þæt gewrit wrat.
 9.15. Mid þy he þurh þa fenland reow, þa com he to sumum
mere, þe wel neah þæt egland wæs; þa wæs þær on middan
þam mere sum hreodbed.
 9.17. Þa hangode seo carte on þam hreode, efne swa hig mannes
hand þær ahengce; and he sona þa bliþe feng to þære cartan, and
he wundriende to þam godes were brohte; and he þa se eadiga wer Guthlac
sæde, þæt þæt nære his geearnung, ac godes mildheortnysse.
 9.23. Wæron on þam ylcan yglande twegen hrefnas gewunode, to
þæs gifre, þæt swa hwæt swa hi mihton gegripan, þæt hi
þæt woldon onweg alædan; and he þeahhwæþere heora gifernysse
ealle æbær and geþolode, þæt he eft sealde mannum bysene his
geþyldes.
 9.27. And nalæs þæt an þæt him þa fugelas
underþeodde wæron, ac eac swa þa fixas and wilde deor þæs westenes
ealle hi him hyrdon, and he hym dæghwamlice andlyfene sealde of his agenra
handa, swa heora gecynde wæs.
 10.1. Hu þa swalawan on him sæton and sungon.
 10.1. Þæt gelamp sume siþe, þæt þær com sum
arwurþe broðor to him, þæs nama wæs Wilfrið, se him wæs geara
on gastlicre þoftscipe geþeoded.
 10.3. Mid þan þe hig þa on manegum gespræcum heora gastlic
lif smeadon, þa comon þær sæmninga in twa swalewan fleogan, and hi
efne blissiende heora sang upahofon.
 10.6. And þa æfter þon hi setton unforhtlice on þa sculdra
þæs halgan weres Guðlaces and hi þær heora sang upahofon, and hi
eft setton on his breost and on his earmas and on his cneowu.
 10.10. Ða he þa Wilfrið lange þa fugelas wundriende
beheold, þa frægn hine Wilfriþ, forhwon þa wildan fugelas þæs
widgillan westenes swa eadmodlice him on sæton.
 10.12. He þa se halga wer Guðlac him andswarode and him to
cwæð: Ne leornodest þu, broðor Wilfrið, on halgum gewritum, þæt
se þe on godes willan his lif leofode, þæt hine wilde deor and wilde
fugelas þe near wæron.
 10.16. And se man, þe hine wolde fram woruldmannum his lif
libban, þæt hine englas þe near comon: forþon se þe woruldlicra
manna spræce gelomlice wilnað, þonne ne mæg he þa engellican
spræce befeolan.
 11.1. Ymb þa glofan, þe þa hrefnas bæron.
 11.1. Swylce eac gelamp sume siþe witedomlice wundor be þisum
halgan were.
 11.2. Wæs sum foremæra man æþelan kynekynnes on Myrcna
rice, þæs nama wæs Æþelbald.
 11.3. Þa wolde he to þæs halgan weres spræce cuman, beget
þa æt Wilfriðe, þæt he hine to þam godes were gelædde; and hi
þa sona on scipe eodon and ferdon to þam yglande, þær se halga wer
Guthlac on wæs.
 11.8. Ða hi þa to þam halgan were comon, þa hæfde
Wilfrið forlæten his glofan on þam scipe; and hi þa wið þone
halgan were spræcon.
 11.10. He þa se eadiga wer Guthlac acsode hi, hwæðer hi
ænig þinc æfter heom on þam scipe forleton, swa him god ealle þa
diglan þingc cuð gedyde.
 11.12. Þa andswarode him Wilfrið and cwæð, þæt he
forlete his twa glofan on þam scipe.
 11.15. Næs þa nænig hwil to þan, sona swa hi ut of þam
in eodon, þa gesegon hi þone hræfn mid þan sweartan nebbe þa glofe
teran uppe on anes huses þæce.
 11.17. He þa sona se halga wer Guðlac þone hrefn mid his
worde þreade for his reþnysse, and he þa his worda hyrsumode; swa fleah
se fugel west ofer þæt westen; he þa Wilfrið mid gyrde of þam huses
hrofe þa glofe geræhte.
 11.22. Swylce næs eac nænig hwil to þam, sona comon
þær þry men to þære hyðe and þær tacn slogon.
 11.23. Þa sona eode se halga wer Guðlac ut to þam mannum mid
bliðum andwlite and gode mode; he þa spæc wið þam mannum.
 11.25. Mid þan þe hi faran woldon, þa brohton hi forð ane
glofe, sædon, þæt heo of anes hrefnes muþe feolle.
 11.27. He se halga wer Guþlac sona to smerciende feng, and heom
his bletsunge sealde, and hi eft ferdon; and he eft ageaf þa glofe þam,
þe hi ær ahte.
 12.1. Hu Hwætred his hæla onfeng.
 12.1. Wæs on Eastenglalande sum man æþeles cynnes, þæs
nama wæs Hwætred.
 12.2. Mid þy he þa dæghwamlice mid arfæstnysse his
ealderum underþeoded wæs, hit gelamp sume siðe, þa he æt his
fæder hame wæs, þæt se awyrgeda gast him on eode, þæt he of
his gewitte wearð, and hine se awyrgeda feond swa swyþe swencte mid
þære wodnysse, þæt he hys agene lichama mid irene ge eac mid his
toþum blodgode and wundode.
 12.8. And nalæs þæt an þæt he hine sylfne swa mid
þam wælhreowum toþum wundode, ac eac swa hwylcne swa he mihte, þæt
he swa gelice tær.
 12.11. Ða gelamp sume siþe, þæt þær wæs mycel
menigo manna gegaderod his maga and eac oþra his nehfreonda, þæt hi hine
woldon gebindan and don hine gewyldne: he þa genam sum twibil, and mid þan
þry men to deaðe ofsloh, and oþre manige mid gesarode.
 12.15. Wæs þa feowor gear, þæt he swa wæs mid
þære wodnysse swiðe geswenced.
 12.17. Þa wæs he æt nextan genumen fram his magum and to
halgum mynstre gelæd, to þon þæt hine mæssepreostas and bisceopas
wið þa wodnysse þwean and clænsian sceoldon.
 12.20. And hi hwæþere on menigum þingum ne mihton þa
yfelan mægn þæs awyrgdan gastes ofadrifan.
 12.21. Ða æt nextan hi eft ham unrote mid þam mæge
ferdon, and hi him deaþes swyðor uþon, þonne he lengc þa men drehte.
 12.24. Ða wæs æt nextan gemærsod se hlisa on þæt
þeodscipe, þæt on þam fenne middum, on anum eglande, þe Cruwland
hatte, wære sum ancra, þæt missenlicum mægnum for gode weohse.
 12.27. Hi þa sona, þa hi þær þone halgan wer acsodon,
þohton, þæt hi woldon þær þone man gebringan, gif þæt godes
stihtung wære, þæt hi þær are findan mihton.
 12.29. And hi hit swa gefremedon, ferdon þyder, þæt hi to
comon to sumum yglande, þe wel neah wæs þam eglande, þe se godes man
on wæs; and þær wæron on niht mid þan seocan men.
 12.33. Þa hit þa on mergen dæg wæs, þa comon hi to
þære foresprecenan eglande, and þa mid þan gewunelican þeawe tacen
slogon.
 12.35. He þa sona se halga wer Guðlac to heom eode mid healice
mægne godes lufan; þa hi þa heora intingan him wepende sædon, þa
wæs he sona mid mildheortnysse gefylled.
 12.38. Genam þa sona þone untruman man and hine lædde into
his cyrican, and þær þry dagas singallice on his gebedum awunode.
 12.40. Þa on þam þriddan dæge, þa sunne upeode, þa
baþode he hine on gehalgedum wætre and bleow on his ansyne, and mid þan
eall þæt mægn þæs awyrgedan gastes on him gebræc.
 12.44. And he þa se ylca man, swa he of hefegum slæpe raxende
awoce, and he eft to his hælo feng and ham ferde; and him næfre
syþþan þa hwile, þe he leofode, seo adle ne eglode.
 13.1. Be Aþelbaldes gefere.
 13.1. Swilce eac gelamp on sumne sæl, þæt þæs
foresprecenan wræccan Aþelbaldes gefere, þæs nama wæs Ecga,
þæt he wæs fram þam awyrgedan gaste unstille; and swa swyþe he hine
drehte, þæt he his sylfes nænig gemynd ne hæfde.
 13.5. Hi þa his magas hine to þam godes men gelæddon.
 13.6. Ða sona, þæs þe he to him com, þa begyrde he hine
mid his gyrdele.
 13.7. Næs þa nænig hwil to þan, sona swa he wæs mid
þam gyrdele begyrd, eal seo unclænnysse fram him gewat, and him syþþan
næfre seo adle ne eglode.
 13.10. Eac se eadiga wer Guðlac witedomlice gaste weox and
fremede, and he þa toweardan mannum cydde swa cuðlice swa þa andweardan.
 14.1. Be þam abbode.
 14.1. Þæt gelamp sume siþe, þæt þær com sum abbod
to him, þe him wæs geara on gastlicre þoftscipe geþeoded.
 14.3. Þa he þa þyder ferde, þa wæron his handþegnas
twegen, bædon hyne þurh leafbene þæt hi moston on oðerne weg
faran, and sædon, þæt him þæs neod wære and eac þearf.
 14.6. Þa geuþe him þæs se abbod, þæs þe hi hine
bædon.
 14.7. Ða he þa se abbod þær com to þære spræce
þæs eadigan weres Guðlaces, mid þan hi þa sylfe betweonum dremdon of
þam willan haligra gewrita, þa betwyx þa halgan gewritu, þe hi
spræcon, ða cwæð Guðlac to him: Ac hwyder gewiton þa twegen, þe
ær fram þe cyrdon?
 14.11. Þa andswarode he him and cwæð: Hi bædon læfa
æt me; wæs heom oþer intingan þæt hi hider cuman ne mihton.
 14.14. He þa Guðlac him andswarode, swa him god ealle þa
toweardan þing onwreah, þæt him wæron swa cuðe swa þa andweardan,
ongan him þa secgan þone sið þara broþra and him cwæð to: Hi
ferdon þær to sumre wydewan ham and þær wæron ondrencte mid
oferdrynce.
 14.19. And nalæs þæt an þæt he him þone heora siþ
sæde, ac eac swilce be heora andleofone, ge eac swilce þa sylfan word,
þe hi þær spræcon, eall he be endebyrdnysse him gerehte.
 14.22. Mid þan þe se abbod his bletsunge hæfde onfangen, he
þa eft ferde.
 14.23. Mid þy þe þa foresprecenan broþra eft to þam
abbode comon, þa fregn he hi, hwær hi wæron.
 14.24. Þa andswarodon hi him and cwædon, þæt hi wæron
on heora nydþearfum swyðe geswencte.
 14.26. Þa axode he hi, hwæþer hit swa wære; þa sworon
hi swiðe, þæt hit swa wære.
 14.28. Þa cwæð he to him: Ac to hwon sweriað git man?
 14.29. Ac wæron æt þisse wydewan hame, and þær þus
yncer lif leofodon, and þisum wordum þus þær spræcon?
 14.30. Þa ongeaton hi heora misdæda, feollon þa to his fotum
and him forgifenysse bædon and him andetton, þæt hit wære, swa he
ær sæde.
 15.1. Be þam broþrum, þe him to comon.
 15.1. Comon eac swylce twegen broðra to him on sumne sæl of
sumum mynstre.
 15.2. Þa hi þa þyderweard ferdon, þa hæfdon hi mid heom
twa flaxan mid ælað gefylde; þa gewearð him betweonan, þæt hi
þa gehyddon under anre tyrf, þæt hi, þonne hi ham ferdon, hæfdon
eft mid him.
 15.6. Ða hi þa to him comon, þa trymede he hi mid his lare,
and mid his manunge heora heortan intimbrede.
 15.7. Mid þan þe hi manig þing heom betweonum spræcon,
ða se eadiga wer Guðlac mid bliþum andwlitan and hlihhende gespræce he
cwæþ to heom: For hwon behydde git þa flaxan under ane tyrf, and for
hwon ne læddon ge hi mid inc?
 15.11. Hi þa swyðe wundrodon þara worda þæs halgan weres
and to him luton and hine bletsunge bædon.
 15.13. And he hi gebletsode, and hi þa eft ham ferdon.
 15.15. Wæs on þa sylfan tid, þæt þone foresprecenan wer
missenlices hades men sohton, ægðer þara ge ealdormen ge bisceopas and
abbodas, and ælces hades heane and rice.
 15.18. And nalæs þæt an þæt hine men sohton of
þære hehþeode Mercnarice, ac eac swylce ealle þa, þe on Bretone
wæron, þe þisne eadigan wer hyrdon, þæt hi æghwonon to him
efston and scyndon.
 15.21. And þa þe wæron aþer oþþe on lichaman
untrumnysse oððe fram þam awyrgdan gaste geswencte and numene, oþþe
oþrum yfelum, þe mannacynn mid missenlicum sorgum and sarum utan ymbseald
ys.
 15.24. And on heora menigum se hiht awacode, þe hi to him
genamon; forþan næs nænig untrum, þæt he ungelacnod fram him
ferde; nænig deofolseoc, þæt he eft wel gewitfæst ne wære; ne on
nænigre untrumnysse, þæt he eft gehæled him fram ne ferde.
 16.1. Be Aþelbaldes gefere.
 16.1. Ðæt gelamp, mid þan þæt manige men for
missenlicum þingum him to comon, þa betweox oþre com þær þæs
foresprecenan wræccan Æþelbaldes gefera, þæs nama wæs Ova,
þæt he wolde þone halgan geneosian and wiþ gesprecan.
 16.5. Ða gelamp hit þan æfteran dæge, þæs þe he
þyder on þære fore wæs, þa eode he ofer sumne þorn on niht.
 16.6. Þa besloh se þorn on þone fot, and swa strang wæs se
sting þæs þornes, þæt he eode þurh þone fot; and he þa
uneaðe þone sið geferde, and þurh mycel gewinn he to þam
foresprecenan eglande becom, þær se eadiga wer Guðlac on eardode.
 16.11. And mid þan þe he þær on niht wæs, þa asweoll
him se lichama ofer healf fram þam lendenum oþ þa fet, and swa sarlice he
wæs mid þam sare geswenced, þæt he naðer þara ne gesittan ne
standan mihte.
 16.15. Mid þy he þæt þam godes were sæde Guðlace,
þa bebead he, þæt hine man to him gelædde.
 16.16. Þa he þa wæs broht to him, þa sæde he him þone
intingan, þurh hwæt he ærest swa geþræst wære, and hu him
ærest þæt earfoð on become.
 16.20. He þa sona Guðlac hine sylfne ungyrede, and þæt
reaf, þe he genehlice on him hæfde, he hit slefde on þone foresprecenan
man.
 16.22. Næs þa nænig hwil to þon, sona swa he mid þan
hrægle swa miccles weres gegyred wæs, þa ne mihte þæt þæt sar
aberan.
 16.24. He þa sona se ylca þorn, efne swa swa stræl of bogan
astelleþ, swa he of þam men afleah, and on þa fyrle gewat; and þa sona
on þa sylfan tid eall se swyle and eall þæt sar gewat fram him; and he
sona to þa sylfan tid mid bliþum mode to þam halgan were spræc, and he
eft þanon ferde butan sceðnysse æniges sares.
 16.30. Swylce eac gelamp, þæt ealle þa men wundrodon, þe
þas þing gehyrdon, and hi on þon wuldredon and heredon heofones god.
 17.1. Be þam halgan biscope Sancte Hædde.
 17.1. Swylce nys eac mid idele to forlætenne þæt wundor,
þæt þurh witedomes cræft wiste and him cydde, forþon him wæs
þurh godes gife seald, þæt he þa word þara æfwearda swa geara
wiste swa þara andwearda, þe him foran gesæde wæron.
 17.6. Gelamp sume siþe, þæt sum bisceop to him ferde,
þæs nama wæs Hædda: efne swa swa he wære mid heofonlicre þeahte
gelæred, þæt he to þære spræce ferde þæs godes mannes.
 17.9. Þa hæfde se bisceop mid hine on his geferscipe sumne man
gelæredne, þæs nama wæs Wigfrið.
 17.11. Mid þan he þa betweox þa oðre þæs bisceopes
þegnas þyder ferde þa ongunnon hi fela þinga be þam halgan were
sprecan, and fela þinga be his wundrum sædon.
 17.13. Sume hi þonne sædon þa heardlicnysse his lifes, þa
wundor, þe he worhte; sume hi þonne twiendlice be his life spræcon, and
þæt cwædon, þæt hi nyston, hwæðer he on godes mihte þa
þing worhte, þe þurh deofles cræft.
 17.18. Þa þa hi þas þing þus heom betweonon spræcon,
þa cwæþ se witega to heom: Ic mæg, cwæð he, cunnian and gewitan,
hwæþer he biþ bigengca þære godcundan æfæstnysse, forþon ic
wæs lange betwux Sceottafolc eardiende.
 17.22. And ic geseah þær manige gode, and on godes þeodscipe
wel heora lif læddon; and hi manigum wundrum and tacnum þurh godes mihte
beforan manna eagum scinon.
 17.24. Of þara manna life, þe ic þær geseah, ic mæg
ongitan, hu gerad þises mannes lif ys, hwæþer he þurh godes miht þa
wundor wyrceð, þe he þurh deofles miht deð.
 17.28. Mid þy þa þe foresprecena bisceop to þære
spræce becom þæs godes mannes Guðlaces, hi þa sylfe betweonum
indrencton mid þam cerenum þære godspellican swetnysse.
 17.30. Wæs on þam eadigan were Guðlace seo beorhtnys
þære drihtnes gife swa swyþe scinende, þæt swa hwæt swa he
bodode and lærde, swa he of engcellicre spræce þa word bodode and
sæde.
 17.34. Wæs eac swiðe mycel wisdom on him, heofonlice snyttro,
þæt swa hwæt swa he gelærde, þæt he þæt trymede mid þa
godcundan haligra gewrita.
 17.37. And he þa semninga se biscop on midre þære spræce,
þe hi heom betwux smeadon, eadmodlice to þam godes were geleat and hine
geornlice bæd and halsode, þæt he þurh hine sacerdlice þenunge
onfengce, þæt he hine moste gehadigan to mæssepreoste and to þenunge
drihtnes weofodes.
 17.41. He þa sona Guðlac his benun geþafode, and he hine
sylfne to eorðan astrehte, and þæt cwæð, þæt he wolde
þæs, þe godes willa wære and þæs biscopes.
 17.45. Þa hi þa hæfdon þa þenunge gefylled, and he
wæs gehalgod, swa ic ær sæde, he þa se biscop bæd þone halgan
wer, þæt he scolde to gereorde fon mid him; and he þa swa dyde, þeah
hit his life ungeþeawe wære.
 17.49. Þa hi þa to gereorde sæton, swa ic ær sæde,
þa locode Guthlac to þam biscopes þegnum; þa geseah he þone
foresprecenan broðor Wigfrið, cwæð þa þus to him: And nu broþor
Wigfrið, ac hwylc þince þe nu, þæt se preost sig, be þam þu
gyrstandæge cwæde, þæt þu woldest gecunnian, hwæþer he
wære god oþþe gal?
 17.54. He þa sona Wigfrið aras, and þa to eorþan leat, and
his synne him andette.
 17.55. He þa sona se halga wer him togeanes fengc, and him his
miltse geaf and sealde.
 17.58. Wæs halgung þæs eglandes Cruwlande and eac þæs
eadigan weres Guthlaces on arfæstlice tide, fif dagum ær sancte
Bartholomeus mæssan.
 18.1. Be Ecgburhe abbodysse.
 18.1. Swylce eac gelamp sume siþe, þæt seo arwyrðe
fæmne Ecgburh abbodysse, Aldwulfes dohtor þæs cyninges, sende þam
arwurðan were Guðlace leadene þruh and þær scytan to, and hine
halsode þurh þa halgan naman þæs upplican kyninges, þæt æfter
his forðfore man his lichaman moste ingesettan.
 18.6. Heo gesende þa gretinge be sumum arwyrðe lifes broþor
and hine het, þæt he him geaxian sceolde, hwa þære stowe hyrde
æfter him beon sceolde.
 18.9. Mid þan he þære arwyrðan fæmnan gretinge luflice
onfeng, ða be þon, þe he geaxod wæs, hwa þære stowe hyrde
æfter him beon scolde, þa andswarode he and cwæð, þæt se man
wære on hæþenum folce and þa git nære gefullod; ac
þeahhwæþere þæt he þa sona com and þa gerynu sceolde onfon
fulluhtbæþes.
 18.15. And hit eac swa gelamp, forþon se ylca Cissa, se þe eft
þa stowe heold, he com þæs ymb litel fæc on Bretone, and hine man
þær gefullode, swa se godes wer foresæde.
 19.1. Be Aðelbalde þam kyninge.
 19.1. Swylce nys eac mid idelnysse to forelætanne þæt
wundor, þe þes halga wer Guthlac foresæde and mannum cydde.
 19.3. Wæs on sumre tide, þæt com se foresprecena wræcca
to him Aþelbald; and hine Ceolred se kyning hider and þider wide aflymde,
and he his ehtnysse and his hatunge fleah and scunode.
 19.7. Ða com he to þære spæce þæs halgan weres
Guðlaces: þaþa se mennisce fultum him beswac, hine þeahhwæþere se
godcunda fultum gefrefrode.
 19.10. Mid þy he þa to þam godes were com, and he him his
earfoða rehte, þa cwæð Guðlac þus to him: Eala, min cniht, þinra
gewinna and earfoða ic eom unforgitende; ic forþon þe gemiltsode, and for
þinum earfoðum ic bæd god, þæt he þe gemiltsode and þe
gefultomode.
 19.14. And he þa mine bene gehyrde, and he þe syleþ rice and
anweald þinre þeode; and þa ealle fleoð beforan þe, þa þe
hatiað, and þin sweord fornymeð ealle þine þa wiþerweardan,
forþon drihten þe bið on fultume.
 19.18. Ac beo þu geþyldig, forþon ne begitest þu na
þæt rice on gerisne woruldlicra þinga, ac mid drihtnes fultume þu
þin rice begytest; forþon drihten þa genyþerað, þe þe nu
hatiað, and drihten afyrreð þæt rice fram him, and hæfð þe
gemynt and geteohhod.
 19.23. Þa he þas word gehyrde, he þa sona Aþelbald his hiht
and his geleafan on god sylfne trymede, and he getrywode and gelyfde ealle þa
þing, þe se halga wer foresæde.
 19.26. Þæt rice beoð onwende and ofanumene, and hit a to
þam ende efesteð; and se rica and se heana, se gelæreda and se
ungelærda, and geong and eald, ealle hi gelice se stranga deað forgripeð
and nymð.
 20.1. Be þæs halgan weres lifes lenge and be his forðfore.
 20.1. Ða gelamp hit on fyrste æfter þissum, þæt se
leofa godes þeow Guthlac æfter þon fiftyne gear, þe he gode willigende
lædde his lif, þa wolde god his þone leofan þeow of þam gewinne
þisse worulde yrmþa gelædan to þære ecan reste þæs
heofoncundan rices.
 20.6. Ða gelamp on sumne sæl, mid þy he on his cyrcan æt
his gebedum wæs, þa wæs he semninga mid adle gestanden.
 20.8. And he sona ongeat, þæt him wæs godes hand to sended,
and he swyþe gebliþe hine het gyrwan to þam ingange þæs heofonlican
rices.
 20.10. Wæs he seofon dagas mid þære adle geswenced, and
þæs eahtoþan dæge he wæs to þam ytemestan gelæded.
 20.12. Þa gestod hine se adl þon wodnesdæg nehst eastron,
and þa eft þan ylcan dæge on þære eastorwucan he þæt lif of
þam lichaman sende.
 20.15. Wæs sum broðor mid him, þæs nama wæs Beccel,
þurh þone ic þa forðfore ongeat þæs eadigan weres.
 20.16. Mid þy he þa com þy dæge, þe hine seo adle
gestod, þa acsode he hine be gehwilcum þingum.
 20.18. Þa andswarode he him lætlice, and mid langre sworetunge
þæt orð of þam breostum teah.
 20.20. Þa he þa geseah þone halgan wer swa unrotes modes,
þa cwæð he to him: Hwæt gelamp þe nywes nu ða?
 20.21. Ac þe on þisse nihte sum untrumnysse gelamp?
 20.22. Þa andswarode he him and him cwæð to: Adle me gelamp
on þisse nihte.
 20.24. Þa frægn he eft hine: Wast þu, min fæder, þone
intingan þinre adle, oþþe to hwylcum ende wenest þu, þæt seo
mettrumnysse wylle gelimpan?
 20.26. Þa andswarode he him eft se halga wer and him cwæð
to: Þes ongitenysse minre untrumnysse ys, þæt of þisum lichaman sceal
beon se gast alæded; forþon þan eahtoþan dæg bið ende þære
minre mettrumnysse; forþon þæt gedafenað, þæt se gast beo
gegearwod, þæt ic mæg gode filian.
 20.32. Þa he þa þas word gehyrde se foresprecena broðor
Beccel, he þa swyþe weop and geomrian ongan, and mid mycelre uneðnysse
his eagospind mid tearum gelomlice leohte.
 20.34. Þa frefrode hine se godes wer Guthlac and him cwæð
to: Min bearn, ne beo þu na geunrotsod, forþon ne bið me nænig
uneþnysse, þæt ic to drihtne minum gode fare.
 20.37. Wæs swa mycel rumnes on him þæs halgan geleafan, and
swa mycele he to þære godes lufan hæfde, þæt se cuþa and se
uncuþa ealle him wæs gelice gesegen on godum dædum.
 20.41. Ða þæs ymbe feower niht com se forma easterdæg; he
þa se eadiga wer Guðlac on þære his mettrumnysse gode lac onsægde
and mæssan sang, and syþþan he þa deorwyrþan lac offrode Cristes
blodes, þa ongan he þam foresprecenan breþer godspellian; and he hine swa
swyþe deoplice mid his lare ineode, þæt he næfre ær ne syþþan
swylc ne gehyrde.
 20.47. Mid þan þe seofoða dæg com þære his
mettrumnysse, þa com se foresprecena broðor on þære sixtan tide
þæs dæges, þæt he hine geneosian wolde; þa gemette he hine
hleonian on þam hale his cyrcan wið þam weofode.
 20.50. Þa hwæþere he ne mihte wið hine sprecan, forþon
he geseah, þæt his untrumnysse hine swyþe swencte; þa
þeahhwæþere he hine æfter þon bæd, þæt he his word to him
forlete, ær þon þe he swulte.
 20.55. He þa se eadiga wer Guþlac hwæthwego fram þam wage
þa werigan limu ahof, cwæð þa þus to him: Min bearn, nu ys þære
tide swiþe neah, ac behealt þu min þa ytemestan bebodu.
 20.58. Æfter þon þe min sawl of þam lichaman fere, þonne
far þu to minre swustor and hyre secge, þæt ic forþon her on
middanearde hire ansyne fleah and hi geseon nolde, þæt wyt eft on heofonum
beforan godes ansyne unc eft gesawon.
 20.62. And hi bidde, þæt heo minne lichaman on þa þruh
gesette, and mid þære scytan bewinde, þe me Ecgburh onsende.
 20.64. Nolde ic þa hwile, þe ic leofode, mid linenum hrægle
gegyred beon, ac nu for lufan þære Cristes fæmnan þa gife, þe heo
me sende, ic wylle to þon don, þe ic heold: þonne se lichama and seo
sawul hi todæleð, þæt man þone lichaman mid þam hrægle bewinde
and on þa þruh gelecge.
 20.69. Ða se foresprecena broðor þas þing gehyrde, he þa
wæs þus sprecende: Ic þe halsige, min se leofa fæder, nu ic þine
untrumnysse geseo and ongite, and ic gehyre, þæt þu þas woruld scealt
forlætan, þæt þu me secge be þære wisan, þe ic næfre ær
næs gedyrstig þe to axianne.
 20.73. Of þære tide, þe ic ærest mid þe on þisum
westene eardode, ic þe gehyrde sprecan on æfenne and on ærenmergen, ic
nat mid hwæne.
 20.76. Forþon ic þe bidde and halsige, þæt þu me
næfre behydigne and sorhfulne be þisse wisan ne læte æfter þinre
forðfore.
 20.78. He þa se godes wer mid langre sworetunge þæt orð of
þam breostum teah, andswarode him þa and cwæð: Min bearn, nelt þu
beon gemyndig; þas þing, þe ic ær nolde nænigum woruldmen secgan
þa hwile, þe ic lifigende wære, ic hit þe wylle nu onwreon and
gecyþan.
 20.82. Ðan æfteran geare, þe ic þis westen eardode,
þæt on æfen and on ænemergen god sylfa þone engcel minre frofre to
me sende, se me þa heofonlican geryno openode, þa nanegum men ne alyfað
to secganne, and þa heardnysse mines gewinnes mid heofonlican engellicum
spræcum ealle gehihte; þe me æfweardan gecydde and geopenode swa þa
andweardum.
 20.88. And nu, min bearn þæt leofe, geheald þu min word, and
þu hi nænigum oþrum men ne secge buton Pege minre swustor and Ecgberhte
þam ancran, gif þæt gelimpe, þæt þu wið hine gesprece.
 20.92. Þa he þas word spræc, he þa his heafod to þam
wage onhylde and mid langre sworetunge þæt orð of þam breostum teah.
 20.94. Mid þy he eft gewyrpte and þam orð onfeng, þa com
seo swetnys of þam muðe swa þæra wynsumesta blostman stenc.
 20.96. And þa þære æfterfylgendan nihte, mid þan þe
se foresprecena broðor nihtlicum gebedum befeall, þa geseah he eall
þæt hus utan mid mycelre beorhtnesse ymbseald; and seo beorhtnys þær
awunode oð dæg.
 20.100. Þa hit on mergen dæg wæs, he þa se godes wer eft
styrede hwæthwego and þa weregan leomu upahof.
 20.101. Þa cwæð he to him þus: Min bearn, gearwa þe, and
þu on þone sið fere, þe ic þe gehet; forþon nu ys seo tid, þæt
se gast sceal forlætan þa weregan limo and to þam ungeendodan gefean
wyle geferan, to heofona rice.
 20.105. Ða he þa þas þingc spræc, he þa his handa
aþenede to þam weofode and hine getrymede mid þam heofonlican mete,
Cristes lichaman and his blod; and þa æfter þon his eagan to heofonum
ahof and his earmas aþenede; and þa se gast mid gefean and blisse to þam
ecum gefean ferde þæs heofonlican rices.
 20.111. Betwux þa þingc se foresprecena broðor geseah eall
þæt hus mid heofonlicre bryhto geondgoten, and he þær geseah fyrene
topp up of þære eorþan to heofones heannysse, þæs beorhtnys wæs
eallum oþrum ungelic, and for his fægernysse þæt seo sunne sylf æt
middum dæge, eall hire scima wæs on blæco gecyrred.
 20.116. And engcellice sangas geond þære lyfte faco he
gehyrde; and eall þæt igland mid mycelre swetnysse wunderlices stences
ormædum wæs gefylled.
 20.119. He þa se foresprecena broþor sona mid mycelre fyrhte
wæs geslegen, eode þa on scip, and þa ferde to þære stowe, þe se
godes wer ær bebead; and þa com to Pege and hire þa eall þa þing
sæde æfter endebyrdnesse, swa se broðor hine het.
 20.123. Þa heo þa gehyrde þone broþor forðferedne, heo
þa sona on eorðan feoll and mid mycelre hefignysse gefylled wearð,
þæt heo word gecweþan ne mihte.
 20.125. Mid þan heo þa eft hig gehyrte, heo þa of þam
breostum inneweardum lange sworetunge teah, and þa þam wealdende þanc
sæde, þæs þe he swa wolde.
 20.128. Hi þa þan æfteran dæge æfter þam bebode
þæs eadigan weres, hi becomon to þam eglande, and hi ealle þa stowe
and þa hus þær gemetton mid ambrosie þære wyrte swetnysse gefylde.
 20.131. Hi þa þone halgan wer on þreora daga fæce mid
halgum lofsangum gode bebead, and on þam þriddan dæge, swa se godes wer
bebead, hig þone lichaman on cyrcan mid arwurðnysse bebyrgdon.
 20.135. Þa wolde seo godcundnysse arfæstlice manna openlice
ætywan, on hu mycclum wuldre he wæs se eadiga wer, syþþan he bebyrged
wæs; forþon þe he ær beforan manna eagum swa manigum wundrum scean
and berhte.
 20.139. Mid þy he þa wæs twelf monað bebyrged æfter his
forðfore, ða onsende god on þæt mod þære drihtnes þeowan,
þæt heo wolde eft þone broðorlican lichaman on oðre byrgene
gesettan.
 20.142. Heo þa þyder togesomnode godes þeowa and
mæssepreosta and cyrclice endebyrdnysse, þæt þy ylcan dæge
þæs ymbe twelf monað, þe seo forðfore þæs eadigan weres wæs,
hi þa þa byrgene untyndon.
 20.145. Þa gemetton hi þone lichaman ealne ansundne, swa he
ær wæs, and þa gyt lifigende wære, and on liþobignyssum and on
eallum þingum, þæt he wæs slæpendum men gelicra myccle þonne
forðferedum, swylce eac þa hrægl þære ylcan niwnysse, þe hig on
fruman ymbe þone lichaman gedon wæron.
 20.151. Þa hi þas þing gesawon, þe þær samod æt
wæron, þa wæron hi swiðe forhte for þig, þe hi þær gesawon;
and hi swa swyðe mid þære fyrhte wæron geslegene, þæt hi naht
sprecan ne mihton.
 20.154. Ða heo þa seo Cristes þeowe Pege þæt geseah,
þa wæs heo sona mid gastlicere blisse gefylled, and þa þone halgan
lichaman mid þære arwurðnysse Cristes lofsangum on oþre scytan bewand,
þa Ecgbriht se ancra ær him lifigende to þam ylcan þenunge sende.
 20.158. Swylce eac þa þruh, nalæs þæt hi eft þa on
eorðan dydon, ac on gemyndelicre stowe and on arwyrþre hi þa gesetton.
 20.161. Seo stow nu eft fram Aðelbalde þam kyninge mid
manigfealdum getimbrum ys arwurðlice gewurþod, þær se sigefæsta
lichama þæs halgan weres gastlice resteþ; and se man, se þe þa stowe
mid ealle his mægne gesecð, þonne þurh þa þingunge þæs halgan
weres he gefremeð and þurhtyhþ, þæt he wilnað.
 20.166. Se eadiga wer Guðlac, he wæs gecoren man on godcundum
dædum and ealra gesnyttra goldhord; and he wæs gestæþþig on his
þeawum, swylce he wæs on Cristes þeowdome swa geornfullice abysgod,
þæt him næfre elles on hys muðe næs buton Cristes lof, ne on his
heortan butan arfæstnys, ne on his mode butan syb and lufu and
mildheortnes.
 20.172. Ne hyne nan man yrre geseah, ne ungeornfulne to Cristes
þeowdome, ac a man mihte on his andwlitan lufe and sibbe ongytan, and a
wæs swetnys on his mode and snyttro on his breostum, and swa mycel
glædnysse on him wæs, þæt he a þam cuðum and þam uncuþum
wæs gelice gesegen.
 21.1. Be Aþelbalde kyningce.
 21.1. Æfter þyssum geacsode Aþelbald se foresprecena
wræcca on feorlandum þæs halgan weres forðfore sancte Guþlaces;
forþon he ana ærþon wæs hys gebeorh and frofor.
 21.4. Þa wæs he semninga mid unrotnysse gestyred, ferde þa
þider to þære stowe, þær þæs godes weres lichama on wæs,
forþon he gehyhte þurh þone halgan wer, þæt him god sealde his
gewinnes frofre.
 21.8. Þa he þa to þære byrgene com þæs halgan weres,
he þa wepende mid tearum þus cwæð: Min fæder, hwæt, þu canst
mine yrmþa, þu me wære symble on fultume on minum unyðnyssum; hwider
wylle ic me nu cyrran, hwa frefreð me, gif þu me forlætst?
 21.13. Mid þy he þa þas þing and manig oþer æt
þære byrgene wepende spræc, þa seo nihtlice tid com; þa wæs he
þær on sumum huse inne, þe he ær be Guthlace lifigendum hwilum on
gæstliþnesse wunode.
 21.16. Ða he þa on þam huse inne wæs, þa wæs he on
þam unrotan mode hider and þyder þencende; him þa æt nyxtan wæron
þa eagan mid þam slæpe betyned.
 21.19. He þa færinga forhtlice abræd: þa geseah he ealle
þa cytan innan mid heofonlice leohte gefylde.
 21.20. Mid þan he þa wæs forhtlice geworden for þære
ungewunelican gesihþe, ða geseah he þone eadigan wer Guthlac on
engellicre ansyne him beforan standan, and him cwæð to: Ne wylt þu þe
ondrædan, ac beo þu anræde, forþon god þe ys on fultume; and ic
forþon to þe com, þurh mine þingunge god þine bene gehyrde.
 21.26. Ac ne beo þu geunrotsod, forþon dagas synt gewitene
þinra yrmða, forþon ær sunne twelf monða hringc utan ymbgan
hæbbe, þu wealdest þises rice þe þu hwile æfter wunne.
 21.30. And nalæs þæt an þæt he him þæt rice
towerd sæde, ac eac þa lengce his lifes he him eall gerehte.
 21.31. Ðas tacna god geworhte þurh þæs halgan weres
geearnunge, æfter þon þe he forðfered wæs and bebyrged.
 22.1. Wæs sum hiwscipes man þæs foresprecena wræccan
Aþelbaldes on þære mægða Wissa, þæs eagan wæron mid fleo
and mid dimnesse twelf monð ofergan.
 22.3. Mid þy his læces hine mid sealfum lange teolodon, and
hit him nawiht to hælo ne fremede, ða wæs he innan godcundlice manod,
þæt gif hine man to þære stowe gelædde Guthlaces, þæt he
þonne his hælo and gesihþe onfengce.
 22.8. Næs þa nænig hwil to þon, þæt him his frynd on
þære stowe brohton to Cruwlande, and hi þa gespræcon to þære
Cristes þeowan Pegan; and heo þæs mannes geleafan trumne and fæstne
gehyrde.
 22.12. Þa lædde heo hine on þa cyrcan, þær se awyrða
lichama inne wæs Guthlaces, genam þa þæs gehalgodan sealtes, þe
Guthlac ær sylf gehalgode, and wætte and drypte in þa eagan.
 22.15. And þa, ær heo oþerne dropan on þæt oþer eage
dyde, þa mihte he mid þan oðron geseon, and on þam ylcan inne he
gearlice oncneow, hwæt þærinne wæs, and he hal and gesund ham
ferde.
 22.19. Sy urum drihtne lof and wuldor and wurðmynt, and þam
eadigan were sancte Guthlace, on ealra worulda woruld, aa buton ende on
ecnysse, Amen.

LS 11 (James)
B3.3.11.
James the Greater: Warner 1917, 21-5.



 1. Of Jacobe, Johannes Broðer.
 2. Ðæt Judeissce folc brohte þan hundredes ealdren feo, for
þy þæt heo mosten Jacoben swa ateon swa heo wolden, & he heom
þæs leafe sealden.
 4. Heo genamen hine þa & hine gehæften.
 4. Þa wearð mycel geflit betwux þan cristenan & þan
hæðenan.
 5. Þa cwæð sum þæt hit riht wære þæt man
lædde Jacoben forð to heora gesamnunge, & geherdan his word æfter
heora æ, & man dyde þa swa.
 7. Þa cwædon þa sunderhalgen to Jacobe, Hwy bodest þu
þone Hælend, þe wæs ahangen, swa swa we ealle wyten, betwux þan
sceððen?
 10. Jacobus soðlice wæs afylled mid þan Halgen Gaste, &
heom to cwæð, Gehyreð nu broðre þa leofeste, ge þe telleð eow
beon Abrahames bearn.
 12. Ure Drihten behet Abrahame ure fæder þæt on his sæde
byð yrfeweardod ealle þeoden.
 13. Soðlice his sæd næs na ofer Ismaele, ac ofer Isaac, swa
swa God sylf cwæð to Abrahame, On Isaac byð þin sæd geceged.
 15. & soðlice ure fæder Abraham wæs geteald to Godes
freond ær þan þe he embsnyðen wære, & ær þan þe he
freolsdæig wurðode, & ær þam þe he ænige godcunde æ
cuðe oððe wyste.
 18. Gyf þonne Abraham is geworden Godes freond gelyfende, hwy
mycele swyðere byð se Godes feond þe ne gelyfð on hine?
 20. Þa Judees cwædon, Hwæt is se þe ne gelefð on God?
 21. Jacobus andswerode, Se þe ne gelefð þæt on Abrahames
cynne byð geerfeweard ealle þeode, & se þe ne gelyfð þæt
Moyses cwæðe to his folca, God awecð eow mycelne wytega & mærne
of eower gebroðren, & þone ge scylan geheren on eallen þingan swa swa
me on þan þe he eow bebeott.
 25. Þiss he forewitegode þurh God sylfne & þurh his
wissunge.
 26. Eft Isaias forewytegode beo ures Drihtenes tocyme &
cwæð, Efne mæden byð geeacnod on innoðe, & cænð cild,
& his name byð Emmanuel, þæt is on smeagunga, God sy mid us.
 29. Eft Jeremias cwæð, Eala þu Jerusalem, efne þin alesend
cumð & þiss byð his tacne.
 30. Blinde eagen he onlihteð, & deafen he forgyfð
gehyrnysse, & mid his stefne he awecð deade to life.
 32. Eft Ezechiel se wytega cwyðð, Eala þu Syon, þin king
cumð & þe gestaðeleð.
 33. Daniel soðlice cwæð, Swa swa mannes bearn God cumð to
mannen, & he geahneð him ealdordomes & ealle mihten.
 35. & soðlice se Halga Gast clypode þurh Dauid & þuss
cwæð, Min Drihten cwæð to mine Drihtene, þu eart min bearn for
þan ic þe todæig asænde to mannen.
 37. Eft fæder stæfne wæs gehyrd of heofone þuss
cweðende, He gecegð me his fæder & ic hine asette ofer eallen
eorðlice kingen.
 39. To Dauiden sylfen God cwæð, Of wæstme þines innoðes
ic sette ofer þinne hehsetle.
 41. Beo his þrowunge soðlice Isaias se witega cwæð, Swa
swa unscaðig lamb God wæs gelædd to slege.
 42. Eft Dauid cwæð þurh þone Halgen Gast, Heo adrifen mine
handen & mine fet & gerimdan ealle mine ban.
 44. Heo soðlice me ymbsceawodan & me beheoldan &
todældan min reaf & hluten heom betwynen.
 45. Eft on oðre stowe se witega cwæð beo ures Drihtenes
þrowunge, Heo sænden on minne mete gealle & on minne drænc eced.
 47. Beo his deaðe soðlice is gecweðen, Min flæsc resteð
on hyhte, for þan þe þu ne forlætest mine sawle on helle, ne þu ne
lætest þine halgen geseon nane brosnunge.
 50. Eft beo his æriste he sylf cwæð to his Fæder, Ic
arise of deaðe & ic cume to þe & mid þe wunige, & for
wædlena ermðen & for heofunga þearefena ic arise of deaðe
cwæð Drihten.
 53. Beo his upastigennysse is awriten soðlice þæt, He asteah
on hehnysse & þa gehæfte he gelædde of hæftnysse & eft, He
asteah ofer cherubin þan ængle werode & swa fleah on heofones.
 56. Eft Anna, Samueles moder, cwæð, Drihten asteah geond
heofones & his mihte ateowde, & manege oðre gecyðnysse synd
gewritene on þære æ beo ures Drihtenes upstige to heofone.
 58. & he nu sitt æt his Fæder swyðre, & cumð to
demen cwican & deaden swa swa se witega cwæð, Ure Drihten Crist
witodlice cumð, & he nane swigeð, & fyr on his ansyne beornð,
& on his embhwyrfte byð swyðlic hreohnysse.
 62. Þas þing synden sume gefyllode eornestlice on uren Drihtene
Hælende Criste & forðgewitene, & þa þa gyt gewitene ne synd,
sculen beon ealle gefyllde, swa swa hit forewitegod is.
 65. Soðlice Isaias cwæð beo þan mycelen dome þe toweard
is, þæt deade ariseð of heora byrigene, & byð geedcwicode ealle
þa þa nu on byrigene resteð.
 67. Eac Dauid se salmscop cwæð, þæt God hæfð þone
mihte þæt he æighwylcen mænn forgelt beo his gewyrhten.
 69. Nu bidde ic leofa gebroðre, cwæð Sanctus Jacobus,
þæt æighwylc eower dædbote do his synnen, þæt he þonne ne
þurfe yfel onfon æfter his geearnunge.
 71. Se þe hine sylfne wat beo ænige dæle scyldigne,
þæt he þæs þrowunge geyfelode þe ealne middeneard mid his rode
alesde, he þæs dædbote do, þa hwile þa he on þyssen life seo.
 73. For þan witodlice ne byð nane mænn dædbote alefd
æfter þyssen life, ac hæfð æighwylc an swa swa he her geearneð
swa god swa yfel.
 75. Eornestlice Dauid cwæð þurh þone Halgen Gast beo
Drihtene, þæt þa Judees agulden him yfel for gode, & hatunge for his
lufe þe he heom gecydde.
 78. Witodlice he arærde creoperes of heora cynne, þe alefede
wæron, & hreoflen he geclænsode, blinde he onlihte, & deoflen he
aflegde of wodsican mannen, & deade he awehte, & swa þeh ealle þa
Judees cwædan anre stefne þæt he wære deaðes scyldig.
 81. & eac þæt wæs forewitegod þurh Dauid hwu his agen
discipul hine belæwde & to deaðe gesealde, þa he cwæð, <foreign>Qui
edebat panem meum ampliauit aduersum me supplantationem</foreign>, þæt is Se þe
ett minne hlaf mid me, þæncð me to beswican.
 85. Ealle þas þing, leofe gebroðre, Abrahames bearn
foresædan þurh þone halgen Gast.
 86. Hwæt wene þe nu gyf ge gelyfen nylleð on God, þæt
ge mugen ætwinden þan ecen wite þonne oðre þeode gelyfeð þære
witegane stefne & þæra hehfædera?
 89. Ic cweðe, þæt ge wel wurðe syn þæt ge gewitnode
beon.
 90. Ac ge ageð mycele þearfe, þæt ge dædbote don eower
synnen mid teare gyten, & mid heofunge, þelæste us belimpe þæt
ilca þe belamp þan wiðerrædan, þe Dauid embe singð on his
salmsange, <foreign>Aperta est terra & deglutiuit Dathan & operuit super
congregationem Abyron</foreign>; Seo eorðe wearð geopened & forswealh Dathan,
& oferwreah wreah heora gesamnunge, þe nolde dædbote don heora
synnen.
 95. & heo mid lege forbærnde wurdon.
 96. Þas þing & oðre gelice, Jacobus bodede þan folca
swa lange, þæt God ælmihtig him getyðede swa mycelne gefean, þæt
eall þæt folc þe þær gegaderod wæs, anre stefne clypode, Eala
þu halge Jacobus, mycel habbe we gesynegod & mycel habbe we to yfele
gedon.
 100. We biddeð eadmodlice nu, þæt þu tæce us dædbote
to done.
 101. Sanctus Jacobus heom andswerede, Eale ge leofe gebroðre, ne
scule ge nateshwan eow forðæncen.
 102. Gelyfeð on God & byð gefulhtnede, þonne byð ealle
eower synnen adilogode.
 103. Æfter feawe dagen soðlice Abiathar se hæðene biscop
geseh þæt swa mycel menige þæs folcas on Drihten gelefde.
 105. Þa astyrede he mycele saca on þan folca, & swyðlice
ceaste þurh his feoh gestreon, swa þæt an of þan sunderhalgen of ða
writeren befeng þæs halgen sweore mid anen rape, & swa hine gelædde
to Herodes cafertone þæs kinges.
 109. Se wæs Archelaus sune.
 109. He het þa þæt me hine beheafdigen scolde, & þa
þa me hine to beheafdunge lædde.
 110. Þa geseh he sumne creopere licgende on his weige &
þuss him to clypigende wæs, Sæinte Jacob Hælendes Cristes
ærendrace, ales me fram þyssen sare, for þan þe ealle mine leomen synd
gecwylmode.
 113. Se halge Jacobus him andswerode, On mines Drihtenes name
Hælendes Cristes, þe onhangen wæs on rode galgan, for þæs lufe me
læt nu to beheafdunge, aris nu upp ansund and bletse þinne Scyppend
middeneardes Hælend.
 117. He þærrihte aras, & ongann blissigende eornen.
 118. & bletsigen Drihtenes name Hælendes Cristes.
 118. Þa se sunderhalge Josias þæt geseh, þe hine ær to
beheafdunge gelædde, ongann feallen to Jacobes foten þuss cweðende, Ic
bidde þe for þines Drihtnes name, þæt þu me forgeofenysse sylle
þæs þe ic wið þe agylt habbe, & do me dælnymende beon
þære ecen myrhðe.
 122. Þa undergeat se halge Jacobus þæt his heorte wæs
geneosod fram þan ælmihtigan Gode, & cwæð to him, Gelyfst þu
þæt se sy soð God, þe þa Judees on rode hengan?
 125. Josias andswerode, Ic gelefe, & þæt is min geleafe nu
oðð þysne time þæt he is þæs lyfigendan Godes Sune.
 127. Þa wæs eall þiss gecyðd þan ealdorbiscope, þe
Abiathar hatte, & he let þa gehæften Josiam & him to cwæð,
Gewisslice gyf þu ne gecerst fram Jacobe, & weregest þæs Hælendes
name þe he bodeð, mid him þu scealt beon beheafdod.
 130. Josias andswerode, Aweregod beo þu & ealle þine lease
godes, for þan þe þu awendest þe fram þæs soðen Godes beboden.
 132. Mines Drihtenes name, soðlice Hælendes Cristes þe
Jacobus bodeð, is gebletsod on ecnysse.
 134. Þa het Abiathar beaten his muð þearle swyðe, &
hine syððen sænde to Heroden, & gewrit mid him þæt me hine
samod beheafdigen scolde mid Jacobe.
 136. Þa heo becomen soðlice to þære stowe þær me hine
beheafdigen scolde, þa cwæð Sanctus Jacobus to þan cwylleren, Ic bidde
eow eadmoddre bene þæt ær þan þe ge us beheafdigen, doð us hider
bringan wæter to, & me brohte heom þa to sesterfulne wæteres.
 140. Se halge Jacobus cwæð to Josiam, Gelyfst þu on ures
Drihtenes namen Hælendes Cristes þæs lyfigenden Godes Bearn?
 142. He andswerode, Ic gelefe.
 142. Se halge Jacobus hine begeat þa mid þan wætere &
him to cwæð, Forgyf me sibbne coss.
 144. Mid þan þe Josias hine cyssinde wæs, þa asænde he
his hand ofer his heafod & worhte Cristes rodetacn ofer his forheafde,
& hine swa gebletsode.
 146. Josias wearð þa fullfremod on geleafen ures Drihtenes
Hælendes Cristes & on ænne time samod mid þan apostole gemartyrod
wearð & ferden swa to Drihtene to heofone rice.
 149. Þan sy wuldor & wurðmynt a on ealra wurlde wurld,
Amen.
