LS 12 (NatJnBapt)
B3.3.12.
Nativity of John the Baptist: Morris 1874-80, 161-9.



 1. Sancte Iohannes Baptista Spel.
 1. MEN þa leofestan, her us manaþ & mynegaþ on þissum
bocum & on þissum halgum gewrite, be þisse halgan tide weorþunga þe
we nu todæg mærsian sceolan & weorþian, þonne is þæt seo
foremære gebyrd Sancte Iohannes þæs fulwihtweres.
 5. Be þyssum we þonne witon magon & ongyton he swiþe us
is þes dæg to mærsienne & to weorþienne.
 6. Forþon þe we gehyrdon þa þæt halige godspel rædd
wæs þæt næniges Godes haligra gebyrd, ne his heahfædera, ne his
witgana, ne his apostola, ciricean ne mærsiaþ nemþe Cristes sylfes &
þyses Iohannes.
 9. Manige halge & gedefe witgan wæran ær Sancte Iohanne,
þa wæron myccle & foremære, & fram Gode seolfum gehalgode,
& mid Haliges Gastes geofum swa swiþe onlyhte & gehalgode swa
þæt hie eal þæt toweard wæs, beforan witgodan & mannum
cyþdon.
 14. & hie wæron gewitan ealra Godes degolra doma, & hie
cyningum & yfelum ricum ealdormannum wiþstandan mihtan.
 15. & hi heofon mid heora mægenum bridlodan, & hie on
swiþe manegum godcundum mægenum ealra wundorweorcum swiþe wuldorlice
ascinon.
 18. & hie þære soþfæstnesse spellodan & tacen
secgende wæron, þa þe Drihten sylf getacnode.
 19. Ac þæt hwæþere be þare nænigum gecweden beon ne
mihte, þæt se Hælende Drihten Crist be þyssum Iohanne gecwæþ,
þæt næfre betuh wifa gebyrdum nænig mærra ne sylra geboren
nære.
 22. & se godspellere sona on fruman his godspell swa be
þære Iohannes gebyrde wrat & cwæþ, On Herodes dagum þæs
cyninges wæs swiþe mycel æweweard, þæs noma wæs Zacharias.
 25. & his wifes nama wæs Elizabeþ seo wæs from Arones
dohtrum þæs heahfæder.
 26. & se halga godspellere swa be him wrat, & cwæþ,
Hie butu wæron swiþe gedefe beforan Gode, & hie eodan on eallum
Drihtnes bebodum butan leahtre.
 29. Eala hu swiþe eadge wæron þa æþelan cennende
Sancte Iohannes, þæm ne sceþede nænig scyld þisse sceþwracan
worlde, ne hie nænigo firen ne gewundode, ne yfel gewitnes ne wregde, ne hie
nænig leahter ne drefde.
 32. Ac hie wæron gemyndige ealra Godes beboda, & on ælce
wisan hie wæron þære godcundan æ swiþe gehyrsume.
 34. & nu seo heora iugoþ & seo midfyrhtnes butan
æghwylcum leahtre gestanden, hwylc talge we þonne þæt seo yldo &
se ende þæs heora lifes wære ne se fruma swylc wæs?
 37. Seo Elizabeþ þonne wæs unwæstmfæst þara
godcundra mægena, & þeah þe heo þæs bearnes lata wære; heo
þonne þæs bearnes noht lata ne wæs, þonne hwæþere æt
þære halgan Elizabet seo hire gebyrd naht gemunan þe heo hire on ylda
þa wære?
 41. Forþon þe mycelre tide ær þære halignesse hus
geclænsod beon sceolde, & seo gastliþnes þæs Cristes
wicsceaweres, & seo gisternes gebuennes þæs Cristes engles.
 44. & seo heall þæs Halgan Gastes swylc templ eallinga
Gode weorþe funden wæs Haliges Gastes snytro on to gerestenne.
 46. & þa þe æghwylc mennisc leahter on þæm eadigan
Sancte Iohanne cennendum gestilled wæs, & hie on eallum heora life
orleahtre gestodan, þa sona seo unwæstmfæstnes fram him fleah, &
sona heora ylda geliffæsted wæs, & geleafa & seo clænnes
onfeng.
 50. Þa wæs acynned se mon Sancte Iohannes, se wæs mara
& selra eallum oþrum mannum.
 51. He wæs gelic Godes englum, & he wæs beme, Cristes
fricca on þysne middangeard, & wæs Godes Suna spellboda, &
segnbora þæs ufancundan Kyninges, & firena forgifnes, & gerihtnes
hæþenra þeoda.
 55. & ic secge þæt se godspellere wæs fæstnung
ægþer ge þære ealdan æ, ge þære niwan ge þonne, forþon
þæs fæder & þære modor godcund mægen beforan wrat þæt
be þære cennendra gewyrhtum þæs bearnes weorþe ongyten wære be
þyson/ eallum oþrum mannum.
 59. Forþon hie þære an his gebyrde oforstag ealle æ
þisse menniscan gecynde.
 60. Ond nu seo Cristes gebyrd æt his æriste, se niwa eorendel
Sanctus Iohannes; & nu nu se leoma þære soþan sunnan God selfa cuman
wille.
 62. Sylle se friccea his stefne.
 63. & forþon þe nu þæt is se dema Drihten Crist, seo
beme Sanctus Iohannes, & nu mid God selfa on þysne middangeard cuman
wile, gange se engel beforan him Sanctus Iohannis.
 66. & forþon þe þæt æghwylces mennisces monnes
gemet is þæt he Sanctus Iohannes lifes weorþunga gesecgan mæge;
forþon þe he mid þære soþfæstnesse stefne gehiered wæs, &
geweorþod.
 69. & he Drihten selfa swa on his godspelle be him cwæþ,
To hwon eodan ge to westenne, witgan to secenne?
 70. Ic hine secge maran & selran þonne ænigne witgan;
Forþon þe nænig mennisc tunge ne geneah þæs acendan engles godcund
mægen to gesecgenne.
 73. Eac spræc se heahengel Sanctus Gabriel & cwæþ to
Zachariam his fæder, Ne wilt þu þe ondrædan Zacharias.
 75. Þin ben is eallunga fram Gode gehyred, end þin wif Elizabet
þe gebereþ sunu, & þu cegst his noman Iohannes, & þe bið
þonne hyht & gefea; & manige on his gebyrd gefeoþ.
 77. He biþ eallinga swiþe mycel beforan Gode; ne drincþ he
win ne ealu, ac he bið gefylled mid Halgum Gaste on his modor bosme.
 80. & manige Israhela bearna he gehwyrfþ to heora Drihtne;
& he gæþ beforan Gode mid Halgum Gaste gefylled & Elian mægene
þæs witgan, Drihtne to geearnienne medome folc.
 82. Uton we þonne, men þa leofestan, gehyran hu swiþe loflice
Sanctus Iohannes wæs mid þæs Halgan Gastes mægenum gefylled, þa
gen/ þa he on his modor bosme wunigende wæs.
 85. & he ær to heofonum becom ærþon þe he eorþan
æthrine, & þær Halgum Gaste onfeng ærþon þe he menniscne
hæfde; & þam godcundum gifum he ær onfeng, ærþon þe he
mennisc lif hæfde.
 89. & he ongan lifgean ongean God, ærþon þe he him
sylfum lifgean mihte; swa Sanctus Paulus se apostol cwæþ, Ne lybbe ic, ac
Crist leofaþ.
 91. Anna þonne þy syxtan monþe þæs þe Sanctus Iohannes
on his modor bosm onfangen wæs, þa þæt wuldres bearn on þysne
middangeard astag, & seo heofencunde weorþung þone fæmnlican bosm
Sancta Marian gefylde.
 94. & þa heo þa into þære hire moddrian eode þære
halgan Elizabethe, sona þæt cild onsprang & ongean his Hlaford hyhte
& hine of his modor bosme on þære fæmnan bosm halette & grette,
& hine ær monnum gecyþan & gesecgan teolode, ærþon þe he
sylfa lifde & mennisc leoht gesawe.
 99. Eala men þa leofoston, hu þæt wæs weallende spelboda
& ungeþyldig heretoga, se þe ær þone Hælend on þysne
middangeard cumendne gesecgean wolde, ærþon þe he þære gerynelican
gegaderunge menniscre gebyrde onfenge.
 103. & he ær to þam cyninge becom & wæpn gegrap mid
to campienne, ærþon þe he to his lichoman leomum become.
 105. & he ær þone feþan sohte, ærþon þe he
þæt leoht gesawe.
 106. & he swa on þære his gebyrde oferswiþde ealle æ
þisse menniscan gebyrde.
 107. Uton we gesceawian þa healican gewyrhto Sancte Iohannes se
þære modor innoþas ongean þam Godes Suna aweahte, se þagen sylfa
wæs butan menniscan innoþe.
 110. & þeah he þa get latode on þissum lichomlicum
gebyrde, hwæþre he on þæm gaste anum þæs godspelleres þegnunga
gefylde.
 112. & sona swa he acenned wæs & geboren, he þam
fæder þa stefne ageaf & þa tungan onlysde, þa se heahengel mid
þære swigunge fæstnunga geband þone fæder, forþon þe he his
wordum ne gelyfde.
 115. Mycel is þonne þeos weorþung þæs halgan Sancte
Iohannes gebyrde, & eal rihtgelyfed folc sceal gefeon on þone his tocyme
& hine bletsian, forþon þe þæt gewrit swa be him cwæþ
þæt monige on þa his gebyrd gefeon sceoldan.
 119. Mycel is se haligdom & seo weorþung Sancte Iohannes
þæs mycelnesse se Hælend Drihten sylfa tacn sægde; & hit cuþ
is þæt betux wifa gebyrdum ne wearþ mara mon geworden þonne Iohannes
se fulwihtere.
 123. Selfa se wæs butan menniscan fæder fram unwemre
fæmnan acenned.
 124. Sanctus Iohannes þonne gæþ beforan eallum oþrum
witgan, & ealra oþerra heahfædera mægen he oferstigeþ on þæm
apostolican gewealde, & he on his mægenes weorþunga oferswiþ ealra
oþerra Godes martira wuldor.
 127. & eallum Godes halgum he is sigefæstra &
gecorenra.
 128. & eall þeos mennisce gebyrd Sancte Iohanne bedyrned is.
 129. Hwæt we gehyrdon, þa þa Esaias se witga ræden
wæs, þæt se Halga Gast swa þurh hine be Sancte Iohanne cwæþ, Ic
sende minne engel beforan þinre onsyne, se greweþ þinne weg beforan
þe.
 132. Þæt wæs þonne swiþe healic nama þæt Sanctus
Iohannes engel wæs nemned; ac þæt his lif þæm his naman wæs
gelice gegearwod, forþon þe he her on eorþan engelice life lifde.
 135. Hwanne gefyrnode.
 136. Be wyrtum & be wudu hunige?
 136. Oþþe hwær agylte he æfre on his gegerelan, se þe
mid þon anum hrægle wæs gegyrwed þe of olfenda hærum awunden
wæs?
 138. Oþþe hu mihte æfre ænig mara beon þe æfre God
on eallum his life lufode þonne se þe næfre fram westenne ne gewat?
 140. Oþþe hwanne besmat hine seo scyld þære
fealasprecolnesse, þone þe swa feor from eallum monnum adælæd
wæs?
 142. Oþþe hu sceþede him seo synn þære swigunga þe swa
stronglice þa Iudeas þreade, þe to him coman toþon þæt hie his
lare gehyrdon.
 144. & he swa cwæþ, Ge næddrena cynn, hwylc æteowde
eow to fleonne fram ðon toweardan Godes erre?
 146. & hine ða þa heapas frugnon, hwæt hie wyrcean
mihton þæt hie Godes erre beflugon, he hie þonne mid ðissum wordum
lærde & manode, & him swa tocwæð, Se þe hæbbe twa tunecan,
selle oðre ðam ðe nane næbbe; se þe mettas hæbbe, do þæt.
 151. Wyrceað ac wesað þancfulle þon Hælende eoweres
andleofan.
 152. Uton we ðonne þus healices & ðus foremæres ures
mundboran lare folgian, þæt we ðone bylewitan cwide ures Drihtnes
gehyran motan, ðe he on ðam egeslican domes dæge to ðæm mannum
cwið, ðe nu on earmum mannum mildheortnesse ne wyrceað.
 156. Soð ic eow secge, swa lange swa ge ðis dydon ðara anum
ðe on me gelyfdon, ðeah hit se læsta wære & se heanosta, þæt
wæs swa swa ge hit me sylfum dydon.
 158. Hwæt sceal ic ðonne ma secgean fram Sancte Iohanne,
cwæð se ðe þas boc worhte, buton þæt he ær eode beforan
Criste, ærðæm þe he beforan him sylfan gangan mihte.
 161. & ðæs fæder & ðære modor & ðæs
suna heortan se ilca Halga Gast mid his gifum gefylde, ðæm is simle wuldor
& weorðung on ealra worlda world, a on ecnesse.
 164. Amen.

 25r.1. Þonon he wæs ferende to þære ceastre þe aleþ

 25r.17. Se halga Machu nan þing metecynnes næs brycende butan

 25r.19. <foreign>De cibo eius in</foreign> He his ansene na þæt an fram wifa
&weardnesse ascyrede, ac eac swylce fram wera þæt he swa fram monnum
ascered geornlice & anhsumlice geanbidode þa engellican tocyme þurh
þa godcundnesse.
 25v.1. <foreign>De uestimento eius in die noctuque</foreign> He bedreste næfre
næfde ne bedreaf ne he næfre his heafod on pyle ne gehelde þæt reaf
þe he on dæg werode þæt ilce he on niht for nescre wulle wæs
brucende.
 25v.4. He hine scrydde mid ruhre hæran þæt betwuh þa tida
þæs slæpes & þære tide stilnesse nære nan rest þæs
lichoman.
 25v.7. Swa myclum swa his weorþmynd wæs weaxende swa myclum he
on mihtum wæs gearweorþad his geleafa wæs scinende þurh missenlicre
lare & his þæt halige lif þurh tacna.
 25v.10. <foreign>De dimedio panis pauperi tradito</foreign> Hit gelamp on sumne
timan þæt hym of his æwlicum gereorde healf hlaf wearþ to lafe þa
cumendum anum þearfan se halga Machu him þone healfan hlaf wæs
sellende.
 25v.14. Wæs se halga & se Godes man swyþor wilnigende
þone healfne hlaf on edleane & on mede behydan þonne on his innoþe.
 25v.17. Þa his efenþeowa þæs noma wæs rifan cumendre
þære tide þæt hy hie gereordan sceoldan he wæs þone healfan hlaf
secende & he hine na ne funde ac þus cwæþ: Ealle her lifiaþ ic her
libban ne mæg.
 25v.21. Þa se halga Machu &swarode & cwæþ: symble
his hæbbende he his þeowum.
 25v.23. He þeah se broþor earfodlice næfde mid þ.
 27r.1. He hine gereorde æfter his geswince &
þeahhwæþre drihten wæs smeagende embe þæs þeowan mete ne he
þafigean nolde þæt he þurh hungre gedreht wære.
 27r.4. Þa butan ælcere eldincge an þara leorningcnihta þe
se halga Machu on mynstre gesette betwuh heora fæstene brohte mænifealde
lac, & he heora mettas gemænigfylde & swa binnan anes dæges
fæce þæt þæt mon þon þearfan her on eorþan sealde mid myclan
edleane of heofonum Gode forestihtendum him wæs geleanod.
 27r.11. Soþlice se halga Machu fram his geoguþe ær þon
þe he þa endebyrdnesse mæssepreosthades underfenge he fram Gode on
mihtum wæs gehalgod.
 27r.14. <foreign>De lan domnec</foreign> Hwæt hit eft sume siþe gelamp þa se
halga Machu wæs geondfarende þa mynstra for lufan þara leorningcnihta
þa wæs he farende neah cellan anes Godes þeowes þæs noma wæs
Domnech se wæs þeowiende Gode dæges & nihtes æfter his mihtum.
 27r.20. Þa he sume dæge hine on his incleofan wæs
gebiddende þa se ealdormon þe þa rixade on tune aleþ þæs noma
wæs Meliau þær farende.
 27r.23. He þa wæs acsiende & he het þa hine to
acsiende/ hu mycel landes he hæfde.
 27v.1. Þa cwæþ he him to: On noman Cristes Godes sunu
þæm þe þu þeowest genim twegen gunge oxan & untemede & hie
gegeoce under anum geoce fylgendre þære sylh , & swa mycel land swa
hie fram sunnan upgange oþ hire niþersige embgangan magan on ecre
yrfedwearnesse ic hit þe selle, & swa hwylc mon swa hit awende þurh
þin gebed sie he awyrged.
 27v.9. He þa sancte Machu ænne þearfan gemette on anre dic
hine selfne hydende & he hine þa acsade hwig he hine þær behydde.
 27v.12. He him to cwæþ: ic fedde mines hlafordes swyn
Domneches.
 27v.13. þa hæfde an sugu eahta fearas under hy.
 27v.14. þa cumendre adle, heo dead gewearþ.
 27v.15. & þis is nu se þridda dæg syþþan ic me
hydde, & ic ne gedyrstlæhte on his &weardnesse cuman.
 27v.17. & he þa sancte Machu hine acsade hwær seo sugu

& he þa sancte Machu þurh mildheortnesse wæs astyred mid his
stæfe suge ætran, & heo þa raþe aras, & he þa se þeow
wæs/ yrnende & his hlaforde mid ormætre blisse gecydde.

 18r.4. & he þa þone dæg & ane niht mid him wæs
& þy mergendlican dæge to his eardungstowe ferde.
 18r.7. Þa se halga Machu farende wæs geond þa scire aleþ
þa wæs þær an dumb cild him on wege farendum ongean cumende.
 18r.9. Þa se halga wer mid his hand wæs handligende þa stowa
þæs cildes welera he natoþoshwon ontynan ne mihte þara toþa gebind.
 18r.12. He sona mid spatle his muþes gebletsade þæt gefeg
þara cecana, & him þam cecan ætrinendum þa teþ sweg agæfan
swylce forslegene wæron þa bryceas þara racantegena.
 18r.15. & he þa dyde on his muþe þæt gemengde spatl
& hine acsade hwæt him wære & hwig he dum wære.
 18r.17. Him þærrihte þæt cild þurh word &swarode hu
he dum gewearþ.
 18r.19. Þa gewearþ þæs eadigan weres hlisa feor &

 18r.21. Þa se heretoga brytlandes ricu þam wæs noma

geþafunge he hine wolde up ahebban on weorþmynte bisceophades and setle on

 18v.3. He þa se halga Machu þa he þæs cinges gebod geherde
he hine mid tacne þære halgan rode gebletsade & to þæs cinges
healle mid his vii leorningcnihtum ferde.
 18v.7. Þa he into þæs cincges healle eode þa wæs
þær an man deofolseoc & mid his toþum gristbitiende se sprecan ne
mihte for þon þe deofol his tungan abysgod hæfde.
 18v.10. Se halga þa him genealæhte & his muþ mid his
fingre æthran, & he þa his tungan of bendum alesde & he spræce
onfeng & he openlice wæs sprecende & deofol wæs þa fram him
fleonde & grymetende, ne seo adl þær nane mihte næfde þær
swylc lecedom brohte.
 18v.17. Þa þis wundor geond ealle þæs cinges healle wæs
gecyd/ þa ealle þa sacerdas & eall folc anrædlice þone cing eft
bædon hym to bisceope aletes gehalgian.
 18v.20. Soþlice God ælmihtig him swa mycle gifu sealde
þæt næs nan þe hine inweardlice ealle cwædon þæt he soþ
Godes þeow wære for þon he geswutulad hæfþ þæt he on
heofonlicum þeawum getyd & gelæred wæs.
 17v.2. Næs he na gemende to mihtigra monna hade ac to þære
æwfæstnesse fægernesse & weorþfulnesse.
 17v.4. Soþlice he wæs æþela Cristes cempa.
 17v.5. He hæfde encgelic hiw he wæs beorht on his spræce
& on his weorce halig, & on his lichoman clæne & gemang þeode
he wæs mycel & on geþeahte he wæs fulfremed & on geleafan he
wæs geleafful & he wæs ful þære soþan lufan & on
estfulnesse he wæs mære & healic & he on Cristes lufan wæs
gelagad.
 17v.11. Þa þæt folc þas þing bodiende wæron þam

& þam halgum Machute geþafigendum & willende þæt he þa ferde
to sancte Martines circean þære toroniscean ceastre biscope, & se cing
þa mid him sende gewrit & bodan þæt he þær bisceopes bletsunga
underfencge.
 17v.18. Hym þa farendum & to þære stowe tocumendum þe
hie to onettan þa wæs þær myclu mænigu standende æt þære
circean dure & wæron mæssan geanbidiende.
 17v.21. Þa seo cirice belocan wæs & se hine scrydende.
 17r.1. Se halga Machu hine on anum lytlan portice ahydde & on
gebedum wæs hleonigende.
 17r.2. Þa wæron þær deofolseoce men & þus
cleopodan & cwædon: eala sancte Machuloua gemildsa us & nelle þu
us her þreagen.
 17r.4. Se halga hie þa þreade & het þæt hie
geswugudan.
 17r.5. Þa men he gehealde & deofla he aflemde, & he þa
into circean eode & þa bletsunge bisceophades underfeng.
 17r.7. Ac hit is wundorlic to secganne of þære tide þe þa
bisceopas heora handa ofer his heafod alegdon þa eft wæs æteowed an
hwit culfre ofer his sweoran, þa he to þære bletsunge gebeah.
 17r.11. & þa þe he hine up arærde mid his bletsunge
gefylledre þære hadunge hym eallum geseondum swyþust þam bodum þe
mid him coman seo culfre to heofonum fleah.
 17r.16. Se halga Machu eft wæs farende mid þam bodum to
þæs cinges hofum.
 17r.17. & þa se cing geherde his bodan reccean þa wundra
þe ælmihtig God sancte Machute sealde he þa sona wæs onfonde
þæs halgan bletsunge managa gifu wæs sellende.
 17r.20. & he þa se halga Machu to aletes þære ceastre
com & þær for e þone wæstm godes weorces geond geleaffulle

 21v.1. & he eft þonon wæs cumende to þon iglande þe is
geciged Aarones igland & þær wæs Gode þeowigende, & þær
men gehælde fram missenlicum adle; & swa he wolde hine fram þweora
monna gesihþa & spræcea asyndrigean.
 21v.5. Him þa þeah þær wuniendum & Gode þeowigende

coman & þone halgan wæron tælende.
 21v.14. He þa se halga þa stowe & þone eþel forlætan
wolde & þone mon þæs noma wæs Gworguecant wæs wyrgiende.
 21v.17. He him þone teonan dyde oþ þæt neogaþe cynryn,

þær sume hwile.
 21r.1. Blostman haligra gewrita & þara þinga þe seo
soþe lufu hym gegearwade hie gemænelice gereordan æfter sacerdlicum

 21r.4. Se halga Machu þonon eft wæs farende & Brytlandes

mid þon wæstme his bodunga to heofona rice gelædde & he þa to

 21r.10. Þa Iudicheles sunu þæs noma wæs Reþwalus þurh

þæs halgan stowe towearpan þurh geswinc getimbrede.
 21r.13. Þa se halga Machu þæt geherde þa ferde he mid his

 21r.16. & þus cwæþ: Warna þe þæt þu nanum men

 23v.1. Þy mergendlican dæge þa scearpnesse his eagena forlet

 23v.3. Rihtlice him þurh Godes dom swa gelamp þæt se þe

 23v.18. & him to cwæþ: Swa hwylce dædbote swa þu me

 23v.20. Þa se Godes wer Machu geseah þone cing eaþmodlice

 23r.3. He þa þon wætere onfeng & wæs þweande þa

 23r.8. <foreign>De interfecto infantulo</foreign> Æfter Iudicheles deaþe se

þæt he þone maran & ufan þam oþrum on þæm rice gedyde.
 23r.13. Ac þa þe he heora wæs ehtende & hie ofslean het
þa se an fleam began & mid his fosterfæder to sancte Machutes cellan
fleonde heolster gesohte.
 23r.16. Þa se arleasa Redwala þæt ongeat he æftergewat

þæs halgan Godes weres cellan & on nihtlicum færelde in eode &
þæs cinges sunu þonon diglice.

 15r.3. Ac se reþa & se wælreowa & se arleasa & se

 15r.12. & he þa se halga þone lichoman weorþfullice

 15v.2. Witodlice ne mæg nan mennisc tunge areccean hwylc he

 15v.4. He hine selfne to lomlicum wæccum gegearwade & he

þa godan weorc aræfnian þonne he on siþfæte ferende wæs symble

 15v.9. His dægsang he gefylde geond þa æwlican tida ne he

oþþe rædende, oþþe writende, oþþe wyrcende symble he his

 15v.13. Þonne he to his misan & gereorde gesæt
þærrihte se rædere ætwæs, & þa godcundan spræcea wæs

 15v.17. Næs nan tid þæt he oþþe oþrum mannum ne

 13r.1. Þa wæron þære circean dura ealle belocene &
cægan wæron sohte, & nane circweardas næron gemette.
 13r.3. Þa se halga mid hand tacen þære halgan rode on þa
duru gesette & hie þa ætforan him & ongean ontynde wæron butan
ælcum bryce & deringe, þa gewat mycel oga & fyrhtu þurh þæt
wundor on mod þara ætstandendra.
 13r.7. & hie ealle God heredon þus cweþende: Sy God
gebletsad þe þis wundor on his þeowe Machute onywde.
 13r.9. <foreign>De homine in die dominico operante</foreign> Hit gelamp witodlice
on þy drihtenlican sunnandæge þa sum mon scos to sellanne seowede
þæt his handa wurþon gebundene & geclencte.
 13r.13. Se þy mergedlican dæge to sancte Machute com mid adle
geþread.
 13r.14. Se halga wer hine þa wæs acsiende hu him seo adl
oncome.
 13r.15. He þa his gylt þurh endebyrdnesse gecydde þurh
hwæt him þæt wite onbecom.
 13r.17. Þa se halga wer his hreowsunge wæs ongetende, he þa
mid haligre bletsunge & mid tacne þære halgan rode his handa
gebletsade/ hale forgæf, & þis wundor geond godes & mære
wæs geworden.
 13r.21. <foreign>De paralitico sanato</foreign> witodlice on þære tide
þy drihtenlican sunnandæge mæssade & him setl wæs tobroht on to
sittenne þa wæs him tobroht sum loma ealra his leoma.
 13v.3. Þa wæron hie ealle þe þæræt wæron for hine
biddende for þon þe he wæs of æþelum cynrene.
 13v.5. Þa sona swa se halga bisceop Machu wæs gemedemad for
hine to gebiddanne.
 13v.7. He þa æfter his gebede þone loman mid halgum
wætere wæs þweande & seo ald ongan stycmælum aweggewitan &
seo miht þære hælo him in eode & swa geedcwicedum innoþum seo
ærru hæl him wæs agifen þurþ þæs halgan geearnunga to þon
swyþe þæt hie ealle drihten heredon þe þas wundorlican wundru þurh
his þeowan Machutem wæs gemedemad to anywanne.
 13v.14. Se halga Machu wæs manþwære on eaþmodnesse he
wæs ful þære soþan lufan & on ælmesdædum he wæs
rumgiful/ & strang on geþylde.
 13v.17. He wæs forhogiende þas weorld þæt he þæt
ece rice geearnode þa eorþlican lofu he forhogade þus cweþende:
Geseoh/ þu mon þæt monna lofu þe na into heofonum edwit þe
þonan abredaþ wlite he forhogade þæt he into Cristes healle þæt
is heofona rice welig ferde.
 16v.2. He þurh his þa godan weorc gelicode Gode & mannum.
 16v.3. þam yfelum monnum & þon ungeleaffullum he na ne
forsceamode to mislicianne.
 16v.4. Blindum he gesihþe forgæf, healtum feþe, deafum hlyst
anhendum edstaloþ.
 16v.6. He þa unclænan gastas of ofsettum lichoman utanedde
& he ealle biternesse þurh þa heofonlican gife fram monnum afyrde.
 16v.9. Soþlice we &dettaþ þæt þa þurhbeorhtan
weorc & dæda þæs halgan Machutes ne mæg nan mennisc gecynd
areccean ne hu myclan lofe hie syndo to heriganne.
 16v.12. <foreign>De eius thesauro</foreign> Se halga & se eadiga sancte Machu he
wæs lufwendlic wer & æþele sacerd þæm wæs geþuht
ormæte leoht his æþelnesse þæt he Criste dæges & nihtes
lufwendlice þeowede & weorodlice hersumade.
 16v.16. Se þe ne genam nan idel gelp for his æþelborenesse
ne ne for his godum weorcum.
 16v.18. He wæs healdende wiþinnan him his goldhord & he
wæs God clyppende mid clænre heortan & he þearfa wæs mid
mihtigum cristenlic þam þingum he hine to þære heofonlican lare
sealde swa þæt he þa sacerlican þenunga weorþlice & estfullice
gefylde.
 16r.3. <foreign>De puero a diabolo obsesso</foreign> Sum cild wæs þæt se
unrihtwisa deofol ofsæt & þurh fif geara rynu wæs of his gemynde se
mid racenteagum gebunden wæs, & to þam halgum were & bisceope
wæs gelæd & beforan his ansene þearle wæs wedende & fela
unweorhlicra þinga wæs donde.
 16r.9. He þa wæs embseald mid tacne þære halgan rode fram
þon halgan bisceope Machute mid his gebede, & he þa sancte Machu fram
him deofol utanedde mid his gebedum & hine agæf his þære ærran
hælo.
 16r.13. <foreign>De horis uigiliarum eius</foreign> Ne mæg na ure sefa areccean
hu mycel caru þara weccena on sancte Machute wunedan.

eahtoþan/ & he þanon ut ne eode butan to his lichoman neode ær

gefylde & geendade.

 33v.4. <foreign>de eloquio eius</foreign> Hwa mæg areccean hu mycel miht wære

LS 14 (MargaretAss 15)
B3.3.14.
Saint Margaret: Assmann 1889, 170-80.



 1. Efter drihtnes þrowunge and his æriste, þæt he of
deaðe aras hælend Crist: on þam dagum his halgan geþrowodon for his
þæra micclan leofan lufan.
 3. Eac þa gewearð hit, þæt þa halga seagntes ofercomen
þa deofle, þe wið heom gewunnon.
 4. And þa ricene, þe on þan dagum wæron, hæfdon heom
geworht godes of golde and of seolfre; þa wæron dumbe and deafe and
blinde, and eal þæt hæþan folc swiðe gelefdon on þan godum.
 8. Sum land is Anthiochia gehaten.
 8. On þam lande wæs an godes þeowa; se wæs Theothimus
gehaten; he wæs swiðe gelæred man.
 11. And þær on lande wæs sum hæþen cyningc, Theodosius
gehaten, and his cwen mid him.
 12. Hit gewearð swa, þæt heo bearn gestreonedon and þæt
wearð geboren mædencild.
 13. And se hæþene cing his fæder hit het ut aweorpan and
men swa dyde.
 14. And se godes þeowe Theothimus gefand þæt cild and he hit
up anam and hit wel befæste to fedenne.
 16. And þa hit andgeat hæfde, he him nama gesette, and
þæt wæs Margareta, and hi syððan to lare befæste, and hi
þæron wel geþeah.
 19. Ðis eadiga mæden se arwurða godes þeowa Theothimus
fedde and lærde and forðbrohte, oð þæt hi <foreign>XV</foreign> wintre eald wæs.
 21. Dæghwamlice hi hire utsanges and hire gebedu georne gefylde
and þæt ungelærde folc swiðe mynegode to ures drihtones hersumnesse,
hælendes Cristes, and þus cwæð: Geherað me, earma þeoda,
ægþer ge weres ge wifes, ge cnihtes ge mægdenes, and healdað fæste
on eowre heorta þæt þe ic eow secge and wissige.
 25. Forwyrpað þa deadan godas, þe ge her beforen to gebugan,
þe beoð mid mannes handen gegrafena, and gebegeð eow to ure sceppende
gode almihtigne, Sanctæ Marian sunu, hælende Criste.
 28. And ic eow behata and on hand selle, þæt ge sculon finden
reste eowre sawlen mid gode and mid his gecorenan innan paradyses myrhþe.
 30. Seo eadiga Margareta wæs Theodosius dohtor; se gehersumode
þan deofle and hi gehersamedo gode and ealle his halgan.
 32. Ða geherde seo eadiga Margareta and hi hit on bocum fand,
þæt þa cinges and þa ealdormenn and þa yfela gerefan ofslogen
æfre and bebyrodon ealle þa godes þeowas, þe þær on lande
wæron.
 35. Sumne hi mid wæpnum acwealdon and sumne mid hatum
wætere.
 36. Sumne hi onhengon be þan fotum and sumne be þan earmum.
 37. Sumne hi pinedon mid wallende leade and mid hatum stanum.
 38. Sumne heo mid sweorde ofslegen, sumne mid spiten betweon felle
and flæsce þurhwræcon.
 39. Eall þæt godes þeowan geþafodon and geþrowodon for
godes deoran lufan.
 40. And þa seo eadiga Margareta þis eall geherde and geseah, hi
hi þæs þe swiðor to gode gebæd and þus cwæð: <foreign>Domine Deus
omnipotens, ego sum ancilla tua</foreign>; Drihten god ælmihtig, heo cwæð, ic
eom þin þeowa clæna and ungewæmmed fram eallum mannum, þe geborene
bið.
 45. Þe ic me betæce ungewæmmode, þæt þu me gehealde
togeanes þæs deofles costnung strange and staþolfæste on þinre
þære sweteste lufa, forþan þe to þe nu is and æfre wæs and
þurh þin help æfre beon sceal min hiht and min hope and min soþe
lufu.
 49. Ða gewearð hit on anum dæge, þæt hire fostermoder
hi het gan mid oþrum fæmnum on feld, sceap to hawienne, and hi swa dydo
spinnende.
 51. Ða ferde Olibrius se heahgerefa fram Asia þæra burh to
Anthiochiam, axiende, hwær þa wæron, þe heora godan here noldan.
 53. Ða he on his wege rad, þa beseah he on þæt eadigan
mæden, þær þe hi sæt wlitig and fæger onmang hire geferan.
 54. Ða cwæð he to his cnihtum: Ridað hraþe to þære
fæmnan and axiað hire, gif hi seo frig.
 56. And gif hi is, þonne wille ic hi habban me to wife.
 56. And gif hi is þeowa, þonne wille ic gifen fih for hire and
hæbban hi me to cefase and hire scel beon wel mid me þurh hire
fægernesse and hire fægre wlite.
 59. And þa cnihtes hire þa to comon and hire to spræcon,
eall swa heom gehaten wæs.
 60. Ða Sancta Margareta heo to eorþan gestrehte and hi hire
georne to gode gebæd and þus cwæð: <foreign>Miserere mei, Deus, miserere
mei</foreign>; Gemiltse me, drihten, gemiltse me, þæt min sawle ne seo awæmmod
þurh þisum hæþenum mannum.
 64. And ic þe wille biddan, þæt deofle mine sawle ne
beswican, ne mine treowðe fram þe ahwerfan, ne minne clæne lichaman
gefylan.
 66. Drihten leof, æfre ic þe lufode, and þu wuldorcyning, ne
læt þu me naht beswican, ne næfre min gewit fram þe gehwerfan, ne min
mægþhad afylan.
 68. Ac asænd me, leofa drihten, þinne halga engel to fultume,
þæt ic min gewitt and minne wisdom forð healdan mote, forþon ic eom
gesett betweonen þisum folce, swa swa sceap betweonon wulfum.
 71. And ic eam befangan eal swa spearwe on nette and eall swa fisc
on hoce and eal swa hra mid rape.
 72. Nu help þu me, leofa drihten, gehelp þu me.
 74. And þa cerdon þa cnihtas to heora hlaforde and cwædon:
Nis þin mægn naht wið hire, forþon þe hi lufað þone god, þe
þine eldran aheongan on rode.
 76. And þa wearð se gerefa swiðe yrre and het hi niman and
him to gebringan.
 77. And he hire to cwæð and hire axode, of hwilcere þeode hi
wære and hwæder hi wære Cristen and frig oððe þeowa.
 79. And seo eadiga Margareta him andwyrde and cwæð: Ic eom
frig and Cristen.
 80. And se cniht hire to cwæð: On hwilcum godum is þin
geleafa, þe þu on gelefst and forð wilt get gelefan?
 82. Seo eadiga Margarete him þa geandswarede: Ic lufige god
ælmihtigne, cwæð hi, and on him ic gelefa, þe is fæder and sunu
and halig gast, þone þe min mægþhad fægre and wel gehealdon
hæfð.
 85. Þæt is se þe þine yldran ahengan and þurh þære
dæde hi losian sculon, forþon þe he is cyning and his rice ne wurð
næfre nan ænde.
 87. And þa wearð Olibrius swiðe yrre and het þa fægre
fæmne genimen and innon his carcerne belucen, þær nan liht inne cumen
ne mihte, and men swa dyde.
 89. Ða þis gedon wæs, þa for se gerefa Olibrius to
Antiochia þære byrig, to his godan him to gebiddenne.
 92. And he þanan to his gereorde eode and amang þan þe he
æt, he to his þegnum spræc and þus cwæð: On hwilca wisa ræde
ge me, hu ic muge þis mæden bismærian?
 94. And hi ealle þa swigedon.
 95. Ða se gerefa het hi ut lædon of þan carcerne and
þæt wæs on þan oðre dæge and het hi bringan beforen him.
 96. And he hire to cwæð: ðu earma fæmna, læt beon
þin mycela mod, þe þu to me hæfst, and gemiltse þinum fægran
lichaman and gebide þe to minum gode and ic þe gife ælc god genoh and
þu scealt eal mines godes wealden mid me selfum.
 100. Sancta Margareta him andswerode and þus cwæð: Drihten
hit wat, þæt ic min mægþhad wel þurh him gehealdan habbe, and ne
miht þu me beswican, ne þu ne miht me becyrran of minum rihtan geleafan, ne
fram minum rihte hlaforde.
 103. And ic eom geara, cwæð hi, on drihten to gelefanne, þe
gesceop heofonas and eorðan, and he sæ bedraf, þær þe heo wrohtað
dæges and nihtes.
 106. Olibrius þa cwæð: Gif þu nylt to minum gode þe
gebiddan, min swyrd sceal þinne þone fægran lichaman eall to styccan
forcyrfan and þine lieman ealle tosindrian, and þine ban ic sceal ealle
forbærnan.
 109. And gif þu woldest me lufian and to minum godum þe
gebiddan, þe sceolde beon eall swa wel, eall swa me selfan.
 110. And seo eadiga Margareta him andswerode and cwæð: Ic
habbe minne licchaman and mine sawla gode bebodan, for he is min hlaford and
min help and min werigend and min fultum wið þe and wið eallum þinum
leasum gewitum.
 114. Crist hine selfne to þan geeadmedde, þæt he for
mancynne micele þrowunge geþrowode and na for his gewyrhtum, ac for ure
alesednesse.
 116. And ic wille, cwæð hi, for his leofan wille bliðelice
þrowian.
 118. Ða het se gerefa hi niman and het hi be þam fotan upp ahon
and mid greatum roddum beaton.
 119. And seo eadiga Margareta hire handan upp ahof and hi to gode
gebæd and þus cwæð: On þe ic gelefa, leofa drihten; and þæt ic
þe bidde, þæt þu ne þole, þæt ic næfre forwurþe, ne
þæt me mine feond næfre oferswiðan ne moten, forþan min hiht is to
þe, leofe drihten.
 123. And hi þa get hire clæne gebedu forð hild and þus
cwæð: æfre wunu þu mid me, leofa drihten heofonlice cyng.
 125. Miltse me and genere me of deofles anwealde.
 126. Ealle þa men, þe hire abutan stodon, to hire cleopoden and
þus cwædon: Hwi nelt þu, earme fæmne, gelefan on ure gode and to ure
hlaforde þe gebugan and lutan.
 128. Æle fægre fæmne, ealle we þe bemænað sarlice,
forþon þe we geseoð þe swa nacode sittan and þinne fægra lichaman
to wundre macian, and us þæt þincþ, þæt he ah þines gewald,
hwæþer swa he wille to deaðe oððe to life.
 132. Gelef on ure gode, þonne most þu mid us lif habban.
 132. Seo eadiga Margareta heom andswerode: æle ge geleasan
witan, gað hraðe to eowrum weorce, forþan ðe min god is mid me on
fultume.
 134. Hwæt, wene ge, þæt me þæt ofþynce, þæt min
lichame þrowige?
 135. Ic wat, þæt min sawle is þæs þe clænre mid
gode.
 136. Ac earme þeode, gelefað get on minum gode, and for he is
strang and mihtful and ealle þan mannen gefultumað, þe mid rihte farað
and mid clænre heorte him to gebiddað, and he heom geofð in paradise
eardingstowe.
 140. Ne þurfe ge næfre þæs wenan, þæt ic æfre
eowrum godum me to gebidde, forþon þe hi syndon dumbe and deafe and blinde
and mid drycræfte geworhte.
 143. Ða wearð se gerefa eorre geworþan and cwæð to hire:
ðu wyrcest þines fæðeres weorc, þæt is se deofol self.
 144. And seo fæmne andswaro geaf: Hwæt, þu nu, earming, mid
leasunge færst and me is min drihten on fultume.
 146. Ða cwæð se gerefa: Hwær is se god, þe mæg þe
gebeorgan of mine handan?
 147. Seo eadiga Margareta him to cwæð: Geswiga þu earmingc,
ne hæfst þu nan þingc on me to donne, ac eall þu eart full and þu
scealt faran into þære nigenda niþhelle and þu scealt þær onfon
þa yfelan geweorc, þe þu her gefremest and gefremed hæst.
 151. Ða het se gerefa hio nimon and be þan fexe up ahon and
bæd wyrcan scearpa piles and het wrecen betweon flæsce and bane.
 153. And seo eadiga Margareta hire handa up ahof and hi georne to
drihtne gebæd and þus cwæð: ðu, drihten leof, beo þu me on
fultume, for me beoð abuton hundes swa manega, and heo willeð minne
lichamen to sticcan gebringan.
 157. Drihten leof, deme mine sawla and þu genere minne lichome,
for ic ne recce þise leasere þrowunge.
 158. Gehelp þu me, drihten, and sænd me fultum, þæt ic
wið minum feondum fihtan muge, þæt ic mid minum eagne twam þe geseon
mote on þine rice.
 160. Ða þa leasan gewiten hi swiðe gepinedon and se gerefa
hire to cwæð: Gecer, earme fæmne, to me and to minum gode, and gif þu
nelt, þu scealt to wundre gewurðan.
 163. Seo eadiga Margareta him andswerode: Gif ic minne lichaman to
þe geeadmede, þonne scealt þu inne þæt wallende pic into helle wite;
þær þu scealt wunian æfre.
 166. Þonne miht þu habban minne lichaman þe to gæmene, and
god hæfð mine sawle fram þe generod.
 168. Ða wearð se gerefa swiðe yrre and het hi innan þam
carcerne belucen.
 169. And hi in eode into þam carcerne and mid Cristes rodetacne
hi hi gebletsode.
 170. And hi seofon tide þæs dæges þærinne gesæt and
hi to gode gebæd and þus cwæð: Drihten leof, þe ic þancige
þeoses domes, þe þu me in sændest, for þu eart ælces mannes
fultum, þe on þe gelefað, and þu eart fæder ealra þære þe
fæderlease syndon.
 174. And ne geswic þu me næfre, drihten leof, ac help þu me,
þæt ic me bewerige wið minum feondum, and ne læt þu me næfre
mine sawle beswican, for þu eart ealre demena dema and nu betweon me and
heom.
 178. Þa com hire fosterfæder gan to hire and þurh an
eahþyrl he hire to spræc and he hire brohte bread and wæter; þæs
wæteres hi gebreac and nanes breades.
 180. And he hire þrowunge fægre sette on godes bocum.
 181. And hit þa færunge gewearð sona æfter þam,
þæt þær inn eode an grislic deofol; his nama wæs Ruffus.
 182. And he wæs swiðe mycel on dracan heowe and eall he wæs
nædderfah.
 183. And of his toþan leome ofstod, eal swa of hwiten swurde, and
of his eagan swilces fyres lyg and of his nasþyrlum smec and fyr ormæte
mycel and his tunge þreowe his sweore belygde.
 186. Sancta Margareta hi to eorðan gestrehte and hire rihtwise
gebedu to gode gesænte and þus cwæð: Drihten god ælmihtig, georne
ic þe bæd, þæt ic hine geseage, and nu ic þe eft gebidde, þæt
ic hine ofercumen mote.
 190. And hi þa upp aras and hire earmes eastweard aðeonode and
þus cwæð: Drihten god ælmihtig, þu þe gesceope heofona and
eorþa and eal mancyn and heora lif, þe on heom syndon, and þa þu on
rode wære gehangen and þu to helle astige and þu þine halgan ut
gedydost and þone mycele deofol Sathan fæste gebunde: gehelp þu me,
leofe drihten, þæt ic þisne deofol fæste mote gebinden.
 196. And se deofol him þa abalhc and þa fæmne forswelgan
wolde.
 197. And seo eadiga fæmne sona mid hire swiðre hand wið
þone sceocca wel gebletsode and on hire forhæfde rodetacna mærcode and
swa wið þone draca wel generode.
 199. And seo eadiga fæmne hal and gesund fram him gewænte and
eall sticmælum toðwan se draca ut of þan carcerne.
 201. And hi nan yfel on hire ne gefelde.
 201. Ac hi sona to eorðan gestrehte and hi geornlice to gode
gebæd and þus cwæð: Drihten leof, lof sy þe selfum and wuldor ealra
þære goda, þe þu me dest and gedon hæfst, and get is min hopa,
þæt þu don wille aa in ealra worulda woruld.
 206. And þa hi hire gebedu gefyld hæfde, þa beseah hio hio
on þære wynstre healfe þæs carcernes and hi oþerne deofol sittan
geseah, sweart and unfæger, swa him gecynde wæs, and he þa up aras and
to hire weard eode.
 209. Þa seo fæmne on him beseah, þa cwæð hi to þam
deofle: Ic wat, hwæt þu þæncst, ac geswic þu þæs geþohtes,
forþon ic wat eall þin yfel geþanc.
 211. And se deofol hire andswerode and cwæð: Ic minne broþor
Rufonem to þe gesænde on dracan gelice, þæt he sceolde þe fordon,
and nu hæfst þu hine mid Cristes rodentacn ofslagen, and ic wat, þæt
þu me mid þinum gebedum ofslean wilt.
 215. Seo eadiga Margareta upp aras and þone deofol be þan fexe
gefeng and hine niþer to eorðan gewearp.
 216. And hi hirne swiðre fot upp on his swire gesette and him to
cwæð: Geswic þu earming, ne miht þu to nahte minne mægþhad me to
beswicenne, for ic hæbbe minne drihten me to fultume.
 219. And ic eam his þeowa and he is min hlaford and ic eom him
beweddod, þe gehalgod is aa in ealra worulda woruld.
 222. Ða hi þis gecwedon hæfde, þa þærinne com
drihtnes engel and þær wearð inne swa mycel leoht, swa hit beoð on
middæg, and he hæfde Cristes rodentacen on hande.
 224. Ða wearð Sancta Margareta swiðe bliðe and hio
þancode gode eall, þæt hi ær and sioððon þurh gode oft and
gelome gesegon hæfde.
 226. And hi þa seo fæmne wið þone deofol wordum dælde
and þus cwæð: Sege me earmingc, hwanan eart þu oððe hwanon come
þu?
 228. Se deofol hire to cwæð: Ic þe gebidde, forþon þe
þu eart gehalgod fæmne, þæt þu þinne fot of minum sweorum alihte,
and ic þe secgan wille eall, þæt ic gedon hæbbe.
 231. And hio þa seo eadiga Margareta hire fot up ahof and he hire
sæde eall, þæt he wiste, and cwæð: Siððan Sathan gebunden
wearð, siððan ic mid mannum æfre gewunode.
 234. And manega godes þeowas ic gehwearf fram gode and næfre
ne mihte me nan man ofercuman buton þu ane.
 235. Minne broþor þu ofsloge and þu mines eall geweald ahst,
forþan ic geseo, þæt god is mid þe.
 237. And get ic þe mare secge of minum dædum ealle syndrige.
 238. For ic nam ealle wæstmes fram mancynne, þe on gode
gelefdon.
 239. Sume ic spræce benam and sume heora hlyste, sumen heora fet
and sume heora handa, and heo þurh þæt creopeles wurðon.
 241. Sumum ic eagen benam and sumum his gewittes.
 241. Sume ic slæpende beswac and sume eac wacigende.
 242. Sume mid winde and sume mid wætere.
 243. Sume mid miste and sume mid drænce, ofte þonne hio
ungebletsodon wæren.
 244. Sume mid slehte and sume on some.
 245. Sume on morðdædum and sume mid oðres mannes wife
gehæmdon.
 246. Sume mid feowerfoted nytene for minum willen gefremedon and
sume heora eldran mid wordon gegræmedon.
 247. Eal þis ic me ane wat and þæt me nu hearde hreowð.
 248. Þin fæder and þin modor mine wæron and þu ane fram
fæder and fram modor and fram eallum þine cynne to gode þu gehwurfe.
 251. And seo eadiga fæmna him to cwæð: Hwanan wearð eow,
þæt ge mihton ahan godes þeowes to beswicenne?
 252. And þa se deofol hire to cwæð: Sege me, hwanen is þin
lif, Margareta, and hwanan beoð þine liman, and hwu and on hwilce wise is
Crist mid þe; and ic þe secge eall, þæt ic wat.
 255. And þa seo fæmne to þam deofle cwæð: Nelle ic hit
þe secgan, forþon þe þu ne eart þæs wurþe, þæt ic wið
þe wordum dæle, for god is swiðe god and him sy geþancod, for ic eam
his nu and æfre ma beon wille.
 258. Se deofol hire to cwæð: Sathana urne cyning, hine
gewræc drihten of paradises myrhþe and him þa twa land agæf; an is
Gamne and oðer is Mambre.
 261. And þider he gebrincð ealle þa þe he begeton mæig
of mancynne.
 262. Nu ic soðlice þe to sprece and for þi ne mæig ic na
læng beon, forþon ic geseo, þæt god is mid þe.
 263. Ac ic þe bidde, eadige fæmne, þæt ic wið þe an
word dælan mote, and ic þe hælsige þurh þinne god and þurh his
sunu and his þone halgan gast, þe þu on belefst, þæt þu me na mare
yfel ne do.
 266. And ic þe behate and þæt þe gelæste, þæt ic
næfre ma nænne mon on þisum life ne beswice and þæt ic þin bebod
fæste gehealdan wille.
 268. And seo eadiga fæmne him andswarode: Gewit þe heonan on
weig and sea eorðe þe forswelge and þu þær wunige to domes dæge.
 271. And þa þæs oðres dæges se gerefa het, þæt me
him þæt mæden toforen brohte.
 272. And þa seo fæmne ut of þan carcerne gelæd wæs,
hio hy sona seneda, þa hio ut eode, and me þær forwerhte men of
Antiochia þære burh gesamnoden, þæt hi þa fæmne geseon woldan.
 275. And þa se gerefa to þære fæmne cwæð: Wilt þu
me get geheran and to minum gode þe gebiddan?
 276. And hi þa andswera ageaf: Ne þe, ne þinum godum ic
næfre ne lufige; ac þe wel gerisde, þæt þu minnen gode wel
geherdest and lufodest, þane þe lufað ælc þære manna, þe hine
mid inweardre heortan lufiað.
 279. Ða het se gerefa hio genimon and bead heom hire claðes of
niman and hi up ahon bi þan fotum, and he het wallende stanes on hire
fægre lichaman geworpan, and heo þa leasan gewitan eac swa dydon.
 283. And þa cwæð se gerefa to þære fæmne: And nylt
þu me get lufian, ne to minum gode þe gebugan, ne þe to him gebiddan?
 284. And seo eadiga fæmne nolde him andswarigen nan word.
 286. Ða wærð se gerefa swiðe eorre and het mycel fyr
onælan and ænne cytel þærofer gesettan and bæd þære fæmne
fet and handan tosomne gebindon and innen þone weallende cetel gesetton.
 289. And seo eadiga Margareta heo georne to gode gebæd and þus
cwæð: Ic þe wille biddan, leofa drihten cyning, þæt þæt
wæter gewurðe me to fulluhtes bæðe and to clænsunge ealra minum
synnum.
 292. And þa þær com fleogan drihtnes ængel and he þa
gehalgode þæt wallende wæter to fonte and þa halga fæmne genam be
þære swiðre hand and of þan wætere þa fæmne gesette and hire
on þan wætere na lað ne gewearð.
 295. Ða þæt geherdon and geseagon þe hire ymbstodan,
wundor heom þuhte.
 296. Hio geherdon stefne of heofone clypion to þære fæmne
þus: Ic eom þin godfæder and þu min goddohtor, and ic eallum gearige,
þe on þe gelefað.
 298. Eadig eart þu, halig fæmna Sancta Margareta, forþon
þe þu þine hande and þinne hige clæne gehylde and for minre lufu
mycel geþrowodest.
 300. And embe lytle fece, næs hit lang to þan, eac hit sona
gewearð þurh þære fæmne þrowunge, þæt þær to gode
gebugan fif þusend manna.
 303. Þa wearð se gerefa swiðe eorra and he het ealle ofslean,
þa þe on gode gelefdon.
 304. And se gerefa cwæð to his þeowum Malcum se ilca
dernunga gode geþenode: Gedrah þu þin swurd, cwæð se gerefa, and
þa fæmne þu ofsleah.
 306. And þa godes wiðerwinnan þa fæmnan genamon, ut of
þære byrig ungerædelice hi togoden, and þa hi þær becomon,
þær me hio slean scolde, and þa leasan witan to Malcum spræcan and
cwæðon: Drah hraþa þin swurd and þa fæmna þu ofsleah.
 310. And hire þa to leat Malcus swa dreohlice and hire georne
bæd and þus cwæð: Gemune þu me earminge on þinum gebedum.
 312. And seo eadige fæmne him to cwæð: Ic wille þe fore
biddan.
 313. And hio hio to eorþan gestrehte and þus cwæð: Drihten
god ælmihtig, þu þe heofones gescope and eorþe and eall þæt men
bi libbað, geher þu mine bene, þæt ælc þære manna synne sy
forgiofene, þe mine þrowunge rædeð, and ælcum þære mannu, þe
hi for godes lufu geheran willæð.
 317. And get ic þe, leofa drihten, biddan wille, þæt þu
ælc þæra manna, þe on minum naman cirice arære, and þan þe me
mid heora lihte gesecan willað and mid oðrum ælmessan and þam þe
mine þrowunge gewritað oððe mid heora figa gebicgað, þæt innan
heora husum nan unhal cild sy geboren, ne crypol, ne dumb, ne deaf, ne blind,
ne ungewittes.
 322. Ac forgif þu, leofa drihten, ealle heora synna for þinra
þære mycele ara and for þinum godcundum wuldre and for þinre þære
mycelen mildheortnesse.
 326. And hio hi eft niðer gestrehte and heore hleor wið
þæra eorþan gelegde and þa ealle, þe hire ymbstodan, feollan heom on
cneowgebedum.
 328. And þa ure drihten him self com of heofonum to eorþan
astigan and hire sona to cwæð: Ic þe geofa and behate, swa hwæt swa
þu bidst and gebeden hæfst, eal hit is þe getyðed.
 331. And eft cwæð ure drihten: ælc þæra þe on
þinre lufa me to gebiddað and ælmessan bringað oððe mid leohte
secað oððe þine þrowunge rædað oððe write oððe mid his
fige gebycge oððe inne his huse hæbbe, ne sceal nan yfel næfre on him
becuman.
 334. And ælc þære þe his synne forgifennesse habban wille
on þinre lufan, eall hit sio forgifen.
 336. Eadig eart þu, Margareta, and ealle þa þurh þe on me
gelefdon and gelefan willað.
 338. And þa seo eadiga Margareta up aras of hire gebedum feagre
gefrefred and cwæð to eallum þam þe hire ymbstodan: Geherað me, mine
gebroðra and swustra, ealda and geunga, ealle gemænelice.
 341. Ic eow bidde, þæt ge gelefan on drihten god ælmihtigne
and on his sunu and on his halgan gaste.
 342. And ic eow bidde, þæt ge me on eowrum bedum gemunnen,
forþan ic eam swiðe synfull.
 344. Þa þa hi hire gebedu gefylled hæfde, þa cleopode hi
swiðe hlude þone þe hi slean sceolde and cwæð: Malche, nim nu þin
swurd and do þæt þe gehaten is, for nu is min time gecuman.
 347. Malcus hire to cwæð: Nylle ic þe ofslean, forþon ic
geseo, þæt Crist is mid þe, and ic geherde, hu he spræc to þe and
cwæð, þæt þu his fæmne wære.
 349. And seo fæmne him to cwæð: Gif þu nylt me ofslean,
nafa þu nan hlot mid me on heofene rice.
 350. And he þa Malcus to hire fotum gefyll and þus cwæð:
Ic þe bidde, leofa eadige fæmne, þæt þu gebidde for me and forgif
þu me þas wite, for min drihten hit wat, þæt ic hit unwillende do,
þæt ic æfre þas dæda gefremme.
 354. And þa seo fæmne hi to gode gebæd and þus cwæð:
Drihten leof, forgif þu him ealle þa synne, þe he gefremeð hæfð.
 356. And he þa Malcus his swurd adroh and þæra eadigra
fæmne þæt heafod of asloh.
 357. And seo eadiga fæmne Margareta hire sawle gode agef, and
Malcus on hire swiðran uppan his swurda feol, and his sawle godes ængles
underfeongan and þurh þæra eadigra fæmne bene gode betæhton.
 361. Ða hit geherdon ealle þa untruman, þe wæron þær
on lande, ealle hi hire lic gesohton and heora hæle þer gefetton.
 363. Sume hi wæron blinde and deafa and sume crypeles and sume
dumbe and sume ungewitfulle.
 364. Ealle hi heora hæle æt þære halgan gæmnan
onfenge, and mycel mancyn, ealle þa þe unhale wære, þære fæmnen
lic gesohton, ealle hi hale and gesunde on heora wege ham gewænton.
 367. And ures drihtnes ænglæs þider comon and þa sawla
underfengon and heo on heofene rice gebrohton.
 368. And nu hi is mid gode and mid eallum his halgum, and þær
hi wunað nu and æfre wunian sceal in ealra worulda woruld a buton
ænde.
 370. Amen.

END_TEXT
START_TEXT

LS 15 (MargaretKer)
B3.3.15.
Saint Margaret: Ker 1957, 228.



 1. Æfter æriste ures drihtenes Hælendes Cristes and his
wuldorfæstan upastigenesse on heofonas to þam ælmihtigan Gode.
 2. On his nama andetnysse maniga martyros wæron þrowiende, and
his apostoli geliffæsste.
 2. Nu ge gebroðra mine, ge gehyrdon be þære eadigan
Margaretan þrowunge, hu heo ofer swiðe ealra deofla mægen gelyfað on
hi and on God ælmihtine.
 4. And doþ gemynd þare halgan fæmnan Sancta Margaretan and
Sancta Marian, and on heora ðanc ælmessan syllað, þæt hi eow onfon
on gesihðe Hælendes Cristes.
 6. Him is lof and wuldor and weorþmynt, and a he lyfaþ mid
englum, and mid heahfæderum, and mid witegum, and mid apostolum, and mid
haligum fæmnum, in ealra worulda woruld a buton ende, Amen.

END_TEXT
START_TEXT

LS 16 (MargaretHerbst)
B3.3.16.
Saint Margaret: Herbst 1975, 62-82.



 1. Æfter þære ðrowunge & þære æriste &
þære wuldorfæstan upastignesse ures drihtnes, hælendes cristes, to
god, fæder ealmihtigum, swiþe þa wæron maniga martyres þrowiende
& þurh þa þrowunge to ece reste becoman mid þære halgan Teclan
ð Susannan; & swiþe manega eac þurh deofles lare beswicanne
wæran, þæt hi beeode dumbe & deafe deofolgeld, mannes handgeweorc,
þe naþor ne heom ne him sylfum to nanre freme beon ne mihton.
 9. Ic þa, þeoþimus, þurh godes gyfe hwæthwugo on bocum
geleornode & geornfullice smeade & sohte ymb Cristes geleafan & ne
fand ic næfre on bocum þæt ænig man mihte to ece reste becuman,
butan he on þa halgan þrynnysse hriht gelifde, þæt is fæder &
sunu & se halga gast, & þæt se sunu onfeng mennisc hiw &
geþrowade deað for eall mankin swa swa hit herbufan cwyþ.
 15. Blinde he onlihte, deafum gesealde hernysse & deadum he
awæhte to life, & ealle þa þe on hine trywlice gelæfþ he
gehærþ.
 17. Ic þa, ðeotimus, wilnode georne to witanne hu se eadega
Margareta wæs wiþ þone deofol gefæht & hine oferswiþde &
þone ece wuldorbeh æt gode onfengc.
 20. Geheraþ nu ealle & ongytaþ hu se eadega Margareta
geþrowade for godes naman & þurh þæt geswenc to ece reste becom
mid þære halgan Teclan & Susannan.
 24. Se eadiga Margareta wæs Ðeodosius dohtor; se wæs
þære hæþenre hehfæder.
 25. Deofolgeld he wurþode & fædde his dohter; se wæs
mid halgum gaste gefylled & þurh fulwiht heo wæs geedniwod.
 27. Heo wæs geseald hire fostormoder to fædenne, nih
Antiochia, ðære ceastre.
 29. & syþþan hire agen modor forþgefaren wæs, of
þisan life se fostormodor hie miccle swyþor lufode þonne heo ær
dyde.
 31. Heo wæs hire fæder swiþe laþ & gode swyþe
leof.
 31. & mid þy þe heo wæs fiftyne wintra eald, heo
lustfullode on hire fostormoder huse to beonne.
 33. Heo gehyrde martyra geflitu, forþon þe mænig blod wæs
agoten on þam tidum on eorþan for ures dryhtnes naman, hælendes
Cristes.
 35. & heo wæs mid halgan gaste gefyld & hyre
mægþhad gode oðfæste.
 37. Sume dæge, þa mid þy þe heo geheold hyre fostormodor
scæp mid oþrum fæmnum, hire heafodgemacum, ða ferde Olibrius, se
gerefa, fram Asia to Antiochia, þære ceastre.
 40. Þa geseh he þa eadegan Margaretan be þam wege sittan
& hræddlice he hire þa gyrnde & cwæþ to his þegnum,
gongaþ ge ofostlice & geneomaþ þa fæmnan & axsiaþ hig gif
heo biþ freo þæt ic hire onfo me to wife; & gif heo þeow biþ, ic
sylle feoh for hire & heo byþ me for cyfese & hyre biþ weol on
minum huse.
 46. Þa cempan þa eodan & hie genoman.
 46. Se eadega Margareta þa ongan Criste clypian & þus
cwæþ: Gemildsa me, dryhten, & ne læt þu mine sawle mid arleasum
forwyrþan; ac gedo me blissian & þe symble herian, & ne læt þu
næfre minne sawle ne min lichoma wyrþan besmitan; ac gesend me to minum
swiþran healfe & to þære winstran sibbe englas to ontynenne mine
sefan & to andswariende mid bylde þyssum arleasum & þissum unrihtum
cwylleras/.
 54. Ic beo nu, drihten, swa swa nytenu onmiddan felde & swa
swa spærwe on nette & swa swa fisc on hoce.
 56. Gefylst my me, min drihten, & geheald me & ne
forlæt me on arleasra manna handa.
 59. Ða cempan þa coman to þam gerefan & cwædon,
hlaford, ne miht þu hire onfon, forþon to gode heo hig gebiddaþ, se þe
wæs ahangan fram Iudeum.
 61. Olibrius, se gerefa, hire gehet to him gelædon & hire
to cwæþ, of hwylcum cynne eart þu, sægæ me, bist þu frig
oðð þeow?
 64. Se eadega Margareta him to cwæþ, ic eom frig.
 65. Se gerefa hire to cwæþ, hwylces geleafan eart þu,
oþþe ic eom geciged.
 66. Se gerefa hire to cwæþ, hwylcne god begæst þu?
 67. Se halga Margareta him to cwæþ, ic gebidde me on
ealmihtigne god & on his sunu, hælend Crist, se þe minne mægþhad
unbesmiten geheold oþ þysne andweardan dæg.
 71. Se gerefa hire to cwæþ, clypest þu on þone Crist þe
mine, fæderas ahengon?
 72. Se halga Margareta hine to cwæþ, þine fæderas Crist
ahengon & þy hi ealle forwurdon.
 74. Ac he þurhwunaþ on ecnysse & his rice is a butan ende.
 75. Se gerefa wæs þa swiþe yrre & het þa halgan
Margaretan on karcerne betynan oþþæt he geþohte hu he hire
mægþhad forswilde.
 78. Se gerefa hire to cwæþ, gif þu ne gebiddest þe on
minne god, min swurd sceal fandian þines lichaman & ealle þine ban ic
tobrysige.
 80. Gif þu me gehyrest & on minne god gelæfst, ætforan
eallum þissum folce ic þe to cweþe þæt ic þe onfo me to wife,
& þe byþ swa wel swa me is.
 83. Margareta him to cwæþ, forþon ic sylle minne lichoman in
tintrego þæt min sawle mid soþfæstum sawlum geresteþ.
 86. Se gerefa hire het þa ahon & mid smalum gyrdum swingan
swiðe.
 87. Se halga Margareta besæh up to heofonum & cwæþ,
on þe, drihten, ic gelæfæ þæt ic ne si gescend.
 89. Loce on me & gemiltsa me of arleasra honda & of honda
þysses cwylleræs, þy læs min heorte her on ege sy.
 91. Send me hælo þæt syn on leohte mine witu & þæt
min sar me me cyme to gefean.
 92. & mid þy þe heo þus hig gebæd, þa cwelleras
swungon hire merwen lichaman þæt se blod fleow on eorþan swa swa
wæter deþ of þam clænestan wyllspringe.
 96. Se gerefa hire to cwæþ, eala, Margareta, gelæf on me
& þe byþ wel ofer oþre wif.
 97. & ealle þa fæmnan þe þær stoden weopen
bitterlice for þæm blode & cwædon, eala, Margareta, soþlice we
sariaþ ealle, mid þe forþon þe we geseoþ þe hnacode & þinne
lichaman beon cwylmiend.
 100. Þes gerefa is swiþe hatheortman & he þe wille
forspillan/ & þin gemynd of eorðan adiligian.
 102. Gelæf on hine & þu leofast.
 103. Se halga Margareta him to cwæþ, eala, ge yfelan
þehteras, gangaþ ge wif to eowrum husum & ge weras to eowrum weorcum.
 105. God me is fultumiende.
 105. Forþon nelle ic eow geheran, ne ic næfre me ne gebidde on
eowerne god, se þe is dumb & deaf.
 107. Ac geleafaþ on minne god, se þe is strang on mægenne,
& hrædlice he gehyraþ þa þe on hine gelæfaþ.
 109. & heo cwæþ þa to þam gerefan, eala, þu
ungeþunggena hund & þu ungefylledlican dracan, mannes ofen,
minnes god me is fultumiend, & þeah þu min lichaman geweald hæbbe,
Crist genereþ mine sawle of þinre þare egeslican honda.
 114. Se halga Margareta besæh up to heofonum & cwæð,
gestrangie me, lifes gast, þæt min gebed þurh heofonum gefare &
þæt hit astige ætforan þinre gesihþe.
 116. & gesend me þinne þone halgan gast fram heofonum, sy
me/ cyme me to fultume þæt ic gehealde ungewæmedne minne mægþhad
& þæt ic geseo minne wiþerweardan se þe wiþ me gefihtaþ, synna
to ansyna.
 120. & þæt sy bysen & blæd a eallum fæmnum þe
on þe geleuat, forþon þin nama is gebletsod on weorulde.
 123. Þa cæmpan þa eodan & cwylmdon hire lichaman.
 123. Ða bewrah se arleasa gerefa his ansyna mid his hacelan,
forþon þe he ne mihte on hire locian for þæm blode, & cwæþ to
þære fæmnan, forhwon ne gehyrsumast þu minan worde, ne þu ne
þines sylfes ne eart mildsigende.
 127. Efne, þin lichoma is gecwilmed for minum þam egeslican
dome.
 128. Geþafa me & gebide þe on minne god, þy læs þu
deaþe swiltast.
 130. Gif þu me ne gehyrast, min sweord sceal wealdan þines
lichoman.
 131. Gif þu me ne gehyræst, ætforan eallum þissum folce
ic þe to cweþe þæt ic þe onfo me to wife.
 133. Se halga Margareta him to cwæþ, eala, þu unsnotra,
forþon ic sylle minne lichaman in tintrego þæt min sawul sy
gesygefæst on heofonum.
 136. Se gerefa hio het on þystrum carcerne betynan.
 137. & mid þam þe heo eode þær in, hio gebletsode
ealle hyre lichaman mid Cristes rode tacne & ongan hire handan blesian
& þus cweþan: Loce on me & gemildsa me, drihten, forþon þe ic
ane beo, her inne & ange mine fæder, he me forlet.
 141. Ne forlæt þu me, min drihten, ac gemiltsa me, forþon
þe ic ongete þæt þu eart dema cwucra & deadra.
 143. Dem nu betwux me & þyssum deoflum.
 144. Efne, ic sarige on minum witum.
 144. Ne yrsa þu wiþ me, min drihten, forþon þe þu wast
þæt ic sylle mine sawle for þe.
 146. Þu eart gebletsod on weorlde.
 147. Ic þa, þeotimus, hi wæs fædende mid hlafe & mid
wætre, & ic gesæh þurh an ehþyrl eal hire geflit þe heo
hæfde wið ða arleasan deofle, & ic awrat ealle hire gebedu.
 150. Þa eode ut of þæs karcernnes hwomme swiþe egeslic
draca missenlices hiwes.
 151. His loccas & his beard wæron gylden geþuhte & his
teþ wæron swilc swa asniden isen & his egan scinan swa searagym &
ut æt his nosu eode micel smoca & his tungla eþode & micel
fulnesse he dyde on þæm karcernne; & he hig þa up arærde & he
hwystlode stranglicere stemne.
 156. Ða wæs geworden micel leoht on þæm þystran
karcerne of ðæm fyre þe ut eode of þæs dracan muþe.
 158. Se halgæ fæmnæ wæs þa geworden swiþe fyrht
& gebigde hire cneowu on eorþan & aþenoda hire honda on gebede
& þus cwæþ: God ælmihti, adwysc þæs miclan dracan mægen
& gemildsa me þearfendra & earfoþra & ne læt ðu me
næfre forwyrðan, ac gescyld me wiþ þysne wilddeore.
 164. & mid þy þe heo þus gebæd hig to Christe, se
draca sette his muþ ofer þære halgan fæmnan heafod & hi
forswealh.
 165. Ac Cristes rode tacen, þe se halga Margareta worhte innan
þæs/ dracan innoþe, se hine toslat on twæigen dælas, & se
halgæ famna eode ut of þæs dracan innoþe, ungewæmmed.
 169. & on þære ilcan tide gesæh heo on hire wynstran
healfe ænne deofol sittende swilcne anne sweartne man & his honda to his
cneowum gebundenne.
 171. & mid þy þe heo þinne gesæh, heo gebæd hi to
drihtene & þus cwæþ: Ic þe herige & wuldrige, þu undeadlica
kyning Christ; þu eart geleafan trymnysse & ælcra snotra fruma &
æghwylcre strengþo staþol.
 175. Nu ic geseo minne geleafan blowiende & mine sawle anlyht
& þysne dracan acwealdne licgan.
 176. Þancas ic þe secge, þu halga & þu undeadlica god;
þu eart ealra hælende hælend; se þin nama gebletsod on weorulde.
 179. & mid þy þe heo þus gebæd hi, se deofol up aras
& genam þar halgan fæmnan hond & cwæþ, þæt genihtsumaþ
þæt þu dydest.
 181. Gewit fram me, forþon þe ic geseo þe on forhæfdnesse
þurhwunian.
 182. Ic sende to þe Hrufum, minne broþur, on dracan gelicnesse,
to þam þæt he þe forswulge & þinne mægþhad & þinne
wlite forlure & þin gemynd of eorþan adylgian.
 185. Þu hine þonne mid Cristes rode tacne acwealdest & nu
þu wilt me acwyllan.
 186. Ac ic bidde þe for þinne mægþhad þæt þu me ne
geswinge.
 188. Se halga Margareta gegrap þane deofol þa be þæm
locce & hine on eorþan awearp & his swyþran ege ut astang &
ealle his ban heo tobrysde & sette hire swiþran fott ofer his swyran
& him to cwæþ, gewit fram minum mægþhade, Crist me is fultumiend,
forþon his nama is scinende on weorulde.
 194. & mid þy þe heo þus cwæþ, þær scan
swiþe micel leoht on þæm þystran quarterne & Cristes rode wæs
gesewen fram eorþan up oþ heofen & an hwit culfre stod ofer þære
rode & heo spræc & þus cwæþ: Secg me, Margareta, þu þe
þurh mægþhad gyrndest þære eacan rice, & forþon hit biþ
þe geseald mid Abraham & mid Isaac & Iacob.
 200. Eadig eart þu þe þone feond oferswiþdest.
 201. Se halga Margareta þa cwæþ, wuldor þe sy, Crist,
þu þe ane dest mænig wuldor.
 202. Ic þe wuldrige & herige, forþon þu eart halig &
micel on eallum þingum, þu þe gemedomast gecyþ þonne þinre þeowen
þæt þu eart ane hiht ealra lifiendra on þe.
 206. Se culfra þa wæs eft sprecende & cwæþ,
Margareta, axia þone þe þu hæfst under þinum fotum be his dædum
& he cyþ þe ealle his weorc, & mid þy þe þu hine hæfst
oferswiþd, þu cymst to me.
 209. Se halga Margareta þa cwæþ to þæm deofle, Hwæt
is þin nama, þe unclæne gast?
 211. Se deofol hire to cwæþ, þu Cristes þeowwe, ahefe
þinne fot of minan swiran þæt ic mine ban lithwan gereste & ic þe
sægce ealle mine dæda.
 213. Se halga fæmne þa ahof hire fot of his swiran.
 214. Þæt and se deofol þa cwæþan ongan: Manigne
soþfæstna man ic genam & ic gefæht wiþ him & ne mihte me nan
oferswiþan.
 216. Ac þu min ege ut astunge & ealle mine ban tobrisdest
& mine broþor acwealdest.
 217. Nu ic geseo Crist wunian on þe & þu dest ealle
soþfæsnesse weorc.
 219. Ic hig ableonde fram geleafan & ic hi gedyde ofergeotan
þa heofenlican gesælþe.
 220. & mid þy þe hy on slæpe wæron, ic com ofer hi
& þa þe ic ne mihte of þæm bedde adon ic hi dyde on þæm
sylfan slæpe singian.
 222. Nu þonne, fram anre gingre fæmnan ic eam oferswiþd.
 223. Hwæt do ic nu, forþon þe ealle mine wæpne synt
tobrecenne.
 224. & me ealra swiþost gedræfþ þæt þin fæder
& þin modor mine wæron & þu ane wiþ me & wið eall hire
cneorise/.
 227. Cristes gefylgendum, þurh þone deofla magen eall to nahte
gebiþ.
 228. Se halga fæmne him to cwæþ, saga me nu þin cynn
& hwa þe gecende.
 229. Se deofol hire to cwæþ, sæcg me, Margareta, hwanon is
þin lif & þin lichama, & hwanon is þin sawul & þin geleafa,
oþþe hu wæs Crist wuniend on þe; saga me þis, þonne secge ic þe
ealle mine dæde.
 233. Se halga fæmne him answarode & cwæþ, Nys me
alifed þæt ic þe to secgæ, forþon þu ne eart ne wyrþe mine
stefne to gehyrenne.
 235. Godes bebodu ic wille gehyran & þæt gecyþan, &
þu, deofol, adumbe nu, forþon þe ic nelle nan word ma of þinum muþe
gehyran.
 237. & hrædlice se eorþe forswalg þone wælhreowan
deofol grimlice.
 239. Ða, on oþran dæge, het se gerefa þa halgan fæmnan
to him gelædan.
 240. & mid þy þe heo wæs ut agangende, heo gebletsode
eall hira lichoma mid Cristes rode tacene.
 242. Se gerefa hire to cwæþ, eala, Margareta, gelæf on me
& gebid þe to minum gode.
 243. Se halga Margareta him to cwæþ, soþlice, þe
gedafenaþ on mine god to gebiddanne.
 245. Se gerefa wearþ þa swyþe yrre & het hi up ahon &
mid kandelum byrnan.
 246. & hio dydan þa nyxtan swa heom beboden wæs.
 247. Se halga Margareta þa cigde & cwæþ, nelle ic
næfre me gebiddan on eowerne god, se þe is dumb & deaf.
 249. Ne magon ge oferswyþan clæne fæmnan.
 249. Crist sylf ge gebletsode minne lichaman & minre sawule he
sylleþ wuldres beh.
 252. Se arleasa gerefa het þider bringan mycel leaden fæt
& het hit mid wætere afyllan & dyde hit ælan swyþe hat &
het bindan fet & honda þære halgan fæmnan & þæron don.
 255. Ða cwylras dyden þa swa heom beboden wæs.
 255. Se eadega Margareta locade on heofonum & cwæþ,
ðrihten, god ealmihtig, þu þe eardest on heofonum geunne me þæt
þis wæter sy me to hælo & to lihtnesse & to fulwihtes
bæþe, unaspringende, þæt hit me aþwea to þam eacan life, &
awyrp me from ealle mine synne & gehæl me on þinum wuldre, forþon
þe þu eart gebletsod on weorulde.
 263. & mid þy þe þæt gebed wæs gefyld, swa wearþ
þær micel eorþhrærnesse geworden.
 264. & on þære ylcan tid com an culfre of heofonum
hæbbende beh on muþe & raþe wæron alysde fet & honda
þære halgan fæmnan & heo eode up of þæm wætere, god
herigende & wuldrigende, & þus cwæþ: wuldor ic þe secge,
drihten god, hælend Crist, forþon þe þu me onlihtest & wuldradest,
& þu me wære mildsiend, þinre þeowene; þu eart a gebletsod on
weorlde.
 271. & mid þy þe heo cwæþ, amen.
 272. Stefn wæs þa geworden of heofonum þus cweþende: Cum,
Margareta, to heofonum; eadig þu eart, þu þe mægþhad gyrndest; for
þon þingum þu eart eadig on ecnesse.
 275. & on þære ilcan tid gelæfde þæs folces xv
þusenda manna, butan wifan & cildan.
 277. Olibrius, se gerefa, het acwyllan ealle þa þæ on Crist
gelæfdon.
 278. & hi wæron acwealde on Limes feolda, butan Ærmeniga,
þære ceastre.
 279. & æfter heom he het acwyllan þa eadegan Margaretan
& mid swurde ofslean.
 281. Ða cwyllras læddon hi þa butan þara ceastre
wealþas, & þa an of heom cwæþ, his nama wæs Malchus gehaten,
aþene þinne sweora nu & onfoh min swurd & gemildsa me, forþon
þe ic her geseo Crist standand mid his englum mid þe.
 285. Margareta þa cwæþ, ic bidde þe, broþor, gif þu
her Crist geseost, are me, oþþæt ic me gebidde to him & minna gast
him oþfæste.
 287. Se cwyllere hyre to cwæþ, bide swa hwæt swa þu
wille.
 289. Se eadega Margareta þa ongan biddan & þus cweþan:
God, þu þe heofenan mid honda gemettest & eorþan on þinre fyst
betyndest geher mine bena þæt swa hwilc man swa writeþ mine þrowunga
oþþe hi geheraþ rædan, of þære tide syn adylgade heora synna,
oþþe gif hwilc man leoht deþ on minum cirican of his geswinge, be swa
hwylcan gylte swa he bidde forgifenesse, ne si him se synna geteold; ic bidde
þe, drihten, þæt gif hwilc mon si gemetod on þinum þam egeslican
dome & he si gemindig minum naman & þines, gefreolsa hine, drihten,
of tintregan; get ic þe bidde, drihten, þæt se þe rærdeþ boc
mines martirhades oþþe on his huse hæbbe, sy his synna eal alætnesse,
forþon þe we syndon flæsc & blod, æfre singiende & næfre
ablinnende.
 302. Get ic þe bidde drihten þæt se þe cyrcan timbrige on
minum naman & þær awrite mine þrowunge oþþe of his gewinne
gebicge, send on hine, drihten, þono halgan gast; & þær boc sy mines
martyrhades, ne sy þær geboren blind cild ne healt ne dumb ne deaf ne fram
unclænum gaste geswenct; ac sy þær sib & lufu &
soþfæstnesse gast; & se þe þær biddeþ his synna forgifnesse;
gecyðe him, drihten his bene.
 310. Ða wæs stefn geworden of heofonum mid þunre & an
culfre com berende rode & cwæþ, aris, Margareta, eadig wæs se
innoþ se þe þe gebær, forþon þe þu gemyndest ealle þingc on
þinum gebed.
 313. Ðurh engla mægen ic þe swerige þæt swa hwæt swa
þu bæde, eall hit biþ gehered ætforan godes gesyhþe, & swa
hwæt swa þu wære gemyndig, þæt forgifeþ þe god.
 316. God gesættet on þinum cyrcan þreo hund engla, to
þon þæt hi onfoþ ælc þæra manna bena þe to drihtene clypaþ
on þinum naman þæt hira synna synt adylgode.
 319. Nu get ic cyþe þe þæt englas cumaþ ongean þe
& neamaþ þin heafod & lædaþ hit on neorxnawange.
 321. & þin lichama biþ wurþful mid mannum, þæt swa
hwa swa ahrineþ þine reliquias, of þære tide fram swa hwylcre
untrumnesse swa he hæfþ he biþ gehæld.
 324. & þær þine reliquias beoþ oþþe boc þines
martirhades, ne genealæcþ þær naþor ne yfel ne se unclæne gast.
 326. Ac þær biþ sib & lufu & soþfæstnesse &
blis & gefean, & nænig on neorxnawonge mare gemetod mid meder ealra
gescippendes nimþe þreo fæmnan.
 328. & se þe þinne naman of ealra heortan cigeþ mid
tearum agotennesse, he biþ gefreolsad fram eallum his synnum.
 330. Eadig þu eart & þa þe þurh þe gelæfað &
se/ stow þær þu to gefundest.
 332. Cum hrædlice to þære stowe þe þe is gegearwod
& site on þa swiþran healfe þære eadegan Teclan & Susannan.
 334. Eadig þu eart, þu þe mægþhad geheolde.
 334. Cum nu, godes lamb, ic þin anbide.
 336. Se halga Margareta besæh on hire embhwyrft & to
cwæþ, ic eow bidde þurh naman ures drihtnes, hælendes Cristes,
þæt ne eow sylle eowra synna forgyfnesse & eow gedon rixian on heofona
rice.
 339. Þancas ic þe secge þu þe me gewuldradest &
gewurþadest on soþfæstra noman.
 340. Ic hine herige & bletsige se þe rixaþ on worulde.
 342. & æfter þam gebede heo hi up arærde &
cwæþ to þam cwyllere, broþor, genim nu þin swurd & ofsleh me,
forþon þe nu get ic oferswyþde þysne middangeard.
 345. He cwæþ ne gedeme ic þæt.
 345. Ne ic ne acwylle halig godedes fæmne.
 346. God wæs sprecende beforan me to þe, ne eam ic gedyrstig
þæt to donne.
 347. Se halga Margareta cwæþ to him, gif þu þæt ne
dest, næfst þu dæl mid me on neorxnawonge.
 349. Se cwylra þa mid gefyrhto genam his swurd & hire heafod
of asloh & gehwyfde hine sylfne & cwæþ, drihten, ne sette þu me
þis on synnæ, & hine sylfne mid his swurde ofstang & gefeol to
þære eadegan fæmnan swyþran healfe.
 354. Þider coman þa þusend engla ofer þære halgan
Margaretan lichaman & gebletsodon hine.
 355. Ða coman twelf englas & genaman hire heafod on hira
fædmum & hi sungon & cwædon, ðu halga, þu halga, þu halga,
drihten god, weoroda wuldorkynincg, fulle syndon heofonas & eorþan
þines wuldres.
 359. & þus singende hi hit gesætton on neorxnawonge.
 360. & ealle þa þe wonnhale wæron, healtte & blinde,
dumbe & deafe, & hi on gehrinon þære halgan fæmnan lichaman,
ealle hi wurdon gehælde.
 363. & ængla stefn wæs gehered ofer hire lichaman þus
cweþende: Eadig eart þu & þa þe þurh þe gelæfeþ, forþon
þe þu gewunne reste a oþ ende mid halgum fæmnum; & ne beo þu
sorhfull be þinum halgan lichaman, forþon þe he is forlætan on
eorþan to þon þæt swa hwylc mann swa hrineþ þine reliquias
oþþe þine ban, on þære tide syn adilgade heora synna & hira nama
writan on lifes bocum.
 371. Ic, þeotimus, genam þa reliquias þære halgan
fæmnan & ic hi gesætte on niwe scrine þe ic sylf ær of stane
geworhte & mid swotum wyrtum gesweotte.
 373. & ic hio geheold on sumes godes wifes huse, hire nama
wæs Sincletica.
 375. Ic, þeotimus, wæs þe hire geþenode mid hlafe &
mid wætere & ic gesæh eall hire geflit þe heo hæfde wiþ þon
arleasan deoflum.
 377. & hire gebed ic awrat & ic hit gesende to eallum
Cristenum mannum.
 378. & se halga Margareta gefylde hire þrowung on Iulius
monþe, on þone þreo & twentegþan dæge.
 380. Ealle þa þe þis gehyraþ on heortan beon bliðe
& þa þe drihten Crist biddaþ & on hine gelifaþ & gemundyt
þære halgan Margaretan þæt hi mid hira benum us oþfæste on
gesihþe hælendes Cristes, þam sy wuldor & lof & wurðmynt &
þrym & anweald & micelnys on ealra worulda woruld, soþlice a butan
ænigum ende.
 386. Amen.
