LS 17.1 (MartinMor)
B3.3.17.2.
Saint Martin: Morris 1874-80, 211-27.



 1. TO SANCTE MARTINES MæSSAN.
 1. Men ða leofestan, we magan hwylcum hwega wordum secggean be
ðære arwyrðan gebyrdo & be ðon halgan life & forðfore
þæs eadigan weres Sancte Martines, ðe we nu on anweardnesse his tid
weorðiað.
 4. Wæs ðæt Gode swiðe gecoren man on his dædum.
 5. He wæs on Pannania þære mægðe ærest on woruld
cumen, in Arrea ðæm tune.
 6. Wæs he hweðre in Italia afeded in Ticinan þære byrig.
 7. Wæs he for worlde swiþe æþelra gebyrda & godra,
wæron his yldran hweðre fæder & modor, buta hæðne.
 9. Wæs his fæder ærest cyninges þegn, & ða
ætnehstan geðeah þæt he wæs cininges þegna aldorman.
 11. Þa sceolde Sanctus Martinus nede beon on his geogoðhade on
ðære geferædenne cininges ðegna, ærest on Constantines dagum,
& ða eft on Iulius þæs caseres.
 13. Næs na þæt he his willan on ðæm woruldfolgaðe
wære; ah he sona on his geogoðe Godes ðeowdom miccle swiðor lufode
þonne þa idlan þreas þisse worlde.
 16. Þa he wæs tyn wintre, & hine hys yldran to
woruldfolgaðe tyhton ond lærdan, ða fleah he to Godes ciricean, &
bæd þæt hine mon gecristnode, þæt se æresta dæl his onginnes
& lifes wære to geleafan & to fulwihte gecyrred.
 20. & he þa sona wæs wuldorlice mid eallum his life ymb
Godes þeowdom abisgod.
 21. Ða he wæs fiftene wintre, þa nyddon hine hys yldran
toðæm þæt he sceolde woroldlicum wæpnum onfon, & on cininges
ðegna geferrædenne beon.
 23. Þa wæs feower gear ær his fulwihte þæt he
woroldwæpno wæg, & he hine hweðre wið eallum þæm healicum
wæpnum geheold, þaðe woruldmen fremmað on menniscum ðingum.
 26. Hæfde he miccle lufan & ealle wærnesse to ælcum
men, & he wæs swiðe geþyldig, & eaðmod, & gemetfæst on
eallum his life.
 28. & ðeah þe he þa gyt on læwedum hade beon sceolde,
hweðre he toðon wærnesse hæfde on eallum ðingum, þæt he efne
munuclife gyta swiþor lifde þonne þonne læwedes mannes.
 31. Wæs he for his arfæstum dædum eallum his geferum leof
& weorð & ondrysne, & hie hine ealle synderlice mid lufan
weorðodan.
 33. & ðeah he þa gyt nære fullice æfter oþerre
endebyrdnesse gefulwad, ah he wæs gecristnod, swa ic ær sægde,
hweðre he þæt geryne þære halgan fulwihte mid godum dædum heold
& fullade.
 36. He wolde þæm winnendum fultmian, & earme frefran,
& hingrigendum mete syllan, & nacode scrydan, & eal þæt he on
his folgaðe begeat, eal he þæt for Godes lufan sealde, buton ðone
dæghwamlican andleofan anne þe he nede big lifgean sceolde.
 41. Gemunde he þæt Drihten bebead on þæm godspelle, <foreign>de
crastino non cogitare</foreign>, þæt se Godes man ne sceolde be þan morgendæge
þencean, þylæs þæt wære þæt he þurh þæt ænig
þara goda forylde, þe he þonne þy dæge gedon mihte, & ða
weninge hweðer he eft þæs mergendæges gebidan moste.
 45. Magon we nu þara arfæstra dæda sume gehyran sæcgan
þe he þes eadiga wer, Sanctus Martinus, sona on his cnihthade gedyde;
þeah þe þara godra dæda ma wære þonne ænig man asecggan
mæge.
 49. Ðæt gelamp sume siðe þæt he ferde mid oþrum
cininges ðegnum on ða burg þe Ambinensus hatte; þæt wæs eac on
middum wintra.
 51. Wæs se winter eac þy geare toþæs grim þæt manig
man his feorh for cyle gesealde.
 52. Þa sæt þær sum þearfa æt ðæm burggeate,
sæt eac nacod, bæd him þa for Gode hrægles & ælmessan.
 54. Þa ferdan hie ealle forð be him & heora nænig him to
cerran nolde, ne him nænigre are gedon.
 55. Ða ongeat se Godes wer Sanctus Martinus þæt Drihten him
ðone þearfan geheold, þæt he him miltsian sceolde, ða þara
oðerra manna him nan arian ne wolde.
 58. Nyste þeah hweðre hwæt he him don sceolde, forðon þe
he naht elles buton his anfealdne gegyrelan, ah healf þæt he mare
hæfde eal he þæt ær beforan on onlic weorc ateah, & for Gode
gesealde.
 61. Geteah þeah his seax & genam his sciccels þe he him on
hæfde, tosnað þa hine ontwa, & healfne sealde þæm þearfan,
& mid healfum hine sylfne besweop.
 64. Ða wæron þær manige men þe þæt gesawon
þæt hie hine on þæm tældon & bismrodan, þæt he his swa
anfealdne gegyrelan tosniðan sceolde.
 66. Sume þonne eft þa ðe betran modes wæron, &
ænige lufe to Gode hæfdan, hie sylfe be þon oncuðon þæt hie swa
ne dydon, & wiston þæt hie mare hæfdon, þæt hie æghweþer
ge þæm þearfan hrægl syllan mihtan, ge hweþre him sylfum genog
hæfdon.
 70. Ða wæs sona on þære æfterfylgendan niht, þa he
se eadiga wer slep, þa geseah he Crist sylfne mid þy ilcan hrægle
gegyredne þe he ær þon þearfan sealde.
 73. Þa wæs him beboden geornlicor þæt he hine urne
Drihten ongeate, & þæt hrægl þe he ær þæm þearfan
sealde.
 75. <foreign>Mox angelorum circumstantium multitudinem</foreign>; ða geseah he
myccle mengeo engla emb hine Drihten sylfne mid swa cuðre stefne to ðæm
englum cweðendne, Martinus, nu ðu eart gecristnod ær þinum fulwihte,
mid þys hrægle þu me gegyredest.
 79. Wæs on þære dæde swiþe cuð þæt ure Drihten
is swiþe gemyndig þæs his cwides þe he sylfa ær gecwæð:
<foreign>Quamdiu fecisti</foreign>; Swa hwæt swa ge cwædon þæt ge hwelcum earmum men
to gode gedoð for minum naman efne þæt ge me sylfum doð.
 83. & he þa wolde þone cwide getrymman on þære
godcundan dæde, & he hine sylfne toðon geeaðmedde þæt he hine
on ðæs þearfan gegyrelan æteowde þæm eadigan were Sancte
Martine.
 86. <foreign>Quo uisu uir non in gloriam elatus est</foreign>; ða he þa se
eadiga wer Sanctus Martinus þa gesihþe geseah, þa ne wæs he hweþre
noht feor on oferhygd ahafen on mennisc wuldor; ah he Godes good on þære
his dæde ongeat.
 90. Ða he þa hæfde twæm læs þe twentig wintra, þa
gefullode hine mon on ðære ciricean endebyrdnesse; wæs he beforan ær
þa þreo gear gecristnod, swa ic ær sægde.
 92. Þa forlet he þone woroldfolgað, & ða gewat to
Sancte Hilarie þæm bisceope, þe on Pictauie þære byrig wæs
bisceop.
 94. Þæt wæs swiðe foremære man for Gode & his god
wæs swiðe gecyðed.
 95. & he þa þysne eadigan wer Sanctus Martinus
fulfremedlice on Godes æ & on Godes þeowdom getyde & gelærde;
toeacan þon þe hine God sylf innan manode.
 98. Wæs he swiðe geþungen on his ðeawum, &
staðolfæst on his wordum, & hluttor & clæne on hie life; &
he wæs arfæst & gemetfæst & mildheort on his dædum &
geornful, & be gewyrhtum ymb Drihtnes lare & on eallum godum for Gode
swiþe fulfremed.
 102. Þa gelamp æfter þon þæt þes eadiga wer Sanctus
Martinus sum mynster getimbrede, & he on ðæm manigra Godes þeowa
gastlic fæder gewearð.
 104. Þa gelamp sume siðe þæt þær com sum gecristnod
man to him, þæt he wolde mid his lare & mid his lifes bysene beon
ontimbred.
 107. Þa wæs he þær dagas wel manige; þa wearð he
untrum on feforadle.
 108. Þa gelamp on þa tid þæt Sanctus Martinus wæs on
sumre fore ealle þry dagas; ða he eft ham com, þa mette he ðane man
forðferedne þe þær ær untrum wæs, & hine efne swa færlice
deað fornam ðæt he ungefullad forðferde.
 111. Þa he þa Sanctus Martinus þæt geseah, þæt þa
oðre broðor ealle swa unrote ymb þæt lic utan stondan, þe weop he
& eode into him.
 114. & him wæs þæt swiþe myccle weorce þæt he
swa ungefulwad forðferan sceolde; getrywde þa hweðre mid ealle mode on
ælmihtiges Godes miht & on his mildheortnesse.
 116. & eode þa on þa cetan þær se lichoma inne wæs,
& heht ða oðre men ut gangan, & þa ða duru inbeleac æfter
him.
 118. & hine ða gebæd, & hine astreahte ofer leomu
þæs deadan mannes.
 119. Þa he þa lange hwile on þæm gebede wæs, þa
ongeat he þæt þær wæs godcundlic mægen ondweard, & he
þære mildheortnesse unsorh abad.
 122. Þa wæs ymb hwile, ða gefelde he þæt se deada man
his leomu ealle astyrede, & his eagan upahof & forðlocade.
 124. Þa he þa Sanctus Martinus þæt geseah, þa wæs he
swiþe gefeonde, & þa cleopode hlude mid mycelre stefne, &
ælmihtigum Gode þære gife þanc sægde.
 126. Ða þæt þa þa oðre broþra gehyrdon þe þær
ute wæron, ða eodan hie into him; þa gesawon hie wundorlice wyrd ðone
man lifgendne þone þe hie ær deadne forleton.
 129. & hine man þa sona gefulwade & he feala geara
æfterðon lifde.
 130. Wæs þis ðara wundra ærest þe þes eadiga wer
openlice beforan oþrum mannum geworhte; & þa æfter þisse dæde
his noma wæs a seoþþan weorð & mære geworden, & hine eal
þæt folc haligne & mihtigne ongeat & apostolicne on his dædum.
 134. Swylce eac eft gelamp oþer wundor þissum onlic; he ferde
sume siðe þes eadiga wer to sumes mannes tune, þe Lupicinus wæs
haten.
 136. Þa gehyrde he þær on tune mycelne heaf & wop, &
manige cleopodan mid mycelre stefne.
 138. Þa gestod he & ahsode hwæt seo cleopung wære; þa
sægde him mon þæt þær wære sum man earmlice deaþe aswolten
swa þæt he hine sylfne awyrde.
 140. Ða he þa Sanctus Martinus þæs mannes deað swa
earmlicne gehyrde, ða wæs him þæt sona swiþe sar & myccle
weorce; & þa eode he in þa cetan þær se lichoma inne læg
þæs deadan mannes, & heht þa oþre men ealle ut gangan & þa
duru betynan, & hine þa þær on gebed astreahte.
 145. Ða he þa hwile on ðæm gebede wæs, þa færinga
wearð se deada man cwic eft, & forðlocade, & teolode to arisenne.
 147. Ða genam Sanctus Martinus hine be his handa, & upheah
arærde, & hine lædde forð to þon cafortune þæs huses, &
hine eft þæm mannum halne & gesundne ageaf, þæm þe hine ær
deadne leton.
 150. Ðas wundor & manig oþer ælmihtig God þurh þysne
eadigan wer worhte, ær þon þe he æfre bisceop wære.
 152. Ah seoþþan he þon bisceophade onfeng in Turnan ðære
byrig, nis nænig man þæt þa wundor ealle asecggan mæge, þa ðe
God seoþþan þurh hine worhte.
 154. & ðeah he þa maran had hæfde, & eac for worlde
ricra beon sceolde, þonne he ær wære, þeh hweþre he hæfde þa
ilcan eaðmodnesse on his heortan, & þa ilcan forwyrnednesse on his
lichoman, æghweðer ge on mete, ge on hrægle, ge on æghwylcum
þinge, efne swa he ær hæfde.
 158. & he his bisceophad swa gedefelice for Gode geheold swa he
hweþre næfde þæt mægen & þa foresetenesse his munuchades
anforlet.
 161. <foreign>Omnes namque unanimiter cupiebant</foreign>; Ond ealle men forneah,
ða þe ðyses eadygan weres lif cuþon oþþe forehyrdon, ealle hie
þæt anmodlice wilnodan þæt hie his word gehyran moston, & his
larum fylgean, forðon þe hie sweotollice on him ongeaton Godes gife &
his blisse.
 165. Wæs he forðon swiþe mære geond middangeard, & he
manig templ & deofolgyld gebræc & gefylde, þær hæþene men
ær deoflum onguldon; & þonne þær he þæt deofolgeld gefylde,
þonne asette he þær Godes ciricean oþþe fullice mynster getimbrede.
 169. Ðæt gelamp sume siðe þæt he ongan bærnan sum
deofolgild, þe mid þæm hæðnum mannum swiðe weorð & mære
wæs.
 171. Þa stod ðær sum nytwyrðe hus bi þæm gilde þe
he þær bærnan ongan.
 172. Ða slog se wind þone leg on þæt oþer hus, &
ðuhte þæt hit eal forbyrnan sceolde.
 173. Þa he þa Sanctus Martinus þæt geseah, þa arn he
sona up on þæt hus, & ða gestod ongean þæm lege.
 175. Þa gelamp wundorlic wyrd þæt se leg ongan slean &
brecan ongean þone wind, & efne swa se wind swiþor slogon þone leg
swa bræc he swiþor ongean þæm winde, efne þæm gelicost swylce
ða gesceafta twa him betweonan gefeohtan sceoldan.
 179. & swa se leg wearð geþreatod þurh Sancte Martines
gebedu, þæt he nænigum oðrum ærne sceþþan ne mihte, buton
þæm deofolgelde anum þe he þær bærnan ongan.
 182. Swilce gelamp eft oþer wunder ðysum onlic.
 183. He com to sumum tune ðe Librassa wæs haten; ða wæs
þær gild þe þa hæþenan men swiðe weorðodan.
 184. Ða wolde he Sanctus Martinus ælce þinga ðæt gyld
abrecan & gefyllan.
 185. Ða wiðstodan him ða hæþenan men & hine mid
teonan aweg adrifon.
 187. Þa eode he ðær rihte big on sume stowe, & hine þa
gegyrede mid hærenum hrægle swiþe heardum & unwinsumum, &
fæste þry dagas, & ælmihtigne God bæd ðæt he þurh his
godcundan miht ðæt deofolgild gebræce & gefylde.
 190. Þa he hit for manna teonan gebrecan ne moste, þa comon
þær semninga twegen englas to him gesceldode & gesperode, & mid
heora geatwum gegyrede, efne swa hie to campe feran woldon.
 193. & cwædon þæt hie God sylf sende þæt hie
sceoldan þæt hæþene weorod geflyman, & Martine gefultmian,
þæt he þæt deofolgeld mihte gefyllan.
 196. Ða eodan hie eft to ðæm tune, & þæt gild
gebræcan & gefyldan eal oþ grund.
 197. & þa hæþenan men tolocodan, ah hie hweþre
wæron mid godcundum mægene toðæs swiðe gefyrhte, þæt heora
nænig him wiþstandan ne dorste.
 199. Ah hie ealle to Drihtnes geleafan gecirdon, & hie
cwædan to him ðæt se an wære soð God se þe Martinus hyrde, &
þæt heora hæþenan gild wæron ealle idelu & unnyt, &
þæt hie nawðer ne him sylfum helpan ne mihton, ne nanum ðara ðe to
him are wilnodan.
 204. Swylce eac gelamp sume siðe, ðær he sum gild bræc
þæt þær gearn mycel menigeo to him ðara hæþenra manna, &
ealle swiðe erre wæron.
 206. Ða wæs heora sum reðra & hatheortra ðonne þa
oþre; gebrægd ða his sweorde, mynte hine slean.
 207. Þa he þa Sanctus Martinus þæt geseah, þa dyde he
sona þæt hrægl of his sweoran, & leat forð to ðæm men ðe
hine slean mynte.
 209. Ða he þa se hæþena man upræhte mid þære
swiþran handa, & hine slean mynte, ða feol he færinga onbæcling,
& nahte his lichoman geweald; ac he wæs mid godcundum mægene
geþread; & he him þa þone eadigan wer forgifnesse bæd.
 213. Swylce wæs eft oþer wundor ðæm onlic.
 214. Þæt gelamp sume siþe þær he sum deofolgild bræc
& fylde, þæt þær gebrægd þara hæþenra manna sum his
seaxe; þa he hine þa stingan mynte, þa nyste he færinga hwær
þæt seax com þe he ær on handa hæfde.
 217. Gelomlic þæt þonne wæs þær he þa idlan gild
bræc, & him þa hæðnan men wiþerwearde wæron, þæt he
þurh his lara & þurh Drihtnes gife heora heortan to Godes geleafan
gecyrde, þæt hie ætnehstan sylfe eac mid heora handum þa idlan gyld
fyldon.
 221. Toþæs mihtig he þonne wæs ælce untrumnesse to
hælenne, & toðæs myccle gife he þæs æt Gode onfeng,
þæt nænig næs toðæs untrum ðe hine gesohte, þæt he sona
hælo ne onfenge.
 224. Ge þæt oft gelamp, þonne man hwylcne dæl his
hrægles to untruman men brohte, þæt he ðonne þurh þæt sona
wearð hal geworden.
 226. & þæs he wæs ðonne ealles swiþost to hergenne,
þæt he næfre nænigum woruldricum men ne cininge sylfum þurh lease
olecunga swiþor onbugan nolde, þonne hit riht wære; ah he a to
æghwylcum soð & riht sprecende wæs & donde.
 230. <foreign>Uere beatus uir in quo dolus</foreign>; ðis wæs soðlice eadig
wer, ne wæs æfre facen ne inwid on his heortan, ne he nænigne man
unrihtlice fordemde, ne nænigum yfel wiþ yfele geald; ne hine nænig man
yrne ne grammodne ne funde, ac he wæs a on anum mode.
 234. & efne heofonlice blisse & gefean mon mihte a on his
mode & on his andwleotan ongytan.
 236. Ne gehyrde nænig man on his muþe oht elles nefne Cristes
lof & nytte spræce, ne on his heortan buton arfæstnesse &
mildheortnesse & sibbe.
 238. Swa eac þes eadiga wer miccle ær beforan þone dæg
wiste his forðfore, & him Drihten þæt gecyþed hæfde, & he
þæt þæm broðrum sægde, þæt hit ða rihte wære þæt
he of ðisse worlde sceolde.
 241. Ða wiste he sumne hired on his bisceopscire, þe þa
ungeþwære & ungesibbe him betweonum wæron, þa ferde he ðyder
mid his discipulum, þeah þe he wiste þæt hit ða æt his daga ende
wære, þæt he huru wolde þæt hie ealle on sibbe wæron, ær he
of worulde ferde.
 245. Ða he þa hæfde þone hired gesibbodne þe he þær
to ferde, & þær dagas wel manige wæs, þa he þa eft mynte mid
his discipulum to his mynstre feran.
 248. Ða wearð he færinga swiþe untrum; ða heht he him
ealle his discipulos to, & him sægde þæt he þa forðferan
sceolde.
 250. Þa wæron hie ealle sona unrote, & sarlice
gebærdon, & þis cwædon to him: <foreign>Cur nos, pater, deseris aut cui nos
desolatos relinquis?</foreign> Forhwon forlætest þu, fæder, us nugit, oþþe
gif ðu gewitest, hwæm bebeodest þu us?
 253. Cumað arisende wulfas, todrifað ðine heorde; hwa
forstandeþ hie, gif ðu hie ne scyldest?
 255. We þæt witon þæt þæt is þines modes willa,
þæt þu mote þas world forlætan & Crist geseon.
 256. Ah miltsa þu hweþre us & gemyne þu ure þearfa.
 257. Ða he þa þas word spræc, & he hine ealle wepende
geseah, þa weop he eac sylf & his mod wæs onstyred mid þæm heora
wordum, swa he wæs manna mildheortost; & he mid wependre stefne ðus to
Drihtne cwæð: <foreign>Si adhuc populo tuo sum necessarius.</foreign> Drihten, cwæð,
gif ic nu git sie þinum folce nedþearflic her on worlde to hæbbenne,
þonne ne wiðsace ic þæm gewinne, ah sie þæs þin willa.
 263. Wæs he toþæs arfæst þæt him wæs
æghweþer on weorce ge þæt he leng from Cristes onsyne wære,
ðæt he þone gesawe.
 265. He þa forðon Drihtnes willan sohte & þus cwæð,
Min Drihten, longe ic wæs nu on ðæm heardan campe her on worlde, ac
þonne hweþre ne wiðsace ic þon þæt ic on þæm campe leng sie,
gif hit þin willa swiþor bið; ac ic mid þinum wæpnum getrymed on
þinum feþan fæste stande & for þinre campunga, þa hwile þe
þin willa bið.
 271. Wæs him ægweðer þæm eadigan were ge seo Godes
lufu toðæs hat & toðæs beorht on his heortan, ðeah he for
ðæm deaþe ne forhtode, ah hine ðæs heardost langode hwanne he of
ðisse worlde moste.
 274. & him þonne wæs eac manna lufu toðæs mycel
þæt him nænig gewin her on worlde to lang ne to heard ne þuhte,
þæs þe he heora saulum to hæle & to ræde gewinnan mihte.
 277. Þa wæs he dagas wel manige mid þære feforadle
swiþe gestanden, ah he þeah næfre godes weorces ne ablon, ah he hwilum
ealle niht þurh wacode on halgum gebedum; & þeah þe se lichoma
wære mid þære untrumnesse swa swiðe geswenced, hweþre his mod
wæs aheard & gefeonde on Drihten.
 281. & þonne he reste hine, þonne wæs his seo
æþeleste ræst on his earan oþþe elles on nacodre eorðan.
 283. Þa bædon hine his discipulos þæt hie mostan huru
sume uncyme streownesse him under gedon for his untrumnesse; þa cwæð he,
Bearn, ne bidde ge þæs; ne gedafenað Cristenan men þæt he elles do,
butan swa he efne on axan & on duste licge; gif ic eow oþres ðinges
bysene onstelle, þonne agylte ic.
 288. & a þær he læg, he hæfde his handa upweardes
& mid his eagum up to heofenum locade, þyder his modgeþanc a geseted
wæs.
 290. Ða bædan hine þa Godes þeowas þa ðe ðær to
him coman, þæt hie hine moston on oþre sidan oncyrran; & þa
cwæð he to him, <foreign>Sinite fratres, sinite, cælum potius respice.</foreign>
Forletað, broðor, he cwæð þa spræce; forlætað me, heofon
swiþor geseon þonne eorðan, þæt minum gaste sie to Drihtne weg
þyder he feran sceal.
 295. Þa he þa þus spræc, ða geseah he þone awergdan
gast deofol þær unfeor standan; ða cwæð he to him, <foreign>Quid adstas
cruenda bestia? nihil in me repperies.</foreign> Hwæt standest þu wælgrim?

START_TEXT

LS 17.2 (MartinVerc 18)
B3.3.17.3.
Saint Martin: Scragg 1992, 291-308.



 1. <foreign>De Sancto Martino Confessore.</foreign>.
 1. Men þa leofestan, magon we nu hwylcumhwego wordum asecgan be
þære arwyrðnesse þysse halgan tide, & be þære arwyrðan
gebyrde & be þam halgan life & forðfore þæs halgan
bisceopes, þysses eadigan weres, þe we nu in andweardnesse his tid
weorðiað & mærsiað, þe Martinus wæs haten.
 6. Wæs he Gode swiðe gecoren on his þeawum.
 6. Wæs he in Pannana þære mægðe in woruld cumen, in
Arrea ðam tune.
 7. Wæs he hwæðre in Italia afeded, in Ticinan þære
byrig.
 8. Wæs he for worulde swiðe godre gebyrde.
 9. Wæron his fæder & his modor buta hæðen.
 10. Wæs his fæder ærest cyninges þegn, & þa æt
nehstan geþah þæt he wæs tribunus, þæt is ealdorman cyninges
þegna.
 11. Þa sceolde he, sanctus Martinus, nyde beon sona on his
giogoðhade on geferræddenne cyninges þegna, & he wæs on
Constantines/ dæge & þa eft on Iulianus dæge, þæs caseres.
 14. Nalles þæt he his on þam willan on þam woruldfolgoðe
wære, ac he wæs on Godes þeowdome mycle swiðor & lufode þonne
þa dreamas & þa welan þysse worulde.
 17. & þa he wæs X wintre, þa tihton hine his yldran to
woruldfolgoðe, & þa fleah he to Godes cirican & bæd þæt
hine man þær gecristnode (þæt bið sio onginnes & se æresta
dæl þære halgan fulwihte), & þa he wæs wundorlice nu on
eallum his life on Godes þeowdome gecyrred.
 21. Þa he wæs XV wintra, þa genyddon hie hine, his yldran,
to þan þæt he sceolde wæpnum onfon, & on cyninges þegna
geferræddenne beon.
 23. Ða wæron þreo gear ær his fulwihte þæt he
woruldlicu wæpen wæg.
 24. & he hine hwæðre wið eallum þam healicum synnum
geheold, þa ðe woruldmen fremmiað in missenlicum þingum.
 26. Hæfde he mycle lufan & ealle swetnesse to ælcum men,
& he wæs geþyldig & eadmod & gemetfæst on eallum þingum
on eallum his life.
 28. & þeah þe he gyt on læwedum hade beon sceolde, &
hwæðre he to þæs mycle forhæfdnesse hæfde on eallum þingum
þæt he munuclif & git swiðor lifde þonne sume gehadode men.
 30. Wæs he for his arfæstum dædum eallum his geferum leof
& wyrð & ondrysne, & hie hine ealle mid synderlice lufan lufedon
& weorðedon.
 32. & þeah ðe he þa gyt ne wære fullice æfter
cierican endebyrdnesse gefullad, ac he wæs gecristnod, swa ic ær
foresægde, hwæðre he þæt geryne þæs halgan fulwihtes mid
godum dædum heold & lufade.
 35. He wolde þam winnendum fultumian, & earme frefran, &
hingriendum mete syllan, & nacode scrydan.
 37. & eall ðæt he on his folgoðe begeat, eall þæt
he for Gode sealde butan þære dæghwæmlican andlyfne anre þe he
nede on lyfian sceolde.
 39. Gemunde he þæt Godes bebod þæt he sylfa on his
godspelle bebead: he swa cwæð þæt se Godes man ne sceolde be ðam
mergendæge þencan, ðy læs þæt wære þæt he ðurh
þæt ænig þara goda forgulde þe he þonne ðy dæge gedon
meahte, in weninge hwæðer he eft þæs morgendæges gebidan moste.
 44. Men þa leofestan, magon we nu þara arfæstra dæda
sume asecgan ðe ðes eadiga wer sanctus Martinus dyde.
 45. He sona in cnihthade gedyde, þeah þara godra dæda ma
wære þonne hit ænig man asecgan mæge.
 46. & þæt gelamp sume siðe þæt he ferde mid oðrum
cyninges þegnum in þa burh þe Ambinensis hatte.
 48. Wæs þæt in midda wintra.
 48. Wæs se winter þy geare to þæs grim þæt efne
manige men wæron þæt heora feorh for cyle gesealdan.
 50. Þa sæt þær sum þearfa æt ðam burggeate wel
neah ðon, & se nacoda bæd him þa for Gode hrægles on
ælmessan.
 52. Þa ferdon hie ealle forð be him, & heora nænig to
him gecyrran nolde, ne him ænige are gedon woldon.
 53. Þa ongeat he, se Godes man, þæt drihten him þone
þearfendan man geheold þæt he him miltsian sceolde, þe þara oðera
manna nan him arian ne wolde.
 55. Nyste þa hwæðre hwæt he him don sceolde, for þan
þe he nowiht elles hæfde butan his anfealdne gerelan, ac eall þæt he
ma hæfde eall he þæt ær beforan in gelic weorc ateah & for Gode
sealde.
 58. Geteah þa his seax, & genam his sciccels þone his lodan
þe he him on hæfde.
 59. Snað þa þone in tu, & þa healfne þam þearfan
sealde & mid healfe hine eft besweop.
 60. Þa wæron manige men þe þæt gesawon þæt hie
hine on þam tældon & besmyredon, þæt he swa his anfealdne gyrelan
tosniðan sceolde.
 62. Sume þonne eft, ða ðe beteran modes wæron &
ænige lufan to Gode hæfdon, hie sylfe on þon oncuðon þæt hie swa
ne dydon, & wiston þæt hie ma hæfdon þæt hie ægðer ge
ðam þearfan hrægl syllan meahton ge hwæðre him sylfum genog
habban.
 67. & þa wæs in þære æfterfylgendan niht ða
þes eadiga wer slepte, & þa geseah he Crist sylfne mid þy ilcan
hrægle gegyredne þe he ær þam þearfan sealde.
 69. & þa wæs him beboden geornlicor þæt he hine,
dryhten, ongeate & þæt hrægl þæt he ær þam þearfan
sealde: & þa geseah he mycle engla weorod ymbe þane dryhten standende,
& þa gehyrde hine, dryhten, eac mid switolre stefne to englum cweðan.
 73. Martinus nu iu, he cwæð þus, gecristnod ær his
fulwihte, he mid þysse hrægle me gegyrede.
 74. Wæs in þære dæde sweotol ðæt ure dryhten is
swiðe gemyndig þæs cwides þe he sylfa ær cwæð: Swa hwæt swa
ge hwylcum earmum men to gode gedoþ for minum naman, efne ge þæt me
sylfum doð.
 77. He ða wolde þone cwide gefyllan in þære godan dæde,
& hine sylfne geeaðmedde to þæn þæt he wolde in þæs
þearfan gierelan ætywan ðam eadigan were sancte Martine.
 80. & ða se eadiga wer sanctus Martinus ða gesyhðe
geseah, þa ne wæs he hwæðre oht ofor þan in oferhygd ahafen, ne in
mennisce wuldore, ac he Godes god in þære ðære dæde he ongeat.
 82. Ða he ða hæfde eahtatyne wintra, ða gefullade hine man
æfter cirican endebyrdnesse.
 84. Wæs he ær beforan þa þreo gear gecristnod, swa ic
ær sægde.
 84. Ða forlet he ealne þone woruldfolgoð an, & ða
gewat/ he to sancte Ilario þam bisceope, þe in Pictauensis þære byrig
wæs bisceop.
 86. Wæs þæt swiðe foremære man, se bisceop, & his
god wæs swiðe gecyðed.
 87. & he þa þysne eadigan wer sancte Martine fulfremedlice
in Godes æ & in Godes þeowdome getyde & gelærde, & eac
þan þe ðæt eaðdæde wæs, þa hine God sylfa swa innan manode.
 90. Wæs he swiðe geþungen on his þeawum, &
gestæððig on his wordum, & hluttor & ærfæst & clæne
on his life, & gemetfæst & milheort on his dædum, & geornful
& biwyrde in dryhtnes lare, & on eallum þingum for Gode fulfremed.
 94. & þa gelamp æfter þan þæt þes eadiga wer
sanctus Martinus sum mynster him getimbrade, & he on ðam manigra Godes
þeowa gastlice fæder gewearð.
 96. & þa gelamp sume siðe þæt þær cwom sum
gecristnod man to him þæt he wolde mid his lare & mid his bysenum beon
ontimbred.
 98. & þa he ða þær wæs wel manige dagas, þa
wearð he untrum, se man, in þære feferadle.
 99. & þa gelamp in ða tid þæt he, sanctus Martinus,
wæs in sumre fore ealle dogor.
 100. Þa he ða eft ham cwom, þa mette he þone man
forðferedne þe þær ær untrum wæs, & hine efne swa
færlice deað fornam þæt he ungefulwad forðgewat.
 102. Ða he ða, sanctus Martinus, þæt geseah þæt þa
oðre broðor ealle swa unrote leton ymbe þæt lic, & hie utan
stodon, þa weop he & eode to him.
 105. Wæs him þæt swiðe mycle weorce þæt he swa
ungefullad forðferan sceolde.
 106. Getreowde hine ða hwæðre on þone ælmihtigan Gode
mid ealle mode & on his mildheortnesse.
 107. Eode he ða hwæðre in þæt hus þær se lichama
inne læg, & het þa oðre men ealle ut gangan, & he ða ða duru
beleac æfter him, & he hine þa on gebed astreahte ofer þæs
aswoltenes mannes leoma.
 110. Ða he ða lange hwile swa in þam gebede wæs, ða
ongeat he þæt þær wæs godcund mægn andweard, & he þara
dryhtnes mildheortnesse unforhtlice onbad.
 112. Þa wæs ymbe hwile þa gefylde he his lare lufian, for
þan he swa cuðe & Godes gife on him wæs & his hlisa wæs
forð swiðe mære geond ealne middangeard.
 154. & he manig tempel & deofulgild gebræc &
gefylde, & he þonne þær asette Godes cirican, oððe fullice
þær mynster getimbrade.
 155. & þæt gelamp sume siðe eac þæt he ongan
onbærnan sum deofolgild þæt mid þam hæðenum mannum swiðe
weorð & mære wæs.
 157. Þa stod þær sum nyttwyrðe hus bi ðam
hæðengilde þe he þær bærnan ongan.
 158. Þa slog se wind þone lig on þæt nyttwyrðe hus,
& him þuhte þæt hit eall forbærnan sceolde.
 160. Þa he ða, sanctus Martinus, þæt geseah, þa arn he
sona up on þæt hus, & gestod he ongen þam lige.
 161. Þa gelamp wundorlice wyrd, þæt se lig ongan
slean/ & brecan ongen þam winde, & efne swa swa se wind swiðor
sloh on þone lig, swa bræc se lig swiðor on ðam winde, efne in þam
gelicnesse swa ða gesceafta twa him betweonan feohtan sceoldon.
 165. & swa wæs þa se lig geþreatod þurh sancte
Martines gebedu, þæt he nænigum oðrum þingum ne derede butan þam
diofolgilde anum þe he ðær bærnan ongan.
 168. Swylce gelamp oðer wundor þyssum onlic.
 168. He cwom to sumum tune þe Libras wæs haten.
 169. Þa wæs þær sum diofolgild þe ða hæðenan men
godgild heton, & hie hine swiðe weorðedon.
 170. Ða wolde sanctus Martinus ælce þinge þæt gild
tobrecan & gefyllan.
 171. Þa wiðstodon him þa hæðenan men, & hie hine mid
teonum aweg adrifon.
 173. Ða eode he ðærrihte bii in sume stowe, & he hine
gegyrede mid hærene hrægle swiðe hearde & swiðe unwynsome, &
fæste þry dagas, & bæd God ælmihtigne þæt he þurh his
godcunde miht þæt deofolgild tobræce & gefylde, þa he hit for
manna teonum gebrecan ne moste.
 177. & þa cwomon þær semninga twegen englas to him,
gescildode & gesweordode & mid heregeatwum gegyrede, efne swa hie to
campe feran sceoldon, & cwædon þæt hie God sylfa to him sende,
þæt hie sceoldan þæt hæðene werod geflyman, & him, Martine,
gefultumian þæt hie þæt diofulgild gebræce & gefylde.
 181. Þa eodon hie eft to þam tune & þæt deofulgild
tobræcon & gefyldon aa oð grund.
 182. & þa hæðenan men tolocedon, & hie hwæðre
wæron mid þy godcundan mægene to þæs swiðe gefyrhte þæt
heora nænig him wiðstandan meahte ne ne dorste.
 185. Ac hie ealle to dryhtnes geleafan gecyrdon, & hie swa
cwædon þæt wære soð God se ðe Martine hyrde, & þæt ða
heora hæðenan gild wæron eall idel & unnytt, & þæt hie
nowðer ne him sylfum gehelpan meahton, ne æniges þæra gehelpan þe
to him ænig are wilnode.
 190. Swylce eac gelamp sume siðe þær he sum hæðengild
gebræc, & þa þær gearn mycel mænio to him þæra
hæðenra manna, & ealle swiðe yrre wæron.
 192. Ða wæs heora sum reðra & hatheortra þonne þa
oðre wæron, & se ða gebrægd his sweorde & mynte hine slean.
 193. Þa he, sanctus Martinus, þæt geseah, þa dyde he sona
þæt hrægel of his sweoran, & leat forð to þam men þe hine
slean mynte.
 195. Ða he ða, se hæðena man, upprihte mid his handa &
hine sclean sceolde, þa feoll he færinga on bæcling, & nahte he his
lichoman geweald.
 197. Ac he wæs mid godcunde egesan swiðe geþread, & he
þa him þone eadigan wer, sancte Martine, forgifnesse bæd.
 200. Swylce wæs eft eac oðer wundor þyssum onlic, &
þæt gelamp sume siðe þær he sum deofulgild bræc & fylde.
 201. Þa brægd þara hæðenra manna sum his seax.
 202. Þa se hæðena man hine stingan wolde, þa nyste he
færinga hwær þæt seax cwom þæt he ær on handa hæfde.
 204. Gelomlice þæt þonne wæs þær he ða idlan gild
bræc & him þa hæðenan men wiþerwearde wæron, þæt he
þurh his lare & þurh dryhtnes gife heora heortan to Godes geleafan
gecyrde, þæt hie eac sylfe mid heora handum þa idlan gild bræcon
& fyldon.
 207. & he to þæs mihtig wæs þæt he ælce
untrumnesse to hælanne, & to þæs mycle gife he ðæs æt Gode
onfeng, þætte ne wæs ænig man to þæs untrum þe hine gesohte
þæt he sona hælo ne onfenge.
 210. Ge þæt oft gelamp þonne hwylc man his hrægles dæl
to untrumum menn brohte þæt he þonne þurh þæt wearð hal
geworden.
 212. In þyssum he þonne wæs ealles swiðost to herigenne,
þæt he næfre nænigum woruldricum men ne cyninge sylfum þurh lease
olihtunge swiðor onbugan wolde þonne hit riht wære.
 215. Ac hie a in eallum soð & riht don wolde.
 215. Þis is soðlice eadig wer, ne wæs næfre facen ne
inwit in his heortan, ne ænigne unrihtlice demde nene witnode, ne he
ænigum yfel mid yfele geald.
 217. Ne hine ænig man yrre ne gramheortne ne geseah, ac he
wæs in anum mode, & efne heofonlice blisse & gefean man meahte a in
his mode geseon & on his andwlitan ongitan.
 220. & ne gehyrde ænig man aht elles of his muðe butan
Cristes lof & nytte spræce, ne aht elles on his heortan butan
arfæstnesse & mildheortnesse & sybbe & eaðmodnesse.
 223. Swylce eac þes eadiga wer, sanctus Martinus, mycle ær
beforan þe he þone dæg wisse his forðsiðe, & him dryhten
gecyðed hæfde.
 224. & he þa his broðrum sægde þæt hit þa
ætrihte wære þæt he of þisse worulde sceolde.
 226. Ða wiste he sumne hired on his bisceopscire þa þe
ungeþweare & ungesybsume him betweonum wæron.
 227. Þa ferde he þyder mid his þegnum, þeah ðe he wiste
þæt hit þa æt his deaðdæge wære, þæt he huru wolde
þæt hie ealle in sybbe wæron ær he of worulde ferde.
 230. Þa cwomon hie to sumre ea, þa gesawon hie þara wel feala
þara fugela þe we scealfras nemnaþ, & hie ða fixas uptugon of
þære ea, & þeah þe heora hwylc þone fisc forswulge, þonne
wæs he eft swa gifre swa he ær wæs, þæt he oðerne gename.
 233. Þa cwæð sanctus Martinus: Hwæt, þas wiht habbað
deofla onlicnesse, swa þe deofol a sætaþ hwær he mæge unware men
beswican, & he næfre to þæs feala berædeð þæt he æfre
ful sie.
 236. Ða bebead sanctus Martinus þam fugelum þæt hie
þanon fram þam wætere gewiten, & on westen & ðrige land
sohton.
 238. & efne on þa gelicnesse swa he þone deoful of stowa
gehwylcre geflymde þær he þonne wæs, swa ða fugelas sona ealle
ætsomne/ on weg gewiton, þæt heora nan ætstod furðun behindan.
 241. & hie þæt wundredon þe þæt gesawon & his
fera wæron þæt ða fugelas sylfe eac sancte Martine gehyrdon.
 243. Ða he þa hæfde þone hyred gesybbodne þe he
þær to ferde, & þær well manige dagas wæs, & þa he ða
eft mynte mid his þegnum to his mynstre feran, þa wearð he færinga
swiðe mettrum.
 245. Þa het he ealle his þegnas him to, & he him sægde
þæt he forðferan sceolde.
 246. Þa weopon hie ealle sona, & sarlice gebærdon for
heora hlaforde, & hie þus cwædon to him: For hwan forlætest ðu,
la fæder, us nu git?
 248. Oððe hwam bebeodest ðu us eac gif ðu gewitest?
 249. Cumaþ rixiende wulfas & todrifaþ þine heorde.
 250. Hwa forstandeð þonne hie gif ðu hie ne scyldest?
 251. We þæt þonne witan þæt þæt is þines modes
willa þæt ðu mote þas woruld forlætan & Crist geseon.
 252. Ac miltsa ðu þonne hwæðre us & gemyne ure
þearfe.
 254. Ða he ða heora spræce þyllice gehyrde & he hie
ealle wepende geseah, þa weop he sylfa eac, & his mod wæs swiðe
onstyred mid heora wordum & mid heora wope, for þan he wæs manna
mildheortost, & he efne mid pependre stefne þus to dryhtne cwæð: Min
dryhten God ælmihtig, gif ic nu gyt sie þinum folce midþearflice her in
worulde to habbanne, þonne ne wiðsæce ic þam gewinne þæt ic nu
gyt mid him sie.
 260. Wæs he to þæs arfæst þæt him wæs ægðer
on weorce, ge þæt he ða broðor forlete, ge huru þone þæt he
leng fram Cristes onsyne wære þæt he ða ne gesawe heofonlican rice
genam.
 300. Hwæt, we nu gehyraþ, men þa leofestan, hu haliglice
þes eadiga wer, sanctus Martinus, his lif for Gode lifde, þa hwile þe he
her on worulde wæs, & hu fægerum edleanum he wæs æt urum
dryhtne onfeng.
 303. And nu a ða hwile þe þeos world standeð, his goð
man mærsað geond ealne middangeard in Godes cirican.
 304. & he nu mid eallum halgum a to widan feore in heofona rice
for dryhtnes onsyne gefyhð & blissaþ.
 306. Ac utan we la tilian, men þa leofestan, þæt we
þæs halgan weres, sanctus Martinus, lif & his dæda onherien
þæs þe ure gemet sie, & wuton hine biddan þæt he us sie in
heofonum þingere wið urne dryhten, nu we her on eorðan hine geond
middangeard wyrðiaþ.
 310. Dryhten us to þam gefultumige se ðe leofaþ & rixaþ
aa in eallra worulda world a butan ende, amen.

Nativity of Mary the Virgin (Oxford, Bodleian Library, MS. Bodley 343): Assmann 1889, 117-37 [N].



 1. <foreign>Natiuitas Sancte Marie</foreign>.
 2. Men ða leofeste.
 2. Wurðie we nu on andweardnysse þa gebyrdtide þære eadige
femne sce marie.
 5. Ðeo wæs godes kenninge ures drihtnes hælendes cristes,
& hiræ nome ireht læfdi oððe cwen oððe sæsteorræ.
 8. Heo is læfdi inemned, forðan þe heo cende þone laford
heofenæs & eorðæn.
 11. And heo is cwen inemned, forðan þe heo com of þam
æðele cynne & of þam kynelyce sæde dauides cynnes.
 14. Sæsteorræ sche is icweden, forþan ðe þeo
sæsteorra on niht cuðeþ scipliðendum monnum, hwider bið east &
west & suð & norð.
 18. Swa þenne wearð þurh þa halig femne icyd þe rihtæ
siðfæt to þam æce life þam ðe ær longe seten on þeostrum
& on deaþes scuan & on þam unstille yðan þare sæ þisses
middaneardes.
 23. And ha syððan wisten alle halige þone frumen
middæneardes & ende & heofene riches wuldor & helle wite.
 27. Þeonn magen we nu hwylcen seogum wordum sæcgæn be
ðare burdtide þære eadigæn femne sce marie, hu heo iboren wæs.
 34. We leorniæð, þæt were sum æþel wer in israel.
 35. His nome wæs ioachim, of iudan cynne.
 37. He wæs heordæ his sceapæ.
 37. He wæs godfyrht mon on bilewitnysse & in fremsumnesse.
 39. And næfde he nænigne oðre gemænenymðe his eowde.
 41. Of þam eowde he fedde alle þa ðe heom drihten
ondredæþ & of þam wæstme he gode þreofealdne lac brohte &
all his æhtæ on ðreo todælde.
 46. Enne del he sealde þearfæn & widewæn &
steopcildum & ælþeodig monnum and oðerne del þæm þe gode ane
seruedæn.
 49. Þriddan dæl he heold him seolfum & his hirede bi to
lyfigenne.
 51. Forþan ðe he þas ðing wæs donde þus, þa myclode
god his woruldæhtæ; on þa tid næs nan mon him ilice on israelæ.
 55. Ðas ðing he ongon don, þa he wæs <foreign>XV</foreign> wintre.
 56. & midþa ðe he hæfde <foreign>XX</foreign> wintræ, þa nom he wif
him to make.
 59. Heo wæs ihaten anna.
 59. Heo wæs achares dohter of his agene cynne, þæt is
ðenne of ðam æþelan cynne dauides þæs kynniges.
 62. Heo þa wæron samod togedere twentig wintræ, swa heo nan
bearn ne bigetæn.
 74. Þa ilamp hit summe dæg, þæt heo eoden to þam
drihtnes temple, & he þa ioachim stod betwyx þam monnum, þe to gode
heoræ lac onsægednesse brohten, & he gearwode his gifu on godes
isihðe.
 80. Him ða to neahlæhte þare bocere sum, his nome wæs
Ruben, & cwæð to him: Nis ðe ilyfed, þæt ðu stonde betwux
þam ðe gode onsegednysse bringæð, forþan ðe godes bletsung ofer
þe ne com, þæt he þe ænig bearn sende.
 87. He ða þær wæs mycle scame þrowiende beforan þam
folce for ðisse wordum.
 89. He þa swa scamiende ut of ðam temple wepende eode & he
þa nolde æft hweorfan to his agene hame, ac he gewat on westene to his
sceapum & þa hyrdæs nom mid him & þær wunode fif monðæ
fæcc, swa þær nan ærendrace ne ferde betweonan him & his
mæccan.
 98. Ða ongon anna hire imæccan bewepen & hire to drihtine
biddan & þus cwæð: Min drihten israele god, þu þe eart strong
& mihtig ofer alle isceaftæ, & þu me naldæst næfre bearn
ofer eorðan syllæn & þu minne wer æt me genome.
 105. & ic nat, hwæder his lif is ofer eorðan; & gif he
forðiwiten is, þonne gearwode ic him byrigenne.
 108. Ða heo ðas word icwæden hæfde, þa eode heo eft on
hire cauertun & hire eadmodlice to drihten bead.
 111. And æfterþan ðe heo hæfde hire bone ifylled, þa
ahof heo hire eagan up to drihtne.
 114. & þa iseah heo an sparewæn nest on anum lawertrewe.
 116. Heo þa mid wependre stefne clypode to drihtne &
cwæð: Drihten, þu almihtiga god, ðu þe sealdest alle isceftæ
byrþor & heo on þon gefoð, ic þe nu þang sæcge, þet þu me
anæ ute atyndest from þine gyfæ þare fremsumnysse.
 123. Hwæt, þu min drihten const & wast mine heortæ.
 124. Hwæt, ic þe from frimþe mine sinscipes bihæt, gif
ðu me sealdest sunu oððe dohter, þæt ic hire wolde þe bringæn
to þine temple.
 128. Ða heo þas word icwædon hæfde, þa æteowde hire
godes engel & cwæþ: Nylt þu ðe ondredan, anna, forþan þin
ðrowung is on godes þohte.
 133. Þæt of þe acenned bið, þæt bið on wundræ
allum monnum oð ðet woruldæ ende.
 135. Þa midþæm ðe he þas word icwedon hæfde, þa
wæs he fram hire eagan ahofen.
 138. Þa wæs heo swyðe forht iworden for þæs englæs
isihðe.
 139. & heo þa eode into hire cleofæ & þær wunede
ðone dæg & þa niht on hire bedum.
 142. Þa wæs morgen iworden; þa laðede heo hire ðinene to
hire & to hire cwæð: Hwæt, ðu me isawe on mine wydewanhade
biswicene & on mycelre nearunysse isette & noldost me toforen cumen?
 148. Þa answarde heo hire unðwærlice & hire to
cwæð: þeah god þinne wær æt þe nome & þin innoð
biluce, hwæt sceal ic þe ðæs don.
 152. Ða þe heo anæ þas word ihyrde, þa ongon heo
wepæn biterlice.
 160. Hwæt, þa on ðare ylcan nihte him æteowde sum swiðe
wlitig wer on ðam westene, þær þær he wæs mid his heordum, &
him to cwæð: For hwam nelt þu ham hweorfan to þinum imæccan?
 166. Þa cwæð ioachi: Twentig wintræ ic wunod mid hire
& me god nan bearn of hire ne sealde.
 168. Ac ic swiðe geæswicod eode ut of þam godes temple;
forþan ic nylle æft ham hweorfan, ac ic wylle her wuniæn þa hwile,
ðe drihten wyle, & þa godes gife for drihtenes nome dælan, swa ic
ær dyde.
 175. Þa andswarde him þe ængel & ðus cwæð: Ic eom
drihtine engel & nu to dæg ic me æteowde þine gemæccan &
hire frefrode, þa þa heo hire wæpende & geomeriende to drihtene
bæd.
 181. & wite þu nu, þæt heo of ðine sæde ieacnod is,
swa swa þu na hit ne wistest.
 183. Ða þe ðu ane forlæte, heo þe cenneð dohter &
heo bið on godes temple fulfremed, & þe halga gast ræstæþ on
hire, & hire eadignyssæ oferstihð all wifcynn, & hire ne bið
ilic ænig þare þe ær wæs oððe æfter cymð.
 190. Cyr nu to ðine imæccan & þu imætest hire
ieacnode, & þas ðonce gode, forþan ðe hire sæd bið ibletsod
& heo bið moder þare æcæn bletsunge iset.
 195. Þa weorðede hine ioachim & him to cwæð: Gif hit
þus iwyrðan scyle, swa ðu cwæst, site mid me on mine huse & bletse
þinne ðeow.
 199. Þa cwæð þe engel to him: Hwi wilt ðu la
cwæðon, þæt ðu beo min ðeowæ, ac þu eart min efenðeowæ,
forþan wit beoð anes godes þeow.
 203. & ic þe secge, þet min mæte and min drync ne mæg
beon from monnum isægen.
 206. Ac swa hwæt swa ðu me to gife tihtest, bring þæt
gode to unsægednesse.
 208. He þa ioachim brohte unwemmed lac & to þam engle
cwæð: Næs ic na geðrystig, þæt ic gode sacerdlice
onsægednesse brohte, gif þu me ne hæte.
 212. Þa cwæð þe engel: Na ic þe ne hate gode sacerdlice
onsægednesse bringan, forþan ðe ic godes willæn to þam ne ongeate.
 216. Þa ferde þe engel samod mid þam stence ðære
onsægednysse into heofenum.
 219. He þa ioachim wearð to þam afyrht, þæt he feol on
eorþan & læg swylce he dead were fram þare sixtan tide þæs
dæges, oð ðet hit euen wæs.
 223. Him þa to nealæhton his heordæs & heo hine þa
isegæn liogan & nysten þenne intingæn on him, ac hofen him up,
& heo cwæden, þæt he wolde hine sylfne acwællæn.
 228. Ða ahof he his heafod up & sæde heom his sihðe,
þe he iseah.
 230. Ða wyrdon heo sonæ afyrhte & eac wundredon, oð
ðet he hit heom all isæd hæfde; & heo alle þa hine tremedon &
lærdon, þæt he ihyrsum wære þæs englæs wordum & þæt
he raþe hwirfde ham to his imæccæn.
 237. He þa ioachim ðreodode on his mode, hwæt he embe
þæt dyde.
 239. Þa wearð he feringæ on slæpe gehwirfed.
 240. Him þa æteowde þe ilcæ engel eft on slepe & him
to cwæð: Ic eom godes engel & from drihtne ic am þe to heorde iset.
 244. Ac fare nu ham orsorh to ðine mæccan & eower
mildheortnysse, þe ge wrohton, & eower nomæ wæs iræded
beforæn drihtnes isihðe on his ðreomsettle, & he eow syllæð swa
mycele grownisse on eowre beorðran, swa he næfre nænne halge ær ne
sealde, ne nu næfre æft ne syllæð.
 253. He þa ioachim of þam slepe aras & his swefen sæde
his heordum.
 255. Heo þa alle hine bedæn & halsedon, þæt he
ihyrsumode þas englæs wordum & ræcene ham cyrde.
 258. Þa wæs he ær igan for his unrotnysse on þam westene
swa feor, þæt he for ðrittige dagene fæcc ne mihte ham to his
mæcce gehweorfan.
 262. Heo þa anna wæs æt hire bede, þa æteowde hire
drihtnes engel & hire cydde ðone hamsið hire imacen.
 266. & heo þa mid hire hinene him ongean eode mid mycle
gefean; swilce eac hire magas & all israelæ bearn mycele blisse
hæfdon bi his hamcyme & be þam lisan hire geeacnunge.
 281. Ða cænde anna hire dohtor & hire nome nemnode maria,
& heo hire þa fedde þreo wintræ æt hire breoste.
 284. Ioachim & anna þa læddon þæt child mid heom to
þare halgan ceastre & þæt lac brohten mid heom into þam drihtines
temple, þe iudea iwune wæs.
 289. & heo þa sealden þæt child on gemæne þære
femenæ, þe dæges & nihtes on godes lofe wunoden.
 292. Heo up eode mid þam oðre femnum on þa <foreign>XV</foreign> stæpes on
þa temple, swa heo ne on beac ne beseah, ne heo na ne tealtrade, ne æfter
hire ealdre ne rymde, swa swa childes gewunæ wæs.
 297. Ac heo wæs on geange & on wordæ & on allum
ibære ilic wunsumen menn, þe hæfde þrittig wintræ, & heo
geornlice & eadmodlice þurhwunode on hiræ bedum, oð ðet þa
biscopæs & all þæt folc wundræde on hire ibærum.
 309. Heo anna þa wæs ifylled mid þam halgan gaste & heo
witegode þa biforen þam folce & þus cwæð: Drihten almihtig god
wæs imundig his wordæ, þe he sylf cwæð, þæt he wolde his
folce secan haligre neosunge.
 315. & þa ðeode, þe mid us arisæn, he wolde
eadmedigan, þæt heo cyrdon to heoræ silfræ heortum & heoræ
earan ontyndon to ure benum & þa bismernesse ure feondum from us
acyrdon.
 321. On þam unbeoðrum æcere blisse, ðe þar igefæn is
on israele, swa me min drihten geaf, þæt ic mot gode icwæme lac
bringan, ær me mine feond ascufon from þare halgan onsægednyssæ for
mine unberendnysse.
 327. Drihten min acerde heom from me & me geaf ecce blisse.
 332. Ða heo þas word icwædon hæfde, þa cyrdon heo ham
mid þam & þæt child forlæten æt þam temple mid þam oðre
femnen.
 336. & heo þa weox & wearð fulfremed on godræ
mægene heanyssæ, & heo þa sonæ godum towcræftum onfeng, &
swiðor þone ænig þare þe heore bearn wæren wifæ & femena.
 341. And heo sette hire sylf haligne regol, swa þæt heo wolde
beon fram þare æreste tyde þæs dæges on hire halig beden wuniende
oð ðet þa ðridde tyde, on þa nigoðæn tide emben hire webweorc.
 347. & æft fram þare nigoðan tyde heo þurhwunode
standende on hire ibedum, oð ðet godes engel hire æteowde & hire
brohte heofenlices swetnysse & heo þaræ burigde of his handa.
 353. & heo syððan wæs betere & swiðre on godes
lufæn & on gastlicræ mægenæ heanyssæ, & heo yldræn
femnæn lærde to godes willæn & heo wæs tyddre & snotere on
þare godes lage, þone ænig þære þe hire biforen wæs.
 359. Heo wæs eadmodre & on godes lufe glædre & on
þohte clænre & on þam dauidisce sange wræstlicre, þone ænig
wære.
 363. & heo wæs ðolemod & steaðig on hire ibærum
& nan mon ne seah hire wrað, ne tælan, ne warigen, ne nan word yfeles
of hire muðe ne com.
 367. Ac hire word weron godes gife fulle & he wæs on hire
heortæn smeagende þone wisdom on godes bocæ.
 371. & ða femnen, þe mid hire weron, heo tymede, þæt
heo on heoræ bedum þurhwynedon & on godes lofe & nan heoræ
stefne on ydele læhtre up ahufe, ne heo on heoræ tungæn teonan ne
cwædon, ne nan yfel word of heoræ muðe ut ne eode.
 378. & of hire aras ærest þe wunæ, þæt ðe mon,
ðe oðerne grete mid leofe worden, þæt he him godcunde bletsunge ongean
sette.
 382. & dæghwamlice heo underfeng mete of þas englæs
handa & mid þan heo ireordod wæs, & þone mete, þe heo æt
þam biscope underfeng on þam temple, þone heo dælde ðearfendum
monnum.
 388. And swa hwilc mon swa hire untrum isohte, æft he eode hal
from hire.
 396. Þa ilamp hit, þæt abiathar, þe sacerd, brohte mycelne
gyfe þam biscope & bæd hine, þet he sealde maria his sune to
imæccæn.
 400. Ða steorde mariæ him & cwæð andredlice: Ne
wurðæþ þæt næfre swa, þæt ic wer grete oððe wer me.
 403. Ða answerden hire þa biscopæs & hire magas alle,
þe on þam temple weron, & cwædon: God wæs on bearnum begangen
& in eaforen weorðaþ, swa ðet iwunelic wæs on godes folce
israele.
 409. Þa answyrde maria & heom cwæð to: Næs nan
rihtwis men, ne halig ær abel, & hine arleaslice unwis ofsloh.
 412. He brohte twyfealde gyfe drihtene luttre onsægednysse &
his lichames clænnysse.
 415. Eac swylce helias wæs of þissere weoruldæ ilæd on
lichame, forþan ðe he his clænnysse heold.
 421. Wæs heo, swylc heo wære feowertene wintræ.
 422. Þa demden pharisei, þæt heo syððan wuniæn
sceolde on þam godes temple.
 425. Ðæt þridde dæg, þa heo þa ðider isamnod
wæron, þa astah þe heahbiscop isacar up on þone ytemeste stæpe
& clypode þa luddre stefne & þus cwæð: Ihyræð nu, israele
bearn, min word.
 430. Ge witon, þæt salomon þis temple timbrode & her
wæron syððan inne kyningæ bearn & witegenæ &
heahsacerdæ, oð ðet heo bicomen to ælicre yldon.
 435. & heo ilimplice heora yldran wæron eawfestæ &
heoræ bearn æft gode icweme lac brohton to þam godes temple & heora
yldrene endebyrdnysse gode icwæmdon.
 440. Nu is ðonne imetod, þæt maria hæfð niwe
endebyrdnysse ongunnen gode mid to cwemene, sægð, þæt heo wyle gode
hire mægðhad bringan.
 443. Uton secan þa andsware æt gode sylfum ure axunge,
þæt god us cyþe, hwylce wære we hire bifæsten sceolen to haldene.
 448. Þa licode þet word alle þare samunge and þa senden lot
ofer þa tweolf cynn israele bearnum.
 451. Þa feol þæt lot ofer iudan cynn, iacobes sune.
 453. Þa bead þe sacerd, þæt iudan cynn come þæs on
mærgen to þam godes temple, ælc þære ðe wif næfde, &
hæfde heoræ ælc gyrdæ on hondæ.
 457. Þa wæs ðonen iworden, þæt ioseph wæs ihaten sum
iwintred mon & eode þider mid gungum monnum & his gerde þider
bær.
 461. Þa nam þe sacerd alle gerdæn & bær ða into
Sancta Sanctorum & bead, þæt heo comen on mærgen & nome ælc
his gyrd, & þonne sceolde an culfre fleon of ðare gyrde foreweardre up
into heofenum.
 467. Þenne scold þe wer beon hyrde þare femnæn.
 468. Ða wæs iworden on mærgen þæs æftren dæges,
þa comen heo alle on þa tid þare onsægednysse, & þa in eode þe
biscop abiathar into Sancta Sanctorum, wæs þæt þare haligræ
halignis ealræ, and he þa nom þa gyrdan & sealde anre gehwylcum heom
on syndron.
 476. Wæs ðare monnum ðreo þusendæ, & þa of nan
þare gyrde þeo culfre ut ne eode.
 478. Þa gescrydde hine abiathar þe biscop mid þam
heahsacerdæ gyrlan & in eode on þa Sancta Sanctorum & onbærnde
þa onsægednysse & his bene to drihtine sende.
 483. Þa æteow him drihtines engel & him to cwæð:
ðeo sæleste gerde is git æfter, þe ðu for noht ne tellest.
 487. Nym þa & syle, þonne cymð þæt tacn of hire,
þæt ðu þer secgst.
 489. Wæs þæt iosepes gyrd.
 490. Þa næs heo na isoht, forþan ðe ioseph wæs eald
& on utemeste stod.
 492. Þa clypode þe biscop hine mycle stefne & hine nemnode
& him his gyrdæ sealde.
 494. & þa on sæmningæ fleah þær culfre ut swiðe
hwit & fleah geond þa hwæmmes þæs temples & þa gewat on
ðone heofen.
 498. Þa wæs ðet folc swiðe gefeonde & cwædon to
iosepe: Eadig eart þu on þine ylde, nu ðe god swa gewurðode, þæt
ðu scealt beon hyrde þare clænen fæmnen.
 503. Eac swylce þa biscopæs cwædon: Onfoh hire nu, ioseph,
forþan ðe þu eart anæ icoren on þine cynne hire to hyrde from gode.
 507. He þa ioseph cwæð bifigendre stefne: Nis min gemet
swylcum cilde to onfonne, forþan ðe ic habbe fela bearnæ & þa
beoð alle yldræ þonne heo.
 512. Þa cwæð þe biscop to him: Gemun þu, hu lamp
daþan; he forwearð & monige eac mid him, þa þe godes willæn
forhogedon.
 516. Þa cwæð he ioseph: Ne forhoge ic na godes willæn on
hire, & god þonne cyðaþ, hwylc geongræ monnæ on mine cynne hire
wurðe bið.
 520. Ac ic onfo þare clænen femnæn, þæt heo wunie mid
me, oð ðet heo hæbbe ælycre ylde.
 523. Ða cwæð þe biscop: Fæmnen beoð mid hyre on
fultume oð þæne dæg incre geamungæ, & ne mæg hire nan
oðer wer underfon.
 527. Þa onfeng ioseph mariam mid oðre fif fæmnum, þe hire
wæron on fultume iseald to iosepes hame.
 530. Þa wæron ihatene, æræst þus: becca, saphira,
Susanna, Abugea & Sehel.
 532. & þe biscop sealde heom alle godeweb to wæfenne of
seolce & of mislice hiwum wahrift to þam temple.
 536. Þa onfeng maria hwite godewebbes to wefanne & þa
oðre mislices hiwæs.
 538. Þa specan heo heom betweonan on gleaw & ðus cwædon:
þu eart ure gingast, þu miht wefan þæt hwite godeweb & þu mihd
beon ure cwæn.
 542. Ða þas word spæcon, ða æteowde heom drihtines
engel & cwæð: Ne sceal eower word beon on ydelnysse, ac hit sceal mit
soðe beon icyðed, forþan þe witegan gearæ sædon, þæt heo
sceolde beon middaneardes cwen.
 549. Þa weron heo alle swiðe afyrhte for þæs engles
isihðe & his worde & heo ongunnon hire weorðian & hire
eadmodlice heran.
 568. Þa ilamp hit sume dæge, þæt heo stod be summere
welle.
 569. Þa æteowd hire þær drihtnes engel & hire to
cwæð: Eadig eart ðu maria, forþan ðe on ðine mode þu gearcost
drihtines eardunghus, & liht cymeð of heofene on ðe & ðæt
lihtæð ofer alne middaneard.
 576. & eft þæs on ðriddæ dage drihtines engel hire
æteowde mid sæcgendlicre beorhnysse & he þa wæs swiðe afyrhted
& abræged for þas englæs isihðe.
 581. Þa cwæð he to hire: Ne ðearft þu ðe ondredæn,
maria.
 582. Drihtenes gife is mid þe.
 583. Þu sceald kennen cyning, þe ah anweald heofenas &
eorðan, & his rices ne bið nan ende.
 588. On þa tid, þe ðis ilamp, wæs ioseph on þæ lande,
þe chapharnaum hatte, ymbe his creft.
 591. He wæs smið & monigteawe wurhtæ.
 592. Þa he þanon cyrde to his agene hame, þa imette he hire
bearn habbende on hire rife.
 595. Ða wæs he sonæ swiðe afurht & sorhful &
þus cwæð; Drihten, drihten min, onfoh min gast.
 598. Me is deaþ sælre, þone lif.
 598. Þa sædon him þa femnen, þe mid hire wæron,
þæt heo geare wistan, þæt hire nan wer ne onran, ac heo wære
andwealdes mægðhades & unwemmed.
 603. & we witon, þæt heo wæs dæges & nihtes on
halgum gebedum & godes engel wið hire spæc & heo dæghwamlice of
þæs engles handæ mete ðigde.
 607. Hu mæg þæt iwurdan, þæt þæt swa beo,
forþan þe we witon, þæt hit mon ne dyde, ac godes engel.
 610. Þa cwæð ioseph: Nis na þet na swa, nat ic, þeah heo
beo biswicen þurh þæs engles hiw.
 613. & he þa weop bitterlice & þus cwæd: Mid
hwilcere bealde mæg ic efre gan into godes temple oððe hu mæg ic
iseon þa onsyne þare sacerdæ for sceame.
 618. Þa he þus cwæð þa ðohte he digollice, þæt he
wolde hire forlæten & faren hi on oðer londe.
 624. Þa on þare ylcan nihte, þe he þis ðohte, æteowde
him godes engel on  slæpe & hi to cwæð: Ioseph, ne ðearft þu
ðe ondrædon.
 628. Þu eard dauides cynnes, onfoh þine imæccan.
 629. Hire eacnung is of þam halga gaste, & heo acennð sunu
& his nome is hælend, forþam ðe he dæð hal his folc fram heora
synnum.
 633. He þa ioseph aras of þam slæpe swiðe gefeonde &
gode ðancode & marian sæde & þam femnen, þe mid hire wæron,
þa fægræ sihðe þæs englæs & ða frofre ðare wordum
& þus cwæð: Ic syngode mid gemynde þæs facnes, þær nan
næs.
 643. Ða wearð æfter ðissum mycel lysa on þam folce,
þæt maria ieacnod wæs.
 645. Þa sume dæge nomæn hine þa ðegnæs þæs
temples & læddon hine to þam biscope & to þam heahsacerdon &
cwædon to him: To hwan forhæle þu us þine gemungæ swa clæne
femne, þe godes engles fædden swa swa culfræn on þam temple.
 653. & heo nolde næfre wære arinæn, ac heo wæs on
godes æ þe ityddeste fæmne.
 655. & gif þu hire nydes on ne sohtest, þone wære heo
clæne.
 657. He þa ioseph hine ladode & cwæð, þæt he hire
næfre ne arine.
 659. Þa biscopas þa & þa heahsacerdæs unarimodum
godcundre gerynæ be þaræ aldan æ acunnodæn soðlice, þæt
heo weron batwa clæne from alle þam synnum, þe ðet folc heom
oncuðe.
 665. Heo þa alle eadmodlice bæden hire bletsunge &
heoræ wohnysse forgifenysse, þæs ðe heo yfele wilnunge bi heom
hæfdon.
 668. & al þæt folc & þa sacerdæs læddon hire
mid þam femnem to iosepes hame mid mycele gefean.
 671. & mid mycelre blisse clypodon & þus cwædon: Beo
drihtines nome iblætsod on worulda woruld, þe ðe cyðlice cydde þine
halignesse on alle israele folcum.
 679. Wæs þeo halig femne, swa we ær sædon, of iesses
wyrttrumæ & of dauides cynne.
 681. & heo wæs drihtines moder, ure hælendes.
 682. Ant heo wæs hortfæt þæs halgan gastes.
 684. & heo is cwen þæs heofenlices kynges.
 685. & heo is englea hiht & allre monne, forþam ðe alle
middaneardes hæle þurh hire becom on ðas woruld.
 688. & forþan englæs hire nu eadigæð & alle
þeode & alle cneornyssæ, hwylc moncynnes ileaffulræ.
 691. & mid þisse blætsunge & herunge heo bicom biforen
gesihte alræ halgenæ, þær heo nu to dæghwamlice þingæþ for
alle þis mennisce cynn.
 695. Ac uton we hire nu eadmodlice biddan, þæt heo us beo
milde mundbore & bliþe þingestre to þam heofenlice mægenðrymme.
 699. Nu we geare witon, þæt heo mæg æt hire þan deore
sunæ biddæn, swa hwæt swa heo wyle, & beon þingere to ure
drihtene, þæt he us gife sibsum lif & ece eadignyssæ a buton ende.
 705. God us to þam fylste.
 705. Amen.

Nativity of Mary the Virgin (Oxford, Bodleian Library, MS. Hatton 114): Assmann 1889, 117-37 [J].



 1. <foreign>De Nativitate Sanctæ Mariæ</foreign>.
 2. Men ða leofestan.
 2. Weorþian we nu on andweardnysse þa gebyrdtide þære
eadigan fæmnan Sancta Marian.
 5. Seo wæs cennystre ures drihtnes hælendes Cristes.
 6. Nu is hyre nama gereht hlæfdige oððe cwen oððe
sæsteorra.
 8. Heo is hlæfdige gecweden, forðan þe heo cende þone
hlaford heofonas and eorðan.
 11. And heo is cwen gecweden, forðan þe heo com of ðam
æðelan cynne and of ðam cynelican sæde Davides cynnes.
 15. Sæsteorra heo is gecweden, forðan þe se steorra on niht
gecyþeð scypliðendum mannum, hwyder bið east and west, hwyder suð and
norð.
 19. Swa þonne wearð þurh ða halgan fæmnan Sancta Marian
gecyþed se rihte siðfæt to ðam ecan life þam ðe lange ær
sæton on þeostrum and on deaþes scuan and on þam unstillum yðum
þære sæ þises middaneardes.
 26. And a syððan wyston ealle halige þone fruman middaneardes
and ende and heofona rices wuldor and helle wite.
 30. Nu wille we eow secgan be ðære gebyrde þære eadigan
fæmnan Sancta Marian, hu seo geworden wæs and acenned.
 34. We habbað geræd on bocum, þæt wære sum swiðe
æþele wer on Israheliscum folce.
 36. Þæs nama wæs Ioachim.
 37. Se wæs of Iudan cynne and he wearð geboren on Galileiscre
scire on þære byrig, þe is gehaten Nazareth.
 41. Se wæs heorda his sceapa and he wæs godfyrht man on
bylewitnysse and on fremsumnysse, and he næfde nænige oðre gymene buton
his eowde.
 45. Of þam eowde ne fedde ealle þa ðe him drihten ondredon
and of ðam wæstmum he gode þryfealde lac gebrohte and ealle his æhta
on þreo todælde.
 50. Ænne dæl he sealde þearfan and wydewan and steopcildum
and ælþeodigum mannum and oðerne dæl he sealde þam þe gode ane
þeowodon.
 55. Ðone þriddan dæl he heold him sylfum and his hirede big
to lifigenne.
 57. Ða midþam þe he þas ðing wæs donde þus, þa
micclode god his woruldæhta, þæt on þa tid næs nan wer nim gelic
on Israhelum.
 61. Ðas þing he ongan don, þa þe he wæs fiftyne wintra.
 63. And midþam þe he hæfde twentig wintra, þa onfeng he
wif him to gemæccan.
 65. Seo wæs gehaten Anna and hyre cynn wæs on þære byrig
Bethleem.
 67. Seo wæs Achares dohtor of his agenum cynne, þæt is
þonne of ðam æþelan cynne Davides þæs cynincges.
 71. Hi ða wæron samod drohtniende ætgædere twentig
wintra, swa hi nan bearn ne begeaton.
 74. Ða gelamp hit sume dæge, þæt he eode to ðam
drihtnes temple, and he ða Ioachim gestod betwyx þam mannum, þe to gode
onsegednysse brohton, and he gearwode his gyfe on godes gesihðe.
 80. Him ða to genealæhte þara bocera sum, þæs nama
wæs Ruben, and cwæð him to: Nis þe alyfed, þæt ðu stande
betwyx þam mannum, þe gode onsegednysse bringað, forðan þe godes
bletsung ofer ðe ne com, þæt he þe ænig bearn asende.
 87. He ða þæs wæs myccle scame þrowiende beforan þam
folce for þisum wordum and he ða swa scamiende ut of ðam temple wepende
gewat.
 92. And he nolde þa eft to his agenum hame hweorfan, ac he gewat
on westenum to his sceapum and ða hyrdas nam mid him and ðær wunode fif
monþa fæce, swa þæt ðær nænig ærendraca betweonan ne ferde
him and his gemæccan.
 99. Ða ongann Anna, his gemæcca, wepende hi to drihtne
gebiddan and ðus cwæð: Min drihten Israhela god, þu ðe eart strang
and mihtig ofer ealle gesceafta, and ðu me noldest næfre bearn ofer
eorðan syllan and ðu minne wer me æt gename.
 106. And ic nat, hwæþer his lif is ofer eorðan; and gif he
forðgewiten is, þonne ne gegearwie ic him byrgene.
 110. Ða heo þas word gecweden hæfde, þa eode heo eft on
hire cauertune and hire eadmodlice to drihtne gebæd.
 113. And æfterðam þe heo hire gebed gefylled hæfde, þa
ahof heo hire eagan up to drihtne.
 116. Þa geseah heo spearwan nest on anum lawertreowe.
 118. Heo ða wependre stefne clypode to drihtne and cwæð:
Drihten, þu ælmihtiga god, þu sealdest eallum gesceaftum byrðor and hi
on þan gefeoð and ic þe nu þanc secge, þæt þu me ane ute
atyndest fram þinre gyfe þære fremsumnysse.
 125. Hwæt, þu min drihten canst and wast mine heortan.
 127. Hwæt, ic þe fram fruman mines gesinscipes gehet, gyf þu
me sealdest sunu oððe dohtor, þæt ic hi wolde þe gebringan to
þinum temple.
 131. Ða heo þas word gecweden hæfde, hwæt, þa hyre
ætywde drihtnes encgel and ðus cwæð: Ne ðearft ðu þe
ondrædan, Anna, forðan þe þin þrowung is on godes geþeahte.
 136. Þæt of ðe acenned bið, þæt bið on wundra
eallum folcum oð þæt woruldes ende.
 139. Þa midþam þe he þas word gecweden hæfde, þa
wæs he fram hyre eagum ahafen.
 142. Þa wæs heo swyðe forht geworden for ðæs engles
gesihðe.
 144. Heo hire þa gewat into hyre clyfan and ðær awunode
þone dæg and ða niht on hire gebede.
 147. Ða þæs on mergen þa gelaþode heo hyre þinene hire
to and cwæð: Hwæt, þu me gesawe on wydewanhade beswicene and on
mycelre nearonysse gesette and noldest me to frofre cuman?
 152. Ða andswarode heo hire ungeþwærlice and hire cwæð
to: ðeah þe god þinne wer æt þe gename and ðinne innoð beluce,
hwæt sceal ic þæs don?
 157. Ða þa heo ane þas word gehyrde, þa ongan heo biterlice
wepan.
 160. Hwæt, þa on þære ylcan tide ætywde him sum
swyðe wlitig wer on þam westene, þær þær he wæs mid his
hyrdum, and him cwæð to: For hwan nelt ðu ham gehweorfan to þinum
gemæccan?
 166. Ða cwæð he Ioachim: Twentig wintra ic wunode mid hyre
and me god nan bearn of hyre ne sealde.
 169. Ac ic swyðe geæswicod eode ut of ðam drihtnes temple;
forðan ic nylle eft ham gehweorfan, ac ic wylle her wunian þa hwile, þe
drihten wile, and ða godes gyfe for drihtnes naman dælan, swa ic ær
dyde.
 176. Ða andswarode him se iunga and cwæð: Ic eom drihtnes
encgel and nu to dæg ic me æteowde þinum gemæccan and hi gefrefrode,
þa þa heo hi wepende and geomriende to drihtne gebæd.
 182. And wite þu, þæt heo is of ðinum sæde geeacnod,
swa swa þu nystest, þa þa þu hi ana forlæte, and heo þe cenneð
dohtor and seo bið on godes temple fulfremed.
 187. And se halga gast resteþ on hyre, and hire eadignyss
astigeð ofer ealle wifa cynn, and hire ne bið gelic ænig þara þe
ær wæs oððe æfter.
 191. Cyr nu to þinum gemæccan and ðu gemetest hi geeacnode,
and ðu þæs gode þanc sege, forðan þe hyre sæd bið gebletsod
and heo bið modor þære ecan bletsunge geseted.
 197. Ða wurþode hine Ioachim and him cwæþ to: Gyf hit
þus gewurðan scule, swa þu cwyst, site mid me on minum huse and gebletsa
þinne þeow.
 201. Ða cwæð se encgel to him: Hwi wylt þu la cweðan,
þæt ðu sy min þeowa, ac þu eart min efenþeowa, forðan þe wit
syndon anes godes þeow.
 206. And ic þe secge, þæt min mete ne min drenc ne mæg
beon fram mannum gesewen.
 208. Ac swa hwæt swa þu me to gyfe tihhie, bring þæt gode
to onsægednysse.
 210. He þa Ioachim gode brohte unwemme lac and to ðam engle
cwæð: Næs ic na gedyrstig, þæt ic gode sacerdlice onsægednysse
brohte, þær þu me ne hete.
 215. Ða cwæþ se encgel: Na ic ðe ne hete gode sacerdlice
onsægednysse brohte, forðam gyf ic godes willan to þan on þe ne
ongeate.
 219. Ða gewat se encgel samod mid þam stence þære
onsægednysse into heofonum.
 222. He ða Ioachim wearð to þam forht, þæt he feoll on
his ansyn and læg swilce he dead wære fram þære sixtan tide þæs
dæges, oð þæt afen wæs.
 226. Him þa to genealæhton his hyrdas and hi hine þa gesawon
licgan and nyston þone intingan on him, ac ahofen hine up, and hi wendon,
þæt he wolde hine sylfne acwellan.
 232. Ða ahof he his heafod up and he him asæde þa his
gesihðe, þe he geseah.
 234. Ða wurdon hi sona afyrhte and eac wundrodon, oð þæt
he heom eall asæd hæfde; and hi ða ealle hine trymedon and lærdon,
þæt he gehyrsum wære þæs engles wordum and þæt he hraþe
gehwyrfde ham to his gemæccan.
 241. He ða Ioachim þreodode and smeade on his mode, hwæt he
embe þæt dyde.
 243. Þa wearð he færinga on slæpe gehwyrfed.
 245. Him þa eft ætywde se ylca godes encgel on slæpe and
him to cwæð: Ic eom godes encgel and fram drihtne ic eom þe to hyrde
geset.
 249. Ac gewit nu ham orsorh to ðinum gemæccan and ingcer
mildheortnyss, þe gyt worhten, is beforan godes gesihðe and ingcer nama
wæs gesædd beforan godes gesihðe on his þrymsetle.
 255. And he drihten ingc syleð swa myccle grownysse on ingcran
beorðre, swa he næfre nænigan halgan ær ne sealde, ne nu eft ne
syllað.
 260. He þa Ioachim of þam slæpe aras and his swefen sæde
his hyrdum.
 262. Hi ða ealle hine bædon and halsedon, þæt he
gehyrsumode þæs engles wordum and ricene ham gecyrde.
 265. Ða wæs he ær gegan for his unrotnysse on þam westene
to ðam feor, þæt he for <foreign>XXX</foreign> daga fæc ne mihte ham to his
gemæccan gehweorfan.
 270. Heo þa Anna wæs æt hyre gebede, þa ætywde hyre
drihtnes encgel and hyre gecigde þone hamsið hyre gemæccan.
 274. And heo ða mid hyre hyrede him ongean ferde mid mycclum
gefean; swylce eac hyre mægðe and eall Israhela bearn mycelne gefean
hæfdon be his hamcyme and be ðam hlisan hire geeacnunge.
 281. Hwæt, þa æfterþan wæron gefylde nigan monað
hire geeacnunge, þa cende Anna hyre dohtor on þissum dæge and hyre naman
gecigde Maria, and heo hi ða fedde þreo winter æt hire breostum.
 287. Ioachim þa and Anna læddon þæt cild mid heom to
þære halgan ceastre and ða lac brohton mid heom to ðam drihtnes
temple, þe Iudea gewuna wæs.
 292. And hi ða sealdon þæt cild on gemanan þære
fæmnena, þe dæges and nihtes on godes lofe wunodon.
 295. Heo þa up eode mid þam oðrum fæmnum on þa fiftyne
stæpas on þam temple, swa heo on bæc ne beseah, ne æfter hyre yldrum
ne murnde, swa swa cildra gewuna is.
 300. Ac heo wæs on gange and on worde and on eallum gebærum
gelic wynsuman men, þe hæfde <foreign>XXX</foreign> wintra, and heo geornlice and
eadmodlice þurhwunode on hyre gebede, oð þæt þa biscopas and eall
þæt folc wundrodon on hire gebære.
 309. Heo Anna þa, Sancta Marian modor, wæs gefylled mid halige
gaste and witegode þa beforan þam folce and ðus cwæþ: Drihten
ælmihtig god wæs gemyndig his worda, þe he sylfa cwæð, ðæt he
wolde his folc gesecan mid haligre geneosunge.
 317. And ða þeode, þe wið us arisan, he wolde geeadmedigan,
þæt hi gecyrdon to heora sylfra heortan and heora earan ontynon to urum
benum, and ða bysmernyssa ura feondum fram us acerron.
 322. On ðam mundbyrdum ecre blisse tuddor forgeafon on Israhelum,
swa me min drihten forgeaf, þæt ic mot gode gecweme lac bringan, ær me
mine fynd ascufon fram þære halgan onsegednysse for minre
unwæstmberendnysse.
 329. Drihten min acerde him fram me and me forgeaf ecne gefean.
 332. Ða heo þas word gecweden hæfde, þa cyrdon hi ham mid
þam and þæt cild forleton æt ðam halgan temple mid oðrum
fæmnum.
 336. Heo ða weox and wearð fulfremed on godra mægna
heanyssum, and heo ða sona godum towcræftum onfeng, swyðor þonne
ænig þara þe heora bearn wæron wifa and fæmnena.
 341. And heo gesette hyre sylfre haligne regol, swa þæt heo
wolde beon fram þære ærestan tide þæs dæges on hyre halgum
gebedum wuniende oð þæt ða þriddan tid and fram þære þriddan
tide oð ða nigoþan tid ymbe hyre webbgeweorc.
 348. And eft fram þære nigoðan tide heo þurhwunode
standende on hyre gebedum, oð þæt godes encgel hyre ætywde and hyre
brohte heofonlice swetnysse and heo onbirigde þære of his handa.
 354. And heo syðþan wæs betere and swyðre on godes lufan
and on gastlicra mægna heannyssum, and heo yldran fæmnan lærde to
godes willan and heo wæs getyddre and snotere on þære godes æ,
þonne ænig þæra þe hyre beforan wæs.
 362. Heo wæs eadmodre and on godes lufan glæddre and on hyre
geþohtum clænre and on ðam davidiscum sangum wrætlicre and wisra,
þonne heora ænig ær wære.
 367. Heo wæs þolemod and gestæðþig on hire gebæran
and ne geseah hi nan man yrre, ne tælan, ne wyrigean, ne nan man ne gehyrde
yfel word of hyre muðe gan.
 371. Ac hyre word wæron godes gyfe full and heo wæs on hyre
heortan smeagende þone wisdom godes boca.
 375. And ða fæmnan, þe mid hyre wæron, heo getrymde,
þæt hi on heora gebedum þurhwunedon and on godes lofa and þæt heora
nan stefne up ne ahofe on idlum leahtre, ne hy on heora tungan teonan ne
cwæden, ne nan yfel word of heora muþe ut ne eode.
 383. And of heom aras ærest se gewuna, þæt se man, se ðe
oþerne mid lufan gegrete, þæt he him godcunde bletsunge ongean sende.
 387. And dæghwamlice heo onfeng mete of ðæs engles hande
and mid þam gereordod wæs, and ðone mete, þe heo æt þam bisceope
onfeng æt ðam temple, heo gedælde þearfendum mannum.
 393. And swa hwilc man swa hi untrum gesohte, eft he eode hal fram
hire.
 396. Ða gelamp hit, þæt Abiathar, se sacerd, brohte myccle
gyfe þam bisceope and bæd hine, þæt he gesealde Marian his sunu to
gemæccan.
 400. Ða styrde Maria him and cwæð anrædlice: Ne gewurð
þæt næfre swa, þæt ic wer grete oððe wer me.
 403. Ða andwyrdan þa biscopas hyre and hyre mægðe on þam
temple and cwædan: God wæs on bearnum begangan and on eaforan
weorþað, swa þæt gewunelic wæs on godes folce Israhelum.
 409. Ða andwyrde Maria and him cwæð to: Næs nan rihtwis
man, ne nan halig ær Abel, and hine arleaslice his broðor ofsloh.
 413. He brohte twyfealde gyfe drihtne hluttre onsegednysse and his
lichaman clænnysse.
 416. Swylce eac Helias wæs on þissere worulde, ac he wearð
alæded mid lichaman and mid sawle to heofonum, forðan þe he his
clænnysse geheold.
 421. Ða wæs heo, swylce heo wære <foreign>XIV</foreign> wintra.
 422. Ða gedemdon þa Phariseas, þæt heo syððan wunian
sceolde on þam godes temple.
 425. Hy ða geþeahtodon, þæt hi Israhela folc gelaðodon
to ðam godes temple þy þriddan dæge.
 428. Ða þa hy þider gesamnod wæron, þa astah se
heahbiscop Isachar up on þone ytemestan stæpe, clypode þa hluddre stefne
and ðus cwæð: Gehyrað nu, Israhela bearn, mine word.
 434. Hwæt, ge witon, þæt Salomon þis tempel getimbrode
and her wæron syðþan inne cyninga bearn and witegena and heahsacerda,
oð þæt hi becomon to ælicre ylde.
 439. And hi gelimplice heora yldran wæron gehyrsume to ælicum
gyftum and heora bearn eft gode lac brohton swyðe gecweme to þam godes
temple and on heora yldrena endebyrdnysse gode gecwemdon.
 445. Nu is þonne gemeted, þæt Maria hæfð niwe
endebyrdnysse ongunnon gode mid to gecwemanne, cweð, þæt heo wile hire
mægðhad bringan.
 450. Nu þonne uton secan þa andsware to gode ure axunge,
þæt god us gecyðe, hwilcum wære we hi befæstan sculon to
healdenne.
 454. Ða gelicode þæt word þære gesamnunge and hy ða
asenden hlota ofer þa <foreign>XII</foreign> cyn Israhela.
 457. Ða gefeoll þæt hlot ofer Iudan cyn, Iacobes sunu.
 458. Ða bebead se sacerd, þæt þæt Iudan cynn come eall
þæs on mergen to ðam halgan temple, ælc þæra þe wif næfde,
and hæfde him gyrda on handa.
 463. Ða wæs þonon geworden, þæt Ioseph wæs gehaten
sum gewintrod man, eode þyder mid iungum mannum and his gyrde bær.
 467. Þa genam se sacerd ealle þa gyrde and bær into þam
Sancta Sanctorum and bebead, þæt hi comon þæs on mergen and name
ælc his gyrde, and ðonne sceolde culfre fleogan of þære gyrde
foreweardre up oð þone heofon.
 474. Þonne sceolde se wer beon hyrde þære fæmnan.
 476. Ða wæs geworden on mergen þæs æfteran dæges,
þæt hi comon ealle on þa tid þære onsægednysse, and he ða inn
eode se biscop into þam Sancta Sanctorum, wæs þæt þære haligra
halignys ealra, and he ða genam þa gyrde and sealde heora æghwilcum his
gyrd on sundran.
 485. Þa wæs þæra manna þreo þusenda, ac ða of nan
þara gyrda seo culfre ne eode.
 487. Ða gegyrede hine Abiathar se biscop mid þare heahsacerda
gegyrlan and eode into ðam Sancta Sanctorum and onbærnde þa onsegednysse
and his bene to drihtne sende.
 492. Ða ætywde him drihtnes encgel and him cwæð to: Seo
seleste gyrd is gyt unseald, seo þe þu for naht ne telest.
 496. Nim þa and syle, þonne cymð þæt tacen of hyre, þe
þu þær setest.
 498. Wæs þæt Iosepes gyrd.
 499. Ða næs he na gesoht, forðan þe he wæs eald and
ytemest stod.
 501. Ða clypode se biscop mid mycelre stefne hine and cydde him
þæt, and he ða sona onfeng þæra gyrda of ðæs bisceopes
handum.
 505. Hwæt, þær of sona fleah culfre swyðe hwit and geond
fleah þa heannysse þæs temples and heo ða gewat into heofonum.
 509. Ða wæs þæt folc fægniende and swyðe bliðe and
cwædon to Iosepe: Eadig eart ðu on þinre ylde, nu þe god swa
gewurðode, þæt ðu scealt beon hyrde þære clænan fæmnan.
 515. Eac swylce þa biscopas cwædon: Onfoh hyre nu, forðan
þe þu eart ana gecoren on þinum cynne hyre to hyrde fram gode.
 519. He ða Ioseph cwæð mid bifiendre stefne: Nis min gemet
swilcum cilde to onfonne, forðan þe ic hæbbe fela bearna and ða synd
ealle yldran þonne heo.
 523. Ða cwæð se biscop to him: Gemune þu, hu hit gelamp be
Dathan, hu he forwearð and manega eac þa ðe godes willan forhogodon.
 528. Ða cwæð he Ioseph: Ne forhycge ic na godes willan, ac
ic hy gehealde, oð þæt ic ongyte godes willan on hyre and god þonne
gecyþeð, hwilc iungra manna on minum cynne hyre wurðe bið.
 534. Ac syle þam clænan fæmnan fultum, þæt heo wunigen
mid hig oð þæt ælice yldo.
 536. Ða cwæð se biscop: Fæmnan beoð hyre on fultume
oð þæne dæg eowra gemænunga, and ne mæg hig nan oðer onfon.
 540. Ða onfeng Ioseph hi mid oðrum fæmnum, þe hyre
wæron on fultume geseald to Iosepes hame.
 543. Ða wæron þus gehatene, ærest Becca, Sephira,
Susanna, Abugea and Sehel.
 545. And se biscop sealde heom eallum godweb to wefanne of seolce
and of mislicum hiwum wahrift to þam temple.
 549. Ða onfeng Maria hwit godweb to wefanne and ða oðre
mislices hiwes.
 551. Ða spræcon hi heom betwynan on gleo and ðus cwædon:
þu eart ure gingast, þe miht wefan þæt hwite godeweb, and ðu miht
beon ure cwen.
 556. Ða þa hi þas word spræcon on gleo, ða ætywde
heom drihtnes encgel and cwæð: Ne sceal eower word beon on idelnyssa, ac
hit sceal beon mid soðe gecyþed, forðan þe witegan geare sædon,
þæt heo scolde beon middaneardes cwen.
 563. Ða wæron hi ealle swiðe forhte for ðæs engles
gesihðe and his worde and ongunnon hi wurþian and hyre eadmodlice hyran.
 568. Þa gelamp hit sume dæge, þæt heo stod be sumere
wyllan.
 570. Þa ætywde þær drihtnes encgel and cwæð hyre to:
Eadig þu eart Maria, forðan on þinum mode þu gearwodest drihtnes
eardunghus, and leoht cymð of heofonum on ðe and þæt lihteð ofer
ealne middaneard.
 576. Ða eft þæs þriddan dæges drihtnes heahencgel hyre
ætywde mid unasecgendlicre beorhtnysse and heo ða wæs swyðe afyrht
and abreged for ðæs engles gesihðe.
 581. Ða cwæð se encgel to hyre: Ne þearftu ðe
ondrædan, Maria.
 584. Drihtnes gifu is mid þe.
 584. Þu scealt acennan cyning, se ah anweald heofonas and
eorðan, and his rice ne bið nan ende.
 588. On þa tid, þe þis gelamp, wæs Iosep on þam lande,
þe Cafarnaum hatte, ymbe his cræft.
 591. He wæs smið and mænigteawa wyrhta.
 592. Ða þa he þanon gecyrde to his agenum hame, þa gemette
he hi bearn hæbbende on hire gehrife.
 595. Ða wæs he sona swyðe forht and sorhfull on his mode and
ðus cwæð: Drihten, drihten min, onfoh minum gaste.
 598. Me is deað selre, þonne lif.
 599. Ða cwædon þa fæmnan him to, þe mid hyre wæron,
þæt hi geare wiston, þæt hyre nan wer ne onhran, ac heo wære
onwelges mægðhades and unwemme.
 604. And we witon, þæt heo wæs dæges and nihtes on
halgum gebedum wuniende and godes encgel wið hyre spræc and heo
dæghwamlice of ðæs engles handum mete þigde.
 609. Hu mæg þæt gewurðan, þæt þæt sy swa,
forðan þe we witon, þæt hit man ne dyde, ac godes encgel.
 613. Ða cwæð he Ioseph: Nis þæt na swa, nat ic, þeah
heo beo beswicen þurh þæs engles hiw.
 615. And he ða weop biterlice and ðus cwæð: Mid hwylcre
byldu mæg ic æfre gan to godes temple oððe hu mæg ic geseon þa
ansyne þara sacerda for sceame.
 621. Ða þa he þus cwæð, þa þohte he digollice,
þæt he wolde hy forlæton and faran him on oðer land.
 624. Ða on þære ilcan nihte, þe he þis þohte, þa
ætywde him godes encgel onslæpe and cwæð to him: Ioseph, ne þearft
þu ðe ondrædan.
 628. Þu eart Davides cynnes, onfoh þinne gemæccan.
 629. Hyre geeacnung is of ðam halgan gaste, and heo cenneð sunu
and ðæs nama is hælend, forðam þe he gedeð hal his folc fram
heora synnum.
 634. He þa Ioseph aras of ðam slæpe swyðe gefeonde and
swyðe bliðe and gode þancode and Marian sæde and þam fæmnum, þe
mid hyre wæron, þa fægran gesyhðe þæs engles and ða frofre
þara worda and ðus cwæþ: Ic singode and gemunde þe facnes, þær
nan næs.
 643. Ða wearð æfter þisum mycel hlysa on þam folce,
þæt Maria wæs geeacnod.
 645. Ða sume dæge namon hine þa þegnas þæs temples
and læddon hine to ðam biscope and to þam heahsacerdum and cwædon to
him: To hwan forhæle ðu us þine gemænunge swa clænre fæmnan,
þe godes englas hy feddan swa swa culfran on þam temple.
 653. And heo næfre nolde were æthrinan, ac heo wæs on
godes æ seo getydeste fæmne, and gyf ðu nedinga hyre on ne sohtest,
þonne wære heo clæne.
 658. He ða Iosep hine ladode and cwæð, þæt he hyre
næfre ne æthrine.
 660. Hwæt, þa biscopas and ða heahsacerdas on unarimdum
godcundre geryna be ðære ealdan æ acunnodan soðlice, þæt hio
wæren butu clæne fram eallum þam synnum, þe þæt folc hi
oncuðe.
 666. Hi ða ealle eadmodlice bædon hyre mildse and heora
wohnyssa forgyfennyssa, þæs þe hi þæs unrihtes hy oncuðan.
 670. And hi and eall þæt folc and ða sacerdas læddon hi
mid þam fæmnum to Iosepes hame mid micclum gefean.
 673. And mid mycelre blisse clypodon and ðus cwædon: Sy
drihtnes nama gebletsod on worulda woruld, se ðe cuðlice gecydde þine
halignyssa on eallum Israhela folce.
 679. Wæs seo halige fæmne, swa we ær cwædon, of Iesses
wyrtruman and of Davides cynne.
 681. And heo wæs drihtnes modor, ures hælendes.
 683. And heo is hordfæt þæs halgan gastes and heo is cwen
þæs heofonlican cyninges gecweden.
 686. And heo is engla hiht and ealra manna frofor and fultum,
forðan þe ealles middaneardes hælo þurh hi becom on þas woruld.
 689. And forðan hi nu englas eadigað and ealle þeoda and
ealle cneorissa, gehwylc mancynnes geleafulra.
 693. And mid þisra bletsunga and herenyssa heo becom beforan
þæt þrymsetl þæs heofonlican deman and beforan gesyhðe ealra
haligra, þær heo nu dæghwamlice þingað for eall þis mennisce
cynn.
 699. Ac uton we nu hi eadmodlice biddan, þæt heo us si milde
mundbora and bliðe þingere to ðam heofonlican mægnþrymme.
 703. Nu we geare witan, þæt heo mæg æt hire þam deoran
sunu biddan, swa hwæt swa heo wile, and beon ðingere to urum drihtne,
þæt he us forgyfe gesibsum lif and ece eadignysse a butan ende.
 709. God us to ðam gefultumige.
 710. Amen.
