LS 19 (PurifMaryVerc 17)
B3.3.19.
Purification of Mary the Virgin: Scragg 1992, 281-6.



 0. <foreign>De purificatione sancta Maria</foreign>.
 1. Men þa leofestan, sægeð us & myngaþ þis halige
godspel be þysse arwyrðan tide þe we nu todæge Gode ælmihtigum to
lofe & to are wyrðiaþ.
 3. þæt is se feowertiga dæg nu todæg ures dryhtnes
hælendes Cristes acennesse, & þy dæge þæt his aldoras hine
brohton in Hierusalem in þa mæran burg, þæt hie hine Gode agefon, swa
swa hit awriten is in dryhtnes naman þæt æghwylc wæpned cildbearn
þe wif ærest acynde sceolde beran ærest Gode gehalgod.
 7. & þa cwomon dryhtnes aldoras to ðam Godes temple &
hie ðær Gode ælmihtigum asægdnesse brohton, swa hit be þan awriten
is in dryhtnes naman þæt hie sceoldon þær bringan to þam temple
twegen turturas oððe twegen culfran briddas, Gode ælmihtigum to lofe
& to wyrðunge to ðam Godes temple.
 12. Ðær wæs þa sum eald man in Hierusalem in þære
byrig in þa ilcan tid se wæs haten Simeon.
 13. He wæs soðfæst & rihtwis, & he bead þære
frefre þære þe he wiste þæt he his folce gehaten hæfde.
 15. & se halga gast wæs mid þone Simeon.
 15. & he þære andsware onfeng fram þam halgan gaste,
& he him cydde & sægde þæt he ne moste deaðes byrigan ær
he mid his eagum dryhten gesege.
 17. He ða cwom þurh haliges gastes gife in þæt Godes templ
on þa ilcan tid þe Cristes aldoras hine þyder brohton, & he þa
þæt dyde beforan him þone ilcan gewunan þe he ær dyde in þære
ealdan æ.
 20. & þa genam se halga Simeon þone hælend on his
earmas, & he hine mid bam handum beclypte, & he hine mid eallre
modlufan sette to his breostum, & he bledsode & wuldrade God fæder
ælmihtigne, & he ðus cwæð: Min dryhten, forlæt þinne þegen
in sybbe faran þa, æfter þinum wordum swa ðu him ær gehehtest, for
ðan, dryhten, mine eagan gesegon þa hælo þe ðu gearwadest to onsyne
eallra folca, & to frofre eallum þeodum & to wuldre þines folces,
Israhela bearnum.
 28. Us is nu to witane, men þa leofestan, þæt for þan
Cristes aldoras þy feowertigan dæge hine brohton to þam Godes temple for
þan þe ðæt wæs þeaw & Godes bebod.
 30. þæt wæs in þære Godes æ þæt swa hwylc wif
swa bearn cende, þæt heo ne moste in þæt Godes templ ingangan ær
ðan feowertigan dæge wære, ac heo sceolde on þam fæce gebidan to
clænsunge hire lichoman.
 33. & þonne þy feowertigan dæge wære, heo þonne
sceolde þæt bearn gebringan to þam Godes temple.
 35. For þan þe ealle wif þe tymende syndon hie sendon on
þam bebodum, þe sancta Maria, Cristes moder.
 36. For ðan seo eadigu cwen sancta Maria, heo clæne abad
þæs feowertigan dæges, nalles þæt heo þæs ænige þearfe
hæfde þæt heo swylc wære on clænnesse hire lichaman, se ðe
þurh æghwæt mid godcunde gestihtunge & mid lifes geearnunge
geclænsod wæs & þurh haliges gastes gife, for ðan þe heo wæs
unmælu & clæne butan eallum synnum, & heo in clænnesse
mægðhade a ðurhwunode, & Crist acende, & æfter þære
acennesse heo a ðurhwunode in clænnesse mægðhade.
 43. & heo eac for þam brohte Crist in þa tid to þam Godes
temple/ þæt heo wolde þæt þæt word wære gefylled þe Crist
cwæð: Ne cwom ic to þam in worulde þæt ic Godes æ towurpe &
tobræce, ac ic cwom to þan þæt ic hie gefylde & getrymede.
 47. Men þa leofestan, us is nu eac to witanne þære burge
naman þe is genemned Hierusalem, þæt is þonne on ure geþeode gereht
sybbe gesyhðe.
 49. Swa þonne bið symble þam soðfæstum & þam
godfyrhtum mannum in sybbe, him bið gegearwad ece lean & ece hælo
& ece gefea & ece blis, & þam mannum þe mid sybbe & mid
geleafan & mid godes willan cumað oft to Godes temple, þæt is
þonne to þære halgan Godes cirican.
 53. & hie sylfe þær Gode ælmihtigum & his ðam
halgan him sylfum bebeodaþ mid halgum gebedum, & hie Godes naman heriað
& wuldriaþ, & hie to him mildheortnesse & forgifnesse biddaþ
& ece reste æfter þysse worulde & eac þysse anweardra
gesyhðe.
 57. & hie þurh þæt geearniaþ æt Gode ælmihtigum
þæt hie moton becuman to þære soðan sybbe gesyhðe, ðæt is
þonne to ures dryhtnes hælendes Cristes.
 59. For þan, men þa leofestan, us gedafenað þæt we
symble in ealle tid rihte lufan & sybbe betweonan us sylfum hæbben we
& healden þæt in us, þurh þæt sy gefylled þæt dryhten sylf
cwæð be þam gesybsumum mannum: Eadige beoð þa gesybsuman men for
þan þe hie beoð Godes bearn genemde.
 64. Broðor mine, us is eac to witanne þæt þæt wæs
þearfendra manna asægdnesse in þære ealdan æ þæt hie sceoldon
þy dæge bringan twegen turturas oððe twegen culfran briddas Gode to
æsægdnesse.
 67. Swylce asægdnesse Cristes aldoras hine mid brohton to þam
Godes temple.
 68. In þan wæs getacnod þæt ure hælenda Crist for ure
lufan wæs þearfende in middangearde, þæt he us eac for his
mildheortnesse eadige & welige & mihtige gedyde on his ðam ecan
rice.
 70. & he for ure lufan astah of heofonum to eorðan, & he
manige ehtnesse & costunge & wiðerweardnesse æt mannum gedreah,
& æt nehstan deað geþrowade for ure lufan & for mancynnes lufan
þære myclan neodþearfe, & to þan þæt he us eac alysde fram
ece deaðe þæt is of helle wite.
 74. & he us eac forgeaf ece lif & ece reste in þære
toweardan worulde, gif we hit mid godum dædum & mid ellenworcum æt
him geearnian willaþ.
 77. & þa fugelas þe we ðær ær gehyrdon nemnan,
þæt syndon þonne turturas & culfran, hie getacniaþ lifes
clænnesse & unsceðfulnesse.
 79. Swa we sculon eac beon in urum life clæne &
unsceððende, þæt be us sie rihtlice þæt word gecweden þæt in
þam halgan godspelle awriten is & gecweden: Eadige bioð þa clænan
mildheortan men, for þan þe God gesyhð heora heortan clænnesse.
 82. Eac we sculon habban mid us Godes soðfæstnesse & his
rihtwisnesse & eaðmodnesse, swa we ær gehyrdon secgan þæt se
eadiga Simeon wæs soðfæst & clæne & godfyrht on his life.
 85. Soðlice he hæfde lifes clænnesse gehealden, ge in
wordum ge in dædum ge in geðohtum & eac in gesiehðe, for ðan him
sægde se halga gast þæt he ne moste deaðes byrian ær þan þe he
meahte mid his eagan dryhten geseon, þone þe ær ealle Godes witigan
toweardne mancynne bodedon & mærsedon, & þæt openlice sægdon
þæt he, þurh haliges gastes inbyrdnesse, þæt he hider cuman wolde
to his folce, to frofre & to hælo & to ælcre alysnesse eallum
þeodum þam þe soðlice in Gode ælmihtigne gelyfan wolde.
 93. Men þa leofestan, we gehyrdon ær in þyssum halgan
godspelle secgan þæt se eadiga Simeon his anes hælo ne bæd he, ac he
bæd ealles folces hælo & frofre & þa he gebeden hæfde.
 95. On ðam he getacnode þæt we sceoldon beon swylces modes
& swylces gewittes & on swylcre willan swa we oðrum mannum unnen,
& we þæt in godum dædum fromigen, þæt we hie þurh þæt
geearnian magon & begitan ða ece hælo & þæt ece lif, &
þæt we sculon, mid þy gewitte & mid þy wisdome þe us God forgeaf
& forgifen hafað, þæt we magon & moton & cunnen & mid
godra bysena dæda & mid godra þeawa forðlædan & læran
þæt we georne to Godes ælmihtiges willan & to his ðam halgan
& eac to ure sawle ræde for Gode & for worulde.
 103. Healdan we eac þæt mid godum dædum & mid
æðelum mancystum þæt we beon godum mannum gelice, in ðam mægenum
þe we don magon & in ðam dædum þe we þurhteon magon, þæt we
þurh ðæt þæs wyrðe syn þæt we Gode ælmihtigne mid godum
dædum & mid wordum herian & wuldrian & bletsian, swa se eadiga
Simeon Gode ælmihtigne gebledsode, & he ðus cwæð: <foreign>Nunc dimittis
seruum tuum, domine, secundum uerbum tuum in pace; quia uiderunt oculi mei
salutare tuum, domine</foreign>.
 111. He swa cwæð: Læt nu, dryhten, faran in sybbe þine
þegnas æfter þinum wordum swa ðu him ær gehehtest.
 112. Efne swa he cwæde: Læt me faran of þære tyddernesse
þysses meniscan lichaman þe ic nu git on eom; læt me geendian þis
deaðlic lif, & læt me becuman to þam ecan life & to þære
ecan reste þe ðu þinum þam gecorenum & þam halgum gegearuwad
hafast.
 116. For ðan þe ic þære andsware onfenc þæt ic ne
moste deaðes byrian ær þan ic ðe, dryhten, mid minum eagum gesege.
 118. & nu gesegon mine eagan þine hælo ða ðe ðu
geearuwadest to leohte & to frofre manigum þeodum & to wuldre þines
folces.
 121. Soðlice ure hælend is ðæt soðe leoht &
þæt soðe ece se ðe inlihteð ælcne mannan ðe in middangeard
cymeð.
 122. & eall mancynn he gebyrhteð & inlihteð mid his
þrymmes mihte & mid his wuldre.
 123. For þan englas hine heredon & wuldredon & him lof
sægdon æt his acennesse & ðus cwædon: Wuldor si ðe, Gode, in
heannesse, & in earðan & sib þam mannum þe synd godes willan
wyrcende.
 126. Þa cyrdon þa englas to ure sybbe & to ure lufan, þa
hie gesegon & ongeaton ðæt dryhten Crist wæs gecyrred &
ymbesald mid mennissce lichoman.
 129. Þonne, men þa leofestan, þeah is swiðe mycel
nydþearf þæt we us in æghwylce tide beon wið synnum & uncystum
gestilde, & þeah hwæðre eallra swiðost & betst us gedafenaþ
þæt we clænlice & haliglice lifigen æt Cristes tidum & on
his þara haligra tid, þonne we þæt secgan gehyran, & eac ure sawle
frætwian mid godum dædum & mid halgum gebedum, & us eac georne
& wislice healden þæt us eac nænig synna on us ne mæge findan,
ne on wordum ne on dædum ne on geþohtum ne on nænigum þingum.
 136. Ac æghwylc man hine sylfne healde & clænsie in
rihtwisnesse & in clænnesse his lifes, þa lytlan hwile þe we her his
brucan moton.
 139. Ac utan we nu for þan, broðor mine, herian we urne dryhten
hælende Crist & hine wuldrian & wyrðian in halgum wordum & in
clænum geþohtum & in clænum dædum, & him þanc secgan
eallra his goda & his gifena & eallra his læna & eallra his
mildheortnessa ðe he us gedon hafað oððe deð oððe nu gyt forð
don wile.
 143. Don we him symle þancas of urum spedum, for þan þe he us
ontynde heofona rices duru þurh his þa halgan acennesse ðe he ða
menniscan lichoman onfencg, & for þam he feala adreah for us, & he
æt neahstan deað geþrowode for mancynnes lufan & hælo, &
þurh þæt he hie alysde of deofles þeowdome & of his anwalde.
 148. Biddan we nu urne dryhten ælmihtigne & sancta Marian
þæt he us forgife for his mildheortnesse & for his þa halgan lufan,
þæt he us þæs wyrðe læte beon þæt we synd gelædde on his
þam halgan rice, þær us bið afyrred æghwylc yfel fram &
æghwylce yrmþo.
 152. & we þær habbað a soðe sybbe & soðe lufan
in ecnesse & soðne gefean & ecne eard & ece wuldor mid hine &
mid his þam halgum, a in eallra worulda woruld a butan ende, <foreign>in sæcula
sæculorum, amen</foreign>.

LS 20 (AssumptMor)
B3.3.20.
Assumption of Mary the Virgin: Morris 1874-80, 137-59.



 1. Men ða leofestan, gehyraþ nu hwæt her segþ on þissum
bocum be þære halgan fæmnan Sancta Marian, hu be hire on þas tid
geworden wæs.
 3. Heo wæs wæccende dæges & nihtes & hie
gebiddende æfter Drihtnes upstige.
 4. Þa com hire to Drihtnes engel & he wæs cweþende, Aris
þu Maria & onfoh þissum palmtwige þe ic þe nu brohte, for þan
þu bist soþlice ær þrim dagum genumen of þinum lichoman, & ealle
Drihtnes apostolas beoþ sende þe to bebyrgenne.
 8. Þa cwæþ Maria to þæm engle, Hwæt is þin nama?
 9. Þa cwæþ se engel to hire, Hwæt secestu minne naman,
forþon he is mycel & wundorlic?
 11. Þa Sancta Maria þis gehyrde þa astah heo on þone munt
þe wæs nemned Oliuete.
 12. & þæt wæs soþlice swiþe scinende palmtwig &
hit wæs þa swa leoht swa se mergenlica steorra, þe heo þær onfeng
of þæs engles handa.
 14. Þa wæs heo swiþe wynsumiende & mid mycle gefean
gewuldrad.
 15. & ealle þa þe þær wæron hie gesawon þæt se
engel þe ær com to hire astah on heofenas mid myclum leohte.
 17. Þa wæs Maria eft hweorfende to hire huse, & heo þa
alegde þæt palmtwig mid ealre eaþmodnesse, þe heo ær onfeng of
þæs engles handa.
 19. & heo eac alegde hire hrægl þe heo mid gegyred wæs,
& þwoh hire lichoman.
 20. & heo hie gegyrede mid þon selestan hrægle & þa
wæs swiþe gefeonde & swiþe blissigende, & bletsode god &
wæs cweþende, <foreign>Benedico nomen tuum et laudabile in secula seculorum</foreign>; Ic
bletsige þinne þone halgan naman, forþon þe he is mycel &
hergendlic in worlda world.
 25. Ic þe bidde min Drihten þæt þu sende ofer me þine
bletsunga.
 26. Þa wæs Maria cweþende, Mid þy þe þu me hate of
minum lichoman gewitan, þonne onfoh þu minre sawle.
 28. Þa wæs se engel cweþende, Ne beo þu, Maria,
geunreted.
 29. Mid þy þe heo þis gehyrde, þa wæs heo cleopigende
& cegende ealle hire magas þa þe þær neah wæron, & wæs
cweþende, Gehyraþ me nu ealle, & gelyfaþ ge ealle on God Fæder
ælmihtigne, forþon þys morgenlican dæge ic beo gangende of minum
lichoman & ic gange to minum Gode.
 34. & ic bidde eow ealle þæt ge anmodlice wacian mid me
oþ þa tid þe on þæm dæge biþ mines gewinnes ende.
 35. & mid þy þe heo þis gecweden hæfde, þa com
þær sona se eadega.
 37. Dura ðæra halgan Marian, & hie gesawon be him tweonum
þæt heo wæs gewuldrod.
 38. & hie þa haletton on hie & hie cwædon, <foreign>Deo
gratias</foreign>, forðon we wæron todæge ealle on annesse gemedemode.
 40. Forðon is soðlice se cwide gefylled Dauides ðæs witgan
þe he cwæð, <foreign>Ecce quam bonum et quam iocundum habitare fratres in unum</foreign>,
Hu good is & hu wynsum þæt mon eardige on ðara gebroðra annesse.
 43. & þa cwæð hira ælc to oðrum, uton gebiddan us
to urum Drihtne þæt he us þæt cuþ gedo þæt he us todæge
wolde on ðisse tide gesomnian.
 46. Þa cwæð Petrus to Paule, Broðor Pawlus, aris þu
& gebide þe ær, forðon þu eart leohtes swer.
 47. &, ealle þa þe ymbe me standaþ hie hie syndan betran
þonne ic & þu eart forelærende on ðara apostola gebede, & þu
eart eal Drihtnes gife full.
 50. Þa wæron ealle þa apostolas gefeonde for Paules
eaðmodnesse.
 51. & swa swa Petrus gesette þysum menniscum cynne, þa
aþenede Sanctus Petrus his handa to Gode.
 52. & wæs cweþende, <foreign>Domine Deus omnipotens, qui sedes
super cherubin æt profundi</foreign>, Drihten ælmihtig God, þu þe sitest ofer
cherubine & ofer deopnesse ealra grunda, & we ahebbað ure handa to
þe on anlicnesse þinre rode, & on þinre cyþþe we ræste
habbaþ, forðon þe þu sylest urum leomum ræste, forðon ðe hie on
þinum noman wunnon.
 58. & þu eallum oferhydigum eaþmodnesse forgifest &
oferswiþest deaþ.
 59. Þu eart soþlice ure ræst, & þu Drihten eart ure
Scyldend, & on þe we cegeaþ, ðu þe wunast on Suna & Fæder on
þe & þu eart ana mid Halige Gaste on worlda world.
 62. Þa ondswaredon him ealle þa apostolas & cwædon,
Amen.
 62. Þa arn se eadiga Iohannes to eallum þam apostolum, &
wæs cweðende to him, <foreign>Benedicite fratres, et dixerunt Petrus</foreign>, Bletsiað
gebroðor þa leofestan, urne Drihten.
 65. Þa cwæð Petrus & Andreas to Iohanne, þu leofa
drihten, gecyþe us hwylce gemete þu come todæg to us.
 67. Þa cwæþ Iohannes, Bletsiað, broþor þa leofestan,
urne god & gehyraþ ge ealle þæt he wæs gongende to dæg on
þas ceastre, & he wæs lærende þæt ge eow gebædon to Gode on
þa nigoþan tid þæs dæges.
 70. & þa semninga astag mycel wolcen on þa ilcan stowe on
þære þe we wæron gesamnode, þær we geherdan Godes word, &
þa sæmninga þa embsealdon ealle þa apostolas þa halgan Marian &
hie gegripan on hire middel.
 74. & þa gesawon hie & ealle þa þe þær wæron,
þæt se eadiga Michael genam & þa slog on þæs huses duru, &
heo him ne forwyrnde ac heo hie ontynde.
 76. & he þær gemette swiþe manig folc þe þær
ætstodan.
 77. & þær eac stod þære halgan Marian sweostor &
heo spræc to þæm weorode & cwæþ, þys myrgenlican dæge heo
biþ gongende of lichoman.
 79. & þa ælc þara þe þis gehyrde wæs swiþe
wepende.
 80. & þa wæs Maria cweþende, <foreign>Nunc fratres audite</foreign>,
Broþor þa leofestan, gehyraþ ge me nu ealle þæt ic beo þys
morgenlican dæge gongende of lichoman.
 83. Þa cwædon þa apostolas to hire, Ne ceara þu, Maria, ne
ne wep, þæt þin folc ne sy gedrefed, forþon þis cwæþ ure
Drihten & ure beboda Lareow, mid þy þe he wæs hlifigende ofer sæs
brim þa he wæs æt his æfengereordum.
 86. Forþon ic eow manige ealle þæt, ge þis folc wepende
þæt her ymbstandeþ.
 88. Þa þæt folc ongan tweogan on heora heortan & hie
cwædon, To hwan ondrædeþ þeos halige Maria hire deaþ, & mid
hire syndan Godes apostolas & oþre þa þe hie beraþ to hire
æriste?
 91. Þa cwædon þa apostolas to þæm folce, Heo bið
swiþor gestrangod be us tweonum þurh Drihtnes gehat & ne tweoge þis
folc be hire untrumnesse, ne be hire geleafan.
 93. & mid þy þe hie þis gesprecen hæfdon, þa com
þær se eadiga Iohannes & wæs ingongende of þære halgan Marian
huse, & halette on hie mycelre stefne & wæs cweþende, <foreign>Aue Maria
gratia plena Dominus tecum</foreign>, Hal westu, Maria, þu eart geofe ful.
 97. Þu eart gebletsod.
 98. Betuh ealle wifcyn & betuh ealle halie gastas.
 98. & heo þa ondswerede & cwæþ, Broþer þa
leofestan, ic eow bidde ealle þæt ge me secgan hwylce gemete ge coman
ealle samod todæg to me, oþþe hwa sægde eow þæt ic sceolde beon
þys mergenlican dæge gongende to heofenum?
 102. & swa anra gehwylc þara apostola biþ geseted to his
synderlicre stowe þæt he bodige his godcundnesse & hire geeacnunge.
 104. & þa apostolas tugon hie up & hie gesetton on
þæm fægran neorxnawange.
 105. Þa wæs Maria wynsumigende on hire gaste & wæs
cweþende, <foreign>Benedico te qui dominaris super omnem benedictionem</foreign>, Ic þe
bletsige, min Drihten, þu þe waldest ealre bletsunge, & ic bletsige eal
þin gehat þe þu me gehete.
 109. Ofer minre gecignesse þu gesettest ealle þine apostolas to
minre byrgenne.
 110. & ic bletsige þinne þone halgan noman þe wunaþ in
ealra worlda world, Amen.
 111. <foreign>Et post hec uocauit Sancta Maria omnes apostolas in cubiculo
suo et ostendit illis omnem indumentum</foreign>, Ond þa æfter þon þa cegde seo
halige Mariæ to eallum þæm apostolum on hire hordcofan, & him
æteowde ealne hire gegyrelan þe heo wolde æt hire byrgenne habban.
 116. & wæs cweþende þis wæs se þridda dæg
geworden on þæm heo gewat of lichoman fram us.
 117. Ond þa cwæþ se eadiga Petrus to eallum þæm
apostolum & to eallum þæm folce, Broþor þa leofestan, ic eow bidde
ealle þa þe on þisse stowe syndon þæt ge wacian mid me & we
bærnan gastlico leohtfato oþþæt Drihten hider cume.
 121. & þa æfter þysum wordum þa com þær ure
Drihten.
 122. & he hie gemette ealle anmodlice wæccende.
 122. & he hie onlyhte mid his þæs Halgan Gastes gife.
 123. & he wæs cweþende to him, Broþor þa leofestan, ne
sy eow nænigu cearo þæt ge geseon þæt þeos eadige Maria sy
geceged to deaþe.
 125. & ne biþ heo no to þæm eorþlican deaþe ac heo
bið gehered mid Gode, forþon þe hire bið mycel wuldor gegearwod.
 127. & mid þy þe he þis gecweden hæfde, þa ascean
samninga mycel leoht on hire huse þæt ealle þa fynd wæron
oferswiþde þa þe þær wæron, & þa þe þæt leoht
gesawon þa ne meahton asecgan for þæs leohtes mycelnesse.
 130. & þa wæs geworden mycel stefn of heofenum to Petre
& wæs cweþende, Ic beo mid eow ealle dagas oþ gyfylnesse þisse
worlde.
 132. & þa ahof Petrus his stefne & wæs cweþende, We
bletsiaþ þinne naman mid urum saulum & we biddaþ þæt þu fram
us ne gewite.
 134. & we bletsiaþ þe & we biddaþ þæt þu
onlyhte ure world, for þæm þe þu eallum miltsast þæm þe on þe
gelyfaþ.
 136. & þis wæs cweþende se eadiga Petrus to eallum
þæm apostolum & he trymede heora heortan mid Godes geleafan.
 138. Æfter þyssum wordum gefylde, þa wæs Maria arisende
& wæs ut gangende of hire huse, & hie gebæd to þæm gebede
þe se engel hire tocwæþ þe þær com to hire.
 140. Þa þis gebed wæs gefylled þa wæs heo eft gangende
on hire hus & heo þa wæs hleonigende ofer hire ræste, & æt
hire heafdan sæt se eadiga Petrus & emb þa ræste oþre Cristes
þegnas.
 143. & þa ær þære syxtan tide þæs dæges þa
wæs semninga geworden mycel þunorrad, & þær wæs swiþe swete
stenc swa þætte ealle þa slepan þe þær wæron.
 146. & þa apostolas onfengon þære eadigan Marian &
þa þre fæmnan þe him Crist ær bebead, þæt hie wacedon buton
forlætnesse & þæt hie cyþdon Drihtnes wuldor be hire & ealle
medemnesse be þære eadigan Marian.
 149. Þa slepan þa ealle þe þær wæron þa com
þær semninga ure Drihten Hælend Crist þurh wolcnum mid myccle mengeo
engla & wæs ingangende on þære halgan Marian hus on þæt þe
heo hie inne reste.
 153. Michahel se heahengel se wæs ealra engla ealderman, he
wæs ymen singende mid eallum þæm englum, mid þy þe Hælend wæs
ingongende.
 155. Þa gemette he ealle þa apostolas emb þære eadigan
Marian ræste, and he bletsode þa halgan Marian & wæs cweþende,
<foreign>Benedico te quia quicumque promisisti</foreign>, Ic þe bletsige min Sancta Maria,
& eal swa hwæt swa ic þe gehet eal ic hit gesette.
 159. Ond þa andswarode him seo halige Maria & wæs
cweþende, Ic do a þine gife, min Drihten, & ic þe bidde for þinum
naman þæt þu gehwyrfe on me ealle eaþmodnesse þinra beboda, forþon
þe ic mæg don þine gife.
 163. Þu eart gemedemod on ecnesse.
 164. & þa onfeng ure Drihten hire saule & he hie þa
sealde Sancte Michahele þæm heahengle.
 165. & he onfeng hire saule mid ealra his leoma eaþmodnesse.
 166. & næfde heo noht on hire buton þæt an þæt heo
hæfde mennisce onlicnesse & heo hæfde seofon siþum beorhtran saule
þonne snaw.
 168. & þa frægn Petrus urne Drihten & wæs
cweþende, Hwylc is of us Drihten þæt hæbbe swa hwite saule swa þeos
halige Marie?
 170. Þa cwæþ ure Drihten to Petre & to eallum þæm
mannum þe þær wæron, þisse halgan Marian saule biþ a gewuldrod
mid Gode, & heo biþ aþwægen mid þæm halgan þweale.
 173. & oþre apostolas beoþ sende beforan hire bære, mid
þy þe heo biþ gongende of lichoman.
 174. & hie ne gemetton nane swa hwite saule swa þære
eadigan Marian wæs, forþon heo lufode ma þeostro for hire synnum &
heo wæs a þeh gehealden fram hire synnum.
 177. & hie gesawon ealle þæt seo eadige Marie hæfde swa
hwite saule swa snaw.
 178. Þa cwæþ ure Hælend to Petre & to þære
eadigan Marian lichoman, þys mergenlican dæge heo bið gangende on
þisse ceastre on þa swiþran healfe mines dæles & ge þær
gemetaþ niwe byrgenne.
 182. Þonne asette ge þone lichoman to þære byrgenne &
hine þær healdaþ swa ic eow bebeode.
 183. Þa mid þy þe he þis gecweden hæfde ure Drihten,
þa cleopode semninga þære eadigan Marian lichoma beforan him eallum
& wæs cweþende, Wes þu gemyndig, þu gewuldroda Cyning, forþon ic
beo þin hondgeweorc.
 187. & wes þu min gemyndig, forþon ic healde þinra beboda
goldhord.
 188. & þa cwæþ ure Drihten to þære eadigan Marian
lichoman, Ne forlæte ic þe næfre min meregrot, ne ic þe næfre ne
forlæte, min eorclanstan, forþon þe þu eart soþlice Godes templ.
 191. & þa he þis gecweden hæfde, þa astah ure Drihten
on heofenas.
 192. Þa nam Petrus & þa oþre apostolas hie, & þa
þreo fæmnan þe þær wacodon, & þwogan þære eadigan Marian
lichoman, & hie þa asetton ofer hire bære.
 194. & þa æfter þon þa arison ealle þa þe þær
slepan & þa brohte Petrus þær þæt palmtwig þæt seo eadige
Marie ær onfeng of þæs engles handa.
 196. Þa cwæþ se eadiga Iohannes, <foreign>Tu es uirgo, tu debes
procidere lectum</foreign>,.
 198. Þu eart seo clænoste fæmne, & þe gedafenaþ
þæt þu leore on þine bære, & we beran þis palmtwig &
cweþan Godes lof.
 199. Þa cwæþ eft se halga Iohannes, þu eart forelærende
on þara apostola gebede, & þe gedafenaþ þæt þu leore on þine
bære, & we beran þis palmtwig & cweþan Godes lof.
 202. Þa cwæþ eft se halga Iohannes, þu eart forelærende
on þara apostola gebede, & þe gedafenaþ þæt þu leore on þine
bære & we þe þonne beran þæt we cuman to þære stowe
þær Drihten bebead.
 205. & ne sy ure nan geunrotsod ac we gesigefæstan þine
bære.
 206. & þa arison þa apostolas, & hie hofan þa bære
& hie bæron mid heora handum.
 208. & Petrus þa soþlice onhof his stefne & wæs
cweþende, <foreign>In exitu Israhel ex Egypto, Alleluia</foreign>, Israhel wæs ut
gangende.
 210. Of ægyptum, & wæs singende, Alleluia & Drihten
is soþlice þisse bære fultumiende.
 211. & þa apostolas wæron gangende on wolcnum & hie
þa bæron þa bære, & hie cwædon Godes lof.
 213. Þa þæt folc þa þæt gehyrde, & þa Iudeas
gesawon þa mycclan mengeo engla & heora stefn wæs swiþe hlud, &
hie heredon God, þa wæron hie swiþe erre on heora mode.
 215. & heora þa ongon ælc cweþan to oþrum, Hwæt is
þeos mengeo & þis folc þe her þus hlude singeþ?
 217. Þa cwæþ þara apostola sum þe þær ætstod,
Maria is nu soþlice of lichoman gewiten, & we cweþaþ lof ymb hie.
 219. & þa raþe eode Satanas þæt deofol & þara
Iudea ealdormen & heora ongan þa ælc cweþan to oþrum, Uton we nu
arisan & acwellan þa apostolas & Marian lichoman geniman & hie
þonne mid fyre forbærnon, forþon þe heo gebær þone biswican.
 223. & þa Iudeas þa arison, & hie þa ongunnon mid
sweordum & mid strengþum þyder gan, þohton þæt hie woldan
ofslean þa apostolas.
 225. & þa on þa ilcan tid þa englas þa þær
wæron on þæm wolcnum, hie wurdon wyldran þonne þa Iudeas &
ongunnan slean þa Iudeas.
 227. & hie þa wurdon sona blinde & feollan to eorþan.
 228. & heora heafdu slogan on þa wagas & hie grapodan mid
heora handum on þa eorþan & nystan hwyder hie eodan.
 230. & þa an þe þær wæs þara Iudea aldorman he
genealæcan þæm apostolum, & he þa wæs geseonde þæt seo
bær wæs gesigefæsted & hie wæron soþlice ymen singende þa
apostolas/ & wæron cweþende, Nu is gefylled þæt mycclle hatheort
& þæt mycclle yrre þyses ealdermannes & Drihten us sealde
eardunga on þisse stowe & on eallum ussum cynne, & he us sealde
orsorh wuldor.
 236. Ond þa sona se arleasa gerefa cleopode mid mycelre stefne
& wæs cweþende, Ic me wille nu onhwyrfan to þisse bære, &
þonne gegripan þæt palmtwig & hit þonne to eorþan afyllan, &
forsearedum him begen dælas forbrecan & forbærnan.
 240. Þa wæs he gongende to þære bære & þa on
middan þæm lichoman on þære bære, þa wearþ he gefæstnod be
þære swiþran handa to þære bære, þæt he hangode to
eorþan.
 242. Þa cleopode he mycelre stefne, & wæs wepende mid
tearum on þara apostola gesyhþe, & wæs þus cweþende, <foreign>Adiuro uos
per Deum uiuum</foreign>,.
 245. Ic eow halsige þurh þone lifgendan God þæt ge me ne
forseon on þisse mycclan nedðearfe tide ond ðe bide ealra swiþost, min
se halga Petrus, þæt þu sy gemyndig hwæt min fæder þe gedyde,
þa he wæs duruweard.
 248. Þa frægn hine soþlice Petrus & cwæþ, Wære
þu mid ðinum fæder þa he me swa ladode þæt hie me ne gegripon?
 250. & þa cwæþ se ealderman eft, Ic eow nu bidde ealle
þæt ge me ne forseon.
 251. Ond þa cwæþ soþlice Petrus to him, Nis þæt
soþlice min miht ne næniges ures, ac gif þu gelyfest on Hælende
Crist, þæt he sy Godes Sunu þæs lyfgendan, & arise fram deaþe.
 254. Gif þu þonne ne gelyfest þæt he sy Godes Sunu,
þonne ne bist þu aseted on eorþan.
 255. Ac we witan þæt þyses menniscan cynnes fynd ablende
eowre heortan þæt Crist ne wære soþ God, & þonne bist þu
gehæled fram him.
 258. Ac gong þu nu soþlice, & cys þas bære, &
cweþ to þysum lichoman þæt þu gelyfe on God Fæder & on
Marian, forþon heo bær Hælendne Crist.
 260. & þa se ealderman þara sacerda bletsode Marian mid his
tungan Ebreiscre stefne þurh wuldor.
 262. & heora nænig þa bære þa hwile ne ahof.
 262. & þa æfter fyrstmearce þa bletsode he eft Marian
lichoman on Moyses boca gewitnesse, & þurh swiðe manigfealde gewreotu.
 264. Ond of eallum þæm he wæs cweþende þæt Maria
wære þæs lifgendan Godes templ.
 266. Þa wæron þa apostolas swiþe wundrigende fram him
& wæron cweþende to him, hwonon him þa wundorlican gereordo coman.
 268. Þa cwæþ Petrus to him, Aræce þine handa &
cweþ þæt þu gelyfe on ures Hælendes Cristes naman, & on ealre
þinre heortan, þonne wesaþ þine handa sona geedneowode & beoþ swa
hie ær wæron beforan þe.
 271. & þa wæs hraþe geworden þæt he gelyfde on his
heortan.
 272. & þa cwæþ Petrus eft to him, Aris nu & onfoh
þysum palmtwige þe her is beforan þisse halgan Marian bære.
 274. & þonne gang to þissa Iudea ceastre to þæm þe
þær ofslegene syndon mid blindnesse, ond sprec to him & cweþ, Swa
hwylc swa ne gelyfeþ on Hælend Crist þæt he sy Godes Sunu þæs
lifgendan, þonne beoþ þæs eagan betynede.
 278. & þonne gif hwylc gelyfe on God, þonne æthrin þu
heora eagan mid þysum palmtwige þe þu her onfenge on þine hand, þonne
onfoþ hie raþe gesyhþe.
 281. Se þonne witodlice ne gelyfeþ on God þonne ne gesyhþ
se næfre on ecnesse.
 282. Ond þa eode se ealdorman þara Iudea & þara sacerda
& wæs cweþende swa him ær bebead se eadga Petrus.
 284. & he gemette swiþe manige on þæm folce wepende.
 284. & wæron cweþende, Wa us la, forþon be us is nu
geworden swa swa on Sodoma byrig wæs.
 286. Þær wæs geworden þæt þær com ofer hie on
fruman mycel broga & hie wæron mid blindnesse slegene.
 288. Ond æfter þon þa sende Drihten fyr of heofenum ofer hie
& hie mid ealle forbærnde.
 289. & hie þa wæron cweþende, Nu soþlice we syndon
gefyllede mid ealre eaþmodnesse.
 291. & þa soþlice him swa wependum, þa com þara sacerda
ealdorman þe Petrus him tosende.
 292. & he þa wæs sprecende to him eallum þæm ilcum
wordum þe him ær Petrus bebead.
 294. & he gehyrde heora þrowunga, & he þa wundrode
æfter þære gesihþe.
 295. Ond he wæs cweþende, Swa hwylc swa gelyfeþ on God
ælmihtigne his wordum þonne wile he onfon rihtre ondetnesse for Cristes
naman Godes Suna þæs lifgendan, þonne onfeh se hraþe gesihþe.
 298. Se þonne witodlice ne gelyfþ on God, þonne wunaþ he on
blindnesse aa on ecnesse.
 299. Ond hie þa wurdan hraþe gelyfde & Crist him sealde
gesihþe.
 300. Ond þa witodlice þa apostolas bæron Marian lichoman
oþþæt hie coman to þære byrgenne þær Drihten him bebead.
 302. & hie þa þær bebyrigdon Marian lichoman, & þa
setton hie æt þære byrgenne dura swa swa Drihten Hælende Crist him
bebead.
 304. & þa him swa sittendum þa com þær semninga ure
Drihten mid myccle mengeo engla, & cwæþ to him, Sib sy, broþor, mid
eow.
 306. & he þa bebead Michahele þæm heahengle þæt he
onfenge þære eadigan Marian sawle mid wolcnum & þa onfeng Michahel
þære saule.
 309. Ond he þa cwæþ to þæm apostolum oþþæt hie
ealle nealæhton to Drihtne Hælendum Criste.
 310. Ond þonne þære sawle onfeng on wolcnum & Drihten
bead þæm wolcnum þæt hie eodan on neorxna wang & þær asetton
þære eadigan Marian sawle.
 312. & on neorxna wange biþ a wuldor mid Gode & mid
eallum his gecorenum soþlice.
 314. On þa soþlice æt þære þriddan tide þæs
dæges, þa com þær Drihten mid myclum menigeo, & halette þa
apostolas & wæs cweþende, Sib sy mid eow, broþor.
 316. & þa andsweredan him þa apostolas & hie cwædon
Wuldor þe sy, God, forþon þe þu dydest ana mycel wuldor.
 318. Þa cwæþ ure Hælend to him, ær ic wæs sended
fram minum Fæder to þæm þæt ic sceolde gefyllan mine þa halgan
þrowunge.
 320. Ond ic þa wæs gehwyrfed on minne lichoman, swa ic eow
ær gehet, & on eallum þæm þe me fylgende wæron on þissum
menniscan cynne.
 322. & ic wæs sittende ofer manna bearnum on minum
mægenþrymme ond wæs sittende ofer eow on minum hehsetle.
 324. & ic demde twelf þeodum on þrim Israhela folcum &
of þæm twelf mægþum.
 325. & be mines Fæder hæse ic wearþ eft on lichoman
geseted.
 326. & for heora halignesse ic me gehalgode to þæm
unbesmitenan temple & heo is seo clæneste fæmne, & heo wæs
fæmne ær hire beorþre & heo wunaþ fæmne æfter hire
beorþre.
 329. Ond þa cwæþ Hælend to þæm apostolum, Hwæt
wille ge nu?
 330. Hwæt ic hire doo?
 330. & þa andswarode him Petrus & ealle þa apostolas
& cwædon, Drihten, þu þe gecure þæt fæt on to eardienne,
& heo is þin seo clæneste fæmne ær ealre worlde, & þu miht
soþlice & gesewenlice þine mihte gecyþan on Marian þinre þeowan.
 334. & þu oferswiþdest deaþ, ond þu eart rixiende on
þinum wuldre, swa þu nu miht þinre modor lichoman eft aweccan fram
deaþe.
 336. & þa raþe wæs Drihten blissiende on heofenas &
wæs cweþende to his apostolum, Wese hit nu be eowrum domum.
 338. & þa hraþe bead Drihten Gabriele þæm heahengle
þæt he wylede þone stan fram þære byrgenne duru.
 340. Ond þa Michael se heahengel geondweardode þære eadigan
Marian sawle beforan Drihtne.
 341. Ond þa wæs Drihten cweþende to Marian lichoman, Aris
þu, min seo nehste & min culufre & mines wuldres eardung, &
forþon þe þu eart lifes fæt, & þu eart þæt heofenlice
templ, & næron nænige leahtras gefylde on þinre heortan, ond þu
ne þrowast nænige þrowunge on þinum lichoman.
 346. Ond þa cwæþ Drihten eft to þæm lichoman, Aris þu
nu of þinre byrgenne.
 347. & þa sona aras Maria of þære byrgenne, &
ymbfeng Drihtnes fet, ond þa ongan wuldrian on God & wæs cweþende,
Min Drihten, ne mæg ic ealle þa gife forbringan þe þu me forgeafe for
þinum naman, & hweþre hi ne magon ealle þine bletsunge gefyllan.
 351. & þu eart Israhela God & þu eart ahafen mid
þinum Fæder & mid þinum þy Halgan Gaste on worlda world.
 353. On þa ahof Drihten hie up & hie þa cyste, & hie
þa sealde Michahele þæm heahengle & he hie þa ahof up on wolcnum
beforan Drihtnes gesihþe.
 355. Ond cwæþ Drihten to þæm apostolum, gangaþ nu to me
on wolcnum.
 357. & þa mid þy þe hie wæron gangende to him þa
wæs Drihten hie cyssende & wæs cweþende, <foreign>Pacem meam do uobis,
Alleluia</foreign>, Ic forlæte mine sibbe to eow þurh mines Fæder þone Halgan
Gast, ond ic eow sylle mine sibbe þurh min þæt hehste lof, ond ic beo
mid eow ealle dagas oþ þa geendunga þisse worlde.
 362. & Drihten cwæþ to þæm englum, Singaþ nu &
onfoh minre meder on neorxnawonge.
 363. & þa apostolas on heora mægene hofan Marian lichoman
up mid wolcnum & hine þa asetton on neorxnawanges gefean.
 365. & nu syndon gesette þa apostolas inhlet æ hie bodian
hire.
 366. Ond we nu ondetton Godes mycelnesse & singan on Marian
naman, <foreign>Magnificat anima mea</foreign>.
 368. Forþon heo þus cwæþ þa heo Magnificaþ sang, Min
Drihten, gemycla mine sauwle.
 369. <foreign>Et exultauit</foreign>, & gedo þæt min gast wynsumige on
þinre hælo, forþon þe þu eart soþ God.
 370. <foreign>Quia respexit</foreign>, forþon þu nu sceawa þines mægdenes
eaþmodnesse.
 371. & min Drihten, cwæþ Sancte Marie, Gedo þu þæt
eall cynn cweþe þæt ic sy seo eadgoste fæmne.
 373. <foreign>Qui fecit</foreign>, forþon þu me dydest mycel & þu eart
mihtig & þin nama halig.
 374. <foreign>Et misericordia</foreign>, & þin mildheortnes is mid eallum
þæm cynne þe þe him ondrædaþ.
 376. <foreign>Fecit potentiam</foreign>, & he dyde mycle mihte on his earman,
& he todælde ealle þa þe þær wæron ofermode on heora
heortan, & noldan on hine getrywan.
 378. <foreign>Deposuit</foreign>, & he asette þa mihtigan of heora setle &
þæt wæs Satanas mid his deoflum, þa he wæs on heofena rice, &
he þa for his oferhygdum & his deoflu mid him wurdon aworpene on helle
grund.
 381. & Drihten ealle eaþmode upahefþ on ecnesse.
 382. <foreign>Esurientes</foreign>, & þa wæs Sancta Maria cweþende
þæt Drihten ealle þa gefylde on heofona wuldres fægernesse þa þe
hie on eorþan leton hingrian & þyrstan for his naman.
 384. & ealle þa men þa þe onfengon welan & on
oferfylle swiþor gehyhton þonne on God, & hie syne swa forleton on
idelnesse, þonne gegearwode he þæm ece forwyrde.
 387. <foreign>Suscepit Israel</foreign>, & Israhel onfehþ eallum his cnihtum
& wæs gemyndig ealre his mildheortnesse.
 389. Swa Matheus wæs cweþende þæt Drihten astige on sume
tid on anne munt mid myccle weorode his haligra & þa gesæt he on
þæm munte.
 391. <foreign>Sicut locutus est</foreign>, & þa eodan his þegnas to him
& þa ontynde Hælend his muð & wæs sprecende to urum
fæderum & to Abrahame & wæs cweþende þæt his sæd
oferweoxe ealle þas woruld.
 394. & he þa lærde his apostolas, him sægde þurh
hwæt seo saul eadegust gewurde & þus cwæþ, Eadige beoþ
þearfena gastas & hie restaþ on heofena rice.
 396. & eadige beoð þa þe þissa eorþwelena ne
gymaþ.
 397. & eadige beoþ þa þe wepaþ nu for heora synnum,
forþon hi beoþ eft afrefrede on heofona rice.
 399. Ac utan we biddan þa fæmnan Sancta Marian þæt heo us
sy milde þingere wið urne Drihten Hælendne Crist ondweardes rædes
& eces wuldres, to þæm us gefultumige ure Drihten, Amen.

LS 20.1 (AssumptWillard)
B3.3.20.1.
Assumption of Mary the Virgin: Willard 1936, 8-10.



 7.1. And mid ðy ðe heo ðys gecweden hæfde, ða com
ðær sona se eadega Iohannes, and slog on ða duru ðæs huses,
þæt heo onarn, and wæs ingangende to hire.
 7.3. And geseah þæt Sancta Maria wæs gedrefedu on hire
gaste, and heo sworette; and heo ne mihte forhabban, þæt heo ne weope; and
wæs cweðende, Fæder Iohannes, westu gemindig min, forðon ðe Drihten
is ðinra beboda lareow, and þæt he me bebead þæt ic gefille on
ðissum dæge.
 7.5. He gewat fram us, þæt he wolde ðrowian for middaneardes
hælo.
 8.1. And ða cwæð se halga Iohannes to hire Hwæt wilt ðu
þæt ic ðe doo?
 8.2. Ða andsworede him seo halige Maria, and wæs
cwæðende, Ne bidde ic ðe nanes ðinges elles buton þæt ðu
gehealde minne lichoman, and hine gesette on byrgenne; forðon ðe ic beo,
ær ðrim dagum, gongende of minum lichoman.
 8.4. Ða gehyrde se halga Iohannes þæt ða Iudeas cwædan,
Uton we nu gan, and acwellan ða apostolas, and Marian lichoman geniman, and
hire forbærnan.
 8.6. Mid ðy ðe ðis gehyrde se eadiga Iohannes, ða wæs he
cweðende, Of ðissum dæge he gewat fram us of lichoman, and he ða
wæs wepende on Godes gesyhðe, and cweðende, Eala, Drihten, hwæt
syndon we ðe ðu gecyddest swa micle sorge?
 9.1. And ða cegde seo halige Maria to ðem halgan Iohanne on
hire hordcofan, and him æteowde ealne hire gyrelan, and þæt scinende
pealmtwig ðe heo onfeng of ðæs engles handa.
 9.3. And heo him æteowde ealle hire medomnesse, and cwæð to
him, Ic ðe bidde, Fæder Iohannes, þæt ðu ðis palmtwig onfo, and
hit ðonne ber beforan minre bæran, mid ðy ðe ic sy gongende of minum
lichoman.
 10.1. Ða cwæð se halga Iohannes to hire, Ne mæge ic
þæt ana don; ac her cumað mine efnapostolas to me, and we ðonne beoð
ealle on annesse gesamnode on ðisse stowe ðurh Drihtnes mægen to
alysnesse ðines lichoman.
 11.1. Mid ðy ðe he ðis gecweden hæfde, ða wæs he
gongende of hire hordcofan; ða wæs semninga geworden micel ðunnorad,
þæt eall seo stow wæs gedrefedu, and eall ða ðe þær wæron
on ðæm huse.
 11.3. And ða semninga ealle ða apostolas tugon hie upp mid
wolcnum, and sume hie wæron gesette beforan þæs huses dura ðære
halgan Marian.

LS 21 (AssumptTristr)
B3.3.21.
Assumption of the Virgin: Tristram 1970, 125-50.



 1. Her sagað ymbe þa halgan marian usses dryhtnes modor.
 3. Mid þy þe dryhten hælende crist for ealre worulde
alysnesse on rode gefæstnod hangode he geseah under þære rode standan
his modor and iohannes þane godspellere þone he beforan his oðrum halgum
lufode for þon he in lychoman þurhwunode.
 8. Þa bebead he him þa halgan marian and him to cwæð,
þis is þin modor, and æfter þon he cwæð to hire, þis is þin
sunu.
 10. And of þære tide seo halie maria on Iohannes gymnesse
þurhwunode swa lange swa hio on þissum life lyfede.
 13. Hwæt la he sende ure dryhten his apostolas geond ealne
middangeard mancyn to læranne þa sæt maria in hire huse be oliuetes
dune.
 16. Ðy þriddan geare æfter þon þe drihten crist in
heofon astah þa sume dæge wæs hio to þon swiðe gyrnende his ansine
þæt hio angan wepan.
 19. And þa sona geseah hio drihtnes engel hire ætstandende
ða grette he hi and cwæð, hal wes þu maria from drihtne gebletsod.
 21. Hwæt la, þis palmtwig of niorhxwonge ic þe brohte
þæt þu gedo þæt he sie boren beforan þinre bære and nu binnan
þy ðriddan dæge þu bist ferende of lichoman and þin bideð þin
sunu drihten hælende crist mid his englum and mid eallum halgum and mid
heahenglum.
 26. Ða cwæð maria to þam engle, ic þe bidde þætte
syn to me gesomnode ealle apostolas mines drihtnes hælendes cristes þæt
ic hi geseo licumlicum eagum ær ðon þe ic swelte.
 30. Ða andswarode hire se engel and cwæð, nu todæge hi
beoð genumene of neorhxnawonges gefean and her to ðe cumað.
 32. Þa cwæð maria eft to þam engle, ic ðe bidde þæt
þu sende þine bletsunge ofer me þætte nænig geweald þæs
wiðerweardan deofles me ongen ne yrne and þæt ic ne geseo þistro aldor
me ongen cumende.
 36. Se engel me to cwæð, þa ecean bletsunge þe sealde
þin drihten godes þeowa and ærenddraca ic eom þætie ðu þonne ne
gesihst ðistra aldor ac ne wene þu þæt ðe sy þæt from me seald
ac from him þone þu in þinum innoþe gebære his anweald is in ealra
worulda woruld.
 41. And se engel þa mid micelre biorhtnesse ðanon gewat and se
palma scan swiþe leohte and his leaf lihton swa se scinenda mergensteorra.
 45. Maria hi ða gegirede mid hire selran gyrelan and hio genam
ðone palman þone þe hio of ðæs engles handa onfeng and eode in
oliuete ða dune.
 47. And hie þær gebæd and cwæð, þancas ic ðe dem
ælmihtig domine ealles þæs þu me to gemedomodest.
 49. Ic næs swa micelre weorðmyndu weorðe þæt þu me
nære mildsiende.
 51. And þa ðus cweðende in hire huse hio wæs gongende.
 52. Mid þy ðe se halga iohannes lærde þæt folc in
effessum on sunnandæge æt underntide þæt þa þunorrada hlynedon
and wæron swiðe micele ligetas gewordene.
 55. And he wæs ahæafen from þara ymbstandendra eagum and he
wæs aset beforan ðæs huses dura þær sio eadige maria inne wunode
and ingangende he hio grette mid þy þe hio ongan wepan.
 58. And hio cwæð to iohanne, ic ðe bidde min bearn iohannes
þætte ðu wes gemindig þines lareowes worda þe he spræc ða he me
þe ætfæste.
 61. And ic gehyrde iudea geðeahtunge hi cwædon, uton onbidan
hwænne ðios swelte þæt we mægen hire lichoman mid fyre
forbærnan, ac for ðon gym þu mynre deaðþenuga.
 65. And ða hio þis gecweden hæfde hio him æteowde hire
lichrægl þe hio of ðæs engles handa onfeng and cwæð to him, gedo
þu þæt þes palma sie beren beforan minre bære þonne min lichoma
sie to byrgene læded.
 70. Se halga iohannes hire andwarode and cwæð, hu mæg ic
ðe ana gedefelice deaðþenuga gegearwian nymðe mine broþor and efne
apostolas hider sin gesamnode?
 74. Þa betweox þas word ealle þa apostolas wæron of þam
stowum þe hie ær lærdon in wolcnum ahafen and asette beforan duru
þæs huses in þæm sio halige marie wunude.
 77. And in gongende hi gretton hi him betwunum and cwædon, for
hwylcon þingon gesamnode us drihten hider todæge?
 80. Mid þy hi þæt spræcon and hi to drihtne gebædon.
 81. Iohannes se apostol cwom to him and he him sæde.
 83. In gongende þa apostolas gretton marian and cwædon, bio
þu gebletsod from dryhtne se geworhte heofon and eorðan.
 85. Hio him andswarode and cwæð, si drihtnes bletsung ofer eow
and sib sie mid eow in drihtnes noman.
 87. Nu þonne mine þa leofan broþor, secgeað me, hu ge hider
cwomon?
 88. Hiere ða apostolas sædon ealle hu hiera anra gehwylc of
ðere stowe þyder com þe he on lærde.
 90. Maria him to cwæð, gebletsod sie drihten se gefylde mine
gyrnesse and he me ne bescyrede eowerre gesyhðe.
 93. Ac he me forgeaf þæt ic eow licumlicum eagum gesio ær
þon þe ic swelte and ic eow ealle bidde þæt ge anmodlice wacien on
ða tid þe domine cume.
 96. Hie ealle þa hire geheton and mid hira wordum fredon and in
godes hirnesse ðurhwunedon.
 99. And ða samnunga æt underne slæp com ofer ealle þa
ðe wæron in þam huse swa þætte nænig wacian ne meahte buton þa
apostolas ane and ða þreo fæmnan þam maria hire deaðþenunga
bebead.
 103. And þa hraþe com drihten mid micele engla werode and
cwæð to þam apostolum, sib sy mid eow.
 105. Broþor ða andswaredon and cwædon, domine sy þin
mildheortnes ofer us swa we gehyhtað in ðe.
 108. Maria hi þa astrehte in ðone flor and hi to drihtne
gebæd and cwæð, wes þu min gemyndig wuldres aldor for þære
stemne þinre þeowenne þætte nænig geweald þæs wiðerweardan
feondes me ongean ne yrne and þæt ic ne gesio þa sweartan gastas me
ongean cumende.
 113. Þa andswarode hire domine and cwæð, mid þy ðe ic
sylf for mancynnes hælo deað þrowode þystra ealdor to me com and mid
þy þe ðu æfter manncynnes æwe deaþes gafol agyldest.
 117. Þu hine gesyhð ac astih of þinre reste and þone
gedefan ende þines lifes gefyl for þon ðin bideþ se heofonlica camphad
þæt he ðe inlædeþ in neorxnawonges gefean.
 121. Þe he domine þus cwæð heo astah ofer hire bedde and
gode þanciende hio onsende hire gast.
 123. And þa apostolas gesawon þære halgan marian sawle swa
micle leohte scinende swa þæt nænig man mid wordum asecgan ne mæg
seo beorhtnes oferswiðde æghwelces dæges hwitnesse and ælces
leohtnesse.
 127. Þa ætfæste se hælend þære haligan marian saule
michaele þam heahengle se is neorxnawonges hyrde ealdormon ebrea ðeoden.
 130. Swylce he cwæð to petre, geheald ðu marian lichoman and
bringað hine in þa swiðran healfe þære ceastre to eastdæle and ge
þær gemetað niwe byrgenne in þære nu git nænig mon gelæd
wæs.
 134. Byrgeað hi þær and onbidað þær oð þone
þriddan dæg and ic hweorfe eft to eow.
 135. And he ða drihten mid sawle his modor and mid þam halgum
englum and in micelre beorhtnesse on weg gewat and ða englas eodon micele
gefean hyhtende and gode lof singende.
 140. Hwæt la, þa þreo fæmnan genamon þone lichoman
þære geadegan marian to ðon þæt hi woldon hie baðigean swa hira
þeaw wæs.
 142. Mid þy þe hine ongiredon se haliga lichoma scean swa
micele leohte þætte he meahte wesan gesewen.
 144. Hi hine þa gegyredon mid hire lichrægle and ða samnunga
þæt leoht þanon gewat and on ansine þære halgan marian wæs
swilce lilian blostman and on micelre swetnesse swæc ut eode of hire
muðe.
 149. And ða apostolas þa gesetton þone halgan lichoman in
bære and iohannes cwæð to petre, þe gedafenað þysne palman to
beranne and þæt þu gonge beforan þas bære for ðon þe þu us
ealle in geleafan þæs apostolhades forgæst.
 154. Petrus him andswarode and cwæð, hwæt þu nu wemmast
for us ealle from drihtne eart gecoren for ðon æt þam æfengereordum
ofer his breost ðu onhlinedest mid þy ðe he us sæde þæt he
þrowian wolde.
 158. And ða he in rode gealgan gefæstnod hangode his þy
arfæstan muðe þe þas ætfæste for ðon þu þisne palman
beran.
 160. Ic bere þisne halgan lichoman mid minum efnapostolum.
 161. Paulus cwæð, for þon þe ic eower ealra gingest eom in
þan apostolhade ic bere þa bære mid þe.
 163. Petrus ahof þa bære æt ðam heafdum, paulus æt
ðam fotum and petrus ongan singan and ealle ða apostolas eodon ymb ða
bære gode to lof singende.
 167. Eac swylce englas of heofnum him on efn sungon swa þæt
eal seo eorðe þæs sanges wynsumnesse and ðæs sweges swiðnesse
wæs gefylledo swa þæt gedafenode to deaðþenunga drihtenes
cenninge.
 171. Ða þis ða gehirdon þara sacerda ealdormen þa eodon
hi mid micelre mænigo of þære ceastre and cwædon, hwæt is þes
sweg on þus micelre winsumnesse?
 174. Him þa wæs sæd maria is forð feredo and cristes
ðegenas hire lichoman to byrgenne berað and ðas herenesse ymb hie
singað.
 177. Mitte þe ðara sacerda ealdormen þis gehyrdon þætte
þa apostolas hyhtende and singende eodon þa wæs he swiðe mid yrre
gefylled and cwæð, þis is modor þæs ðe us gedrefde and ure cyn
eode to þære bære and hie wolde oferweorpan and to eorðan afyllan mid
þy ðe he hire onhran.
 183. Hraðe his handa wæron fæste in þære bære and
he hangode on þære bære swa he no eorðan æthran ac micele wite he
wæs ðread.
 185. And ða apostolas eodon swiðe hyhtende domine.
 186. Englas þa wæron in þære bære lyfte hi slogon
þæt folc mid micelre blindnesse þe of þære ceastre ut eode.
 189. Þara sacerda ealdorman se wæs fæst in þære
bære he cwæð to petre, ic þe bidde þu halga petrus þæt þu me
ne forseoh in þisse nydþearfe.
 192. Ac gemyne mid þy ðe sio duruþiowen þe hearm speceð
and þe þære dura wyrnde ic þe wæs wel specende, for ðon mildsa me
þurh domine.
 195. Cwæð him petrus, to gelyf in god þone þeos gebær
in hire innoþe, þæt is drihten hælende crist.
 198. Petrus het þa bære asettan and þara sacerda ealdormon
cwæð, ic gelyfe on godes sunu urne drihten hælende crist þone þios
gebær in hire innoþe.
 201. And þa sona his handa wæron ungefele and þæt wite
þa git ne gewat from him.
 203. Cwæð him petrus, to gong to þissum lichoman and cweð,
ic gelyfe in drihten hælend þone þios gebær in hire innoþe and
fæmne hio þuruhwunude æfter beorðre.
 206. Mid þy ðe he þus dide hraðe his hælo him wæs
agifen and he wuldrode drihten and herede god.
 209. Cwæð him petrus to, genim þisne palman of iohannes
handa and gong in þas ceastre.
 211. Þonne gemetest þu þær micel folc ablended sete þone
palman ofer hira eagan and cweð,  gelyf in god fæder ælmihtigne.
 212. And ðonne swa hwylce swa gelyfan willað onfoð gesyhðe,
þa ðe ne willað gelyfan hi sweltað.
 216. And þa onfeng se ealdormon þane palman and eode in þa
ceastre.
 218. Þa gemette he þær micel folc cigendra and cweþendra,
wa us mid micelre blindnesse, we syndon slagene.
 220. Hie þa gehirdon word þæs ealdormonnes and god gelifdon
and þa sona onfengon hi gesyhþe.
 222. Fife þara manna and þuruhwunedon in hira ungeleaffulnesse
sona hi wæron deaþ sweltende.
 224. And se ealdormon brohte þone palman to þam apostolum and
him sæde ealle þa þing þe þær gedon wæron.
 227. And ða apostolas brohton marian lichoman to þære stowe
þe him domine bebead.
 229. Hi hire alegdon in þa byrgenne and mid stane þa byrgene
behlidon and þær æt gesetton.
 230. And þa þy þriddan dæge on underne com ure hælend
mid micele engla werode and cwæð to þam apostolum, sib si mid eow.
 233. Þa gebædon hi him to drihtne and cwædon, wuldor þe
hælend þu ana wyrcest micel wuldor.
 235. Cwæð him hælend to, hwæt la, þa ic lichomlice mid
eow wæs ic eow gehet, þe me fylgende weron mid þy þe he sitte on þam
dome ofer ðam setle mines mægenþrimmes ge sittað ofer twelf heahsetlum
demende twelf israela mægða.
 240. And þa sona of israhela mægðe ic geceas for ðon þe
hio fæmne þurhwunude æfter þam beorðre and fæmne hio wæs
ær ðam beorðre and nu þone gedafenan ende hire lifes hio gefilde.
 243. Hwæt willað ge, hwæt ic hire do?
 245. Petrus and ða apostolas cwædon, drihten nu is geþuht
þinum þiowum þætte swa swa ðu deaþe oferswiðdum ricsast in
wuldre swa awece þu lichoman þinre modor and mid þe bliþne in hiofen
gelæd.
 250. Þa cwæð drihten to þam apostolum, sy þæt
æfter eowrum worde.
 251. And þa het drihten gabriel þone heahengel þæt he
wylede þone stan from þære byrgene dura.
 253. And gabriel se heahengel brohte Saule þære halgan marian
beforan drihtene and cwæð, aris wuldres aldor and gecorenesse fæt and
heofonlic tempel.
 257. And mid þy aras sio halige fæmne of þære byrgene and
hio hi onhylde to hælende and hine wuldrode and cwæð, ælmihtig
drihten þe eal þes middangeard fullice gehiran mæg, sy hwæðre þin
nama gebletsod and up ahafen in worulda worold.
 262. Hwæt la, ure drihten hi up ahof and hi cyste, bebead hi
þa michaele þam heahengle and hio þa wæs sona up ahafen beforan
drihten in þæt wolcen mid þam englum.
 266. Þa cwæð he hælend to þam apostolum, gongað to
me.
 267. And mid þy ðe hi to him eodon þa cyste he hi sona ealle
and him to cwæð, mine sibbe ic eow selle and to forlæte and ic beo mid
eow eallum dagum oþ þisse worulde ende.
 270. And þa he þis gecweden hæfde mid þam singendum englum
and mid his meder he wæs onfangen on neorxnawonge and þa apostolas
wæron þurh drihtnes mægen up in þæt wolcn ahafen.
 274. And þanon hi wæron anra gehwylc hiora eft aseted in þa
stowe ðær he ær lærde and hi wæron secgende drihtenes word and
ondettende godes þa micelan mihte se liofað and ricsað in ealra worulda
woruld, a butan ende, amen.

LS 22 (InFestisSMarie)
B3.3.22.
'In festis sancte Marie': Warner 1917, 134-9.



 1. <foreign>Sermo in festis sancte marie virginis</foreign>.
 1. Se godspellere Lucas sæigð on þyssen godspelle, þæt
se Hælend com into sumen cæstele, & sum wif hine underfeng into hire
huse, þære wæs to name Martha.
 3. Seo hæfde ane suster þe wæs genæmd Maria.
 4. Seo wæs sittende æt ures Drihtenes foten, & hlyste his
worden.
 5. Ac Martha beswanc & bestuddede þa lichamlice behefðen.
 6. Seo stod & cwæþ to þan Hælende, La, Drihten, nis
þe na gemynde, þæt min suster lætt me anen þenigen?
 7. Sæge hire, þæt heo me fylste.
 8. Se Hælend hire andswerede & cwæð, Martha, Martha,
þu eart bisig & gedrefd on feale þingan, ac anlypig þing is behefe.
 10. Maria hæfð gecoren þæt betste dæl, þæt hire
næfre ne byð wiðtogan.
 11. Sume ungelærede mænn wundrigeð, hwæt þiss godspell
belimpe to þære eadigen Marien Cristes moder, & hwi man æt hire
þenunge geræde þiss godspell, ac us þincð, þæt hit rihtlice to
hire gebyreð, beo þan þe ure larðeawes us doð to understandene.
 15. Ðes cæstel, þære ure Drihten in com, betacneð
rihtlice þæt synderlice unwæmme mæden Maria Cristes moder.
 17. For cæstel is geclypod sum heh stepel, þe byð mid wealle
betrymed, swa þæt æigðer oðre bewereð wið unwinen gewinne.
 19. Ðyssen cæstele is rihtlice wiðmeten þæt synderlice
mæden Marie Cristes moder, for heo wæs fæstlice betrymed mid mæigne
unwæmmes mægeðhades on lichame & on geðanca, swa swa mid strangen
cæstelwealle, swa þæt hire næfre ne mihte genelæcen nan lichamlic
galnysse, ne forðen to hire geðanca nan ungelefed hæmeðe.
 24. & for þan þe mægeðhad stranglice mæig
wiðstanden þære galnysse, þæt hit ne byð þurh þæt
oferswiðen, modignysse gelomen gewinð þa infare, for þan wæs
eadmodnysse stepel on hire, & wal þe aferseð ealle modignysse fram
þan mægeðhade.
 27. & for þan þe eadmodnysse wiðstant modignysse,
þæt heo ne byð þurh þæt oferswiðen, galnysse gelomen gewinð
þa infare, for þan þæs mægeðhades weall on hire, þe stranglice
aferrseð ealle galnysse fram eadmodnyssen steple.
 31. & swa is mægeðhades weall, & eadmodnysse stepel
& æigðer mid oðren gestrangod, þæt on hire mægeðhade
næfre ne mihte gefæstnigen modignysse, ne on hire eadmodnysse nan
besmitenysse.
 34. Ac æfre hire wæs on eadmede mægeðhad, & clæne
eadmodnysse.
 35. Genyme we us þæt godspell to gewittnysse hire
mægeðhades & hire eadmodnysse.
 36. Ða þa se ængel hire cydde, þæt heo cænnen scolde
Godes Sune, heo andswerede & acsode, Hwu sceal þiss gewurðen, for ic ne
cann naht of weres gemane?
 38. Gyf ænige mædene, þe hæfde gemynt were to underfone,
wære/ gesæd þæt heo scolde sune geberen, ne þuhte hit hire sellic,
ne heo axigen nolde, Hwu sceal hit gewurðen, þæt ic sune gebide?
 41. Ac eaðe þeos mihte axigen, Hwu sceal þiss gewurðen,
þæt ic sune habbe?
 43. For þeh heo Josepe gehandfæst wære, þehhweðere he
hæfde anrædlice on hire gemynte, þæt heo næfre weres
gemænnysse nolde cunnen.
 45. Emb hire eadmodnysse we mugen eac secgen.
 45. Ða þa se ængel hire brohte gretinge fram heofone rice,
& gewiterede heo, hwu heo wæs þan Hælende to moder gecoren, &
þehhweðere gehealdene mægeðhade and gebletsod ofer ealle wifen, heo
andswerede mid eadmodnysse, Ic eam Drihtenes þenen.
 50. On oðre stowe heo cwæð, Drihten, beseh to minre
eadmodnysse, & þurh þæt me sculen ealle mægðen eadige tellen.
 51. Eale hwu heh mæden Godes moder, Hwæt mihte beon herre?
 52. Eala hwu eadmode moder Godes þinen, Hwu mihte heo eadmodlucor
andswerigen?
 54. Sume næmmeð þone cæstel Magdalum, þe Maria wæs
of Magdalenisc geclypod, & þæt becumð wel to þyssere trahtnunge.
 56. For Magdalus is stepel geclypod, & betacneð eadmodnysse.
 56. Here he nis beo name gecyðed, ac is gesæd sum cæstel,
& þæt nis na on idel gedon.
 58. For sum cæstel, þæt is sunderlic cæstel, þæt
wæs þæt mæden Maria.
 59. For þeh manege oðre habben mægeðhades weall, &
eadmodnyssen stepel, swa þæt heo mædene beon & eac eadmode,
þehhweðere ne mugen heo gehealde ne mægeðhade & modres beon, ne
bearn geberen, swa þeos synderlice dyde, & for þan heo is rihtlice
geclypod sum cæstel, þæt is synderlic cæstel.
 64. For heo wæs synderlice moder & mæden, swa nan oðer
ne mihte ne næfre ma ne mæig, & þeh hit eall gelumpe, þæt
ænig hæfde þa geðincðe, þæt heo mihte mæden beon & eac
cildes moder.
 66. Þehhweðere ne fullcumð næfre nan to þære
mærðe, þæt heo þone ilca sune gebere, oððe ægne his gelica.
 68. For þan rihtlice heo is synderlice se ilca cæstel,
þær ure Drihten in com.
 69. Þæt geat, þær he inn com, þæt is hire geleafe.
 70. For þurh þæt, þæt heo þæs ængles worden
gelefde, hit wearð fullfremod on hire þæt þæt se ængel hire
sæde.
 71. Ne for þæs Hælendes infare, næs se cæstel hire
mægeðhades ne hire eadmodnyssen gewæmmed.
 73. For he is Hælend & na awerdend.
 73. Þa awerde þing he gehælð, & þa gehale he
gefæstneð on strencðe.
 74. His weorc synden, swa swa his name sweigð.
 75. Sum wif hine underfeng on hire hus, þære wæs Martha to
name.
 76. Seo hæfde ane suster þe wæs geclypod Maria.
 77. Ðas twa gesustre, beo þan þe ure larðeawes us
cyðeð, betacnigeð þa twa lif, þe man lætt on rihtwisnysse.
 79. Martha þæt geswyncfulle lif þe we one drohtnigeð,
Maria þæt ece lif þe we to willnigen.
 80. Martha swanc & becarcade to geforðigene þan Hælende
& his þeowen þa lichamlice behefðen.
 82. Maria fæstlice wunede abuten þan Hælende & hlyste
his worden.
 83. Seo studdede emb þa uterlice þing, þeos oðer þa
inweardlice þing gemyndelice besceawode.
 84. Swa swa ure hlæfdige is synderlice þæs Hælendes
moder, swa byð eac synderlice on hire gehealdene, þa weorc þære twegre
lifen, þe þas twa gesustre betacnigeð.
 86. On nanre oðre næs Marthe studdinge on nanen time swa
fullice geforðed toweard Gode, & toweard his leomen, swa on ures
Drihtenes moder.
 89. Ne Marien besceawunge, ne hire hlystinge to Godes worden,
næs næfre on nanre oðre swa fullice geforðed swa on ure Drihtenes
moder.
 91. Uten nu getrehtnigen Marthen weorc, & syððen Marien
sceawunge.
 92. & swa þæt we hit þæs þe openlucor mugen
understanden, trahtnigen we hwæt oðre halgen wyrceð on Marthen wisen,
& hwæt þeos, & hwæt oðre halgen behealdeð & hercnigeð
on Marie wisen, & hwæt þeos.
 95. Oðre underfoð sumne cume leoflice for þæs Hælendes
lufe, ac þeos nænne oðerne cume bute þone Hælend sylf, na
synderlice on oðren herbyrge, bute on hire agene innoðe.
 98. Oðre bescrydeð sumne hnacodne mid ateorigendlicen reafe, ac
þeos gelichamede Godes ungeseowenlicne Sune mid clænen & unbesmitenen
lichame, þe næfre on ecnysse ne seareð, ne ne forroteð, ac on
unwæmme þurhwuneð.
 102. Oðre fedeð sumne hungrigne oððe þurstigne mid
uterlicen mete oððe drænce, ac þeos na feorlucor bute of hire agene
breostes meolca fedde, & fostrode þone þe is God & mann, þa þa
he wæs on mænniscen gecynde hungrig & þurstig.
 105. And swa swa we hit mugen scortlice belucan, ealla þa six
mildheortnysse weorcas, þe God geopeneð on domesdæige loc hwænne he
cweðð, Eall þæt þæt ge dyden anen minre læsten, þæt ge
dyden me sylfen, ealla þa ilca heo dyde synderlice & furðerlucor þone
ænig oðer, na on ænigen oðren lytlen, ac on þan sylfen Godes
Sunen.
 111. Swa swa leofne gyst heo hine husede & innlice
herebyregode.
 112. Ðonne he hnacod wæs, heo hine bewreah mid lichame &
mid reafe.
 113. Ðonne he wæs hungrig & þurstig, heo hine estlice
gefylde mid hire meolca.
 114. On his cildlicen unfernysse, heo hine baðede, &
beðede, & smerede, & bær, & frefrede, & swaðede, &
roccode, swa þæt man mæig rihtlice beo hire secgen, Martha wæs bisig
& cearig emb þa þenunge.
 117. Ða þa he wæs genumen & on rode gefestned, swa swa
on cwarterne gedon, þæt heo com, swa swa hit awriten is, Big þæs
Hælendes rode stod Maria his moder.
 119. Onmang þyssen þingen heo wæs bisig & gedrefd.
 120. Gedrefd heo wæs, þa þa heo fleah into Egypte for Herode
kinge, þe hire Cild wolde fordon.
 122. Gedrefd heo wæs, þa þa heo understod þæt þæt
Judeisce folc wiðsette hire Sune to deaðe.
 123. Æt þan ænde heo wæs inlice gedrefod, & swa swa
Symeon hire hwilen ær gewitegode, his slege þurheode hire sawle, þa þa
heo geseh hire swylcne Sune nymen, binden & swingan, & bespæten his
ansene, cynehelmigen hine mid þornen, earplættigen, & on rode
fæstnigen, sweltan & bebyrigen.
 128. Beo hire man mæg rihtlice secgen, Martha, Martha, þu eart
bisig & gedrefed on feala þingan.
 129. Ne tweonige nane mæn, þæt seo gedrefde moder nolde
beon gescild wið þære gedrefednysse, & þæt hire Sune, gyf him
gewill wære, hire gehulpe mid þære godcunden strængðe þe heo on
him wyste, þe betacneð Marie Magdalene.
 133. Ðæt betacneð þæt Martha bemænde to þan
Hælende, þæt heo næfde fultum of hire suster to þan lichamlicen
geswynce, þiss is Marthe dæl.
 135. Ac hwa mæig, swa wurðlice swa hit gebyrede, gereccen hwu
herigendlice is on þære eadigen Cristes moder Marien dæl, þæt
þæt se Hælend herede?
 137. Syððen hit is swa swa we sæden, & betere þone we
sæden on þæs Hælendes moder, Marthan geswyncfulle wica, þe se
Hælend naht ne herode, ac þehhweðere he hit na ne tælde.
 140. Hwylc wæs on hire þæt dæl þe Maria geceas, þe
ure Drihten herede & cwæð þæt hit selest wære, & heo eac
eadig, for hit næfre hire ne wurde benumen.
 142. Eala hwu mycel swotnysse wæs mid þære eadige cwen,
þa þa se Halge Gast on hire becom, & þæs hecsten mihte heo
bescadewode, swa þæt heo of þan ilcan Halgen Gaste wearð
bearneacninde.
 145. Hwæt wanode hire of Godes wisedome, þa þa inne hire
lutede eall Godes wisedom, & God sylf on hire innoðe timbrede him sylfen
mænnisc lichame.
 147. Se apostel Paulus cwæð, On Criste synd beclysede Godes
mihten & his wisedom, & ealle þa hord wittes & wisedomes, &
Crist on Marien, & swa is Godes mihte & his wisedom & ealle þa
hord wittes & wisedomes on Marien.
 151. Ðeos sæt wel þan Hælende æt foten & æt
heafde hlystinde his worden.
 152. Heo understod ealle þa word þære ænglen, &
þære herdan, & þære tungelwitegan, & eac forðen þæs
sylfen Hælendes, & heold gemyndelice on hire heorte.
 154. Næfre ær ne æfter, nan oðer swa forðlice ne
gesmæhte, hwu swote is ure Drihten.
 156. Heo wæs wel beo þæs witegan cwide þurhdrænct mid
þære welle Godes huse, & of þan streamen his esten hire wæs wel
gescænct, þæt næs nan wunder, for innen hire wæs se rihte spryng
þære lifes welle, þær of flowð eall seo fullfremednysse þære
twegre lifen þe we embe specað.
 160. Emb feala þing heo wæs swa swa Martha bisig &
cearig.
 161. Anlypig þing hire wæs este & gemynde swa swa Marian,
for an þing is beheflic, þa feala þing hire byð wiðtogene, þæt
an hire is belæfd, for þan we secgeð þæt heo synderlice
fullforðede Marthen geswyncfulle wica, & synderlice heo gehealt þæt
seleste Marien dæl.
 165. Ac hire is Marthe dæl benumen, for heo nis na læng bisig
to fostrigen hire Sune swa swa cilde, nu him þenigeð ænglena werod swa
swa Hlaforde.
 167. Nu ne carcað heo to befleon Herodes ehtnysse into Egypte mid
hire Cilde, for he is gestogan into heofone, & Herodes is beflogen his
ansyne into helle þeostre.
 170. Nu nis heo namare gedrefd for þære Judean ehtnysse
toweard hire Sune, for ealle þing him synd underðeodde.
 171. Ne sculen namare þa Judees hire Sune swingan ne cwellen, for
he is arisen of deaðe, & ne swelt næfre ma.
 173. Heonenforð næfð se deað nænne styde on him.
 174. Ðuss hire is Marthen geswyncfulle lif eall ætbroigden,
& to hire freome hire is Marie dæl belæfd, þæt hire næfre ne
byð benumen, for heo is up ahafen ofer ænglene werod.
 176. & eall hire wille hire is geforðed on godnysse, for heo
gesihð hire Sune eall ealswa he is, neb wið nebb, & wuneð on ecere
blisse mid him.
 179. Ðiss is þæt seleste dæl þæt hit næfre ne
byð hire wiðtogen, þæs dæles us geunne God þurh hire þingunge
þæt we beon dælnymende þurh his mildheortnysse.
