LS 23 (MaryofEgypt)
B3.3.23.
Mary of Egypt: Skeat 1881-1900, II, 2-52.



 1. <foreign>DE TRANSITU MARIAE AEGYPTIACE</foreign>.
 1. ÐAS HERIGENDLICESTAN GEHWYRFEDNYSSE ægþer ge dæda ge
þeawa, and þa micclan hreowsunga, and swa ellenlic gewinn þære
arwurðan Egyptiscan Marian, hu heo hyre lifes tida on þam westene gefylde,
of grecisc geþeode on læden gewende Paulus se arwurða diacon sancte
Neapolis þære cyrcan.
 6. Witodlice hit is geræd þæt Raphahel se heahengel wære
to Tobie sprecende, æfter þæra eagena forlætnysse, and eft æfter
þæra wulderfæstan onlihtnysse, and æfter þam forðgewitendum
frecednyssum þe he of genered wæs, and þus cwæð, Soðlice hit is
swiðe derigendlic þæt man mancynnes digle geopenige.
 10. And eft þære sawle is micel genyðrung þæt mon þa
wuldorfæstan Godes weorc bediglige.
 12. For þam þingum ic nænige þinga ne forsuwige þa
halgan geræcednyssa, se me gecydde þæt ic on gefealle on þone
genyðredan cwyde þæs slawan þeawas, se þone onfangenan talent fram
his hlaforde butan geweaxnysse ahydde on eorðan.
 16. Ac ne sy me nan man to ungeleafful be þam þingum writende,
þe ic gehyrde and geaxode on þissa wisan; ne gewurðe hit þæt ic on
þam halgum gerecednyssum wæge oþþe ic þa spræce forsuwige: <foreign>ITEM
RATIO DE EADEM</foreign>.
 19. SUM WER WÆS ON ANUM MYNSTRE ON PALESTINA ÐÆRE
mægþe.
 20. On his lifes þeawum he wæs swiþe gefrætewod, se
wæs fram cildhade on munuclicum þeawum healice getyd and gelæred, se
wæs gehaten Zosimus.
 22. Ðes witodlice, swa ic ær cwæð, on anum Palestina
mynstre fram frymþe drohtnode, and he wæs on forhæfednysse weorcum se
afandedesta geworden on eallum þam munuclicum regolum.
 25. And he ealle þæs regoles bebodu, and fulfremednysse
þæs munuclican þeowtscypes untallice geheold, and he eac swilce wisan
him þær sylf toeacan geihte, forþan þe he gewilnode his flæsc þam
gaste underþeodan.
 28. Swa soðlice he wæs fulfremod on eallum munuclicum
þeawum, þæt wel oft munecas of feorrum stowum and of mynstrum to him
comon, þæt hi to his bysne and to his larum hi gewriðon, and to
þære onhyringe his forhæfednysse hi underðeoddon.
 32. Ðas wisan he ealle on him hæbbende wæs, and he næfre
fram þam smeagungum haligra gewrita his mod awenda.
 34. And ealle þa godnyssa þe he bebreac, he wæs gast
brucende, and an weorc he hæfde unforswigod and næfre geteorod, þæt
wæs sealmsang mærsung and haligra gewrita smeagung.
 37. Wel oft eac swilce þæs ðe hi rehton, þæt he wære
gefremed wyrðe beon þære godcundan onlihtnysse þurh æteowednyss
fram Gode þære gastlican gesihþe, swa þæt nan wundor is ne eac
ungelyfedlic þincg, be ðæm þe Drihten sylf cwæð; Eadige beoð
þa clænheortan, forðan þe hi God geseoð.
 41. Swa miccle ma þa gesceawiað þa opennysse þære
godcundan onlihtnysse þe heora lichaman symle geclænsiað mid syfrum
þeawum, and mid þurhwæccendlican mode forð heonon to underfonne þa
toweardan mede on þære ecan eadignysse.
 45. Witodlice swa he sylf sæde Zosimus, þæt he sylf wære
fram þam modorlicum beorðrum on þæt mynster befæst.
 46. And oþ þæt þreo and fiftigðe gear he wæs þær
on þam regole drohtnigende.
 48. And æfter þysum he wæs gecnyssed fram sumum geþancum,
swa swa he wære on eallum þingum fulfremed, and he nanre mæran lare
bysene ne beþorfte on his mode.
 50. And he wæs þus sprecende, hwæðer ænig munuc on
eorðan sy þæt me mage aht niwes getæcan oððe me on ænigum
þingum gefultumian þæs þe ic sylf nyte, oððe þæt ic on þam
munuclicum weorcum sylf ne gefylde, oþþe hweðer ænig þæra sy þe
westen lufiað, þe me on his dædum beforan sy.
 55. Ðas and þysum gelicum him þencendum, him ætstod sum
engel and him to cwæð, Eala þu Zosimus swiðe licwyrðlice þu
gefyldest, swa þeahhwæðere, nis nan man þe hine fulfremedne
æteowe.
 58. Miccle mare is þæt gewinn þæt þe toweard is,
þonne þæt forðgewitene þeah þu hit nyte.
 59. Ac þæt þu mæge ongytan and oncnawan hu miccle synd
oþre hælo wegas, far ut of þinum earde, and cum to þam mynstre
þæt neah Iordane is geset.
 62. He þa sona witodlice of þam mynstre for, þe he fram his
cildhade on drohtnode, and to Iordane becom, ealra wætera þam halgestan.
 64. He eode þa innon þam mynstre þe him se engel bebead.
 65. Þa ongan he ærest sprecan to þam munece þe þæs
mynstres geat bewiste, and he hine þam abbude gecydde, and him to
gelædde.
 67. Ða æfter þam onfangenum gebede, swa hit mid munecum
þeaw is, he him to cwæð, Hwænne come þu hider broðor, oþþe
for hwilcum þingum geðeoddest þu þe to swa eadmodum munecum?
 70. Zosimus him andwyrde, Nis me nan neod, fæder, þe to
secgenne hwanon ic come, ac ic for lare intingan eow her gesohte, forþon ic
her fela gastlica þeawa on eow geaxode, and beforan þa synd beforan
gesegnesse Gode licwurðe.
 73. Se abbod him to cwæð, God, se þe ana gehealt and
gehæleð, swa fela mettrumnyssa, he þe and us on his godcundum bebodum
gestrangige, and us gerecce þa weorc to begangenne þe him licige.
 76. Ne mæg ænig mann oþerne getimbrian buton he hine sylfne
gelomlice behealde, and he mid syfrum andgyte þæt beo sylf wyrcende, God
to gewitan hæbbende.
 79. Ac swa þeahhwæðere forþan þe þu cwæde þæt
þe Cristes soðe lufu hyder us gelædde, eadmodne munuc us to gesecenne,
ac wuna her mid us gif þu forðy come, and us ealle se goda hyrde
ætgædere fede mid þære gife þæs halgan gastes.
 82. Ðysum þus gecwedenum wordum fram þam abbode, Zosimus his
cneowa gebigde, and onfangenum gebede on þam mynstre wunode.
 84. Þær he geseah witodlice ealle witon on þeawum and on
dædum scinende, and on gaste weallende, and Drihtne þeowigende, þær
wæs unablinnendlic staþolfæstnys Godes herunge æghwylcne dæg, and
eac nihtes.
 88. And þær næfre unnytte spræce næron, ne geþanc
goldes oðð and seolfres, oþþe oþra gestreona; ne furðon se nama
mid him næs oncnawen.
 90. Ac þæt an wæs swiðost fram heom eallum geefst,
þæt heora ælc wære on lichaman dead and on gaste libbende.
 91. Mid þam soðlice hi hæfdon ungeteorodne þæt wæron
þa godcundan gespræcu.
 93. Heora lichaman witodlice mid þam nydþearfnyssum anum
feddon, þæt wæs mid hlafe and mid wætere, to þam þæt hi þe
scearpran on þære soðan Godes lufu hi æteowdon.
 95. Þas weorc Zosimus behealdende hine sylfne geornlice to
fulfremednysse aþenede gemang þam emnwyrhtum, þe þone godcundan
neorxnewang butan ablinnendnysse geedniwodon.
 98. Þa æfter þysum genealæhte seo tid þæs halgan
lenctenfæstenes þe eallum Cristenum mannum geset is to mærsigenne, and
hi sylfe to clænsunga for wurðunga þære godcundan þrowunga and his
æristes.
 101. Ðæt geat soðlice þæs mynstres næfre geopenod
wæs, ac symle hit wæs belocen, and hi swa butan æghwilcre
gedrefednysse heora ryne gefyldon.
 103. Ne hit næfre næs to geopenigenne buton wenunga hwilc
munuc for hwilcere nydþearfe ut fore.
 105. Seo stow wæs swa westen and swa digle, þæt næs na
þæt an þæt heo wæs ungewunelic, ac eac swilce uncuð þam
landleodum him sylfum.
 107. On þas wisan wæs se regol fram ealdum tidum gehealden,
and fram þysum weorcum is to gelyfanne þæt God Zosimus on þæt
mynster gelædde.
 109. Nu ic wille æfter þysum areccan hu þæs mynstres
gesetnysse healdende wæs.
 110. On þam drihtenlican dæge þære forman fæstenwucan
þe we nemniað halgan dæg, þær wæron gewunelice gedone þa
godcundan gerynu.
 112. And þonne gemænsumedon heo þæs libbendan and
þæs unbesmitenan lichaman ures Drihtnes Hælendes Cristes.
 114. And þonne æfter þam ætgædere hwon gereordende
syþþan, wæron ealle on þæt gebædhus gegaderode, mid gebigedum
cneowum and eadmodum gebede heora ælc oþerne grette, and heora abbudes
eadmodlice bletsunga bædon, þæt hi on þam godcundan gewinne þe
fæstlicor gestrangode wæron.
 119. Ðysum þus gefylledum þæs mynstres geatu wæron
geopenode, and hi þone þisne sealmsang sungon togædere; <foreign>Dominus
illuminatio mea et salus mea quem timebo</foreign>.
 121. And swa ætgædere ut foron.
 122. Ænne oððe twegen on þam mynstre hi forleton, næs
na to þam þæt hi þa begytanan gestreon heoldon, næs þær
swilces nan þincg, ac þæt hi þæt gebedhus butan þam godcundan
symbelnyssum ne forleton.
 125. And heora æghwilc hine sylfne metsode swa swa he mihte
oþþe wolde.
 126. Sum him mid bær þæs lichaman genihtsumnysse, sum
þæra palmtreowa æppla, sum beana mid wætere ofgotene, sum nan
þincg buton þone lichaman ænne and þone gegyrlan, ac hi wæron
gefedde him þæs gecyndes neadþearfnysse abæde, þæt wæs mid
þam wyrtum þe on þam westene weoxon.
 131. And hine þær æghwylc sylfne on forhæfednysse band
swa him sylfum geþuhte, swa þæt heora nan nyste oþres wisan oþþe
dæda.
 133. Ðonne hi hæfdon Iordane þa ea oferfaren þonne
asyndrede hine æghwilcne feor fram oþrum, and heora nan hine eft to his
geferum ne geþeodde.
 135. Ac gif heora hwilc oþerne feorran geseah wið his weard, he
sona of þam siðfæte beah and on oþre healfe wende, and mit him sylfum
leofode and wunode on singalum gebedum and fæstenum.
 138. On þas wisan witodlice þæt fæsten gefyllende, hi eft
to þam mynstre cyrdon ærðan drihtenlican æristes dæge, þæt
wæs on þam symbeldæge þe we palmdæg gewunelice nemnað.
 141. Æghwilc on his agenum ingehyde mid him sylfum habbende
wæs his agenes geswinces gewitnysse hwæt he wyrcende wæs, and hwilcra
geswinca sæde sawende.
 144. And heora nan oþerne ne axode on hwilce wisan he þæs
geswinces gewin gefylde.
 145. Ðis wæs witodlice þæs mynstres regol, and þus
fulfremodlice wæs gehealden æghwilc swa ic ær cwæð, þæt hine
sylfne on þæt westen to Gode geðeodde, and mid him sylfum wunnon
þæt hi mannum ne licodon buton Gode sylfum.
 148. Ða witodlice Zosimus mid þære gewunelican æ þæs
mynstres Iordane þæt wæter oferfor, lytles hwega for þæs lichaman
nedbehæfednyssum mid him hæbbende.
 151. And on þæs regoles mærsunge geond þæt westen for,
and on þære tide þæs gereordes and þæs gecyndes nydþearfnysse
brucende, on niht on eorþan sittende and hwon restende, and slep swa hwær
swa hine seo æfenrepsung gemette.
 155. And eft on ærnemergen forgangende swa he wæs
unablinnendlice on fore geseted and begangende, forðan þe he gewilnode swa
swa he eft sæde þæt he sumne fæder on þam westene funde, þe hine
on sumum þingum getimbrede þæs ðe he sylf ær ne cuðe.
 159. And swa six and twentig daga þæt færeld þurhteah,
swilce he to sumum menn mid gewisse fore.
 160. Ða þa seo tid middæges to becom, þa oðstod to
sumere hwile hine fram þam siðfæte ahæbbende, and eastweardes
wendende, and hine gewunelice gebæd, forþan þe he gewunode on þam
gesettum tidum þæs dæges þone ryne his siðfætes gefæstnian,
and standende singan and mid gebigedum cneowum gebiddan.
 165. Ða þa he soðlice sang and mid þære geornfullan
behealdnysse up locode and þone heofon beheold, þa geseah he him on þa
swiðran healfe þær he on gebedum stod, swa swa he on mennisce gelicnysse
on lichaman hine æteowan, and þa wæs he ærest swiþe afyrht,
forþan þe he wende þæt hit wære sumes gastes scinhwy þæt he
þær geseah.
 170. Ac sona swa þeahhwæþere mid Cristes rodetacne
getrymmede hine, and him þone ege fram awearp.
 172. Ða eac witodlice se ende his gebedes wæs gefylled, he
þa his eagan bewende, and þær soðlice man geseah westweardes on
þæt westen efstan, and witodlice þæt wæs wifman þæt þær
gesewen wæs; swiðe sweartes lichaman heo wæs for þære sunnan
hæto, and þa loccas hire heafdes wæron swa hwite swa wull, and þa na
siddran þonne oþ þone swuran.
 177. Ða wisan Zosimus georne behealdende wæs, and for
þære gewilnedan swetnysse þære wuldorfæstan gesihðe, he fægen
gefremed ofstlice arn on þa healfe þe he efstan geseah þæt him
þær æteowde.
 180. Ne geseah he witodlice on eallum þam dagum ær nane
mennisclice gesihðe, ne nanre nytena oþþe fugela oððe wildeora hiw,
and he forðy arn geornlice, and gewilnode to oncnawenne hwæt þæt
wildeora wære þe him æteowde.
 184. Sona swa hi geseah Zosimus þa witodlice his ealdan ylde
ofergetiligende, and þæt geswinc his syðfætes ne understandende mid
hrædestan ryne þenigende arn, forðam þe he gewilnode hine geðeodan
þam þe ðær fleah; he witodlice hire wæs ehtende, and heo wæs
fleonde.
 188. Ða wæs Zosimus ryna hwæðra sticmælum near
gefremed.
 189. Ða þa he swa neah wæs þæt heo mihte his stemne
gehyran, þa ongan he forð sendan þyllice stemne mid hluddre clypunga
wepende and þus cwæð, Hwi flihst þu me forealdodne syngigan, þu
Godes þeowen?
 192. Geanbida min for þam hihte þæs edleanes ðe þu swa
micclum geswunce.
 193. Stand and syle me þines gebedes bletsungan þurh þone God
þe him nænne fram ne awyrpð.
 195. Ðas word soðlice Zosimus mid tearum geypte.
 196. Þa becom heo yrnende to sumere stowe on þære wæs
getacnod swilce fordruwod burna.
 197. Þa ða hi witodlice þyder becomon, þa sceat heo inn on
þone burnan, and eft upp on oþre healfe.
 198. Zosimus þa soðlice clypigende, and na hwider
furðclypigende/, stod þa on oþre healfe þæs burnan þe þær
gesewen wæs, and to geihte þa tearas þam tearum, and gemænigfealdode
þa sworetunga þam siccetungum, swa þæt þær nan þincg gehyred
næs buton seo geomerung þæs heofes.
 203. Ða witodlice se lichama þe ðær fleah ðyllice stemne
forðsende and þus cwæð, ðu abbod Zosimus miltsa me for Gode, ic ðe
bidde, for þon ic ne mæg me þe geswutelian, and ongeanweardes þe
gewenden, forþon ic eom wifhades mann, and eallunga lichamlicum wæfelsum
bereafod, swa swa þu sylf gesihst, and þa sceame mines lichaman hæbbende
unoferwrigene.
 209. Ac gif þu wille me earmre forworhtre þine halwendan gebedu
to forlætan awyrp me þonne hyder þinne scyccels þe þu mid bewæfed
eart, þæt ic mæge þa wiflican tyddernysse oferwreon, and to ðe
gecyrran and þinra gebeda onfon.
 212. Ða gegrap Zosimus swiðlic ege, and fyrhtu witodlice
forþan þe he gehyrde þæt heo be his naman næmnede hine þone ðe
heo næfre ær ne geseah, ne næfre fore secgan ne gehyrde, buton
þæt he swutellice ongeat þæt heo mid þære godcundan
foresceawunge onliht wæs.
 216. He þa fæstlice swa dyde swa heo bebead hine þam
scyccelse ongyrede þe he mid bewæfed wæs on bæclincg gewend hire to
wearp.
 218. Heo þa þæs onfeng, and hire lichaman oferwreah, and
gegyrede hire be þam dæle þe heo mæst mihte and mæst neod wæs
to beheligenne.
 221. Heo þa to Zosimam wende and him to cwæð, Hwi wæs
þe la abbod Zosimus swa micel neod me synful wif to geseonne, oððe
hwæs wilnast þu fram me to hæbbenne, oþþe to witenne þæt þu
ne slawedest swa micel geswinc to gefremmanne for minum þingum?
 225. He þa sona on þa eorðan hine astrehte, and hire
bletsunga bæd, heo ongean hine astrehte, and his bletsunga bæd.
 226. Ða æfter manega tida fæce cwæð þæt wif to
Zosime, ðe gedafenað abbud Zosimus to biddenne and to bletsigenne, forþan
þu eart underwreðed mid þære sacerdlican lare, and þu eart tellende
Cristes gerynu mid þam gyfum þæra godcundlican æt his þam halgan
weofode manegum gearum þeowigende.
 231. Ðas word witodlice gebrohton on Zosime micelne ege and
fyrhtu, and he wæs byfigende; and he wæs geondgoten mid þæs swates
dropum.
 233. Ða ongan he sworettan swa swa eallunga gewæced on þam
oreðe belocen, and ðus cwæð, Eala ðu gastlice modor, geswutela nu
hwæt þu sy of þære gesihþe, forþam þu eart soðlice Godes
þinen.
 237. Geþinga me nu of þam geongran dæle for þyssere
worulde dead gefremed on þam geswutelað on þe seo godcunde lufu ealra
swiðost þæt þu me be naman næmdest, þone þu næfre ær ne
gesawe.
 240. Ac for þam þe seo gyfu ne bið oncnawen of þære
medemnysse, ac gewuna he is to getacnigenne of þære sawla dædum; bletsa
þu me for Drihtne, ic þe bidde, and syle me þæt unbereafigendlice
gebæd þinre fulfremednysse.
 243. Ða ongan heo hire onemnþrowigan þæs ealdan witan
staðolfæstnysse, and cwæð, God sy gebletsod se ðe is sawla hælu
tiligende.
 245. Ða forgeaf heo Zosime andswarigende.
 246. AMEN; ða arisan hi butu of þære eorþan þa ongan
eft/ þæt wif sprecan to þam ealdan and ðus cwæþ, Eala man for
hwylcre wisan come þu to me synfulre?
 250. Swaþeah hwæðre forþam þe seo gyfu þæs
haligan/ gastes to þam gerihte þæt ðu hwylce þenunga minon
lytlan lichaman to gehyðnysse gegearwige, sege me hu nu to dæge on
middanearde Cristes folc sy gereht, and hu ða caseres, oððe hu is nu
gelæswod seo heord Cristes rihtgeleaffullan gesamnunga.
 255. Zosimus hire andswarode, Eala þu halige modor þinum
halgum gebedum God hæfð forgyfen staðolfæste sibbe.
 257. Muneces and for drihtne middanearde and for me synfullum
þæt me ne wurðe geidlod þæt geswinc þises siðfætes, and
se weg swa myccles westenes.
 260. Þa cwæð heo, ðe gedafenað abbot Zosimus for me
and for eallum gebiddan forðam þe þu sy on þam scaderhade swa
swa ic ær cwæþ.
 262. Ac for ðinum þingum and for þam þe we habbað
þæt gebod hyrsumnysse, þæt þe me þurh ðe geboden is
mid/ godum willan ic do.
 264. And þus cweðende hi to þam eastan gewend upahafenum
eagum on þa heahnysse and aþenedum earmum ongan gebiddan mid þære
welera styrungum on stilnesse swa þæt ðær næs eallinga nan stemne
gehyred þæs þe man ongyten mihte, þæs gebedes eac swylce Zosimus
nan þing ongytan ne mihte.
 268. He stod witodlice swa swa he sylf sæde, byfiende and þa
eorþan behealdende, and nan þing eallinga sprecende.
 270. He swor witodlice God him to gewitan on his wordum
foresettende, þæt ða get þa þa heo þus þurhwunode on þære
gebedes astandendnysse he his eagan lythwon fram ðære eorðan upahof
þæt he geseah hi upahefene swa swa mannes elne fram þære eorðan,
and on þære lyfte hangiende gebiddan ongan.
 275. Ða þa he þis geseah þa wearð he gegripen mid
mycelre fyrhto, and hine þa on eorðan astrehte and mid swate ofergoten
wearð and swiðlice gedrefed.
 277. Naht geþrystlæhte specan, butan wið him sylfum
þæt an.
 278. Ða þa he on þære eorðan læg astreht þa
gedrefed/ wearð he on his geþance, smeagende hwæðre hwon hit
gast wære ðæt ðær mid hwylcere hiwunga gebæde hi.
 281. Heo ða þæt wif hi bewende and þone munuc up
arærde þus cweðende, To hwy gedrefest þu abbot þine geþohtas to
geæswicianne on me swylce ic hwylc gast syrwiende gebedu fremme.
 284. Ac wite þu man þæt ic eom synful wif,
Swaþeahhwæðere/ utan ymbseald mid þam halgan fulluhte, and ic nan gast
ne eom ac æmerge and axe and eall flæsc and nan gastlice.
 287. Ða heo ðus cwæþ heo hire andwlitan gebletsode
mid þære halgan rodetacne, and hire eagan and weleras and eac hire
breost mid þære bletsunga heo getrymede and þus cwæð, God us alyse
abbot Zosimus fram urum wiðerwinnan and fram his anbrincgellan forðam þe
his æfst is mycel ofer us.
 291. Ðas word se ealda hyrende hine adune astrehte.
 318. Þa ðincg þe be me synd, sona þu flihst fram me on þi
gemete swilc man næddran fleo.
 319. Ac swa þeahhwæðere ic þe arecce naht forhælende,
and þe ærest bidde, þæt þu ne geteorige for me gebiddan, þæt
ic geearnige and gemete on domes dæge hwilce hwugu mildheortnysse.
 322. Se ealda mid tearum ofergoten ongan biterlice wepan.
 323. Þa ongan þæt wif cyðan and gereccan eall þa þincg
þe be hire gedone wæron þus cwæðende, ic hæfde broþor and
eðel on Egyptum and þær mid minum magum wunode.
 325. Þa on þam twelftan geare minre ylde, þa ongan ic heora
lufu forhycgan, and to Alexandrian þære byrig becom.
 327. Ac me sceamað nu to gereccenne hu ic on þam fruman
ærest minne fæmnhad besmat, and hu ic unablinnendlice and unafyllendlice
þam leahtrum, and þæra synlusta læg underþeoded.
 330. Þis is nu witodlice sceortlice to areccanne; ac ic nu
swaþeah hraðor gecyðe þæt þu mæge oncnawan þone unalyfedan
bryne minra leahtra þe ic hæfde on þære lufe þæs geligeres.
 332. Ac miltsa me abbud; eac on <foreign>xvii</foreign> wintrum ic openlice folca
meniu geondferde on þam bryne forligeres licgende.
 334. Ne forleas ic na minne fæmnhad for æniges mannes gyfum,
oððe ic witodlice ahtes onfenge fram ænigum þe me aht gyfan woldon, ac
ic wæs swiðe onæled mid þære hatheortnysse þæs synlustes,
þæt ic gewilnode butan ceape þæt hi me þe mænigfealdlicor to
geurnon, to þy þæt ic þe eð mihte gefyllan þa scyldfullan
gewilnunga mines forligeres.
 340. Ne þu ne wen na þæt ic aht underfenge for ænegum
welan, ac symle on wædlunge lyfde, for þon ic hæfde swa ic ær
sæde unafyllendlice gewilnunga swa þæt ic me sylfe unablinnendlice on
þam adale þæs manfullan forligeres besylede and þæt me wæs to
yrmðe, and þæt ic me tealde to life þæt swa unablinnendlice
þurhtuge þæs gecyndes teonan.
 345. Þa ic þus leofode þa geseah ic on sumere tide miccle
meniu Affricana and Egypta togædere yrnende swa swa to sæ.
 347. Ða gemette ic færunga heora sumne, and þone axode
hwæþer he wende þæt seo mæniu efstan wolde.
 348. He me andswarode and þus cwæð þæt hi to Hierusalem
faran woldon for þære halgan rode wurðunga þe man æfter naht
manegum dagum wurðian sceolde.
 351. Ða cwæð ic to him, Wenst þu hwæðer hi me
underfon willan, gif ic mid him faran wille?
 352. Ða cwæð he, Gif þu hæfst þæt færeht ne
forwyrnþ þe heora ænig.
 353. Ða cwæð ic to him, Broðor soðlice næbbe ic nan
færeht to syllanne, ac ic wille faran, and an þæra scypa astigan, and
þeah hi nellan hi me afedað, and ic me sylfe heom befæste, and hæbben
hi minne lichaman to gewealde for þam færehte, þæt hi me þe
hrædlicor underfon; Miltsa me, abbud, forðon ic gewilnode mid him to
farenne, þæt ic þe ma emwyrhtena on þære þrowunge mines wynlustas
hæfde.
 359. Ic cwæð ær to þe, ðu halga wer miltsa me, þæt
þu me ne genyde to areccenne mine gescyndnysse.
 361. God wat þæt ic heora forhtige, for þam þe ic wat
þæt þas mine word ægðer gewemmað ge þe ge þas lyfte.
 362. Zosimus soðlice þa eorðan mid tearum ofergeotende hire
to cwæð, Eala þu gastlice modor, sege for Gode ic þe bidde, and ne
forlæt þu þa æfterfylgednysse swa halwendre gerecednysse.
 365. And þus cwæð, Se geonglincg gehyrde sona þæt
bysmor minra worda, and hlihhende me fram gewat.
 367. Ic þa sona þa swingle me fram awearp, þe ic seldon
gewunode on handa to hæbbenne, and to þære sæ arn, þær þær
ic hi geseah gesamnode.
 369. Þa geseah ic tyn geonge men, ætgædere standende be
þam waruðe, genoh þæslice on lichaman, and on gebærum, and ful
licwurðe me þuhte to mines lichaman luste.
 372. Ic me þa unsceandlice swa swa ic gewuna wæs, tomiddes
heora gemengde and him to cwæð, Nimað me on eower færeld mid eow, ne
beo ic na eow unlicwyrðe.
 374. And ic hi þa ealle sona to þam manfullum leahtrum and
ceahhetungum bysmerlicum astyrede, mid manegum oþrum fullicum, and
fracodlicum gespræcum.
 376. Hi þa witodlice mine unsceamlicam gebæra geseonde me on
heora scip namon to him and forð hreowan.
 378. Eala Zosimus, hu mæg ic þe areccan, oþþe hwilc tunga
mæg hit asecgan oþþe eara gehyran, þa mandæda þe on þam
scipfærelde wæron, and on þam siðfæte gefremede, and hu ic to
syngigenne genydde ægðer ge ða earman willendan, and þa earman
syllendan.
 382. Nis nan asecgendlic oððe unasecgendlic fracodlicnysse
hiwung þæs ic ne sih tihtende and lærende, and fruma gefremed.
 384. Beo la nu on þysum gehealden, forþan þe ic wundrige hu
seo sæ aðolode and adruge mine þa unrihtlican lustas, oððe humeta
seo eorðe hyre muð ne untynde, and me swa cwyce on helle ne besencte þe
swa manega sawla on forspillednysse grin gelædde, ac þæs þe ic hopige
þæt God mine hreowsunga sohte, se ðe nænne ne forlætað
forwurðan, ac ealle hale gedeð þe on hine gelyfað.
 390. Forðon soðlice he nele þæs synfullan deað, ac
langsumlice his gehwyrfednysse bið.
 391. We þa swa mid micclum ofste, witodlice to Hierusalem foron,
and swa mænige dagas swa ic ær þære rode symbelnysse on þære
ceastre wunode mid gelicum fullicum weorcum me gemængde, and eac wyrsum.
 395. Næs ic na genihtsumigende on þam geongum, ðe on
þære sæ mid me, oððe on þam soðfæte hæmdon, ac ic eac
swilce mænga ælðeodige and ceastergewarena on þa dæda minra scylda
gegadrigende/, and beswicende besmat.
 398. Ða þa seo symbelnyss becom þære halgan deorwurðan
rode upahefennysse, Ic foregeode þa geongan swa swa ær on þæt grin
forspillednysse teonde.
 400. Þa geseah ic soðlice on ærnemergen hi ealle anmodlice
to þære cyrcan yrnan.
 401. Þa ongan ic yrnan mid þam yrnendum, and samod mid heom
teolode toforan þam temple becuman.
 403. Þa þa seo tid becom þa halgan rode to wurþigenne, þa
ongan ic nydwræclice gemang þam folce wið þæs folces þringan, and
swa mid micclum geswince ic ungesælige to þæs temples dura becom mid
þam þe þær ineodon.
 406. Þa ic sceolde in on þa dura gangen, þa ongunnon hi butan
ælcere lættinge ingangan; me witodlice þæt godcunda mægen
þæs ganges bewerede, and ic sona wæs ut aþrungen fram eallum þam
folce, oððe ic ænlipigu on þam cafertune to læfe oþstod.
 410. Þa ongan ic þencan þæt me þæt gelumpe for
þære wiflican unmihte, and ic me þa eft ongan mæncgan to oþrum,
þæt ic wolde on sume wisan inn geþringan.
 412. Ac ic swanc on idel, mid þam þe ic þone ðerscwold
þæra dura gehran.
 414. And hi ealle þyder inn onfangene wæron butan ælcere
lettinge, þa wæs ic ana ut asceofen.
 415. Ac swilce me hwilc strang meniu ongean stode þæt me
þone ingang beluce, swa me seo færlice Godes wracu þa duru bewerede,
oððe ic eft standende on þæs temples cafertune wæs.
 418. Þus ic þrywa oþþe feower siþum þrowode minne
willan to geseonne, and eac to fremanne, and þa ða ic naht ne gefremode,
þa ongan ic ofer þæt georne wenan and min lichama wæs swiðe
geswenced for þam nyde þæs geþringes.
 421. Ða gewat ic witodlice þanone, and me ana gestod on sumum
hwomme þæs cafertunes, and on minum mode geornlice þohte and smeade for
hwilcum intingum me wære forwyrned þæs liffæstan treowes ansyn.
 424. Þa onhran soðlice min mod and þa eagan minre heortan
hælo andgit mid me sylfre þencende þæt me þone ingang belucen þa
onfeormeganda minra misdæda.
 427. Ða ongan ic biterlice wepan, and swiðe gedrefed mine
breost cnyssan, and of inneweardre heortan heofonde forðbringan þa
geomorlican siccetunga.
 429. Ða geseah ic of þære stowe þe ic on stod, þære
halgan godes cennestran anlicnysse standende.
 431. And ic cwæð to hire geornlice and unforbugendlice
behealdende and cweðende, Eala þu wuldorfæste hlæfdige þe þone
soðan God æfter flæsces gebyrde acendest, geara ic wat þæt hit nis
na gedafenlic ne þæslic.
 434. Þæt ic þe swa grimlice forworht eom, þæt ic
þine anlicnysse sceawige, and gebidde mid swa mænigfealdum besmitenum
gesihþum.
 436. Þu wære symle fæmne oncnawan, and þinne lichaman
hæbbende clæne and unwemmed; forþon witodlice genoh rihtlic is me swa
besmitenre fram þinre clænan ungewemmednysse beon ascirod, and fram
aworpen.
 439. Ac swa þeahhwæðere forþan ðe ic gehyrde þæt
God wære mann forðy gefremod þe þu sylf acendest, to þon þæt he
þa synfullan to hreowsunge gecygede, gefultuma me nu anegre ælces fylstes
bedæled.
 442. Forlæt me and me þa leafe forgif to geopenigenne þone
ingang þinre þære halgan cyrcan, þæt ic ne wurðe fremde geworden
þære deorwurþan rode gesihðe, on þære gefæstnod wæs ealles
middaneardes Hælend, þone þu femne geeacnodost eac swilce fæmne
acendest, se þe his agen blod ageat for minre alysednysse.
 446. Ac hat nu þu wuldorfæste hlæfdige, me unmedemre for
þære godcundan rode gretinge, þa duru beon untynede, and ic me þe
bebeode, and to mundbyrdnysse geceose wið þin agen bearn.
 449. And inc bam gehate þæt ic næfre ofer þis minne
lichaman ne besmite þurh þæt grimme bysmergleow þæs manfullan
geligeres.
 451. Ac sona ic halige fæmne þines suna rode geseo, ic mid
þam wiðsace þissere worulde, and hire dædum mid eallum þingum þe
on hyre synd, and syððan fare swa hwider swa þu me to mundbyrdnysse
geredst.
 454. Þus cwæðende, ic wearð þa gelæd mid þære
hætu þæs geleafan, and mid þam truwan oþhrinon, and be þære
arfæstan Godes cennestran mildheortnysse þrystlæcende, ic me of
þære ylcan stowe astyrede ðe ic þis gebæd cwæð, and me eft to
þam ingangendum gemengde.
 459. Syþþan næs nan þincg þe me utsceofe oþþe me
þæs temples dura bewerede, and ic þa ineode mid þam ingangendum.
 460. Ðe gegrap me witodlice stranglic fyrhto, and ic wæs eall
byfigende gedrefed, þa ic me eft to þære dura geðeodde þe me wæs
ær ingang belocen; swilc me eall þæt mægen þe me ær þæs
inganges duru bewerede æfter þan þone ingang þæs siðfætes
gegearwode.
 464. Swa ic wæs gefylled mid þam gastlicum gerynum innon þam
temple, and ic wæs gemedemod gebiddan þa gerynu þære deorwurðan and
þære geliffæstan rode.
 467. Ða ic þær geseah þa halgan godes gerynu, hu he symle
geare is þa hreowsigendan to underfonne.
 468. Ða wearp ic me sylfe forð on þa flor, and þa halgan
eorðan gecyste.
 469. Ða ic uteode þa becom ic eft to þære stowe of
þære ic ær þære halgan cennestran geseah, and mine cneowa gebigde
beforan þam halgan andwlitan þysum wordum biddende.
 472. Eala þu fremsumesta hlæfdig, þe me þine arfæstan
mildheortnysse æteowdest, and mine þa unwurðan bena þe fram ne
awurpe ic geseah þæt wuldor þe we synfulle mid gewyrhtum ne geseoð.
 475. Sy wuldor ælmihtigum Gode, se þe þurh þe onfehð
þæra synfulra and forworhtra hreowsunge and dædbote.
 477. Hwæt mæg ic earm forðoht mare geðencan oððe
areccan?
 478. Nu is seo tid to gefyllenne, and to gefremmane swa ic ær
cwæð, þinre ðære licwurðan mundbyrdnysse.
 479. Gerece me nu on þone wæg þe þin willa sy; beo me nu
hælo latteow æteowod and soðfæstnysse ealdor, beforan me gangende on
þone wæg þe to dædbote læt.
 482. Ða ic þus cwæð, þa gehyrde ic feorran ane stefne
clypigende.
 483. Gif þu Iordane þæt wæter oferfærst, þær þu
gefærst and gemetst gode reste.
 484. Ða ic þas stemne gehyrde, and for minum þingum ongeat
beon geclypode, Ic wepende spræc and to þære godes cennestran
anlicnysse hawigende, and eft clypigende, Eala þu hlæfdige ealles
middaneardes cwen, þurh ðe eallum menniscum cynne hælo to becom; ne
forlæt þu me.
 489. Ðus cwæðende ic þa ut eode of þæs temples
cafertune, and ofstlice for.
 490. Ða gemette ic sum man, and me þry penegas sealde, mid
þam ic me þry hlafas gebohte.
 491. Ða ic me hæfde genoh gehyððo to mines siðfætes
geblædfæstnysse.
 492. Ða axode ic þone þe ic þa hlafas æt bohte, hwilc se
wæg wære þe to Iordane þære ea rihtlicost gelædde.
 494. Ða þa ic þone weg ongæt ic wepende be þam
siðfæte arn symle þa axunga þære æscan towriðende; and gemang
þam ðæs dæges siðfæt wepende gefylde.
 496. Witodlice þæs dæges wæs underntid þa ða ic
gegyrnode þa halgan deorwurðan rode geseon, and sunne heo þa to setle
ahylde, and þære æfenrepsunge genealæhte.
 499. Ða ic becom to sanctes Iohannes cyrcan þæs fulwihteres
wið Iordanen gesette, and ic me þyder inn eode, and me þær gebæd.
 501. And sona in Iordane þa ea astah, and of þam halgan
wætere mine handa and ansynu þwoh, and me þær gemænsumode þam
liffestan and þam unbesmitenum gerynum ures drihtnes Hælendes Cristes on
þære ylcan cyrcan, þæs halgan forryneles and fulluhteres Iohannes.
 505. And þær geæt healfne dæl þæs hlafes, and
þæs wæteres ondranc, and me þær on niht gereste, and on
ærnemorgen ofer þa ea for.
 507. Þa ongan ic eft biddan mine lættewestran SANCTA MARIAN,
þæt heo me gerihte þyder hire willa wære.
 509. Ðus ic becom on þis westen, and þanone oð ðisne
andweardan dæg ic feorrode symle fleonde minne God anbidigende, and
gehihtende, se þe hale gedeð ealle fram þissere worulde brogan þa ðe
to him gecyrrað.
 512. Zosimus hire to cwæð, eala min hlæfdige nu mænige
gear synt nu þæt þu on þysum westene eardodost?
 514. Þæt wif him andswarode, Hit is for seofon and feowertigum
wintrum is þæs þe me þincð, þæt ic of þære halgan byrig ut
for.
 516. Zosimus hire to cwæð, and hwæt mihtest þu þe to
æte findan, oþþe be hwilcum þingum feddest þu ðe oþþis?
 518. Heo him andswarode, Twægen healfa hlafas ic brohte hider
mid me, þa ic Iordanem oferfor; naht micclan fæce þa adruwodon hi swa
swa stan and aheardodon; and þæra ic breac notigende to sumere hwile.
 521. Zosimus hire to cwæð, And mihtst þu swa manegra tida
lencgu oferfaran, þæt þu ne freode þone bryne þære flæsclican
gehwyrfednysse.
 523. Heo þa gedrefedu him andswarode, Nu þu me axast þa
ðincg þe ic swiðe þearle sylf beforhtige gif me nu to gemynde becumað
ealle þa frecednysse þe ic ahrefnode, and þæra unwislicra geþanca
þe me oft gedrefedon, þæt ic eft fram þam ylcan geþohtum sum geswinc
þrowige.
 528. Zosimus cwæð, Eala hlæfdige ne forlæt þu nan
þincg þæt þu me ne gecyðe, ac geswutela ealle þa þincg be
endebyrdnysse.
 530. Ða cwæð heo, Abbud gelyf me, seofontyne wintre ic wan
on þam gewilnunga þære manðwæra fullra, and ungesceadwisra
wildeora lustum.
 532. Þonne me hingrigan ongan, þonne wæron me þa
flæscmettas on gewilnungum.
 533. Ic gyrnde þara fixa þe on Egyptum wæron.
 534. Ic gewilnode þæs wines on þam ic ær gelustfullode to
oferdruncennysse brucan, and nu hit is me eac swilce swyðe on gewilnunga,
forþon þe ic his ær ofer gemet breac, þa ic on worulde wæs.
 537. Eac ic her wæs swiðe geþrest for þyses westenes
wæterwædlnysse uneaðe þa frecendlican nydþearfnysse adreogende.
 539. Me wæs swilce swiðlic lust þæra sceandlicra
sceopleoða me gedrefdon, þonne hi me on mode gebrohton þa deoflican
leoþ to singanne þe ic ær on worulde geleornode.
 541. Ac ic þonne mid þam wepende mine breost mid minum handum
cnyssende, and me sylfe myngode mines foregehates, and þære mundbyrdnysse
þe ic ær fore geceas.
 544. And swa geond þis weste hreafigende þurh min geðoht
becom toforan þære godan and þære halgan Godes cennestran anlicnysse,
þe me ær on hyre truwan underfeng.
 546. And ic beforan hyre wepende bæd, þæt heo me fram
aflymde þa fulan geðances, þe mine earman sawla swencton.
 548. Ðonne ic soðlice oferflowendlice sorgigende weop, and ic
heardlice mine breost cnyssende, þonne geseah ic leoht gehwanon me ymbutan
scinende, and me þonne sona sum staþolfæstlic smyltnyss to becom.
 551. Ara me nu abbud; hu mæg ic ðe gecyðan mine geþances,
ða ic me ondræde eft genydan to þam geligre þæt swyðlice fyr
minne ungesæligan lichaman innan ne forbernde.
 554. And me eallunga þræscende to þære hæmetes geseah,
þonne þyllice geþohtas agonnon on astigan, þonne astrehte ic me sylfe
on eorðan, and þa wangas mid tearum ofergeat.
 556. Forðon þe ic to soðan gehihte me ætstandan, þa ðe
ic me sylfe ær of þære eorðan, ær me seo swete stemn gewunelice
oferlihte, and me ða gedrefedan geðohtas fram aflymde.
 559. Symle ic witodlice minre heortan eagan to þære minre
borhhanda on nydþearfnysse up ahof, and hi biddende þæt heo me
gefultumode on þysum westene to rihtre dædbote, þa þe þone ealdor
æghwilcre clænnysse acende.
 562. And þus ic seofontyne geare rynum on mænigfealdum
frecednyssum swa swa ic ær cwæð, winnende wæs on eallum þingum
oþ þisne andweardan dæg, and me on fultume wæs and mine wisan
reccende seo halige Godes cennestre.
 566. Zosimus hire to cwæð, and ne beþorftest þu nanre
andlyfene oððe hræglunge.
 567. Heo him andswarode and cwæð, seofontyne gear swa ic þe
ær sæde, ic notode þære hlafa, and syððan be þam wyrtum
leofode þe ic on þysum westene funde.
 570. Se gegyrla witodlice þe ic hæfde sona swa ic Iordanen
oferfor, mid swiðlicre ealdunge totorene forwurdon, and ic syþþan
mænigfeald earfeðu dreah, hwilum þære isihtan cealdnysse þæs
wintres, hwilum þæs unmætan wylmes þære sunnan hæto.
 573. Ic wæs grimlice beswæled for þam micclan byrne, and
eft for þære micclan forstigan cealdnysse þæs wintres, swa þæt
ic for oft ofdune on þa eorðan, and forneah eallunga unastyrigendlic butan
gaste læg.
 577. Þus ic wæs lange on mænigfealdum, and mislicum
nydþearfnyssum, and on unmætum costnungum winnende and wraxligende.
 578. And me ða siþþan oþ þeosne andweardan dæg, and
mine earman sawle and minne lichaman þæt godcundlice mægen geheold, mid
me sylfre symle smeagende of hu micclum yfelum heo me alysde.
 581. Soðlice ic eom afeded of þam genihtsumestan wistmettum
minre fylle.
 583. Þæt is mid þam hihte minre hæle, and ic eom
oferwrigen mid þam oferbrædelse Godes wordes, se ðe ealle þincg
befehð and befædmað.
 585. Ne leofað ne se man soðlice be hlafe anum, ac of
æghwilcum worde þe forðgæð of Godes muþe.
 586. Zosimus þa witodlice gehyrende þæt heo þæra
haligra boca cwydas forðbrohte, ægðer ge of þam godspelle and of
manegum oþrum.
 588. And he hire to cwæð, Eala modor leornodest þu æfre
sealmas oþþe oþre halige gewritu?
 590. Ða heo þis gehyrde þa smearcode heo wið his weardes
þus cweðende, Gelyf me ne geseah ic nænne man buton þe oððe
wildeor oþþe æniges cynnes nyten, siððan ic Iordanen þæt
wæter oferferde, and ic hyder on þis westen becom.
 593. Ne ic stæfcyste witodlice ne leornode ne þæra nanum ne
hlyste þe þa smeadon and ræddon.
 595. Ac Godes word is cucu and scearp innan lærende þis
mennisce andgyt, and þis is se ende nu þæra þinga þe be me gefremede
synd.
 597. Nu ic þe halsigende, andbidde þurh þæt geflæscode
Godes word, þæt þu for me earmlicre forlegenre gebidde.
 599. Ða heo þis cwæð, ða arn se ealde wið hire weardes
mid gebigedum cneowum to þon þæt he hine on þa eorþan astrehte, and
mid wopegum tearum hlude clypigende, gebletsod sy God, se þe þa
mænigfealdan wundru ana wyrceað.
 602. And sy þu gebletsod Drihten God, þe me æteowdest þa
wuldorfæstlicnysse þe þu ondrædendum gyfest.
 604. Nu ic to soðan wat þæt þu nænne þæra ne
forlætest þe ðe gesecað.
 605. Heo þa soðlice þone ealdan forene forfeng, and him ne
geþafode fulfremodlice on þa eorðan astreccan, ac cwæð to him, þas
þincg þu gehyrdest mann.
 607. Eac ic þe la halsige þurh þone Drihten Hælendne Crist
urne alysend, þæt þu nanum menn ne asecge ærþan þe me God of
flæsces bendum alyse.
 610. Ac þas þincg ealle þus oncnawenne, far ham mid sibbe.
 610. And ic þe eft binnan geares fyrste on þyssere ylcan tide
æteowe, and þu me gesihst.
 612. And do þu huru soðlice, swa ic þe nu bebeode, þi
halgan lenctenfæstene þæs toweardan geares efthwyrfende, ne oferfar
þu na Iordanen swa swa gewuna synt of eowrum mynstrum to farenne.
 615. Ða ongan eft Zosimus wundrian, þæt heo swa gewislice
þæs mynstres regol cuðe, and he elles nan þincg ne cwæð, þæt
he God wuldrode se þe mænigfealdlicor gifað mannum þonne he seo
gebeden þam þe hine lufiað.
 618. Heo þa eft cwæð, Onbid nu Zosimus swa swa ic ær
cwæð, on þinum mynstre forðon witodlice þeah þu ær wille faran
ahwyder þu ne miht.
 620. Þonne to þon halgan æfenne þæs halgan gereordes,
þæt is to þam halgan þurresdæge ær þam drihtenlican
easterdæge/ genim sumne dæl on gehalgodum fæte þæs godcundan
lichaman, and þæs gelyffæstan blodes, and hafa mid ðe, and geanbida
min on þa healfe Iordanen þe to worulde belimpeð oþþe ic þe to
cume.
 625. Ða lyffestan gerynu to onfonne soðlice siþþan ic on
þære cyrcan þæs eadigan foreryneles þæs drihtlican lichaman, and
his blodes me gemænsumode ær ic Iordanen oferfore, næfre syððan
ic þæs haligdomes ne breac oððe þigde.
 629. And forþon ic bidde þæt þu mine bene ne forseoh, ac
þæt þu huru me bringe þa godcundan and þa liffæstan gerynu to
þære tide þe se hælend his ðægnas ðæs godcundlican
gereordes dælnimende dyde.
 632. Cyð þu eac Iohanne þæs mynstres abbude þe þu on
bist, þæt he hine sylfne georne besmeage and eac his heorde forþon
þær synd sume wisan to gerihtenne and to gebetenne.
 635. Ac ic nelle þæt þu him æt þysum cyrre þas
þincg cyðe, ærþam þe God bebeode þus cwæðende.
 636. Heo eac fram þam ealdan gebedes bæd, and to þam inran
westene hrædlice efste.
 638. Zosimus þa hine soðlice forð astrehte on þa floras
cyssende on þæt hire fet stodon God wuldrigende and miccle þancas donde;
and eftcyrrende wæs herigende and blætsigende urne Drihtne Hælendne
Crist.
 641. And he wæs eftcyrrende þurh þone ylcan siðfat
þæs westenes þe he ær þyder becom, and to þam mynstre ferde on
þære ylcan tide, þe heora eastergewuna wæron togædere becuman.
 644. And eall þæt gear geornlice þa gesihðe forsweogode
læstra þinga geðrystlæcende aht secgan þæs ðe he geseah, ac
symle mid him sylfum geornlice God bæd þæt he him eft æteowde þone
gewilnodan andwlitan.
 647. And he on mænigfealdum sworettungum þa lætnysse
ðæs geares rynes geanbidode.
 648. Ða þa seo halige tid lenctenfæstenes becom on þone
drihtenlican dæg, þe we nemniað halgan dæg, þa gebroþru æfter
þam gewunelican gebedum and sealmsangum ut foron, and he sylf on þam
mynstre to lafe wearð, and þær gewunode for sumre lichamlicre
mettrumnysse gehæft.
 652. And he eac swiðe georne gemunde Zosimus þære halgan
gebod, þa heo him sæde þeah he ut faran wolde of his mynstre þæt he
ne mihte.
 654. Swaþeahhwæðre æfter naht manegum dagum he hine
þære seocnysse gewyrpte, and on þam mynstre drohtnode.
 656. Soðlice þa þa munecas ham cyrdon, and on þam halgan
æfen þæs gereordes hi togædere gesamnodon, þa dyde he swa him
ær beboden wæs, and on ænne lytelne calic sende sumne dæl þæs
unbesmitenan lichaman, and þæs deorwurðan blodes ures Drihtnes
Hælendes Cristes.
 660. And him on hand genam ænne lytelne tænel mid caricum
gefylledne, and mid palmtreowa wæstmum þe we hatað fingeræppla, and
feawa lenticula mid wætere ofgotene.
 663. And on hrepsunge becom to Iordanes ofrum þæs wæteres,
and þær sorgigende gebad þone tocyme þæs halgan wifes þa heo þa
þyder becom.
 665. Zosimus nænige þinga hnappode, and geornlice þæt
westen beheold, and mid him sylfum smeagende þohte, þus cweðende, Eala
hwæðer heo hider cumende syð, and me ne gyme, and me eftcyrrende
hwearf.
 668. Þus cwæðende and biterlice weop, and his eagen up to
þam heofone hæbbende, and eadmodlice God wæs biddende, þus
cwæðende, ne fremda þu Drihten þære gesihðe þe þu me ærest
æteowdest, þæt ic huru idel heonone ne hwyrfe, mine synna onþreagunge
berende.
 672. Ðus he mid tearum biddende, him eft oþer geþanc on
befeoll þus cweðende, and hu nu gif heo cymð?
 674. Hu sceall heo þas ea oferfaran nu her nan scip nys þæt
heo to me unwurðan becuman mæge?
 676. Eala me ungesæligan swa rihtwislicre gesihðe afremdad
me.
 676. Ða he þis þohte, þa geseah he hwær heo stod on
oþre healfe þæs wæteres.
 678. Zosimus soðlice hi geseonde mid micclum wynsumigendum
gefean, and God wuldrigende up aras swaþeahhwæðere on his mode
tweonigende, hu heo mihte Iordanes wæteru oferfaran.
 681. Þa geseah he witodlice þæt heo mid Cristes rodetacne
Iordanes wæteru bletsode, soðlice ealra þæra nihte þeostru þa
ðæs monan byrhtnysse onlihte sona swa heo þære rodetacn on þa
wætru drencte.
 684. Swa eode heo on uppan þa hnescan yða wið his weardes
gangende swa swa on drigum.
 685. Zosimus wundrigende, and teoligende his cneowu to bigenne hire
ongeanweardes, heo ongan of þam wættrum clypigan and forbeodan, and þus
cwæð, Hwæt dest þu abbud?
 688. Wite þæt þu eart Godes sacerd, and þa godcundan
geryne þe mid hæbbende?
 689. He þa sona hire hyrsumigende up aras.
 690. Sona swa heo of þam wæterum becom þa cwæð heo to
him, fæder, bletsa me.
 691. Witodlice him an gefor swiðlic wafung on swa
wuldorfæstan wuldre, and þa þus cwæð, Eala þu soðfæsta, god
is se þe gehet him sylfum gelice beon þa þe hi sylfe ær
clænsiað.
 694. Wuldor sy þe, Drihten God, þu þe me þurh þas þine
þeowene æteowdest hu micel ic on minre agenre gesceawunge on þam gemete
þæra oþra fulfremodnysse þus cwæðende.
 696. Ða bæd heo, Maria, þæt heo ongunne þæt riht
geleaffulnysse gebæd, þæt is credo in deum, and þær æfter
þæt drihtenlice gebæd, pater noster.
 698. Þyssum gefylledum þa brohte heo þam ealdan sibbe coss,
swa swa hit þeaw is, and þær onfeng þam halgum gerynum, Cristes
lichaman and blodes, mid abrædedum handum.
 701. And in þa heofon locigende and mid tearum geomrigende, and
þus cwæð, forlæt nu drihten þine þeowene æfter þinum worde
in sibbe faran, forþon þe mine eagan gesawon þine hælo.
 704. And eft to þam ealdan cwæð, miltsa me abbud, and gefyl
nu oþer gebæd minre bene.
 705. Gang nu to þinum mynstre mid Godes sibbe gereht, and cum nu
ymb geares rynu to þam burnan, þe wytt unc ærest gespræcon.
 707. Ic þe bidde for Gode þæt þu þis ne forhæbbe, ac
þæt þu cume, and þu me þonne gesihst swa swa God wile.
 709. Þa cwæð he to hire, Eala wære me gelyfed þæt ic
moste þinum swaðum fyligan, and þines deorwurðan andwlitan gesihðe
brucan.
 711. Ac ic bidde þe modor, þæt þu me ealdan anre lytelre
bene getyðige, þæt þu lytles hwæthwegu gemedemige underfon me
þæs ðe ic hider brohte, and þus cwæð, do hider þone tænel
þe ic me mid brohte.
 714. Heo þa sona mid hire ytemestan fingrum þære lenticula
þæt syndon pysan heo onhran and on hire muð sende þreora corna
gewyrde, and þus cwæð, þæt þæs gyfe genihtsumode, þe
þære sawle staðol unwemme geheold, and heo cwæð to þam ealdan,
gebide for me, and for mine ungesælignysse gemunde.
 719. He sona hire fet mid tearum oþran, biddende þæt heo on
þa halgan Godes gesamnunga gebæde.
 720. And hine þa alet wepende and heofende, and he ne
geðrystlæhte æniga ðinga heo to lettenne.
 722. Heo æniga þinga gelet beon ne mihte, heo þa eft mid
ðære halgan rode gedryncnysse Iordanem oþhrinan ongan, and ofer þa
hnescan yða þæs wæteres eode swa swa heo ær dyde þyderweardes.
 724. Zosimus þa soðlice wearð micclan gefean cyrrende and
færlice wearð mid micclan ege gefylled swiðlice hine sylfne hreowsigende
þreade þæt he þære halgan naman ne axode.
 727. Þeahhwæðere hopode þæt he þy æfterfyligendan
geare þæt gewiste.
 728. Þa æfter oferfarenum þæs geares ryne becom on
þæt widgille westen, and geornlice efste to þære wuldorlican
gesihðe, and þær lange hyderes and þyderes secende for, oþ þæt
he sum swutol tacn þære gewilneden gesihðe, and wilnunge þære stowe
undergeat, and he geornlice mid his eagena scearpnyssum hawigende ge on þa
swiðran healfe ge on þa wynstran, swa swa se gleawesta hunta gif he
þær mihte þæs sweteste wildeor gegripan.
 735. Ða he þa styrigendlices nan þincg findan ne mihte, þa
ongan he hine sylfne mid tearum ofergeotan, and mid upahafenum eagum gebæd
and cwæð, Geswutela me Drihten, þæt gehydde goldhord, þe þu me
sylfum ær gemedemodest æteowan, ic bidde þe Drihten for þinum
wuldre.
 739. Ða he þus gebeden hæfde þa becom he to þære
stowe þær se burna getacnod wæs þær hi ærest spræcon, and
þær standende on oþre healfe geseah swa swa scinende sunne, and þæs
halgan wifes lichaman, orsawle licgende, and þa handa swa heo gedafenodon
alegdon beon and eastweardes gewende.
 744. Ða sona þyder arn, and hire fet mid his tearum þwoh; ne
geþrystlæhte he soðlice nan oþer þæs lichaman oðhrinan.
 745. And þa mid micclum wope þære byrgenne gebæd
geworhte, mid sealmsange and mid oþrum gebedum þe to þære wisan
belumpon.
 747. Þa ongan he þencan hwæðer hit hire licode.
 748. Þa he þis ðohte, þa wæs þær an gewrit on
þære eorðan getacnod þus gecweden, bebyrig abbud Zosimus, and miltsa
Maria lichama; ofgif þære eorðan þæt hire is, and þæt dust to
þam duste.
 751. Geic eac gebiddan þeahhwæðere for me of þyssere
worulde hleorende on þam monðe þe aprilis, þære nigeþan nihte,
þæt is <foreign>idus APRELIS</foreign>, on þam drihtenlican gereorddæge, and æfter
þam huslgange.
 754. Þa se ealda þa stafas rædde þa sohte he ærest hwa
hi write forþan þe heo sylf ær sæde þæt heo næfre naht
swilces ne leornode, swaþeah he on þam swiðe wynsumigende geseah
þæt he hire naman wiste, and he swutole ongeat sona swa heo þa
godcundan gerynu æt Iordane onfeng þære ylcan tide þyder becom and
sona of middanearde gewat.
 759. And se siðfæt þe Zosimus on xx dagum mid micclum
geswince oferfor, þæt eall MARIA on anre tide ryne gefylde, and sona to
Drihtne hleorde.
 761. Zosimus þa soðlice God wuldrode, and his agene lichaman
mid tearum ofergeat and cwæð, Nu is seo tid, earmincg Zosimus, þæt
þu gefremme þæt þe beboden is.
 764. Ac hwæt ic nu ungesælige forþon ic nat mid hwi ic
delfe nu me swa wana is ægþer ge spadu ge mattuc.
 765. Þa he þus on his heortan digollice spræc, þa geseah
he þær swilc hwugu treow licgende and þæt lytel.
 767. Ongan þa þær mid delfan, witodlice swiðe georne, and
seo/ eorðe wæs swiðe heard and ne mihte heo adelfan forþon he wæs
swiðe gewæced ægðer ge mid fæstene ge on þam langan geswince,
and he mid sworettungum wæs genyrwed, and mid swate and hefiglice of
þære heortan deopnysse geomrode.
 772. Þa he hine beseah þa geseah he unmættre micelnysse leon
wið þære halgan lichaman standan, and hit his fotlastes liccode.
 773. Þa wearð he gefyrht mid ege þæs unmætan wildeores,
and ealre swiðost forþon þe þæt halige wif him ær to cwæð,
þæt heo þær nænig wildeor ne gesawe.
 776. Ac he hine sona æghwanon mid þære rodetacne
gewæpnode.
 777. And mid mægene þære licgendan.
 777. Þa ongan seo leo fægnian wið þæs ealdan weard, and
hine mid his leoðum styrgendum grette.
 779. Zosimus þa soðlice to þam leon cwæð, Eala þu
mæste wildeor, gif þu fram Gode hider asend wære, to þon þæt
þu þissere halgan Godes þeowene lichaman on eorþan befæste, gefyll
nu þæt weorc þinre þenunge.
 782. Ic witodlice for yldum gewæht eom, þæt ic delfan ne
mæg, ne naht gehyðes hæbbe þis weorc to begangenne, ne ic efstan
ne/ mæg swa myccles siðfateshider/ to bringanne.
 785. Ac þu nu mid þære godcundan hæse þis
weorc/ mid þinum clifrum do, oþ þæt wit þisne halgan lichaman on
eorðan befæston.
 787. Sona æfter his wordum seo leo mid hire clifrum earmum
scræf geworhte, swa micel swa genihtsumode þære halgan to byrgenne.
 789. And he mid his tearum hire fet ðwoh, and mid forðagotenum
benum/ mænigfealdlice bæd þæt heo for eallum þingode; and swa
þone lichaman on eorðan oferwreah, swa nacode swa he hi ærest gemette
buton gewealdan þæs toslitenan rægeles, þe he Zosimus hire ær
towearp, of þam Maria sumne hire lichaman bewæfde.
 793. And heo þa ætgædere cyrdon, seo leo in þæt inre
westen gewat, swa swa þæt mildeste lamb.
 795. Ða gewat Zosimus to his mynstre, God wuldrigende and
bletsigende, and mid lofum herigende.
 796. Sona swa he to þam mynstre becom, þa rehte he heom eallum
of/ fyrmðe þa wisan, and naht ne bediglode ealra þæra þinga þe he
geseah oððe gehyrde, þæt hi ealle godes mærða wurðodon and mid
ege/ and lufan and micclan geleafan mærsodon, þære eadigan
forðfore dæg.
 801. Iohannes soðlice ongeat sume þa mynsterwisan to gerihtanne
swa swa seo halige ær foresæde, ac he þa sona Gode fultumigendum
gerihte/; and Zosimus on þam mynstre wæs drohtnigende an hund wintra, and
þa to Drihtne hleorde.
 804. Wuldor sy urum Drihtne Hælendum Criste, þe leofað and
rixað a on worulda woruld.
 806. AMEN.

LS 24 (MichaelTristr)
B3.3.24.
Saint Michael: Tristram 1970, 152-61.



 1. Men ða leofestan, us is to worðianne and to mærsianne seo
gemind þæs halgan heahengles, Sancte michaeles, se wæs wundorlic
ærendraca ðæs ælmihtigan dryhtenes.
 4. Eac swilce nu todæge þam getriwum folce he wæs inlihted
and gebirhted.
 6. For ðon ðonne men ða leofestan, blission we and gefeon in
þisne simbelnisse dæg þæs halgan heahengles Sancte michaeles se is on
hefenum gecweden swa swa god sylfa age.
 10. Gehyron we for þon sinderlice drihtnes he is efenrixiende, he
is swiðe mihtig þam heahenglum þa standað dæges and nihtes beforan
þrymsetle dryhtnes, se is eallra haligra fultum.
 13. And he is reccend eallra haligra saula and he is nergende godes
folces and he is strong on gefeohte wið ðane miclan drocan.
 16. Swa hit sagað her on pocalipsis þære bec.
 18. Blission we on heofonas and on ða þe on heofnum sint for
ðon ðe Sanctus michael he is strong feohtend wið þone miclan dracan,
þæt is ðonne wið ðam awyrgedum gæstum.
 21. On þisne heahengel we sculon gelyfan and biddan us on fultum
on ægehwilcere frecennesse þam cristenum folce.
 25. Ðis is se halga heahengel, Sanctus michael se wæs andfengo
abeles saule þæs ærestan martires ðone his broðor cain for
æfstum ofsloh.
 29. Ðis is se halga heahengel, Sanctus michael se is hæleda
healdend and dryhtne fultummendum.
 31. Hira feorh he generede þæt wæs þonne noe and his suna
þry and hira feower wif in þam micelan flode.
 34. Ðis is se halga heahengel, Sancte michael þæs gemynd we
nu todæge se wæs abrahames anlysend þæs heahfæderes ofer caldea
þeode cumende fultumendum.
 37. And he wæs latteow þam ðrym heahfæderum abrahame and
isace and iacobe þurh ða ælðydigan land and ða uncuðan wegas he
wæs him simle onweard fultum on æghwilcere frecydnesse.
 42. Þis is se halga heahengel, Sancte michael se wæs ferende
on eastron þurh israela hus and egypta frumbearn he ofsloh and israela bearn
he gefryðode.
 46. Þis is se halga heahengel, Sancte michael se ðe drihtne
fultummendum þæt cristene folc mid his gescyldnisse in þam westene
feowerti wintra he hit ferede and fedde.
 50. Ðis is se halga heahengel, Sancte michael se gesigefæsted
stod beforan canonica cinne and þurh iobes handa þæt israelica folc he
gelædde to þam gehatlande þæt is flowende hunie and meolce.
 55. Þis is se halga heahengel, Sancte michael and se æþela
forestihtend in þæra cræftena handa þe salamones templ timbredon.
 58. Þis is se halga heahengel, Sancte michael se wæs strong
scyldend þam þrym cnihtum þa wæron sende in ofen birnendes fires.
 60. And he þa him bistod se engel and snitera gast, he dihtode in
hira muð þæt wæs þonne se halga, <foreign>Benedicete</foreign>.
 64. Þis is se halga heahengel, Sancte michael and se æþela
scyldend wið deofles swipornesse swa se witega sægde þæt þæt
deofol þohte þæt he scolde gelæran þæt folc þæt hi
worðodon moyses lichaman for god for his fægernesse.
 68. Ða cwæð him to se halga engel, ic ðe beode mid mines
drihtnes worde þæt ðu þæge þristnesse ne gedo þæt ðu his
folc ne gescildige.
 72. Þis is se halga heahengel, Sancte michael se ðe a onweard
fultum þurhwunode and drihtnes witigan mid him in æghwilcere stowe.
 76. Þis is se halga heahengel, Sancte michael þam dryhten
befæste Sancta marian saule æfter hire forðfore and he hi him bebead.
 79. Þis is se halga heahengel, Sancte michael se ðe onra
gewilces soðfæstes mannes saule gelædeð þurh þa gatu þæs
ecan lifes to hefena rice.
 83. Þis is se halga heahengel, Sancte michael se ðe anra
gehwilces haliges mannes bene gelæteð in dryhtnes gesyðe and he his
hiredes gewyrht mid frofre he him eft to forlæteð.
 88. Þis is se halga heahengel, Sanctus Michael and se snotora
dihtend ðære cynelecra husa and his is se getreowa hierde ðære halgan
heofonlicon ceastre.
 92. Þis is se halga heahengel, Sanctus michael and se gleawamod
bigena ðæs cynelican wingerdes se ðe ðisne getreowne gedeð and þa
berian he gesamnað.
 95. And ða winestran he ut awirpð and ðane wæstm þæs
godan wingerdes he agifeð his hlaforde hwæt sindon þa beorgas ðe he
þær samnað þæt sindon haligra manna and soðfæstra saule.
 100. Þis is se halga heahengel, Sanctus michael se goda hirde
ðæs dryhtenlican eowdes se ðe ne læteð wulf ne ðeof nane wuht
gewirdan on his hlafordes heorde.
 104. Þis is se halga heahengel, Sanctus michael and se
gesundfulla sawend cristes æcera and se wæstmberenda riftere ðæra
hwitra ðeodlanda se his hlafordes bernas gefelleð mid þy clænestan
hwæte and ða egelan and ða fulnesse ut aworpeð nymðe ðæt sindon
ða soðfæstan ðe he ascadæt fram ðam sinfullum saulum.
 111. Þis is se halga heahengel, Sanctus michael and se getreowa
þeow þane dryhten gesette ofer ealne hiwscipe þæt he him mete sealde
on ða rihtan tid.
 114. Hwæt is se mete nymðe ðæt he sceal on domesdæge
anra gehwelcum men his dæda edlean forgildan?
 117. Þis is se halga heahengel, Sanctus michael and þæt
beorhte tungel þæt bið ascinende dæges and nihtes on hefonum betwexh
ðam/ gæstelicum tunglum beforan ðam godcundan cyninge.
 121. Þis is se halga heahengel, Sanctus michael and se æðela
nowend and se gleawa frumlida and se þancwirðesta stigend se ðe his scip
gefelleð and mid heofonlicum wælum hit gefylleð þæt is ðonne mid
þam halgum saulum.
 126. And mid ðy wrygelse ðære godcundan gefillnesse ofer
þæs sæs yðe he hit gelædeð þæt is ðanne ofer ðisses
middangeardes frecennesse and þa halegan saula gelædeð to þære
yðe ðæs heofoncundan lifes.
 131. Þis is se halga heahengel, Sanctus michael se ðe com on
fultum þam crystenon.
 132. Swa hit sægð in actum apostolorum þæt on sumere
ceastre ðære nama wæs træleg and æghwelce geare hæðen here
ayddon ða ceasterware.
 135. Ða gecwædon ða ceasterware him betweonum ðreora daga
fæsten.
 137. And þa þæt fæsten geendod wæs ða com him to
Sanctus michael and he wæs to gefeohte gearu.
 139. Ða stod he ofer ðæs ceasteres burugate and hæfde him
ligen sweord on handa and he aflimde ða elðeodigan sona þæt hi flugon
on oðer ðeodland and hi næfre ma ðær oðeowdon.
 143. Þis is se halga heahengel, Sanctus michael and se mycila
mundbora se nu todæg his stowe ætywde on eorðan þæt men sceolden
hi ðære dæghwamlice dryhten weorðian.
 147. Þis is se halga heahengel, Sanctus Michael se ðe ær
þisse worulde ende ofslihð þone ealdan feond þæt is se micla draca
se ðe æt frymðe middangardes gesceapen wæs to ðam beorhtestan
engle.
 151. Ac he selfa hit forworhte mid ði he cwæð, ic hebbe min
heahsetl to norðdæle and ic beo gelic þam heahstan cyninge.
 154. And þa gefeol he and gehreas mid his werode on niwulnesse
grund efene se illca antacrist se ær ðisse worlde ende cymeð on ðisne
middangeard to ðam þæt sceal gesamnian ða ðe his sindon.
 158. Þanne cymeð Sanctus michael and hine ofslihð for ðon
ðe he hit æfre geðohte þæt he scolde gelic beon ðan heahstan
cyninge.
 161. Þis is se halga heahengel, Sanctus mihael se ðe on þam
neahstan dæge worulde ende and æt þam egesfullan dome he ðonne ða
deadan aweceð mid dryhtenes hæse beoruhtere stefene.
 165. He clipað and þus cwið, <foreign>Surgite Surgite</foreign>, arisað
arisað.
 166. And þonne arisað ealle ða deadan ðe eorðe forswealg
oððe sæ bescencte oððe fir forbærnde oððe wildeor abiton
oððe fuglas on lande tobæren oððe wirmas on eorðan fræten.
 171. Þis is se halga heahengel, Sanctus mihael se ðe ða godan
to life gelaðað and gelædeð and þa yfelan on deað bescenceð.
 173. And þonne ða halgan saula to heofona rice he gelædeð
and þa geomriendan he blisað and þa wanhalan he gelacnað and þa
elðeodegan he afrefreð and þam winnendum he ræste forgifð
lærnerum gefean he ontyneð and þam lærrendum ongit he gerue
læteð.
 180. Uton þonne nu men ða leofestan biddan we þone halgan
heahengel, Sanctus mihael þæt ura saula sie anfenge and hi gelæde on
heofoncund rice to þam dryhtene ðe lifað and rixað mid fæder and mid
suna and mid þam halgan gaste in ealra worlda world a butan ende, amen.

END_TEXT

LS 25 (MichaelMor)
B3.3.25.
Saint Michael: Morris 1874-80, 197-211.



 1. TO SANCTAE MICHAHELES MÆSSAN.
 1. MEN ða leofestan, manaþ us & myngaþ seo ar æ seo
eadignes þæs hean & þæs halgan heahengles tid, þæt we
hwæt hwugu be þære his eadgan gemynde se þe is on ealra ymbhwyrfte to
weorþienne & to wuldrienne his ciricean, gehweþer ge his agen geweorc
ge on his naman gehalgod.
 5. & þus ærest mannum æteawde & gecyþde.
 6. Heo þonne nalles on goldes wlite & on seolfres ne
scineþ, ac on sundorweorþunge þurh godcundra mægen heo gewuldrad
stondeþ.
 8. Heo is eac on onsyne utan yfeles heowes, ac heo is innan mid ece
mægene geweorþod.
 10. Swa hit eaþe beon mæg þæt se halga heahengel of
heofenum cumen wære, & wære gemyndig manna tyddernesse, þæt he
hine geeaðmedde þæt he hie mid his sylfes handum gesette & geworhte,
to þæm þæt he wolde þæt þær mihten deaþlice men gyrnan
þara uplicra burhwara & þæs ecean geferscipes.
 15. Þonne is seo halige cirice Michaeles geseted on þæm hean
cnolle sumes muntes, on scræfes onlicnesse wæs æteowed; þonne is seo
cirice on Campania þæs landes gemæro.
 18. Ðonne is þær on neaweste sum swiþe mære burh betwih
þære sæ seo is nemned Adriaticus on þæm munte Garganus geseted, se
is haten Sepontus.
 20. Þonne syndon from þære burge weallum twelf mila ametene
up to þæm hean cnolle, þe ic ær big sægde, þæs hean engles
ciricean; & heo mid gefean & mid blisse growende standeþ.
 23. Ðas circean heo þonne þus æteowde & gecyþde
æt fruman seo ilce boc seo on þære ciricean funden wæs &
gemeted.
 25. Segeþ þæron þæt sum rice man & for worlde
æhtspedig wære on þære burh þæs nama wæs Garganus.
 26. Se welega man þæm munte gesette þone ilcan naman swa swa
he hatte.
 27. Se man ahte mycelne welan; mid þy þe þas welegan mannes
ungeendod weorod & unarimed mengeo on hryþrum & on manigfealdum
ceapum geweox & gewridode, toþon þæt he wæs geond þæs muntes
feld mid þy feo oferbræded & beþeaht.
 31. Þa gelamp þæt sum fearhryþer þæs oþræs
ceapes geferscipe oferhogode, & him gewunode þæt he wæs geond
þæt westen sundorgenga, & þa æt nehstan eft hwyrfende wæs
toþæm yrfe & to þæm ceape & to heora gesetum.
 35. He þa se fear þæs hyrdes drafe forhogode & him on
þæt westen gewunode to sumes scræfes dura.
 37. Ða þæt se hlaford geahsode þæt þæt hryþer
swa on wlencu geond þæt westen ferde, þa forbealh he hine forþon þe
þæt hryþer him þuhte onwedenheorte þe þær swa ferde geond
þone widgillan munt.
 40. Þa gesamnode he mycel weorod his manna & hwearf æfter
wegum ge buton geond þone wudu, & sohton þæt forwlencte
hryþær.
 42. Ða gemette he hit æt nehsstan on þæs muntes cnolle,
& geseah þæt hit stod an sumes scræfes dura.
 44. Þa wæs he mid yrre swiðlice onstyred, forðon þe hit
swa wedende eode, & swa ofermodlice ferde.
 45. Þa genam he his bogan & hine gebende, & ða mid
geættredum stræle ongan sceotan wiþ þæs þe he geseah þæt
hryþer stondan.
 47. Ða sona mid þan þe se stræl on flyge wæs, þa com
swiðe mycel windes blæd foran ongean, þæt seo stræl instepe
wearð eft gecyrred, & ða þone ilcan welegan mon, þe heo ær from
sended wæs, he sceat, þæt he sona dead wæs.
 51. Ða þæt gesawon ða burgware, ða wurdon hie swiðe
forhte for ðæm fære þe heo næfre swylc wundor ne gesawon.
 53. Ond þa ne dorstan hie þære stowe genealæcan þe hie
þæt hryþer gesawon æt stondan.
 55. Ða wæs on þa ilcan tid on þære heora byrig se
wæs haten Sepontus halig biscep.
 56. Þa gesohtan hie hine & him þæt wundor sægdon,
& hie hine lare beahsodan, hwæt him þæs to donne wære.
 58. Þa lærde he hie & him to ræde fand þæt hie
þry dagas fæston, & to Sancte Michaele þæt hie wilnodan þæt
God gecyþde þæt mannum bemiðen wæs & bedigled.
 61. Þa hie þæt gedon hæfdon ge on fæstenne, ge on
sealmsange, ge on ælmessan, ða wæs þæm ilcan biscepe ætiewed on
niht se hea & se halga heahengel Michahel.
 63. & him þa eaðmodlice & luflice tospræc &
þus cwæð, Weoroldlice & wislice ge dyde þætte mannum bedigled
wæs on eorðan þæt ge þæt on heofenas to Gode sohtan.
 66. Wite þu eac þæt se mon se þær mid his agenum
stræle ofsceoten wæs, þa þæt wæs mid minum willan gedon; &
min nama is Michael; ic eom heahengel Heofoncyninges & ic on his gesihþe
simle stonde.
 70. Secgge ic þe nu eac þæt ic onsundrum þa stowe her on
eorðan lufige, & ofer ealle oþre ic hie geceas & eac gecyþe on
eallum ðæm tacnum þe þær gelimpeð, þæt ic eom ðære
stowe on sundran scyppend & hyrde.
 73. Þa þæt wæs þus gesprecen & gecyðed, hie þa
þa burgware swiþe bliþe & gefeonde mid þon heora halgan bisceope
þa stowe sohtan.
 75. & þa æfter heora gewunon þær þone lifgendan God
& þone halgan heahengel Michael meagollice gebædon; & Gode
þær eaðmodlice lac onsægdon.
 78. & hie þa ðær twa dura sceawodan on þære
ciricean; ðær wæs seo suðduru hwæt hwega hade mare.
 79. & þa gyt hi ne mihton ofer þæt scræf swa
swæðhlype þær hi gongan, ærðon hie gerymdon þone upgang &
geworhtan.
 81. Ac hie daga gehwylce geornlice þær ute heora gebedum æt
fulgon.
 83. On þa ilcan tid Neapolite ða heora nehgeburas þa þe
þa giet on hæðenum þeawum dwelgende wæron, & deoflum hyrdon.
 85. Hie þa þa burgware Beneuentius & Sepontanus hatton,
þa twa leode, hie þa ongunnon anwigges biddan & heora land to bismere
oferhergodan, & him ðæs nænige bote dydon, buton ofermodlice wig
& þreatunge.
 88. Hie þa lærde se heora halga bisceop, & him to ræde
fand þæt hie dydon þreora daga fæsten & manigfealde ælmessan
& halige lofsangas, & to ðæm heahengle Michaele, swa to ðæm
getreowestan mundboran, þæt hie him frofre & fultomes wilnodan,
þæt hie moston ðara feonda searo beswican & ofercuman.
 93. Þa on þa ilcan tid þa hæðnan bysmerlice &
synlice heora þa leasan godas mid mislicum deofolgeldum hie him laþodan on
fultum.
 95. Þa on ða ilcan tid wæs se eadiga engel Michahel
ætiewed þæm hera bisceope on gesihþe, & him sige toweardne
geheht, & him sægde þæt heora bena wæron æt Gode gehyrede,
& hie lærde ðæt hie æt þære þriddan tide on morgenne hie
forð trymedan ongean heora feondum.
 100. & him eac geheht, þæt he wolde him sylfa geseon heora
gebæro, & him þær on fultume beon.
 101. Hie þa swa bliþe on morgenne wæron, & gefeonde
ferdon ongean þæm heðnum.
 103. & hie wiston be þæs engles sægenum, ge be heora
sige, ge eac be þara hæþenra manna fleame & ondfylle.
 105. & þa sona on ðære frymþe þæs gefeohtes, ða
wæs Garganus se munt, se þe hie onfeohtan sceoldan, mid mycclum brogan
& mid ongryslan eall oferlæded; & unhierlic storm of ðæm munte
astag, & mid þystrogenipum þæs muntes cnoll eal oferswogen wæs.
 109. Ða flugon þa legetu swylce fyrene strælas ongean þa
hæðnan leode, toðæm þicce þæt hie nænige þinga ongean
locian ne mihton for ðæs leges bryne.
 111. Þa wæs gefylled þæt se witga foresægde; &
Drihten herede & þus cwæð: <foreign>Qui facit angelos suos spiritus et
ministros suos ignem urentem</foreign>; Hwilum se ilca God sendeþ his engla gastas to
ærendwrecum, hwilum he sendeþ þurh fyres leg.
 115. Ða flugon þa hæðnan leode, & gelice se leg hie
cwylmde, gelice þa Cristenan him mid heora wæpnum hyndon & onsetton,
oþþæt hie unsofte þo Neapulite & ofercomon ða hæþnan
leode, þa þe lifdon heora burh healfcwice, & oferfeollan þa ðe þa
frecennesse & yrmþo genæson.
 120. Þa us þa wæs gecyþed Cristenum leodum, se Godes engel
þær cwom on fultum & on frofre.
 121. & þa sona ealle eaðmodlice to þæm cyninga
Cyninge, to Criste sylfum, onhnigan.
 123. & him ealle on hand eodan þa hæðnan leode, & be
þara Cristenra lare lifdon & fulwihte onfengon.
 124. & hie ongeaton geornlice þæt þæm Cristenum
leodum com Godes engel on fultum & on frofre.
 126. & þa mid þy þe þa Cristenan leode þæt wel
sceawodan, ða gesawon hie & getealdon þæt þær wæs eac syx
hund manna mid þy lege anum & mid þæm fyrenum strælum acweald,
buton þæm þe hie mid heora wæpnum acwealdon & ofslogan.
 130. Hie þa swa sigebeorhte & swa gebegde mid mycelre blisse
to ham foran, & sona þæm ælmihtigan Gode & þæm heahengle
Michaele to þære halgan ciricean hie eaðmodlice & luflice þancudan
þæs siges ðe hie gefered hæfdon.
 134. Þa gemittan hie eac beforan ðære norðdura þære
ciricean on þæm marmanstane swylce mannes swaðu, þon gelicost þe
þær sum mon þa gestode.
 136. & þa fotlastas wæron swutole & gesyne on þæm
stane, swa hie on wexe wæron aðyde.
 137. Þa ongeaton hie geornlice þæt se eadiga Michael
þær wæs toweard him to fultome, ða hwile ðe hie æt þæm
gefeohte wæron.
 139. & him sylfa þæt tacn þæs siges gesette, &
gecyðde into þy swiðan slæpe.
 140. On ðæm stane hi þa sona ðær ciricean
ofergetimbredon & þær weofod inne wlitelice geworhtan &
gegyredon.
 142. & þa stowe mid mycclum gefean seoþþan weorþodan
& beeodan, hie þa hæfdan miccle lufan & geleafan to þære
ciricean.
 144. Ond eac healico ondrysnu þa leode.
 145. & him wæs on mode myccle weorce & mycel tweo
hwæt hie be þære dorstan don, hweþer hie þa ciricean halgedon,
oþþe hwæt ðæs Godes willa wære, & þæs halgan wyrhtan
þe hie his hand geworhte.
 148. Hie þa þæt to ræde ærest fundon, þæt hie
ciricean arærdon be eastan þære stowe, & þa gehalgodan on Sancte
Petres naman, þæs halgan Cristes ðegnes.
 151. & þær gedydon twa weofedu in, & gehalgodan on
Sanctæ Marian noman Cristes modor, & oðer on Sancte Iohannes
Baptistan, Cristes fulwihtfæder.
 153. Him þa se heora arwyrða bisceop eadiglice &
halwendlice geðeaht forðbrohte, & hie lærede þæt hie raðost
to Rome sendon to ðæm papan, & ðone papan & þæt papseld
þæt hie befrinon & beahsodan hwæt him þæs to ræde þuhte,
hweþer hie þa ciricean halgian dorston on oþre wisan.
 158. Þislic ærende se eadiga papa ða ðær eft onsende
& þas word cwæð, Gif hit sie mannes gemet þæt he ciricean
halgian sceole, ðonne is hit ealles gerisnost þæt hit sy on ðæm
dæge ðe se sige onseald wæs.
 161. Gif hit þonne hwæt elles ðæm halgan hirede be
þære stowe licige, & him leofre sie, þonne is hit ealles selest to
ðæm dæge to secenne hwæt þæs willa sie.
 164. Ond þonne seo tid nealæce uton wit þonne begen don mid
uncrum burhwarum feower daga fæsten, & ða halgan þrynesse georne
biddan þæt heo þæt lac þæt hie þurh ðone halgan heahengel
ærest æteowde mannum wundorlic tacn, þæt hie þæt mannum to
fylgenne on cyðde, forðgelædde & gebringe.
 169. Hie ða ealle eaðmodlice, swa heora æþela bisceoþ
lærde, feower daga fæsten gedydon.
 170. Þa ðære nihte þe hie þæt fæsten gefæst
hæfdon, þa wæs Sanctus Michael þæm bisceope on gesihþe
æteowed & him cwæð to, Nis eow ðæs weorces þearf þæt ge
ða ciricean halgian, forðon þe ic hie geworhte & ic hie gehalgode.
 174. Ge þonne nu þyder ingongað & me ætstondað,
& geornlice mundbyrde gelyfað to ðære stowe, & hie genehge mid
gebedum seceað.
 176. Ðin is þonne þæt þu þær to morgne mæssan
inne gesinge, & þis folc þær after ðeawe to husle gange.
 178. Min is þonne þæt ic mid arwyrðnesse tacne æteowe
& gecyþe hine, þurh hine sylfne hie gehalgode & gebletsode.
 180. Hie ða sona on morgenne swiðe gefeonde for ðære
andsware mid mycelre anrædnesse gebeda & mid haligra lofsanga lacum
þyder coman, & ða eodan ealle on ða ciricean.
 182. Of ðæs portices dura þæs ðærscwolde wæs
gesyne þæt þa swaðo wæron ærest utwearde ongunnen, ðe ic ær
sægde þæt þær ærest on ðæm marmanstane gemeted wæron.
 185. Þeos circe mid þys portice mihte hu hwego fif hund manna
befon & behabban.
 186. Ðonne wæs æteowed þæt arwyrðe weofod wið
þone suðwag to middes hu hwega ðæs wages.
 188. Wæs hit eac bewrigen & oferbræded mid baswe
godwebbe.
 189. Wæs þæt ilce hus eac hwem dragen, nalas æfter
gewunan mennisces weorces þæt þa wagas wæron rihte, ac git swiðor
on scræfes onlicnesse þæt wæs æteowed.
 191. & gelomlice ða stanas swa of oðrum clife
stæðhylplice ut sceoredon.
 193. Eac swylce se hrof wæs on mislicre heanesse; on sumre stowe
he wæs þæt man mid his handa nealice geræcean mihte, in sumre
eaþelice mid heafde gehrinan.
 195. Ic þonne gelyfe þæt se heahengel ures Drihtnes miccle
swiðor sohte & lufode þære heortan clænnesse þonne þara stana
frætwednesse.
 197. Ðonne wæs se cnoll swa hit nu cuð is, þæt se munt
is mycel uteweard; & he is styccemælum mid hsomige wuda oferwexen; sum
mid grenum felda oferbræded.
 200. Ond þa æfter þon þe ðær wæron ða halgan
lofsangas & mæssan gefyllede, hie ða mid mycclum gefean & blisse
& mid þæs engles bletsunga eft hwyrfende wæron to heora husum.
 203. Se bisceop þa ðær gesette gode sangeras &
mæssepreostas & manigfealdlice ciricean þegnas, þa þær
seoððan dæghwamlice mid gelimplicre endebyrdnesse weorðode.
 206. Næs hweðre nænig man þe þær æfre nihtes
tidum dorste on þære ciricean cuman.
 207. Ac on dægred siþþan hit frumlyhte, hie þyder
inwæron to ðæm lofsangum gesamnode.
 208. Þonne wæs þær eac of þæm ilcan stane þære
ciricean hrofes on þa norðhealfe þæs weofodes swiþe wynsum ond
hluttor wæta utflowende, þæt þa biggengan þe on ðære stowe
stille wunodan.
 212. Þonne wæs ongean ðyssum wæterscipe glæsen fæt
on seolfrenre racenteage ahangen þæt ðæs wynsuman wætan þær
onfeng.
 214. Þær wæs gewuna þæm folce þonne hie to husle
gegangen hæfdon, þæt hie æfter hlæddrum up to ðæm
glæsenum fæte astigon & þære heofonlican wætan hie þær
onfengon & onbyrigdon.
 217. Seo þonne wæs wynsumu on ðære onbyrignesse, &
heo wæs on þæm innoðe halwende.
 218. Is þis eac to tacne þæt manige men on feforadle &
on mislicum oþrum untrumnessum þurh þyses wætan onbyrignesse wurdan
sona gehælde.
 220. Eac swylce oþrum gemetum unarimede manna untrumnessa
ðær wæron oft & gelome gehælde.
 222. & manigfeald onlic wundor ðysum, ðam þe heora miht
wæs gelimplic & arwyrðe, ðær wæron & gyt beoð æteowed
& gecyðed, ealles oftost hweðre on ðæm dæge þe seo tid bið
& his weorðung.
 225. Ðonne of ðæm þeodlande þæm þe þær
ymbsyndon ða folc þær cumende beoð, þonne is to gelyfenne &
geare to witenne þæt þær manigfealde & mislice untrumra manna
beoð gehælde.
 228. & ðæs engles mægen & his wundor þær
þonne weorðod bið, & oftost æteowed on þæm dæge.
 229. Swa cwæð Sanctus Paulus, <foreign>Qui ad ministrum summis</foreign>;
Englas beoð to ðegnunge gæstum fram Gode hider on world sended, to
ðæm ðe þone ecean eðel mid mode & mid mægene to Gode
geearniað, þæt him syn on fultume ða þe wið þæm awergdum
gastum syngallice feohtan sceolan.
 234. Ac uton nu biddan þone heahengel Sanctus Michahel & ða
nigen endebyrdnessa ðara haligra engla, þæt hie us syn on fultume wið
helsceaðum.
 236. Hie wæron þa halgan on onfenge manna saulum.
 237. Swa Sanctus Paulus wæs geseonde on norðanweardne þisne
middangeard, þær ealle wætero niðergewitað, & he þær
geseah ofer ðæm wætere sumne harne stan.
 240. & wæron norð of ðæm stane awexene swiðe
hrimige bearwas, & ðær wæron þystrogenipo, & under þæm
stane wæs niccra eardung & wearga.
 242. & he geseah þæt on ðæm clife hangodan on
ðæm isigean bearwum manige swearte saula be heora handum gebundne.
 244. & þa fynd þara on nicra onlicnesse heora gripende
wæron, swa swa grædig wulf.
 245. & þæt wæter wæs sweart under þæm clife
neoðan.
 246. & betuh þæm clife on ðæm wætre wæron
swylce twelf mila.
 247. & ðonne ða twigo forburston þonne gewitan þa saula
niðer þa þe on ðæm twigum hangodan, & him onfengon ða nicras.
 249. Ðis ðonne wæron ða saula þa ðe her on worlde mid
unrihte gefyrenode wæron, & ðæs noldan geswican ær heora lifes
ende.
 251. Ac uton nu biddan Sanctus Michael geornlice þæt he ure
saula gelæde on gefean, þær hie motan blissian abuton ende on ecnesse.
 253. AMEN.

LS 26 (MildredCockayne)
B3.3.26.
Saint Mildred: Cockayne 1864-6, III, 422-8.



 1. <foreign>Sancte Mildryð</foreign>.
 1. On drihtnes naman Sanctus augustinus gefulwihte æþelbryht
cantwara cyning & ealle his ðeode.
 2. Þonne wæs eadbald cyning æþelbryhtes sunu &
byrhtan his cwene & æþelburh heora dohtor, oðre naman tate, forgifan
eadwine norðhymbra cyninge to cwene & Sanctus paulinus mid hire for &
gefullode ðone cyning eadwine & ealle his ðeode.
 7. & æfter his life hio eft cantwara byrig gesohte &
hire/ broðor eadbald þæne cyning & paulinus se bisceop eft mid hire
com.
 9. & hio hyre þa betstan madmas to cantwaran cyricean brohte
hire to gebedrædene & þæs cyninges sawle þe hi begæt, ða man
gyt þær inne sceawian mæg.
 12. & he ða paulinus onfeng þa bisceoprice æt
hrofeceastre on godes willan & ðær his lif geendode & godes rice
begeat.
 14. Ðonne wæs eormenred cyning & eorcenbyrht cyning &
Sancte eanswyð, hi wæron ealle eadbaldes bearn & imman his cwene, hio
wæs francna cynges dohtor.
 17. & Sancte eanswið resteð on folcanstana þæm mynstre
þæt hio sylf gestaðelode.
 19. Þonne wæs eormenburh & oðre naman domne eafe &
eormengyð & æðelred & æðelbriht wæron eormenredes bearn
& oslafe his cwene.
 22. Ðonne wæs domne eafe forgyfon to myrcna landa merwalde
pendan sunu cynges to cwene & hi þær begeatan Sancte mildburge &
Sancte mildryðe & Sancte mildgyðe & Sancte merefin þæt halige
cild.
 25. & hi þa æfter ðan for godes lufan & for þisse
worolde him todældon & hiora bearn & hiora woruld æhta gode
forgeafan.
 27. & hiora yldeste dohtor & Sancte mildburh resteð æt
wynlucan þæm mynstre on mercna lande þær wæron hire mihta oft
gecyðede & gyt synd.
 30. Sancte mildryð resteð binnan teneð on ðæm iglande
& ðær wæron oft hyre mihta gecyþede & get synd.
 32. Sancte mildgyð resteð on norðhembran þær wæron
hire mihta oft gecyðede & get syndon þonne wæs.
 34. Sancte merefin þæt halige cild on iogoðhade to gode
gelæd.
 35. Þonne wæron æðelred & æðelbryht þa halgan
æþelingas befæste egcbrihte cynge to fostre & to lare for þan hi
wæron æt hiora yldran befeallenne & wæs he se cyning heora
fæderan sunu eorcenbrihtes & Sexburh his cwene.
 40. Þa wæron hi sona on geogoðe swyðe gesceadwise &
rihtwise swa hit godes willa wæs.
 41. Ða ofðuhte þæt anum þæs cyninges geferan se
wæs þunor haten & wæs him se leofestan ðegen to his bearnum.
 43. Ða ondrædde he him gif hi leng lifedon þæt hi wurdon
þam cynge leofran ðonne he.
 45. Ongan hi þa hatian dearnunga & wregean to þam cyninge
& cwæð þæt gif hi libban moston þæt hi ægðer ge hine ge
his bearn þæs cynerices benæmde.
 48. Ongan hine ða biddan þæt he moste þa æþelingas
dearnunga acwellan ac se cyning him lyfan nolde for ðam þe hi him leofa
wæron & gesibbe.
 51. & þa git se ðunor hine oft & gelome bæd þæt
he him leafe sealde þæt he moste don embe ða æþelingas swa he
wolde.
 53. & he ða sona swa dyde swa he ær gyrnende wæs &
he hi on niht sona gemartirode innan ðæs cyninges heahsetle swa he
dyrnlicost mihte.
 55. & he geðoht hæfde þæt hi þær næfre uppe
ne wurdan ac ðurh godes mihte hi þanon gecydde wurdon emne swa ðæs
leohtes leoma stod up þurh þære healle hrof up to heofonum.
 59. & he ða se cyning sylf embe forman hancred ut gangende
wæs & he þa him sylf geseonde wæs þæt wundor.
 61. Þa wearð he afyrht & afæred & het hi hrædlice
þæne þunor to feccean & line ahsode hwær he his mægcildum
cumen hæfde ðe he him forstolen hæfde.
 63. He him andsworode & cwæð þæt he sylf wiste &
he him secgan nolde buton he nyde sceolde.
 65. He ða se cyning cwæð þæt he be his freondscipe hit
secgan sceolde.
 66. He him andsworode & cwæð þæt he hi innan his
healle under his heahsetle bebyrged hæfde.
 68. & he þa se cyning swyðe unrot geworden wæs for
þæs godes wundre & for þære gesihþe ðe he ðær gesewen
hæfde & he þa be ðam gearo wiste þæt he gode abolgen hæfde
swyþor þonne his ðearf wære.
 72. & þa on morgen swyðe hrædlice him to gefeccean het
his witan & his þegnas þæt hi him geræddon hwæt him be ðam
selost ðuhte oððe to done wære.
 75. & he þa & hi geræddon mid ðæs
ærcebisceopes fultume Deusdedit þæt man heora swustor on mercna lande
þe hio to forgifen wæs gefeccean het to ðam þæt hio hyre broðra
wergild gecure on swylcum þingum swylce hyre & hire nyhstan freondum
selost licode.
 80. & hio ða swa dyde þæt hio þæt wergeld geceas
þurh godes fultum on ðam iglande þe teneð is nemned, þæt is
þonne hund eahtatig hida landes þe hio ðær æt þæm cyninge
onfeong.
 83. & hit ða swa gelamp þa se cyning & hio domne eafe
ærest þæt land geceas & hi ofer þa ea comon þa cwæð se
cyning to hire hwylcne dæl þæs landes hio onfon wolde hyre broðrum to
wergilde.
 87. Hio him ða andsworode & cwæð þæt hio his na
maran ne gyrnde þonne hire hind utan ymbe yrnan wolde, þe hire ealne weg
beforan arn ðonne hio on rade wæs.
 90. Cwæð þæt hire þæt getyðed wære þæt hio
swa myceles his onfon sceolde swa seo hind hire gewisede.
 91. He ða se cyning hire geandsworode & cwæð þæt he
þæt lustlice fægnian wolde.
 93. & hio ða hind swa dyde þæt hio him beforan hleapende
wæs & hi hyre æfterfiligende wæron oð þæt hi comon to
ðære stowe þe is nu gecwedon þunores hlæwe.
 96. & he ða se þunor to ðam cyninge aleat & he him to
cwæð, leof, hu lange wylt ðu hlystan þyssum dumban nytene þe hit eal
wyle þis land utan beyrnan?
 99. Wylt ðu hit eal ðære cwenon syllan?
 99. & ða sona æfter þyssum wordum se eorðe tohlad.

END_TEXT

LS 27.1 (MildredForst)
B3.3.27.1.
Saint Mildred: Forster 1914, 333-4.



 1. <foreign>Benedicta & beata sis semper is aeternum & in thronum
Dei, Connumerata & computata sis cum choris uirginum.</foreign> ða hyre modor hi
mid þyssere bletsunge hyre ðus onfangen hæfde, heo hy aþenedum limum
ætforan þam halgan wefode astrehte & hy mid teara agotennysse to
Drihtne gebæd.
 5. Ða heo hyre gebed geendod hæfde, heo upastod & to hyre
modor cneowum onbeah.
 6. & heo hy ða mid sibbecosse gegrette & ealle da
geferrædene samod & hy hire wæter to handa bæron æfter
regollicre wisan.
 7. Him ða eallum ætgæderum sittendum ongan seo abbodyssa,
hyre modor, of ðam Dauiticum sealmum gyddian & þus cweðan,
<foreign>Suscepimus, Deus, misericordiam tuam in medio templi tui</foreign>.
 10. Swaswa Anna seo halige wuduwa & Simeon se ealda sungon
& drymdon, ða hy þæt mycele & þæt formære bearn mid
heora earmum beclypton & into ðam temple bæron & offrodon.
 12. Heo sang þa oðer fers, <foreign>Confirma hoc, Deus, quod operatus
es in nobis a templo sancto tuo, quod est in Hierusalem</foreign>.
 14. Heo sang þæt ðridde,<foreign>Saluos nos fac, Domine Deus noster,
& congrega nos de nationibus, ut confiteamur nomini sancto tuo &
gloriemur in laude tua</foreign>.
 16. Ðylicum & fela oðrum godcundlicum wordum heo hyre leofe
bearn georne lærde & to Gode tihte.
 18. Wæs hit hyre eac eaddæde, swa lange swa hyre ingehyd
wæs eal mid Godes gaste afylled.
 19. Næs heo, swa nu æðelborene men synt, mid ofermettum
afylled ne mid woruldprydum ne mid nyðum ne mid æfeste ne mid teonwordum.
 21. Næs heo sacful ne geflitgeorn.
 21. Næs heo swicol nanum þæraþe hyre to dohte.
 22. Heo wæs wuduwena & steopcilda arigend & ealra earmra
& geswincendra frefriend & on eallum þingum eaðmod & stille.
 24. Wæs heo swyðe gemyndi, þæt we ealle of twam mannum
comon & of eorðan lame gescepene & geworhte wæron & to þam
eft gewurðan sceolan.
 26. Gemunde.
