LS 27.2 (SeaxburghForst)
B3.3.27.2.
Saint Seaxburgh: Forster 1914, 334-5.



 1. Ðær cuðe wæron & gyta syndon.
 2. & sancta Eadburh þa to ðam mynstre feng æfter sancte
Myldryþe.
 2. & heo ða cyricean arærde, ðe hyre lichama nu inne
resteð.
 4. Ðonne wæs sancte Seaxburh & sancta æþeldryð
& sancta Wihtburh, hy wæron Annan dohtra, EastEngla cynges.
 6. Ðonne wæs sancta æþeldryð forgyfen twam werum,
Tondbryhte Suðgyrwena ealdormæn & Ecgferðe Norðhymbrena cynige, to
cwene.
 7. & heo ðeahhwæþere hyre mægðhad geheold oð hyre
lifes ende.
 8. & heo ða hyre licreste geceas on Eligbyrig & ðær
hyre mihta oft cuðe syndon.
 10. Ðonne wæs sancte Eormenhild, Ercenbrihtes dohtor &
Seaxburge, forgyfen Wulfhere, Pendan sunu Myrcena cinges, to cwene.
 11. & on hyra dagum Myrcena ðeod onfeng fulluht.
 12. & ðær hi begeaton sancte Wærburge ða halige
fæmnan.
 13. & heo resteþ on ðam mynstre, þe is gecweden
Heanburh.
 14. Ðonne resteð sancte Eormenhild on Eligbyrig mid hyre meder
& mid hyre modrian sancte æþeldryða & heora mihta ðær oft
cuðe syndon.
 16. & sancta Seaxburh & sancta Eormenhild onfengon
haligrifte on ðam mynstre, þe is gecweden Middeltune on Kentlande.
 17. & þæt igland on Scæpyge hyrð into Middeltune
& hit is ðreora mila brad & seofan mila lang.
 19. Ða gelicode ðære halgan cwene Seaxburge, þæt heo
ðærbinnan for myrhde & for mærðe hyre ðær mynster getimbrode
& gestadelode, swa geo men cwædon, þæt ðrittigum gearum ne
gestilde næfre stefen cearciendes wænes ne ceoriendes wales.
 22. Ða þæt mynster getimbrod wæs, ða com hyre to Godes
engel on nihtlicre gesihðe & hire bodode, þæt ær feala gearum
hæðene leod sceolden ðas þeode gewinnan.
 24. Hæfde heo þa gehealdan þæt cynerice þrittig wintra
hyre suna Hlodhere to handa.
 25. & heo ða æt him gebohte his dæl ðæs eardes to
freodome into ðam mynstre, ða hwile ðe cristendom wære on Englalande
gehealden.
 27. & þa gebletsunge heo þærto on Rome begeat, þamðe
þa are to Godes þeowdome.

LS 28 (Neot)
B3.3.28.
Saint Neot: Warner 1917, 129-34.



 1. Of Seinte Neote.
 1. Mæn þa leofeste, we wylleð eow cyðen beo sumen dæle
emb þyssen halgen, þe we todæig wurðigeð, þæt eower geleafe
þe trumre seo for þan mancynn behofeð godcundre lare, þæt heo þurh
þa mugen to lifes wege becumen.
 4. Hit sægð on þan halgen godspelle, þæt þæt liht
on Godes gelaðunge na behydd beon ne sceal, ac up asett ofer þan
candelstafe, þæt þa þe þær in gað, mugen þone leome geseon
& on lihte beon.
 7. Swa eac ne mihte Sanctus Neotus behydd beon ne bedigelod, þa
þa God hine geupped habben wolde.
 9. He wæs on iugeðe, þæs þe bec secgeð, to boclicre
lare gesett, & to godcunden þeawen becom, & georne smeade þa he
andgitfull wæs emb þæt ece lif, & hwu he stiðlucest her on life
for Gode libben mihte.
 12. Swa hit awriten is, þæt se weig is sticol & neare,
þe to þan ecen life belimpð, & nan mann þær to ne becumð, bute
þurh mycel geswync & forhæfednysse.
 14. Swa dyde Sanctus Neotus, forhæfde hine sylfne fram
gelustfullunge þysses lifes.
 15. He wæs manðwære & milde ealle mannen & he
dæighwamlice to his Drihtene clypode æfter Dauides sange þuss
cweðende, Drihten, þine weges ic lufige, & þine æ ic folgigen
þænce.
 18. Do beo me æfter þinre mildheortnysse & tæc me
þine rihtwisnysse.
 19. Soðlice þæt ilca gebed us is alefd, gyf we wylleð
inweardlice to Gode clypigen & his mildheortnysse biddan.
 21. Hit sæigð on gewritan, þæt þes halge were to
Glæstingebyrig gecerred wære on Sanctes ælfeges dagen þæs halgen
biscopes, & æt him underfeng þone halge sacerdhad, & hine wel
geheold, & þær under wel geðeah, & wæs eallen mannen eadmod
& lufigendlic.
 25. & his salmes & oðre gebedan he geornlice beeode
dæiges & nihtes.
 26. & his gewune wæs, þæt he wolde on dæig gelomen
his cneowe gebegen, & eac swylce on niht to þan ælmihtigen Gode, swa
se halge apostel Sanctus Bartholomeus dyde, hund siðen on niht & eall swa
oft on dæg.
 29. He gemunde symle his synnen, þe he on his iugeðe gefremede,
& þa geornlice beweop & bereowsede, & oðre gode forbisnen
æteowde.
 31. He geneosode Romeburh seofe siðen Criste to lofe & Seinte
Petre, & þære his synnen forgyfenysse underfeng.
 33. He wæs on eallen Godes beboden swyðe fullfremed.
 34. Sohte þa weste stowe geond eall þiss land on to wunigene,
& þa gemette he þurh Godes foresceawunge.
 36. Seo is wæstdæles þysses landes, ten milen fram
Petrocesstowe þa me hatt Neotes stoca.
 37. & he him þær wununge getimbrode on swyðe fægeren
stowe, & myrige wæterseaðes þær abuten standeð, & þa
synden swyðe wynsume of to þycgene.
 39. Þær se Godes þeowe Sanctus Neotus his lif adreah on
mycelre forhæfednysse, ofer mæn oðre modes & mæignes
þeowwigende þan, þe hine to þeowe geceas, þæt wæs Gode sylfen.
 42. Ne mæig nan mann fullice gecyðen, hwu stiðlice he his
lif adreah ær his mæssepreosthade ne æfter.
 44. Ne glæingde he his lichame mid deorewurðen scrude, ne he
mid estmeten his innað ne gefyllde.
 45. Mid þan þe he þuss lange gedrohtned hæfde on þære
stowe, þe we won ær fore sæden, þa ongann se ungeseowenlice feond him
togeanes andigen, swa him ælc god ofðincð.
 48. Ongann þa sænden his ættrige wæpnen, þæt synd
costnungen, togeanes þan halgen were.
 49. Ac he þone feond oferswað mid rihten geleafen þurh Godes
gescyldnysse.
 50. Him comen gelomen to halige Godes ængles and hine
gefrefreden & wel geherten, & hine manoden, þæt he ne geswice
Godes word to bodigenne ealle mannen oðð his lifes ænde, & beheten
him gewiss þæt ece lif, þe he nu mid myrhðe onwuneð.
 54. He dyde swa se ængel bebead.
 55. Bodede ealle mannen rihtne geleafe.
 55. Þan synfullen & þan þe heora synnen andetten wolden
& æfre geswican, he behet Godes godnysse & his mildheortnysse.
 57. & þær toecan þæt ece lif, þa gode he manode,
þæt heo on heora godnysse þurhwunedan.
 58. Hit gelamp sume dæige, þæt se halge were on
ærnemorgen digellice ferde to his wæterseaðe, & þær his
drohtnunge & his salmsanges on þan wætere hnacodan leomen adreah, swa
his gewune wæs.
 61. Þa geherde he færinge ridenda menige.
 62. He þa hrædlice mid mycelen ofste fram þære welle
onette, nolde þæt his drohtnung ænigen eorðlice mæn cuð wurde
on his life bute þan anen, þe ofer eallen rixeð.
 64. Forleas þa on þan færelde his ænne scoh, &
oðerne mid him to his gebedhuse ham gebrohte.
 66. Mid þan þe he his salmes & his gebeden &
rædingan embhydiglice smeade, þa becom him to gemynde his oðer scoh,
þæt he hine on þan færelde forleas.
 68. Clypode þa him to his þeign, & bebead him þæt he
him his sco gefeccen scolde.
 69. He þa wæs his fæder bebodan gehersum, & hrædlice
ferde to þære welle, & þær on þan wegge wunderlice wise
gemette.
 71. Þæt is þæt an fox, þe is geapest ealra deora,
þær arn geond dunen & denen wunderlice beseonde mid egen hider &
þider, & færinge becom to þære stowe, þære se halge were his
fet geðwoh, & þone scoh gelæhte, & ætfaren þohte.
 75. Þa beseh þær, to se arfæste Drihten & nolde,
þæt his þeowe on swa medemlice þingen geunrotsed wære.
 76. Gesænde þa slæp on þone fox, swa þæt he his lif
alet, habbende þa þwanges of þan sco on his fracede muðe.
 78. Se þeign þa þær to geteignde & þone sco genam
& þan halge gebrohte, & him cydde eall hwæt þær gelumpen
wæs.
 80. He þa, se halge, þæs mycele wundrode, & bebead þan
þeigne on þæs Hælendes name, þæt he hit nanen ne cydde ær his
lifes ænde.
 81. On þan time wæs ælfred king, & to þan halgen
gelomen com emb his sawle þearfe.
 83. He hine eac þreade manega worden & him to cwæð mid
forewitegunge, Eala, þu king, mycel scealt þu þoligen on þyssen life.
 85. On þan towearden time, swa mycele angsumnysse þu gebiden
scealt, þæt nan mænnisc tunge hit eall asecgen ne mæig.
 87. Nu, leof bearn, geher me, gyf þu wylt, & þine heorte to
mine ræde gecerre.
 88. Gewit eallinge fram þinre unrihtwisnysse, & þine synnen
mid ælmessen ales, & mid tearen adigole, & gebring þine lac to
Romeburh, Martinum þan pape, þe nu wealt Engliscre scole.
 91. Se king ælfred dyde þa swa se halge hine bebead, & his
beboden georne hlyste, & he him feala foresæde mid forewitegunge, swa
him syððen aneode.
 93. Se halge eft cwæð oðre wordan, Ic nylle þe
bedigeligen, gode king, þæt me toweard is forneh se dæig mines
forðsiðes, þone ic gernde simble mid ealre heorte.
 95. Ac ic secge get, þæt æfter minen forðsiðe þu
feale þoligen scealt, & fram Deniscre þeode þu aflemed byst of
þinen cynerice, & þine cæmpen & heretogen þe fram gewiteð
& tostæncte byð.
 98. Swa hit on Drihtenes þrowunge awriten is þæt, þone se
herde aflemed & ofslagen byð, þonne byð þa scep ealle
tostæncte.
 100. Ac þonne þe ealre angsumest byð on þine mode,
geðænc þu min, & ic þe gescilde on Drihtenes name.
 102. Þa se king þas word geherde, þa forhtode he þearle
swyðe, & his bletsunge abæd, & aweig gewende.
 104. Him aneode syððen swa Sanctus Neotus him foresæde.
 104. Ðæs halgen untrumnysse weox þa fram dæge to
dæige, & þa on þan ytemesten dæige his handbreden up to heofone
astrehte, & mid blisse his gast asende, & to reste gewende.
 107. Soðlice engles togeanes his sawle comen, & heo
gelædden mid mycelen gefean to heofonrices myrhðe.
 109. His leorningcnihtes þa bebyrigden his lic mid mycelen
wurðmynte innen þære cirice, þe he sylf on ær gesette.
 110. Þær becom þa on þære hwile mycel swetnysse
stænc, swylc hit eall gestreawod wære on þære stowe mid wynsume
blostmen & wyrtgemangum, þær wurden eac feale untrume gehælde fram
mistlicen brocen þurh Godes mihten & þæs halgen geearnunge.
 114. & eft binnen seofen gearen his ban up genumen wurðen
& on oðre stowe mid wurdmynte aleigd, neh þan altere, & þær
eft wearð mycel swotnysse stænc geworden on þære styrunge.
 117. Hwæt, þa word ealle gefyllede beon scolden, þe se halge
foresæde beo þan kinge.
 119. Com þa Guðrum, se hæðene king, mid his wælreowen
here ærest on eastdæle Sexlandes, & þær feala manne ofsloh.
 120. Sume eac fleames cepten, & sume on hand eodan.
 121. Þa ælfred king, þe we ær embe spæcon, þæt
ofaxode, þæt se here swa stiðlic wæs, & swa neh Englelande, he
sone forfyrht fleames cepte, & his cæmpen ealle forlet, & his
hertogen, & eall his þeode, madmes & madmfaten, & his life
gebearh.
 125. Ferde þa lutigende geond heges & weges, geond wudes
& feldes, swa þæt he þurh Godes wissunge gesund becom to
æðelingege, & on sumes swanes huse his hleow gernde, & eac swylce
him & his yfele wife georne herde.
 128. Hit gelamp sume dæige, þæt þæs swanes wif
hætte hire ofen, & se king þærbig sæt hleowwinde hine beo þan
fyre, þan heowen nytende, þæt he king wære.
 130. Þa wearð þæt yfele wif færinge astyrod, &
cwæð to þan kinge eorre mode, Wænd þu þa hlafes, þæt heo ne
forbeornen, for þan ic geseo dæighwamlice, þæt þu mycel æte
eart.
 133. He wæs sone gehersum þan yfele wife, for þan þe he
nede scolde.
 134. He þa, se gode king, mid mycelre angsumnysse &
siccetunge to his Drihtene clypode, his mildse biddende.
 136. Hwæt, þa abuten him aneode ealswa se halge him
foresæde on ær, & mare eorfoðe he adreah, þone we nu areccen
mugen, ac he wearð eft forraðe gefrefrod þurh þone halgen Neoten.
 139. He com to him anes nihtes on swefne swyðe brihte scinende,
& him to cwæð, Eala, þu king, hwæt wylt þu to mede gesyllen
þan þe þe fram þyssen uneðnyssen alyseð.
 141. He wearð afyrht on swefne færlice swyðe, & þeh
þan halgen geandswerode, Eala, leof, he cwæð, hwæt mæig ic
syllen?
 143. Ic eam ealles godes benæmed & mines kynerices.
 144. Se halge him andswerode, Ic eam Neotus, þin freond, & ic
nu blissige mid heofene Kinge.
 145. Gehyht nu on his mihte, þonne becumst þu æfter Eastern
to þinen æðele, & þe togeanes cumð þin todræfed here, &
þines cymes þearle fægenigeð.
 148. Ic þe toforen fare, þu me æfterfolge, & þin folc
samod.
 149. Ic soðlice todræfe ealle þine wiðerwinnen, &
þone king, þe þe togeanes winð, to geleafen gebege.
 150. Hit gelamp þa eall swa, & Guðrum se hæðene king
com to ælfrede þan cristene kinge, mid þreottene cæmpen, &
friðes wilnode, & to fulhte feng.
 152. & he twelf dages æfter þan her on lande wunede mid
mycelre blisse, & syððen gesund gewende mid his herelafe to his agenen
earde mid ealre sibbe.
 155. Þa weox ælfredes cynerice, & his word wide sprang,
þæt he on godcunden gewriten wel gelæred wæs, swa þæt he
oferðeah biscopes & mæssepreostes & hehdiacones, & cristendom
wel þeah on þan gode time.
 158. Eac is to wytene, þæt se king Ælfred manega bec þurh
Godes gast gedyhte.
 159. & binnen twam & twentig gearen his cynerices þiss
eorðlice lif forlet, & to þan ecen gewende, swa him God geuðe for his
rihtwisnysse.
 161. Eala, mæn þa leofe, þa wæron gode dages on þan
gode time for cristenes folcas geearnunge, & rihtwisra heafodmanna.
 163. Nu is æighwanen heof & wop, & orefcwealm mycel for
folces synnen.
 165. & wæstmes, æigðer gea on wude gea on felde, ne
synd swa gode, swa heo iu wæron, ac yfeleð swyðe eall eorðe wæstme,
& unrihtwisnysse mycele wexeð wide geond wurlde, & sibbe tolysnysse
& tælnysse.
 167. & se þincð nu wærrest & geapest, þe oðerne
mæig beswican, & his æhte him of anymen.
 169. Eac man swereð man mare þone he scolde, þy hit is þe
wyrse wide on eorðe, & beo þan we mugen understanden, þæt hit is
neh domesdæge.
 171. Ne spareð nu se fæder þan sune, ne nan mann oðren, ac
ælc man winð ongean oðren, & Godes lage ne gemeð, swa swa me
scolde.
 173. Beo þan we mugen ongyten, þæt þiss wurld is
aweigweard & swyðe neh þan ænde þysser wurlde.
 174. Eale, gesælig byð se þe hine sylfen on time
gebyregeð.
 175. Uten nu bidden georne Seinte Neoten & oðre halgen,
þæt heo ure þingeres beon to þan Heofonkinge, þæt we næfre
ealles to yfelne time ne gebiden on þyssen earmen life, & þæt we
moten æfter forðsiðe to ecere reste becumen.

LS 29 (Nicholas)
B3.3.29.
Saint Nicholas: Dictionary of Old English transcript, edited from Cambridge, Corpus Christi College, MS. 303.



 1. Witoðlice ælc þære wyrhta þe unwislic wyrcþ
aginð to wyrcenne ne mæg beon feager ne staðelfæst geteald.
 3. Ne eac þæt gewrit þe unwis mann onginð to macigenne ne
bið hit na wislic to sprecanne ne god to understandenne.
 4. Ne hæfst þu me ofte gebedon leofe fæder anastasi
þæt ic þe ut arehte mid lædenlicre spræce þæs eadigestan
nicholaes gebyrdtida and his arwurðe lif and þa manigfealde tacne þe
drihten dyde þurh him.
 7. And ic iohannes sanctus ianuaries þeowe þe eom nu gebunden
mid diaconhade and þæs hades unwurðe eom þe geandwyrde mines litles
andgytes þæt ic gewilnode swiðor to leornigenne þonne swilce þincg
to writenne forþon ic wat me to beonne unscadwis on swa deorwurðra
spræca.
 10. Ac swa þeah forþan apostolican cwide þe þu hæfst on
þon halgan nicholae, ic nylle þe na beon ungehersum ac ic ondræde gif ic
hit onginne þæt þa godan mægstres geond þas woruld me sculan
getealan and eac unwurðra betwuxen heom.
 13. Nu forþan ic bidde þe arwurðe fæder anastasi þæt
þu and ealle þine gebroðre biddan þam ælmihtigan gode þæt he
untene mine tunge and anopenige min andget to þises mannes spæce eal swa
he geopeneð þæs cilde tunga and hit wel sprecole macað.
 16. Eac oððre stunde þonne his willa is he geopeneð
þære dumben nytene muð to innaniscere spæce.
 17. Swa he mæg eac minne muð geopenian þurh eowre bene gif
his willa sy þæt ic onginne to herigenne mid lædenlicre spæce.
 19. Ic hit wille nu onginne mid godes fylste eallum þam mannum to
wurðmente þe on him blissiað.
 20. Eac ic bidde eadmodlice ealle þa wise ræderes þe to
þissere rædinge ganggað þæt heo me ne fordeman gif heom þær on
aht mislicige ac gemiltsigan hi ic bidde minre elde and minre gecynde.
 22. Gemunan heo eac hu ic eom nu fiftene gear on elde tydderlic of
gecynde.
 23. Swa þeah ic awrat þæs halgenes gebyrðtide and his
derewurðe lif and þa manigfealde tacne þe drihten dyde þurh him mid
lædenlicre spæce eal swa theodi se heahfæder hit awrat on greciscere
tunge and hit swa seoððan sænde þan ealdormen theodore to
wurðmente.
 26. Nu leofe broðre biddan we þisum direwurðen halege
þæt he us to drihtne geþingie and þæt we moton þurh his halige
geearnige þæs deofles costnunge wiðstandan and æfter þisum life
þa ecan blisse underfangen.
 30. Se eadige nicholaus of æþelan cynne wærð up asprungen
and he wunode on þære burh patera gehaten.
 31. Witodlice his fæder and his moder wæron æfre mid þam
heagestan and mid þam betstan geteald innan þæra ilcan burh.
 33. Ac þeah þe hi wæron on swa mycelan wurðscipe wunigende
swa þeah hi hæfdon mare heare geþanc to þam upplican rice þonne
ænigum geglænge to hæbbone on eorðe.
 35. Hi fandodon hu hi hæbban mihton clæne lif betwuxon heom.
 35. Micel godes gife wæs on heom forþon þe hi cunnedon hu hi
mihton heo selfe betst gehealdan fram flæsclicum lustum and þa þa hi
wæron on heora iugeðe ærest togædere gedon and hi hæfdon begeton
þis gesælige cild, þa oftuge heo heom selfum ealle flæsclice lustes
and sohton to godes huse swiðe gelome and þær georne þancedon ure
hlaforde criste þæt he of heom geuðe cild to gestreonenne and mid ealre
eadmodnesse dæghwamlice heara bedu gefyldon.
 41. Witodlice drihten geherde þa heora bena and geteoþedo heom
be þam cilde þæt þæt heo æt him geornlice bædon and he þa
æteowde his mildheortnesse on þam cilde.
 43. Eal swa hit geboren wearð and hit sucende wæs on his modor
breoste þa wæs he gewune ælce wornesdæge and ælce fridæge
þæt he nolde sucan buton ænes on dæg and belaf þonum swa forð to
þam oðrum dæge.
 45. Soðlice be þisum godes tacn wæs ateowod hu mære man
he gewurþen scolde.
 46. He weox þa and ongan wel to þeonne and eal swa he of
cildhade to mare elde becom þa ne cepte he nan þincg of þises
middaneardes welon ac wæs oðer hwile mid his fæder and mid his moder
and oðer hwilce he eode ane to cirican and swa hwæt swa he þærinne
geherde rædan of halgan gewritum eall he hit on his heorte behydde and
fæste belaf on his gemynde.
 51. Ða gelamp hit þæt his fæder and his modor wæron of
þisan life gewitene and he smeade þa on his geþance oft gelome þæt
ure hlaford crist cwæþ on his godspelle, <foreign>Qui non renuntiauit omnum que
possidet non potest meus esse discipulus</foreign>; ðæt is se þe ne forwyrpð
eall þæt he ah ne mæg he naht beon min leornige cniht.
 55. Ða þohte he eall swa to donne æfter þan halige godes
worde ac he ondræd him manne ymbe spæce and þæt hi sceoldon þine
wurþian for swilce þingum and hit þonne wære his drihtne þæs þe
ungecwemre.
 57. Eall þis he geþohte ane on his geþance and nolde hit
nanum mannum cyþen buto gode anum þe ealre manne þohtes symle
besceawað.
 58. Hine he bæd swiðe geornlice þæt he moste his eahte
swa befadian swa hit his drihtne licwurþest wære þæt him ne arise nan
heriunge þær of fram mannum.
 60. Under þan þe he þis wyle on his mode þa wunode þær
an god man on þæra ilcan burh se wæs swiðe spedig and swiðe
wurðfull geteald betwux þan æþelboren mannum ac he wearð þær
æfter swa hafeleas and swa swiðe earm þæt he næfde swa micel to
gode þæt he mihte his earme lif mide forðbringen.
 64. He hæfde eac þreo dohtra ealle mædene and for heora
hafeleaste forhogode earme menn on heom to wifienne.
 66. Ða wolde heora fæder læton heo beon horan þæt hi
mihton his earme lif huru mid þan forðbringan.
 67. Hwæt þa buto þæt seo miccle sceame wearð cuð þa
swa wid swa seo burh wæs and þæt folc hæfde miccle spæce þær
ymbe.
 69. And eal swa se halige wer nicholaus þæt geherde þa hreaw
him swiðe se earme man and his dohtra þe wæron of æþele byrde
gecuman and þohte heom to helpone of þære æhte þe wæs þa get
on his gewealde þæt seo unrihte dæde wurðe þurh þon niðer alegd
and þa mædene ne sceoldon wurþen befylde mid þan openlice hordome.
 73. Witodlice he nolde þæt hit ænig man witen sceolde buton
criste ane.
 74. Hwæt þa se godes deorlincg ongan to besceawinne on hwilce
time he hit mihte swa digollice don þæt se þe hit habban sceolde ne
mihte witon hwæt he wære þe him god dyde.
 76. Ða cepte he anes times nihtes þa þa menn on heora bedde
wæron and hit swiðe gedrih wæs and nam him þa god dæl goldes and
geband hit innen anum claþe and for to þæs wrecces mannes huse and wearp
þæt gold inn þurh anum eahþyrle wel stillice and eode sona aweg
þæt hit nan mann nyste.
 80. On ærnemorgan þa se mann aras and gefand þæt gold
þær þær hit geworpan wæs, þa wundrede he hi swa swiðe þæt
he eall wiðerhypce and ongan to weponne for fægennesse and þancode his
drihtene swiðe geornlice þæt him swa mycel mihte wæs onbesceawod for
his lufan.
 83. Geaf þa sona his heldesta dohter anum godum men to wife mid
rihte wedlace eal swa hit gewunelic wæs mid cristenum mannum.
 85. And æfter þam he ongan swiðe geornlice to spyrigenne
hwæt manne he wære þe him swa micel to gode gedon hæfde.
 86. Ða rædlice eft com se godes þegn nicholaus we digollice
on niht and gebrohte þam gode mann eall swa micel gold eal swa he ær dyde
swa þæt hit nan man nyste.
 88. Soðlice eal swa hit dæg wæs and se man beseah on
þæt gold, þa ongan he eft to wepone for fagennesse and þus cwæð,
Drihten ic bidde þe þæt þu ateowige me synfullum hwæt he beo þe
me swa fela goda to hande bringað.
 91. He cweþ eft, Witodlice ic sceal wacian and slæp forberan
oð þæt se ælmihtiga god me atewige his mildheortnesse hwilc his
þeowa is þe wunað onmang mannum and færð on clænnesse eal swa
drihtnes engel.
 93. Ða æfter feawum dagum com se eadiga nicholaus on niht and
gebroht eft þa þriddan siðe eal swa micel gold eal swa he ær dyde and
wearp hit into þæs mannes huse and hit feol swa hlude þæt se wrecce
mann þær rihtes awehte and hrædlice up aras and arn æfter þam
godes deorlinge and him þus to cweþ, Wiðstand hlaford wiðstand for gode
ic bidde þe þu me na læng ne forfleo.
 98. Soðlice ic hæbbe ofte gebedan to minum drihtene þæt
ic þe mid minum eagnum geseon moste and he oftoc hine þa and gecneow hine
þeah þe hit þeoster niht wære and feol niðer and his fet cyste and
ongan swiðe to wepenne and se eadiga nicholaus him mildelice forbead to
donne.
 101. Eac he bæd him swiðe georne þæt he næfre ne
sceolde hit nanum menn cyðan hwæt he him gedon hæfde þa hwile þe he
on life wære for þon þe he nolde hæbben þær of ænig lof on
þisum life ac on heofone he þohte him gode mede to geearnienne þær mid
and to begytene.
 105. Witodlice he betæhte hine selfne dæghwamlice þam
ælmihtigan gode se þe scyfteð and dihteð ealle þincg swa hwanne swa
he wile and swa hu swa he wile.
 107. Witodlice þa þe þis wæs eall þus gefaran þa
wearð se erchebisceop dæd of þæm godan burge þe is gehaten mirrea.
 109. And eal swa þa bisceopes þe him under wæron geþeodde
þis geherdon, þa ongunnon hi swiðe sarlice to wepenne forþam þe he
wæs eallum mannum leof and wurð for his godum geearnungum.
 111. Hig gegaderodon heom þa on anre stowe mid eallum heora
clercum to þam þæt hio wolden sceawigen swilcne man to biscope þe
drihtne licwurþe wære.
 113. Ða wæs þær sum arwurþe bisceop betweonan heom se
wæs swa wis þurh þæs halgan gastes gife þæt ealle þa oðre
bisceopes swa mycel to his hræde abugon þæt swa hwilcne man swa he
nænnian wolde to þam wurðmente þone hi wolden ealle hæbban, þa
nolde se bisceop nænne man næmnian þa gyt ac bebead heom þreore
dagene fæsten and þæt hi sceoldan biddan mid ealre geornfulnesse þam
ælmihtigan gode þæt he heom ateowde þurh his micclan mildheortnesse
hwilcne man his wille wære þæt þær sceolde gefyllan þone stede
betwuxan þan apostolan þe iudas forleas.
 120. Hi gewæntan þa mid ealre heorte to criste.
 121. Swylce heom si mynegunge wære of heofone gebodan and
bæden heora drihtne þam þe is ece heorde ealre manne þæt he
forsceawode heora neode and þæt he heom nytwurðne heorde ateowian
sceolde and þe his sceap cuðe wel healdan.
 124. Soðlice þa þa heo þurhwunedon þus on heora gebedum
þa geherde se gode biscop ane stæmne up of heofonum and seo him bebead
þæt he sceolde gan to þære cirice gatas and þone mann þe he
ærest geseawe ontihten þider cuman and þone hi scolden halgian to
bisceope and his name wære gecleopod nicholaus.
 127. Se bisceop þa hit gecydde þan oðrum bisceopum hwæt
seo stæmne him bebodan hæfde and cwæþ þus to heom, Leofe broðra
ge sculon biddan anrædlice ures drihtnes miltse her wiðinnen and ic sceal
þær ute geornlice cepnian þæt þe us god behaten hæfð.
 130. Þa þa he to heom þus gecweden hæfde þa eode he ut
and begemde þære cirican gate mid micelre lufa and mid haligre ieapscipe.
 131. Witodlice þa þa ge uhte time com þa efste se halige
nicholaus swilce he fram gode selfe gesæne wære æt fore eallum oðrum
mannum toweard þære circan and eal swa se godes deorlincg com to þære
gate, þa gefeng se biscop hine mid his handum and axode hine mid mycelre
eadmodnesse hwæt his nama wære.
 135. Se godes man him andwyrde mid gastlicere stæmne and mid
niðeralotenum hæfde and acwæþ þæt he hete nicholaus.
 137. Se bisceop cwæþ þa to him, Cum nu leofa cild hider mid
me forþon þe ic hæbbe sum þing digeles wið þe to sprecone.
 138. And eal swa hi comon in to þære cirican þa clypode se
biscop mid hludre stæmne to eallum þam godes þeowan and þus cweþ,
Sceawiað nu leofe broðra þæt þæt drihten cweþ, <foreign>Quid cum que
petierias in nomine meo credite qua accipietis et fiet uobis</foreign>; ðæt is, swa
hwæt swa ge biddað on minum naman gelefeð þæt ge hit sculon
underfon and hit geweorð eow.
 142. Blissiað and fægniað nu forþon þe we hæbbeð nu
underfangen þæt þæt we æt drihtne gebædon and þis is se ilca
þe ge ymbe biddende wæron.
 144. And eal swa heo hine geseawen þa heroden hi ealle mid hludre
stæmne þæs hæl nama and wuldrodon on his mycclan mildheortnesse.
 146. Biscopes wæron glæde forþon þe hi mosten begeton
swylcne gefera.
 147. Gereces fahnedon forþon þe god swilcne heorde heom geunnen
hæfde.
 148. Hwæt wæs þær þa mare buton þæt hi setton
hine on þone bisceopstol his unþances and he hit lange wiðsoc ac swa
þeah hio bædon him swa lange þæt he heom þæs geteogðode and
þone bisceopdom underfeng.
 150. Eornostlice æfter þan þe he bisceop wæs geworðen
and hæfde þone wurðment on hande, þa wunede he swa þeah æfre
forð on his micclan eadmodnesse and on þære ilcan godnesse þe he ær
wæs to gewunod.
 153. He wacode gelome on his gebedum and his licchame he gepinode
mid fæstenum.
 154. Glædlice he lærde menn to gode weorce and eadmodlice he
underfeng þearfan widewan and stipcildum and ealle þa þe mid
earfoðnesse wæron geswæncte he besorgode and healp heom eal swa hit
his agen neode wære.
 157. Ricum monnum he lærde þæt heo earmum mannum nan þing
mid unrihte ne benamen gif he gesawe ænige mann befeallen on ænige
ungelympe he gebette sona his uneðnesse and hine mildheortlice gefrefrode.
 160. Ðus weox his godnesse dæghwamlice mare and mare and ealle
men blissoden of swa gode biscope and drihten hine gestrangode on manigfealdum
mihtum.
 162. Ða wearð he swa mære and swa wurðfull þurh godes
wille þæt he mihte gebetan ælces mannes sarignesse wære on lande
wære on sæ and he cleopode þone halgan him to fultume þær rihte he
hine alesde of ealre his gedræfodnesse.
 164. Ða gelamp hit on sumere tide þæt sume scipmenn wurdon
swiðe færlice bestandene ut on þære sæ mid swa micclan storme
þæt hi wendon þær rihtes ealle adrincan.
 167. Eac hi wæron mid swa micclan cele fornumene þæt hi ne
mihton nan þinge heoras selfos geweldon and eal swa hi wæron on swa
micclan earfoðnesse þa cleopoden hi ealle mid hludre stæmne and þus
wæron cweþende, Eale þu godes þeo nicholae gif þa þinge syndon
soþe þe we ymbe geherd habbað, gecyð hit nu on us þæt we moton
gode þancian and þe ures lifes alesednesse.
 171. Witodlice onmang þam þe hi þus cleopoden þa ateowde
heom an man and cwæð to heom, Ic com her forþon þe ge me cleopoden and
þærrihtes he ongan heom to helpane on rapum and on mæstum and on þam
oðrum sciptauum swilce he wære an of heom.
 175. Ða næs hit naht lange æfter þam þæt eall se
steorm feoll and seo sæ wearð liþe and milde þurh heora sceppendes
bebodu and þa scipmen hreowen þa forð mid micelre blisse and comon þa
hrædlice to þæra ilcan hæfene þe heo to woldon and eal swa hio
wæron gegan upp on þæt land þa axode hi hwær se godes þegn
wære nicolaus.
 179. Heom wearð þa gecydd þæt he wære innan circan and
heo þæs godes þancoden and eode þider inn.
 180. Soðlice hi ne gecniwen hine næfre ær and swa þeah hi
gecneowen hine swa hraðe swa hi hine gesawen innen þære cirice buton
ælces mannes tæce.
 182. Heo feollan þa to þæs halgan fotum and ongunnon ealle
to weponne for fagennesse and þancedon him swiðe inweardlice þæt hi
wurþon þurh his helpe of deaþe alesde and tealdon him eall hu heom wæs
gelumpon on þære sæ.
 185. Ða cweþ se eadiga wer to heom, Leofe broðra ne wene ge
na þæt hit swa gewurðe þurh mine mihte ac god þurh his gewunelicere
miltse eow alesde for þam godum geleafan þe ge to him hæfdon.
 187. Soðlice dæghwamlice we beoð gesweinte for urum synnum
and swa þeah gif we gecerran willað mid ealre mægne to ure mildheortan
drihtene, sone he us gemiltsað and alest of eallum þan yfelum þe us an
becymð.
 190. And forþon leofe broðra ne wandige naht wel to donne,
eadmodnesse to folgienne and wreccum mannum bliðelice to helponne and
gelefeð hu mycel mægn hæfð clæne geleafa and soþa gebedu to
drihtene.
 193. Witodlice ure ealdefæder adam siððan he wæs geworpen
ut of paradyse for his misdæda into þisum middanearde, nis nan þincg
gode swa gecweme swa him is ælmessa, gif man hit ne deð na for þisra
worulda wuldra.
 196. Ðus eadmodlice tihte se halige wer heo to gode weard and let
hio siððan fram him gewændan mid his bletsunge.
 197. Eft hit gelamp þurh godes forsceawunge þæt mycel hunger
wearð on þan lande þe se halige wer onwunode forþon þe þæt
ungeleaffulle folc nolde geheran þam rihtan geleafan þe se eadiga nicolaus
heom wæs symle tæcende.
 200. Soðlice forþon þæt ofteah se ælmihtiga god heom
heora corn and eac ealle oðre goda swa þæt hi nan þingc næfdon of
hwan hi libben mihton.
 202. Ða wearð þær micel unrotnesse betwuxan þan folce
and comon þa rædlice and gesohten þas halgenes fet and bæden hine
swiðe inweardlice þæt he heom to drihten geþingode.
 204. Ða andwyrde se godes man and cweþ þæt he wolde heom
fore þingian gif hi wolden lufian heora drihten of ealra heortan.
 205. Hi cwæden þa mid wependre stæmne þæt hi wolden
healdon ealle þa þing þe drihtene licwurðe wæron.
 207. Hwæt þa se godes deorling nicolaus eode into drihtenes
temple and gebæd swiðe geornlice for þæt earme folc and þurhwunode
þa swa lange on his gebedum þæt man com and cydde him þæt þær
wære gecumene wel manega scipes up æt þære hæfene þe is
gecleopod adriaticum and þa wæron wel gehladone mid hwæte.
 210. Ða se godes man þis geherde he eode þa swiftlice þider
and þus cweþ to þam scipmannum, Eale ge godes freond tyðið me ane
bene þe ic wille bidden æt eow.
 212. Hi andwyrdon and cwædon þæt hi wolde þæt
bliðelice don.
 213. Se halige wer cweþ, ðis landfolc is wel neh dead of hungre
and ic com nu hider forþan þæt ic wolde biddan æt eow sumne fultum of
eowre corne þæt þis earme folc mid ealle ne forwurðe.
 215. Hi andwyrdon and cwædon, Eala þu arwurþe fæder ne
durre we na wanian þirne hwæte forþon þe me hine mæt swiðe
nærulice us an hand æt alexandria and we hine sculon eal swa nærulice
ongemeten þæs caseres þening mannum.
 218. Ða cweþ se biscop eft, Leofe gebroðra gyþiað me huru
of æghwilce scipe an hundred gemitte hwæte gif ge na mare nelleð
þæt þis earme folc furþor ne losige and ic behate eow fullice þurh
mines drihtnes gife þæt ge næfre þe læsse ne sculon habben þonne
ge ham cumað and hine betæcen ongean sculon.
 222. Witodlice eal swa þa scipmen þis geherdon hi wæron
swiðe ofwundredo and þohten hwæþer hit æfre swa mihte gewurþen
and æt læsten him gelefdon and getyðedon him þæs þe he to heom
gewilnedo.
 224. Hi mætan him þa upp of æghwilcum scipe an hundred
mitte/ hwætes and eal swa hraðe swa þæt wæs gedon swa heom com god
weder and mid spedigum winde segledon ham to constantinopole.
 226. Soðlice eal swa heo ham wæren gecumene þa mæten hi
þæt corn ut of heora scipen eal swa hi hit underfengon æt alexandrian,
þa fundon hi hit eal swa fullice swilc þær an corn nære fram gedon.
 229. Hi ongunnon þa ealle to wepenne for fægennesse and
tealdon þa eal þæs caseres mannum hu hit wæs geworden and eal swa heo
þæt geherdon, þa ongunnon hi ealle gode to herigenne mid mænigfealdum
blitsungum, Eale hu wunderlic þingc we geherdon nu of þisum corne ac mare
wunder gewurð of þam dæle þe mid þam halgan were belæfde.
 233. Soðlice se arwurþe nicolaus todælde þæt corn þe
he begeoten hæfde ælc man be þan þe ne neode hæfde and se
ælmihtiga god ge manifylte þæt litle corn swa swiðe on his handum
þæt eall þæt landfolc hæfdon genoh ofer eall þæt gear and eac
hi seowan heora land of þan ilcan corne and hit weox heom to manigfealdum
wæstmum.
 237. Witodlice he nolde geþafigen þæt ænig hæþengeld
wære gewurðed on þære scire licia, siððen he wærð gehalgod
to biscope ac he todræfde eall þæs deofles weorc.
 239. He afligde ut of his biscoprice ealle þa hæþena godes
and ealle þa drymen and þa wiccen þe he æfre of axian mihte.
 240. Eac heafyrsede þa scandfulla gydena diana of þam lande and
eall hire wurðment he todræfde mid his drihtenes fultume.
 242. Þa wearð se deofol swiðe yrre ongean þan halgan were
nicolae and þohte fela yfela þing ongean his deorwurða geswince þe he
symle geswanc for his drihtnes gewillan.
 244. Soðlice he ne swa næfre to swincenne ymbe þæt earme
folc þe se awergode gast hæfde fæste begripan oðþæt he hi alesde
of þæs deofles anwealde and forþon he þohte þa sum þingc yfeles
ongean þan godes þegne.
 246. Ða com se deofol on anre nihte to sumum dreomen þa
wæron swiðlice gelærde on eallum yfelum dædum and het heom þæt
hi sceoldon hwætlice gearwian ane cynnes ele þe is gecleopod mediacon.
 249. Soðlice þæt ilce ele is swa mihtig and swa strange
þæt swa hwæt swa hit on tæcþ þærrihtes hit eall
forbærnð.
 250. Ða drymenn dydon þa eal swa se scocca heom bebead,
gearwedon þa rædlice þæt ele and betæhte hit þan deofle and se
deofol hine þa selfne gehiwode swylce he an eald wif wære and for in to
þære sæ and com rowende on anum bate to sumum scipfull mannum þe
wolden secan þæt haligum mynster þæs halgan nicholaes mid heora
ælmessan.
 254. Se scucca for eac swa litellice eac þider faren wolde and
cweþ þus to heom, Leofa broðra ic geseo þæt ge fundiað toward
þam hlaforde nicolae and ic eac earme wrecce wolde faran mid eow þider and
his bletsunge hæbban gif ic nu mihte, ac me strent nu oþer neode an
þæt ic æt þisum ceare ne faran.
 258. Nu hæbbe ic her an litel ele þæt ic wolde þær
mide lacnian þam godes freond forþon þe min geþanc is swiðe mycel to
him weard and ic bidde eow leofe freond þæt ge bringan þis litle lac to
his mynstre and smyriað þa wages eall onbuton þær mide on mine
gemynde.
 262. Ða scipmen andwyrdon and sædon þæt hi wolden
þæt bliðelice don.
 263. Se scucce þærrihtes betæhte þæt manfulle ele and
hreow fram heom and rædlice aðwan of heore gesibbe.
 264. Soðlice þa scipmen ne cuþon nan þingc of þan facne
ac reowan heom forðwærd swa swa heo ær dydon mid mycelre bilehwitnesse
and þa þa heo ane litle hwile gerowen hæfdon þa gesawen heo færlice
an scipful manna þa wæron swiðe fægre gehiwode and on middan heom
eallum sæt an man swiðe gelic nicolao se ongan heom sona to acsigenne and
þus cweþ, Eale ge goda men hwæt wæs þæt wif þe litle ær
spræc þus to eow.
 269. Ða men him þærrihtes tealden hwæt heo spræc to
heom and hwæt heom betæht hæfde and ateowden heom eac þæt ele.
 270. And he cweþ eft to heom, Witodlice þæt wif þe spæc
þus to eow þæt wæs seo unseofulle gydena diana and gif ge willað
witen hwæt se ele is þe hi eow on hande sealde, þonne awyrpe ge hit nu
rædlice fram eow ut into þære sæ.
 273. Hi dydon þa hwætlice eal swa heom getæht wæs and
sona swa þæt ele toc on þæt wæter, þa aras þær upp swiðe
mycel fyr and seo sæ bærnde lange hwile.
 275. Soðlice þæt wæs ongean rihtum gecynde.
 275. And eal swa þa scipmenn þæt wunder beheoldan, þa
wurdan þa scype swa fyr totwæmde ægþer fram oðren þæt heo ne
mihton of cleopigen þa oðre menn ne eac of axien hwæt he wære se þe
wið heom spæc.
 278. Ac ferde þa forð al swa heo ær gemynt hæfdon and
eallum þan mannum þe heo gemetton hi tealdon hu heom gelumpan wæs.
 279. Eac þa þa heo comon to þam godes þeowe nicolaus þa
cwæden hi ealle on anre stefne to him, Soðlice þu eart se mann þe us
ateowdest þæt tacen innen þære sæ.
 281. Soðlice þu eart riht godes þeow and fon þinre godra
geearnunga we wurdon alesde fram þæs deofles costnunge and þa þa hi
þus hæfdon gesæd þa tealdon hi him eall be endebyrdnesse hu heom
gelumpon wæs.
 284. Ða se eadiga nicolaus þas þincg geherd hæfde, þa
ongan he gode to herigenne eal swa his gewune wæs and lærde þa men
þæt heo geornlice heo selfe gode betæhten and he geaf heom his
bletsunge and hi foran þa mid bliðum mode fram him to heora agena
æþele.
 287. Þa gelamp hit rædlice æfter þon þæt an scipfolc
þe is gecleopod attraiphala wearð swiðe wiðerweard ongean þam casere
constantino and swa modige þæt hi noldon gedon him nan þære
gehersumnesse þe ealle oðre þeoda dydon ac æfre wiðcwædan his
healice bebodu.
 290. Witodlice eal swa se casere þis geherde þa het he beodan
ut micel scipferda and bebead his þreom þegnum þære nama wæron
þus geclypode nepotianus, ursus, arrilatio, þæt heo foran to þan lande
frigian and steordan þæt folc þe wæs wiðerweard ongean god and
ongean him.
 293. Hi dydan þa eal swa se casere heom bebead and eal swa
þæt scipferde wæs eal gegaderod, þa ferdon hio forð on þa sæ
and hæfde swiðe god weder and fægre sæ on to færenne.
 295. Ac þa þa hi comon to þære sæ þe is wið þam
lande þe se hlaford nicolaus onwunode þa weox swa strang wind ongean heom
þæt hi na furþor ne mihton ac wurþen gedrifene into þære
hæfene adriaticum heora unþances and eodon upp on þæt land.
 298. Sume hi eodon þa to þæt ceapstowe and bereafoden
þær þæt landfolc and eal swa heo þæt unriht dydon, þa wearð
hit hrædlice gecydd þan godes men nicolao þanon ofer þreom milen innan
þære burh patera.
 300. Soðlice eal swa hraðe swa he þis geherde, þa eode he
swiðe efstlice and gecneow þær þæs caseres þry dirlingas
nepotianum and ursum and arpilatium and cyste heo and þus cweþ, Leofa
broðra hwæðer come ge hider mid sibbe oððe to gefeohte, hi
andwyrdon, Hlaford mid sibbe we comon hider ac we sculen faren to frigiam on
þæs caseres ærnde and gebygen þæt wiðerwearde folc to him mid
godes fylste and mid þinen, ac we ne magon nu na furðar forþon þe
strancg wind us hæfð hider gewrecan.
 306. Nu bidde we þe leofe fæder þæt þu us fultumige mid
þinum gebedum þæt we þas þincg to wurðlican ende gebringan moton.
 308. Se godes man bæd heom þa swiðe eadmodlice þæt hio
sceoldan gesteoran heora cnihtan fram ælcere saca and ferdon siððan mid
him to þære burh patera þæt hi his bledsunge þær underfengon.
 310. Ða þreo þegnes dydon þa rædlice eal swa se biscop
heom bebæd, forbudon þæt geflit and dyden þæt ælc man hæfde
his agen æhte.
 311. Witodlice eal swa þis wæs þus gedon, þa comon sume
menn þær to þam biscope and sædon þus to him, Hlaford biscop geond
me læt þry iunga menn to slege and eal þæt folc sarlice bemænð
þæt þu þær ne eart for þon gif þu þær wære þonne
noldest þu naht geþafian þæt hit swa gewurðe.
 315. Soðlice heora deað is deorlice geboht æt þam aldormen
and hi bið gedemde to deaðe butan ælcen gylte.
 316. Ða se eadiga nicolaus þis unriht geherde þa bæd he
þam þrim þegnum þæt hi sceoldan gan mid him þider and hi swa dydon
and eal swa hi comon wiðinnan þære burh to anum stede se is geclypod
leonthi, þa axode se bisceop hwæþer þa þreo iunge menn leofedon þa
get, þe wæron fordemde to deaðe.
 319. Ða burhmen him andsweroden and þus cwædon, Efst nu
arwurðe fæder swiðe forþan mid godes fylste þu finst heo get
libbende on dioscheres stræte.
 321. Se biscop and þa þegnes urnen þa swiðe efstlice
þiderweard and eal swa hio comon to þære stræte þær þe hi
wæron þa wæron hi gelæde þanon.
 323. Se godes man axode eft hwider hi wæron gelædde and me
him andswarode, Hlaford nu me hi lædað ut æt þære portgate and swa
forð to þære cwealmstowe þe is geclypod bisrand.
 325. Ða se halige wer þæt geherde þa ongan he eft swiðe
to eornenne þeah þe he werig wære and eal swa he com to þære
cwealmstowe, þa geseah he þa iunge men sittan on heora cneowan and heora
eahne wæron gebundene and se cwellere stod mid agotenum swurde ofer heora
bara sweora.
 329. Hwæt þa se godes deorling nicolaus arn swiðe deorflice
uppan þam cwellere and abræd þæt nacode swurd of his handum and
bæd þæt he scolde hine ofslean for heom.
 330. Soðlice nan þam cwellere ne dorste an word cleopigen
ongean his willan forþon þe hi wysten ful wel þæt he wæs swiðe
licwurðe þam ælmihtigan gode.
 332. Se biscop unband þa rædlice þa iunglinges and
gelædde hi forð mid him and eal þæt folc him æfterfolgoden
oððæt hi becomen to þæs ealdormannes botlan eustachii se þe
hæfde ær fordemed þa þreo iunglinges to deaðe.
 335. And eal swa se ealdorman geseah þone bisceop, þa eode he
swiðe efstlice ongean him and gegrette hine, ac se bisceop nolde underfangen
his gretunge ac cweþ þus to him mid mycelre wræððe, Eale þu godes
feond hu dærst þu besceawien on minne andwlite þe þus micel yfel
hæfst gefremed.
 338. Eala þu wealbreowesta mann ælces godes ungemyndig for hwi
ne þohtest þu hwæt þæt halige writt us bebytt þæt we ne sculon
na fordemen rihtwise menn to deaðe.
 340. Se eorl eustachi him andwyrde and cweþ, Hlaford for hwi
þreatest þu me þus swiðe soðlice ic nam naht swa scyldig of þisum
gylte swa beoð þas burhgerefan symonides and eudoxi forþon þe heo bið
æfre geare men to acwellene.
 343. Ða cweþ se eadiga nicholaus, Eala þu gitsere and ealra
manne forcuðost, ic wat ful wel þæt symonides ne eudoxi ne neddan þe
þæt þu þas unsceaðie iunglingles to deaðe fordemdest ac þu self
heo beleawdest to deaðe þurh þinre micelan grædignesse þe þu
hæfst to golde and to selfre.
 346. Soðlice ic secge þe þæt hit sceal beon gecydd þam
casere hu þu todælst his cynerice and hu þu selst unscyldigum in to
deaðe and hu þu forstelst his gold and his seolfer and ealne þone
wurðment þe he self hæbben sceolde and æfter þon þe he þis
unriht hæfð geherd he sceal niman rihte lage of þe.
 350. Ða se eorl eustachi þas strange spæce geherde, þa
bæd he nepotianum and ursum and arpilatien þæt heo geþingoden him to
þam biscope and hi þa swa dydon mid ealre geornfulnesse.
 352. Hwæt þa se godes mann wearð gefrefrod mid þæs
halgan gastes gife and ealle his wræððe þærrihtes niðer alegde
and for þære þegna bene he forgeaf þan eorle eustachio eall þone
gylt.
 354. Soðlice æfter þisum eode se biscop ham to þære
burh patera and þa þreo þegnas æton and druncon þær mid him and
æfter þære gereordunge he gebletsode heo and swa mid his halgan
bletsunge heo him fram gewændon.
 357. Hi foran þa mid bliðum mode to heora scipe and se eadiga
nicholaus bæd for heom to drihtene þæt hi moston sundfullice becuman to
þam lande frigiam.
 359. Eac he bæd swiðe inweardlice for þæt dysige folc
þe wunedo on frigiam þæt god sceolde awænde heora mod to his willan
and drihten geherde mildelice his bene and ageaf þan þrim þegnan gode
gewyderu and hi segledan forð mid spedigum winde oððæt hi becomen into
frigiam mid eallum þæs caseres here and eal swa raðe swa þæt
landfolc þis geherde, þa sændon hi hire bodan to þam þreom þegnum
and cydde heom þæt hi woldon hersumian þam casere eal swa oðre þeode
dydon.
 364. Ða þa nepotianus and ursus and arpilatio þis geherdon
þa wæron hi swiðe bliðe and þæs gode þancodon and þan halgan
nicolao þe heom hæfde to drihtene swa mildelice geþingod.
 366. Hi foran þa ofer eall þæt land mid fullan griðe and
nænne man ne ofslogen ac geheoldon heore hande ungewæmede wiðutan
ælce blodgyte.
 368. Hi tobræcen ealle hæþengeldas and mid fyre
forbærnden and upp arærdon godes lof and bebuden þam folce þæt hi
fullice forsocen þone deofol and eall his weorc and gode geoffrodon
licwurðe lac and hi dydon eal swa heom beboden wæs.
 371. Witodlice eall swa þa þreo þegnas hæfdon geseoc
þæt land swa swa hi hit hæbban wolden to þæs caseres wurðscipe,
þa gewænton hi ongean to constantinopole and sona swa se casere constantin
geherde þæt hi þær neh wæron þa eode he ut of þære burh mid
micclan folce ongean nepotianum and ursum and arpilationem and underfeng hio
mid micclan wurðscipe.
 375. Se casere gewurðedo hi þa swiðe and gelufedo hio swylce
hi his agene cild wæron and eall þæt folc blissode for heora sige and
eac þe swiðer þæt hi næfdon þær nænne mann ofslagen.
 377. Ða wæron þær sume yfele geþancode menn þa þe
hæfdon micelne nið ongean þa þri þegnes and þohten swiðe
geornlice hu hi mihton heora wurðscipe gelitlian and hi mid ealle fordon.
 379. Hi eodon þa on sumum dæge to þam aldormenn ablaium se
wæs hegost and mihtigost under þan casere and ongunnon hi to wregenne mid
manegum leasungum and æt læste hi sædon on heom þæt hi wæron
ymbe þes caseres swicdome and þæt sceolde hrædlice wurðon cuð
eallum mannum.
 383. Ða se aldormann ablaui þis geherde he wearð swiðe
ofwundrad and heom naht ne gelefde.
 384. Hi noldon swa þeah forlæton heora yfelnesse ac budon him
gold and seolfor and feola oðra gersumen and gewænton hine swa to heora
manfulnesse and to þæra unsceaðira manna swicdome.
 386. Ablaui eode þa into þan casere swilce he swiðe sarig
wære and þus cweþ to him, Eale þu min deorewurðe hlaford, warne þe
nu rædlice wið þine þreom þegnum þe þu sædest on þinre
ærnde to frigiam.
 389. Soðlice hi þænceð dæg and niht ymbe þinne
swicdom and hio behateþ micelne rice ælc þære manne þe heom
þær to fultumian willað.
 390. Ða cwæþ se casere, Be hwan wast þu hit swa
soðlice.
 391. Se manfulle ablauius cwæþ, Hlaford ic hit geherde of
heora agenum mannum on niht þær þær hi hit stillice runedon betweoxen
heom.
 393. Hwæt se casere him soðlice gelefde eal swa his eldestum
and deorwurðestan mannum and het þa rædlice nimen nepotianum and ursum
and arpilationem wiðuton ælce gylte and on cwærterne bescufan and
þær inne fæste belucen and hit wearð þa swa gedon.
 396. Soðlice eall swa þa forsædon wregeres geaxoden þæt
þa þegnes wæron gesette on quarterne and næron þa gett ofslagene,
þa wæron hi swiðe sarige and comon eft rædlice to þam man fullum
ablauium and brohten him micelne lac and þus cwæðon to him, Hlaford for
hwi leton gelibben eowre fynd swa lange þæt hi næron þærihtes
ofslagone, wende ge þæt ge mihton þus godne ende don on heom buton ge hi
mid ealle ofslogen.
 401. Soðlice buton hio þæraðor wurðon fordon, hit eow
sceal sare hreowan and þonne ge læst wenað ge sculon wurðon
beswicone.
 403. Ða wearð ablaui swiðe yrre and eode to þan casere and
him þus to cweþ, Hlaford þa þreo cnihtes þe þu hete don inn to
þam cwarterne, hy nelleð get swa þeah forlæton heora unræd ac
wændeð swiðe geornlice dæges and nihtes to heora rædgifen and
biddað þæt heo on þe færlice behræson and þe ofslean.
 406. Hwæt þa se casere wærð swa yrre swilce he his agene
deað ætforen him geseage and het þa rædlice ac wellan þa þreo
unsceadige cnihtes.
 408. Ða se ablaui þis wunder geherde þa wearð he swiðe
bliðe and sænde to hylarianum þe bewiste þæt cwarterne and het him
þæt he hæfde geare þa þri cnihtes onsundrig fram oðrum mannum
þæt he hio þæs oðres nihtes dearnelice ofslean mihte.
 411. Witodlice eal swa hilarian þis geherde, þa wearð he
swiðe sarig and arn toforen to þam cwarterne and cweþ to þan cnihtum
mid micclum wope, Wala wa þæt ic eow æfre geseah.
 413. Wala wa þæt we sculen todæg beon swa sarlice
gesundrode.
 414. Ða axoden heo for hwan hio swa spæcon.
 414. Hylarian heom andwyrde and cweþ þæt þær wæs
færlice gecuman wæs fram þam casere þæt heo sceolden beon
ofslagene þæs ilcan nihtes and forþan ic bidde eow þæt ge
forestihten eowre þinge þa hwile þe ge first hæbbeð þe læs ge
willeð þonne ge ne magon.
 417. Soðlice gimerunge, Wala wa hwa geherde grimlicne cwide
geherden, þa cwædon hi mid micelre gimerunge, Wala wa hwa geherde æfre
þus mycele grimnesse þæt we sculon nu sweltan eal swa utlages and
þæt we ne moton nanre ladunge beon wurðe.
 420. Ða onmang þæt heo swa sarig wæron,þa beþohte
nepotian se æþela cniht hu se eadiga nicolaus alesde þa þrio iunge
cnihtes fram þara manne hande þe heo ofslean woldon.
 422. And eal swa he þis beþohte þa gebæd he hine to
drihtene mid wepindre stæmne and þus cweþ, Hlaford crist, help us
earmingum and geher ure bene for sæintes nicolaes geearnunga þines
þeowen and ales us fram þes swurdes ecge eal swa þu alesdest þa þreo
cnihtes for his lufan æt patera þære burh þær þer þe we on
loceden.
 426. Drihten we gelefað soðlice þeah þin þeowa her ne be
lichamlice mid us swa þeah he mæg beon gastlice swa hwær swa he wile
and þurh þinre gife he mæg helpan eallum þan þe him to cleopieð
mid godre heorte and þu hlaford god help us nu þurh his bene.
 429. Ðus bæd nepotian him to gode and begen his geferan forð
mid him and æfre hio cleopoden mid wependre stæmne þus cweþende,
Hlaford sancte nicolae help us and geteoðe us þæt we þe gett geseon
moton and þine halige fett cyssen.
 432. Ða gelamp hit on þære oðre niht þæt se casere
and ablaui gesawen begen ane gesihðe on swefone.
 433. Ðam casere þuhte þæt se eadige nicolaus come to him
and þus wæs cweþende, Constantine for hwi hete þu don þa þri
unsceadige men on cwarterne and heo to deaðe fordemdest.
 435. Aris nu rædlice and hat heo alesan.
 435. And gif þu elles dest and me swa forsihst ic bidde þone
heofonlicen casere þæt he arære uppon þe micel gefeoht and læton
þe þær beon ofslagen and agifen þin flæsc deorum and fugelum.
 437. Ða cweþ se casere, Hwæt eart þu swa dyrstig mann
þæt þu come nu into me on þisum tune and me swa openlice
geþreatest.
 439. Ic eom se synfulle nicolaus erchebisceop on mirren and mid
þisum wordum he gewænte to ablauium and him þus to cweþ, ðu witlease
mann hwilc neod wæs þe þæt þu forwregdest þa þreo unsceadige
cnihtes to deaðe.
 441. Aris nu rædlice and do þæt me heo læte ut of þan
cwærterne and gif þu þus ne dest ic bidde þone heofonlicne cyninge
þæt he læte þinne lichame wyrmum to mete and eallum þam mannum þe
þe to langiað sculon eac sweltan on sarlicum deaðe.
 444. Ablaui cweþ mid dreorigum mode, Hwæt eart þu þe me
þus openlice þreast.
 445. He cweþ, Ic eom nicolaus archebisceop of mirrea and mid
þam ilcan worde he gewænde fram him.
 446. Soðlice æfter þisum wearð se casere aweht and se
manfulle ablaui eal swa and heora ægþer oðrum his swefen rædlice
arehte and sona swa hit dæg wæs, þa het se casere lædan þa þreo
cnihtes ut of þam cwarterne and hit wearð þa swa gedon.
 448. Hi wurdon þa rædlice gebrohte ætforan þam casere and
eal swa heo he geseah þa cweþ he to heom mid mycelre wræððre.
 450. Secgeð me mid hwilcum wiccecræfte ge swægnten us to
niht on swefene.
 451. Witodlice eal swa heo þas spæce geherdon þa wæron
heo swiðe ofwundrode and ne geafon him nan andswære.
 452. Se casere cweþ eft, Geopeniað us eowre drycræftes.
 453. Nepotian þa andwyrde ane for heom eallum and þus cweþ,
Hlaford constantine to soðan þinge we þe secgað þæt we nane
wiccecræftes ne cunnon ne næfre nane ne geleornedon.
 455. Eac we nabbað geworht nan þære gylte ongean þe ne
ongean þinum folce þæt we sceolden fore deaðes sweltan.
 456. Se casere cweþ, Cunne ge ænigne mann þe hatte
nicolaus.
 457. Soðlice eal swa hraðe swa hi geherdan næmnian nicolaum
swa hio ahofen upp heora handa and mid hludre stefne cwædan, Gebletsod si
þu drihten þu þe helpst eallum þam þe on þe fæstlice gelefað,
þu help us eac nu and ales us of þeosum leasungum þurh þines þeowan
gearnunge nicolaes.
 460. Eal swa þu hulpe þam þreom iunglingan on ure gesihðe.
 461. Se casere heo gestilde þa and het heo openlice secgan
hwæt heo mænden and hwæt se nicolaus wære.
 462. Ða ongan nepotian to tellanne þam casere eall be þan
halegan nicolao hu hi comon to him and hu he þa iunge cnihtes alesde of
deaðe and hu bilehwit man he wæs on godnesse and hu heo ealle þa niht to
him cleopoden and hu mildheortlice he hæfde heom þa geholpen.
 466. Hwæt þa se casere wearð swiðe ofwundrod eal swa he
þas spæce geherde and cweþ to heom, Farað nu rædlice to þan godes
þeowa and þanciað him and eac gode þe eow þurh hine alesde and
bringað him þas lac of minre healfe to cristes þenunge.
 468. Ðæt wæron twegen gyldene candelsticcan and ænne
gyldene hnæpp mid þan deorcynnestum gymmum gefrætwod and ane cristes
boc eal besmided mid deorwurðan golde and mid gimstanum gesett and his
gewritt forð mid þan lace biddende þam godes menn þæt he hi
gemiltsode to þam þæt he him æfre ma gehersumian wolde and for him to
drihtne gebiddan and for his rices sundfulnesse.
 473. Heo dydon þa eal swa se casere heom bebead foren to þan
hlaforde nicolaum and sona swa heo hine gesegen heo feollan niðer to
þære eorðan and cysten his fett mid micclan wope and þus wæron
cweðende, Eale þu godes freond nicolae, soðlice þu eart to herigenne of
ealre manne muðe forþon þe þu eart ealre manne helpind on sæ and on
lande.
 476. Soðlice þurh þe we sind alesde fram deaðe to life.
 477. Heo tealdon him þa eall be endebyrdnesse hu hie hæfdon
gefaren and geafon him þæs caseres lac and his gewrit and eal swa he þis
geherde and geseah, þa hof he upp his handa to heofonum and ongan to
herigenne gode þus cweþende, Micel eart þu hlaford god and micel is þin
mihte and þin wisdom næfð nan getæl.
 481. Ðu eart welig on eallum þingum and þu ane eart ealre
manne heorte.
 482. Soðlice eal swa he þas þinge gesæd hæfde þa
bewende he hine to þam þrim cnihtum and bodedu heom lange stunde ymbe godes
rice and lærde heo hu heo sceolden dæla heora æhte þærfum and hu
hio sceolden libben heora lif on þissere worulde.
 485. Hwæt þa butan eal swa se eadiga wer hæfde his spæce
geendod,þa let he heo badian and sceran of heora side locces þe heom
wæron ongewexane innan þan cweartne and scydde heo siððan eall mid
niwen scrude and het heo þa faren ongean mid sibbe to þam casere
constantine.
 488. Ða cnihtes dyden þa eal swa se godes inan heom
bebead,foran þa ongean to þære burh constantinopolim blitsigende on
drihtene and on þone halgan nicolae.
