LS 34 (SevenSleepers)
B3.3.34.
Seven Sleepers: Skeat 1881-1900, I, 488-540.



 1. <foreign>DE SEPTEM DORMIENTIBUS</foreign>.
 1. Her efne onginð þæra eadigra seofon slæpera
ðrowung, ðara haligra naman scinað on heofenum, lihtað eac on eorðan
beorhte mid Cristenum mannum.
 3. Ðara is se forma his geferena heretoga Maximianus, ðærto
se oþer Malchus, se geþensuma, and se ðridda þærto Martinianus,
þonne se feorða Dionisius, se halga Iohannes fifta, þonne ðæs sixtan
Seraphion nama is, æt nextan ðæs seofeþan Constantinus.
 7. Ðara seofen haligra freolstid bið on geare fif nihton ær
hlafmæssan.
 8. On ðam gefyrn gewitenan ðære mycelan ehtnysse timan, þa
ða hæðenan mann Cristendomes leoman mid ealle adwæscan woldon, and
ælcne myne ofer eorðan adylgian, and þa ða eadigan martyras for his
naman mænigfealde earfoðnyssa ðafedon.
 12. Ða Decius se þweora heold rice ofer eall Romana rice, and
him for ðissere worulde wel on hand eode þæt he Godes þa gecorenan
witnode, and hi on yrmðum getintregode, and hi buton gewande getucude eall
swa he wolde; ða gelamp hit æt sumum cyrre þæt he ferde into anre
byrig þe man Constantinopolim nemneð, seo wæs heafodburh on Greclande,
and of ðære he for into Cartagine, and ðanon into Efese.
 19. Ða he ða þreo burga gefaren hæfde, ða het gelangian
him to swiðe hraðe ealle ða burhwara togædere, cwæð þæt he
gemot wið hi habban wolde.
 21. Sona swa hi þæt geaxodon ða þe on God belyfdon, ða
wurdon hi ealle ðearle afyrhte, and heora gesomnunga ealle wurdon sona
tosceacerode and þa halgan sacerdas and ealle ða godan færlice geyrmde
hreowlice wurdon.
 25. He þa, Decius se casere, þa he for into Efese mid ðrymme
and mid prasse, he ða his heortan ahof swa upp ofer his mæðe swilce he
God wære.
 27. Ongan ða timbrian deofolgyld on cirican, and bead þæt
mid him ðærrihte ælc man be his heafde deofle sceolde offrian; and
gehwa dyde swa for ðæs caseres ege, and elles ne dorston; ac ælc hine
sylfne on lichaman and on sawle mid þam hæþengylde earmlice gefylde.
 32. Ðær ðær ænig deofolgyld wæs aræred, eall seo
burhwaru fram dæge to dæge be ðæs caseres bebode com togædere,
and man sloh ðær hryðera and gehwilces cynnes nytenu, and ðær geond
eall ða hæþenan byrnende gleda streawodon, and ðæronuppan deofle
offrodon, and ða þicnyssa smices and ða bræðas ðæs flæsces
stigon upp on ælce healfe geond þa byrig eall swilc hit mist wære,
þæt man nan þincg forneah ðær geseon ne mihte buton smic ænne.
 39. And þonne ða hæþenan on swilcon deofolscinne
blissedon, ðonne weopon and geomredon þa þe on God belyfdon, and hi on
ðære mæstan dreorignysse wunedon þæt hi mid heora eagum swilce
yrmða æfre geseon sceoldon swilce hi ðær gesawon, þæt æfre on
mancynne swa mycelne anweald deofol habban sceolde.
 44. Ne hi niston hwæt hi his dydon, ne hi na mare don ne mihton
buton bitere tearas hi symle aleton and hnipiende eodon, and hi sylfe behyddon
þær þær hi mihton.
 47. Ac færlice ymbe ðreo niht sende se casere his bydelas and
bead þæt man swiðe georne sceolde cepan Cristenra manna, and gehwa
þær he mihte heora be feore hente, and gif man ahwer ofaxian mihte
þæt hi manna ænig on genere heolde þæt se wære his heafdes
scyldig, and se þe hi ameldode þæt se wære mycelre mede wyrðe.
 52. Hi ða, þa bydelas and feala oðre, eall swa hi to ðam
sceatte hopedon, ferdon and sohton swa hwær swa hi mihton findan þa
Cristenan menn, and hu hi mihton ðam casere gecweman þæt hi sumne sceatt
æt him gelæhton; and hi ða hæþenan men þonne hi Cristene men
ahwær fundon, hi hi ut drifon, and him beforan feredon swilce lytle
gærstapan, and to ðam folce læddon ðær ealle men hæðengyld
mid ðam casere wurðedon, and þa Cristenan nyddon þæt hi mid heom
deofle on hand gangan sceoldon, and hi sume swa dydon, swa heom earme þa
gelamp, ða þa hi gesawon swa mænigfealde ogan on mistlicum witum, ða
wurdon hi sona ungeheorte and feollon adune astrehte, and deofle offredon
beforan eallum ðam folce swa him æfre se sið hreowan mihte; and þa
oðre Cristenan þe ðær gehydde wæron þa hi swilce yrmða
gehyrdon, hi biterlice on wope heofodon, and ðara sawla sarlice bemændon
þe to heofona rice faran sceoldon, þæt hi Gode swa earmlice
ætlumpon.
 68. Ac þa ðe anrædlice gelyfdon þa ðe ðider gelædde
wæron and fæste heora geleafan on God hæfdon, and for nanes mannes
geþreate heora Drihtne wiðsacan noldon, þam man eac nan þingc ne
wandode, ac hi to eallre yrmðe getucode, and heora lima man ealle tobræd
ælc fram oþrum, eall swa windes blæd swæpð dust of eorðan, and
hi man holdode and hi ealle hricode, swilce oðer wæterflod swa fleow heora
blod, and ða heafodleasan man hengc on ða portweallas, and man sette heora
heafda swilce oþra ðeofa buton ðam portweallon on ðam heafodstoccum,
and ðær flugon sona to hrocas and hremmas and feala cynna fugelas, and
þara haligra martyra eagan ut ahaccedon, and flugon eft into ðære byrig
geond þa portweallas, and tosliton ða halgan Godes dyrlingas, and on heora
blodigon bilon ðæra martyra flæsc bæron, ðearmas and inneweard,
and þæt eall fræton.
 82. Earfoðfynde wæs ðar se man þe swilc ne mihte hreowan,
næs ðær eac nan man on fare þe gryre and ege fore ne stode, for ðam
mycclum yrmðum þe hi ðær gesawon; wundorlic wæs þæt martyrcynn
and wið deofol strang gewinn, þær wæs Godes ege gesewen and open on
fulre dæde.
 86. Swilc mihte campdom beon, swilce man ðær mihte geseon
þæt hi God inweardlice lufedon þa hi for ðære lufe his naman
yrmðe geþafedon, and þone sylfan deaþ to ðan swiðe þafedon; and
na þæt an mænan mihton and heora eorfoða behreowsian, ac gif we
ðær wæron we mihton gehyran swa swa ealle ða gehyrdon þe ðær
æt wæron, þæt wæs onmang ðam mycclan geðryle and on ðam
egeslican geþryngce ða man þa martyras cwylmde, þe wolde þincean
færunga swilce ealle ða anlicnyssa ðe on þære byrig to Godon geond
ealle gesette wæron ðæt hi ealle ætgædere oncwædon and anre
stemne clypedon, þæt hi mid ealle aweg ðanon woldon for þam mycclan
yrmðum þe ða Godes halgan for heora ðingan þolodon, and swilce þa
stræta ealle eac oncwædon, for ðam halgan banum þe toworpene him
onuppan geond ealle ða byrig lagon; eac swilce þa burhweallas cwacedon and
bifedon, swilce hi feallan woldon for þam halgum lichamum þe on heom geond
þa birig on ælce healfe hangedon.
 102. La, hwæt mæg beon wop oððe sarignys, gyf þæt
næs se mæsta ægðres, oþþe hwæt mæg beon geomrung and
wanung gyf þæt næs se fulla ægðres, þa siðþan man þus þa
halgan hæfte and gebende and hi man swang and bærnde, and swilce
ofsticode swin holdode, and to ealre yrmðe tucode?
 106. And ða magas beheoldon hu heora magas ðrowodon, and on
ðam portweallon to wæfersyne hangodon, and se broðor beheold his swuster
on wite, and seo swuster beheold hire broðor on yrmðe.
 110. Se fæder wiðsoc his bearne, and þæt bearn wiðsoc
þone fæder, and æt nextan ælc freond wiðsoc oðres for ðam
micclan egsan þe hi ðær gesawon, and heom for an þa witv gemynte
wæron, buton hi ðærrihte urnon and ðam deofolgylde geoffrodon and
Drihtne wiðsocon.
 114. Þa ne mihte na lengc manna ænig hine sylfne bedyrnan, ac
gehwa to sæles moste clipian and openlice mid dædum cyðan, to
hwæþeran hlafordscipe he wolde gebugan, þe to ures ecean Drihtnes, þe
to ðæs awyrgedan deofles; hwæðer him leofre wære þe he ðam
witum ætwunde, þe he hi for Godes naman acome.
 119. Ða wurdon ðær ameldode seofon halige men, Gode
getreowe, ðæra naman we awriton on ðære frumspræce heora halgan
ðrowunge; hi wæron gemetfæste on geleafan þæs lifigendan Godes
suna, and his ðæt halige rodetacn on heora lichoman getreowlice bæron
þa þa hi gesawon ða mænigfealdan wawan þe Cristes þa gecorenan
dæghwamlice for his naman ðafedon and þoledon, hi þonne ða seofon
geomredon and weopon, and heora nebwlite þurh ða mycclan sorhge mid ealle
ahlænsode, and seo wlitige fægernes heora geogoðhades weornode and
wanode, and hi on ealne weg, on wæccan and on fæstenum and on halgum
gebedum, geomrigende lagon; and þæt eall hi dydon for ðæs caseres
ðingon, for þon hi him ær on hirede swiðe neahgangele wæron.
 131. Þonne swa oft swa hi gesawon þæt se yfela casere and
eall seo burhwaru togædere comon þæt hi onsægednyssa deoflan offrian
woldon, hi ðonne ðas seofon halgan eodon him onsundran þær hi ðonne
mihton, and hi ðonne astrehton on ðære eorðan, and to Gode hi
gebædon þæt he heora gehulpe swa swa he wolde.
 136. Ða gelamp hit amang þam þæt sume hlosniende menn
ðær betweonan eodon, and þisra seofona georne heddon, swa oft swa man
gehwilcne mann sohte þæt he deofolgylde offrian sceolde; and þonne
gemetton hi ðas seofon halgan halige cnihtas ealle ætgædere on anum
bure to Gode gebiddende, and mid aþenedum lichoman to him heora neode
geomerlice mænende.
 142. And hi ða Godes fynd butan gewande sona into þam ciningce
eodon, and him ðus to cwædon; þeoda hlaford, us se besorgesta, gelimpe
þæt ðu lange libban mote on myrhþe and on mærðe þines
cynerices.
 145. Ðu leof cyningc leodscipas, ðine wide and side þu
hætst þæt mann manige manna gehwilcne, þæt he ðam mæran Gode
offrie, and her on gehendnysse syndon þe þine deorlingas beon sceoldon;
þe sylfne hi forfleoð, and þine hæse forseoð, and ealle æfter
gewunan Cristenra manna dæghwamlice offriað.
 150. Þæra is se yldesta Maximianus, and his six geferan þe
on ðissere byrig synd yldest getealde.
 151. Þa se casere þis gehyrde, ða wearð he þearle
gedrefed on his mode, and bead þæt hi man ðærrihte to him gelædde,
and hi sona comon mid floteriendum eagum for ðære micclan angsumnysse;
ealle heora heafda wæron mid duste besyfte, wæs þeh eall heora myne
fæst on tohopunge þæs ecean Drihtnes.
 156. Þa axode he se casere and ðus clipode, hwi synd ge
asceadene fram eowra geferena gemanan, þæt ge min bebod healdan noldon,
þæt ge ðam mærum godum offrunga ne brohton?
 159. Ac nu ic eow bidde and ægðer gebeode þæt ge hit
geornlice beginnon, and þæt swiðe hrædlice gefyllon, and þæt
buton gewande don swa ic eow bebeode, and swa ealle menn doþ wide on
æghwilcere þeode.
 162. Ða andwyrde him an ðæra cnihta, Maximianus se halga,
ana for hi ealle, and cwæð to þam casere unearhlicere stemme, ænne we
wurðiað ecne Drihten, ðæs mihta gefyllaþ heofenas and eorðan; him
we offriað anum, and his ðam halgan bearne Hælende Criste, þe for ure
neode on menniscnysse eode on ðam halgan gaste, þe of fæder and of suna,
unasegcendlic forðstæpð and ealla gesceafta gehalgað.
 169. Þas untodæledlican ðrynnysse we gebiddaþ mid
eadmodnysse; þisan Gode we offrunga gelome bringað, and ure bena to him
sendað, lichaman and sawle clænnysse, and modes and muðes andetnysse;
þas we him beodaþ gedefe, and þinon awyrgedan deofolgildan we næfre
nellað offrian, þy læs ðe we us sylfe gebringað on fylðe, and
siððan on yrmðe ecere helle.
 174. Gode anum we ure neode betæcað, and him ure sawle
befæstað, hine we næfre ne forsacað, ac hine we wurðiaþ æfre.
 176. Ða Decius se casere þas word gehyrde, ða na gestod he na
ælcne onsundran; ac heora ælces sweordfætelsas he het forceorfan, and
hi mid bendum fæste het gewriðan, and cwæþ to heom eallum, Nu ge
þam mærum godum offrian nellað, ne beo ge me næfre heononforð swa
wurðe ne swa leofe swa ge ær wæron, ac fram me ge beoð ascyrede and
fram ælcere myrhþe, oðþæt ic eft eow gestande and ic ðonne wið
eow stiðlicor aginne, ðonne ic tale wið eow habban wylle.
 184. Ne ðincþ hit me þeah nan ræd, ac ic eow læte
unbeheafod þæt ge swa earme eow sylfe and eowre ðeondan geogoðe
fordoþ and forspillaþ, on witon and on wawon and on mistlicum yrmðum.
 187. Ac ic eow nu gyt sumes fyrstes geann þæt ge eow sylfe
beþencean.
 188. And on beteran mode gebringan, þæt ge eower þæt
wlitige lif magon generian.
 189. Þa se casere hi ðus gesprecen hæfde, þa forðan þe
hi him leofe wæron, he het hi eft ealle unbindan, and unbundene aweg
forlætan þæt hi frige moston faran aweg swa hwider swa hi woldon.
 192. And se casere for to oðre burhware worhte þæt sylfe
þæt he ær beeode, Cristene menn drehte swa he swiðost mihte.
 194. Maximianus ða, se Godes halga, and his six geferan Gode ða
gecorenan, syððan hi fyrstos onfengcon and ænigne timan hæfdon, þa
halgan weorc þe hi ær begunnon, ær hi beforan ðam casere stodon, hi
ða fullice gefremedon.
 198. Namon æt heora magon þa sceattas genoge, sylfrene and
gyldene ungefoge, and þa eawunga and dearnunga ealle Godes ðances spendon,
and dældon hafenleasum mannum, and heom betweonan ræddon and þus
geþwærlice cwædon, Betere we ahreddon us sylfe of ðissere burhware
gehlyde; faran us into þam mycclan scræfe her geond on Celian dune, and we
us ðær georne to Gode gebiddan, and ðær we magon full eaðe on
genere wunian oððæt eft se casere into þissere birig fare; and he
ðonne deme swa swa he wylle, and us nan þingc on worulde fram Gode ne
gehremme.
 207. Ac do he ymbe us swa swa his willa sy, þæt we ætforan
ðam casere þurh his fultum magon martyrdom gefremman, and æt him ðone
ecean cynehelm underfon buton ende mid his halgum.
 210. Ða hi ðus sprecende wæron seofon ða gecorenan halgan,
þa sealdon hi heom fæstnunge betweonan þæt hi ealle þis woldon
healdan oð heora lifes ende.
 212. And þæt feoh þæt hi ær læfdon hi mid heom to
þam scræfe gemænelice hæfdon, and ealle þider inn eodon and
mænigne dæg ðærinne wunedon; and on aþenedum lichaman hi to Gode
geornlice gebædon, þæt he heora gemiltsode swa swa his wylla wære.
 216. Setton him þa ænne wicnere getreowne, and swiðe
gesceadne.
 217. Ðæs eadigan nama wæs Malchus se goda, æt þam
wæs gelang eall heora foda; se heom on ealre hwile metes tilian sceolde, and
he ða mid eadmodnysse fengc to ðære gehyrsumnysse, and swa oft swa he
into ðære byrig eode, he hine on wædlan hywe æteowde, and dearnunga
wæs smeagende hu hit on ðæs caseres hirede ferde, and georne ðæs
þe he mihte earmum mannum ælmyssan dælde, and his geferan mete bohte
and to heom þone gebrohte; and heom ælc þæra worda cydde þe he be
heom binnan porte ahwær sprecan gehyrde.
 226. Þa gelamp hit betweonan þam ðe þas þing gewurdon,
þæt se casere eft mid fyrde ferde into Efese byrig, and he ðærrihte
het gelangian Maximianum þone halgan, and mid him his six geferan, þæt
hi ealle ætgædere sceoldon deoflum offrian.
 229. Þa þa he mid ungemete heom behet ælcne hete, þa
wurdon getreowe hi ealle, and mid ogan ofsette, and gehwa sohte gener
þærrihte ðær he ænig findan mihte, and he Malchus se getreowa
fleah of ðære byrig sona mid ege and mid ogan, hæfde mid him þeah
eaþelicne fodan, and com to his geferan and heom eall cydde hu egeslice se
casere be heom beboden hæfde, þæt hi mon æghwanone secan sceolde,
and hi ða halgan þa hi þæt gehyrdon ealle hi forhtedon, and to Gode
clypedon, and on geomrunge ðære mæstan him heora lif eall befæston.
 238. A wæs þeah amang þam Malchus heora ðenigmann, and
þa eaðelican þenunga þe he ðider brohte heom geornlice þenode,
þæt hi be dæle hi gereordodon, and þæt hi wurdon þe geheortran
wið þam awyrgedan strangan, and þone ealdan wiðerwinnan.
 242. Ða þa hi ealle ætgædere comon, and to middes ðam
scræfe sæton þæt hi gemænelice gereordodan, ða wurdon heora
eagan afyllede mid tearum and angmode geomrodon ealle heora heortan.
 245. Mid þi þe hit æfnian wolde and seo sunne sah to setle
onmang ðam þe hi on wope wæron, and hi on uneaðnysse spræcon.
 247. Hi ða heom betweonan an and an hnappodon, and swa lange hi
hnipedon þæt hi ealle ætgædere on slæpe wurdon; ealle him
wæron gehefgode ða eagan of ðam menigfealdum biterlicum tearum þe hi
ðær aleton, and on ðam sare þam mycclan hi lagon and slepon.
 251. Ac God ælmihtig scyppend, þe is ealra gesceafta wealdend,
þe his gecorenan bið swa milde swa modor bið hire agenum cilde, he sylf
þas seofonum halgum bebead þæt hi swa slepon for his micclan wundrum,
þe eft he gedon habban wolde, þa halgan ðe he ealre worulde furðor
onwreon gemynte.
 256. He sylf ðas þingc swa gescifte, and mid his ðære
mæran fadunge gedihte, þæt heora nan gefelan ne mihte hu hi gewurdon on
slæpe, ne heora nan nyste hwær heora sawla reston.
 258. Eall hit wæs heom uncuð, ac hit wæs Gode ful cuð.
 259. Ealle hi lagon slæpende geond þa eorðan, and swa on
Godes naman andetnysse hi gewurdon on ðære seftnysse, and þæt feoh
þæt hi hæfdon ðær on heora seodum læg eac mid þam halgum
uppan ðære eorðan.
 263. Ða seo sunne begann ðæs on morgen onywan eallum mannum
hire ðone beorhtan leoman, þa het se casere georne smeagan hwær mann
æfre þa halgan geaxian mihte.
 265. Ælc mann þa æfter ðam gebode ofer eall ferdon, mann
smeade uppan lande, man axode on porte.
 267. Ðær man gengde geond eall abutan þone portweall man
scrutnode/ on ælcere stowe þær man hi æfre geaxian cuðe, ne mihte
hi nan man na hwer findan.
 269. He þa se casere, dreorigan mode, cwæð to his þegnum
mid ðyllicum wordum, Mycel is me unbliss minra dyrlinga miss, þæt hi us
swa færlice mid ealle syn ætlumpene.
 272. Swa mære cynnes menn swa swa hi wæron, forþi hi
onsæton and mid ealle ondredon, þæt we heom forðon grame beon woldon,
forðon þe hi ær us hyran noldon.
 274. Ða cwæð se casere to ðam embstandendum, Nese la man
wat, and ic eac þæt sylfe wat, geseo we ænigne mann þe georne hine
sylfne to urum godum bugan wylle, eall þæt he ær agylte læsse
oþþe mare, we lætað hit of gemynde swilce hit næfre ne gewurde.
 278. Æfter swilcum wordum and mænigfealdum oðrum, stopon
þa in to ðam casere ða yldestan þe on his hirede wæron, and þa
halgan to him wregdon and be heom þus spræcon, Ealra manna hlaford geond
þas widan worulde, we biddað þinne cynescipe þæt þu nan ðingc ne
beo dreorig oððe sarig for ðan geongan cnihton ealra goda feondum, for
ðan hi under ðe, leof, oð þisne andweardan dæg on yfele
þurhwunodon, ðæs þe we gehyrdon siððan þu heom tolete þone
timan þæt hi hi sylfe beþohton, a hi ymbe þæt wæron hu hi ðe
mid ealle miscwemdon.
 287. Eall þæt yfel þæt hi ær ðan begunnon hi
þæt eall syððan ful dydon; namon æt heora magon ungerime sceattas,
and ealle ða towurpon geond þas ruman burhwegas, and synd nu bedyrnde and
on diglon behydde þæt hi nan man ne mæg na hwær gefindan.
 291. Gyf ðin cynescipe swa cwyð, hit geworden bið sona
þæt man heora magas gelangie, and hi man stiðlice ðreatige þæt hi
be wite hi ameldian, and to þe, leof, gebringan.
 294. Ða se casere ðas word gehyrde, he his mod sona gehyrte.
 295. Het þa ða magas gefeccan and began heom ðas word segcan,
Hwær syndon þa wiðersacan eowre lyðran magas þe min bebod
forhogedon, þæt hi ðam wurðlicum godum nane lac ne offredon?
 298. Buton ge hi nu her ameldian, ge sceolon heora wite astundian.
 299. Ða andwyrdon þa magas and sealdon micele aðas and ðone
casere bædon and ofdrædde him tocwædon, we biddað þe leof hlaford,
þæt ðu gehyran wylle ure word.
 301. We þin cynelice gebod nahwær ne forgymdon, ne we ða
weorðlican godas næfre ne forhogodon.
 303. Hwi wilt þu us leof witnian for oðra manna þingon þe
þin gebod forsawon, and ure sceattas forspendon geond ealle eorðan?
 305. Her hi synd full gehende geond on Celian dune, on sorge and on
ege behydde, ne we be him naþor nyton swa hi ðær libban, swa hi ðær
deade ligcon.
 307. Ða hi ðus hi sylfe earhlice betealdon, þa het se casere
hi faran swa hwider swa hi woldon, and hi feorhfagene him fram sona ðanon
eodon, and se casere eft sona þohte and smeade hwæt he þam halgan don
mihte, oððe hu he æfre embe hy sceolde; and þa þa he him hearmian
nolde for þi hit swa geweorðan sceolde, God ælmihtig him þa þæs
geuðe ðeah he ðæs wyrðe nære þæt God hine geneosode.
 313. Æfre ðeah for his halgena earnunge, him ða ðis
geþanc on mode asende, þæt he het þæs scræfes ingang ðær hi
inne lagon eall hit mid weorcstanum forwyrcan, for ðan God wolde þæt hi
ðær stille reston, and ungehrepode on ðam scræfe slepon oþ þas
yðtogenan tide þe he hi eft mancynne þurh his mycclan mærðe for
micelre neode geswutelian wolde.
 319. And he ða, Decius, let him to ræde þæt he þa
gerædde and he ða his geðanc geopenode.
 320. And ofer eall clypode, fare man swiðe hraðe þyder geond
to þam scræfe þær þa wiðersacan inne dariað behydde, and hi man
mid weorcstane on æghwilce healfe ealle swa cuce ðærinne forwyrce,
þæt hi sunnan leoman næfre lengc ne geseon, ne hi myrhðe mid us
heononforð nabbað, nu hi ure bebod healdan noldon.
 325. Ac beon hi ðær on yrmðe on ælce hand beclysede,
oððæt hi mid ealle deað forswelge.
 327. Swa he let on his geðance, se casere, and mid him eall seo
burhwaru, þæt hi ða halgan swa lifigende on ðam scræfe wurdon
beclysde.
 329. Ða gelamp hit þæt ðær betweonan eodon ðæs
caseres dyrlingas hi twegen, wæron him swiðe leofe, and hi
ðehhwæðere wæron dearnunga Cristene begen.
 331. Se an wæs genemned þeodorus, and se oðer Rufinus.
 332. Þa spræcon hi him betweonan swa hit nan man nyste butan
him sylfon, þæt hi woldon ðisra haligra martyra martyrrace awritan, and
þæt gewrit mid þam halgum ðærinne lecgan, swa man in to ðam
scræfe gan sceolde, þæt hit mid him þærinne læge, to swutelunge
oð ðone byre þe hi God ælmihtig awehte, and hi mancynne geswutelian
wolde þæt ealle men ðurh ðæt gewritt eft ongytan mihton hwæt
þa halgan wæron þe man ðærinne funde þonne þæt Godes wylla
wære.
 339. And hi ða twegen getreowfæste wæron dydon
þærrihte eall swa hi ær gemynton, eodon in to ðam scræfe dearnunga
onsundran, and þas halgan martyrrace eall swa heo gewearð on anum leadenum
tabulan ealle mid stafon agrofon, and hi ðæt gewrit mid twam sylfrenan
inseglum on anre teage geinsegledon, and wið þa halgan ðærinne swiðe
digollice ledon; and ðæs scræfes locstan hi wel fæste beclysdon, and
him ðanon syððan hamweard gewendon; and þa ealle þas ðingc þurh
Godes fadunge þus wurdon gedyhte.
 347. Ða ymbe þæt utene, forðferde Decius se yfela casere,
and æfre ælc dæl eall his cynnes; and feala oðra casera æfter him
rixodon ælc æfter oðrum on heora cynescipes wuldre, and on heora
anwealdes myrhþe; and hi, sume hæþene and sume Cristene, feala geara
rixodon, oððæt þeodosius se mæra casere, Archadies sunu, fengc to
rice.
 353. And embe eahta and ðrittig geara þæs þe he rixode,
asprang gehwær on Godes folce mycel gedwyld, and ferdon yfele menn geond
eall þær hi mihton, and Cristene men on gedwylde brohton, sædon
þæt se geleafa naht nære þe ealle geleaffulle men buton tweonunge
gelyfað, þæt is þæt ealle men on domes dæg sceolon arisan mid
þam ylcan lichaman þe gehwa ær her on life leofode, and þonne
æghwilcum men æfter his geearnungum bið gedemed, swa to yrmþe on
helle wite, swa to myrhþe on heofona rice.
 361. Ðisne geleafan woldon gedwolmen aidlian, and of Cristes
gelaðunge mid ealle adwæscan; and on ðam timan þe ða bisceopas beon
sceoldan and Godes þæt halige folc on rihtne weg gebringan, hi swiðost
ælces gedweldes tiledon, and ælc gedwyld hi upp arærdon.
 365. Twegen ðær wæron bisceophades men þe ælces yfeles
heafodhebban wæron; se wæs gehaten Theodorus, and se oðer Gaius.
 366. Hi næron furðan wyrðe þæt man heora naman on
ðisre haligra martyrrace sceolde awritan, for ðan þe hi Godes gelaðunge
swiðost drehton, and mid heora gedwolspræce eall folc amyrdon.
 369. And Theodosius se mæra casere þa he swilce ungewitt
ælce dæge gehyrde, he wearð sarig ðearle on his mode, and he wepende
on his geþance hit bemænde þæt æfre on his timan se Cristena
geleafa swa earmlice ætfeallan sceolde.
 373. Sume þa yldestan gedwolmen sædon þæt menn of deaðe
næfre arisan ne sceoldon.
 374. Sume hi cwædon þæt se lichama þe æne bið
formogod and to duste gewend and wide tosawon, þæt he næfre eft
togædere ne come, ac ða sawla ana on domes dæg butan ælcan lichoman
sceolden underfon ðære myrhðe heora æriste.
 378. Þus hi dweledon mid heora leassagulan spræce, and heora
modes andgytu mid ealle hi fordytton, þæt hi nan ðæra worda
geðencan ne mihton þe ure Hælend sylf on ðam godspelle be ðære
æriste cwæð, <foreign>Amen amen, dico uobis, quia uenit hora, quando mortui in
monumentis audient uocem filii hominis, et uiuent.</foreign> þæt is on urum
geþeode, Soð soþ, ic eow secge þæt se tima cymð þonne ealle
deade menn on heora byrgenum mannes bearnes stefne gehyrað, and hi ealle
acuciað.
 386. Ðyllice halige word, and ungerime oðre ðe on halgum
bocum synd awritene, þæt God ælmihtig mænigfealdlice, ge ðurh his
witegan, ge þurh hine sylfne, and be ðæra martyra, æriste wæs
sprecende; and ðeah ealra þæra worda hi wæron forgytene.
 390. Namon him þa gedwollmenn ænlipige to gemynde, and lagon
on heora gedwylde, and Godes worda swetnysse hi awendon him sylfum to
biternysse, þe swa Godes folc drehton; and ðonne for ðisum wearð
Theodosius se mæra þearle ahwæned, and he his lic for ðære
sarignysse mid wacan hreafe scrydde, and wæs him ana cnihtleas on his inran
bure, and hine sylfne ðærinne beclysde, and þær hreowlice beforan
Gode gebærde, forðan þe he nyste hwæs he gelefan sceolde, þa hine
þa swyðost drehton and on ungewisse gebrohton þe his witan beon
sceoldon.
 398. Ac ælmihtig God se milda þe ælcne mann mid fulre
mildheortnysse underfehþ þe hine mid fulre eadmodnysse gesehð, þa he
ðæs caseres mycclan hreowsunga geseah, him eac sona þæt hreow and his
þæt sarlice anginn, and hine þa na lengc ahwænedne habban nolde; ne
he eac þa na lengc geþafian ne mihte þæt his halige folc læge on
gedwylde; ac he for his mycclan mildheortnysse ægðer ge ðam godan casere
frofre geuþe, and eallum folce ðæs swiðe ungefyrn he geswutelian wolde
hwæs gehwa gelyfan sceolde mid gewisse, and he his ða halgen gelaþunge
ðæs ful tidlice of ðæra gedwolmanna gedrecednysse ahredde, and hira
eac ða toweardon ealra manna æriste, mid his ðam beorhtan and ðam
soðan leohte geopenode on ðus gewordenre dæde.
 410. Ða on ðam timan þe se Cristena and se goda Theodosius
fullice on God ælmihtigne wæs belyfed swa his yldran beforan him manega
wæron, and he his neode to Gode swiðe georne mænde, þa gelamp hit on
ðam dagum þe ðas forsprecenan þingc gewurdon, þæt God ælmihtig
gescifte ænne swa geradne mann, þe ahte geweald ealles ðæs splottes
æt Celian dune, þar þæt scræf wæs tomiddes þe ða seofon
halgan lagon inne slapan, and he ða se ilca goda mann let ðær aræran
ealle abutan ða dune his hyrdecnapan cytan, þæt hi ðær gehende mid
heora hlafordes yrfe lagon, and wið cyle and wið hæton hi sylfe
geburgon.
 420. And hi georne, þa hyrdecnapan, and mid heora handgemacan,
sume twegen dagas on an ymbe þæt wæron, oð þæt hi werige fornean
comon ðær ða seofon halgan full gehende lagon; and hi ðær sona
unmyndlinga swiðe fæsthealdne weorcstan upp ahwylfdon, and æfre swa hi
near and near eodon, hi fundon ælcne stan on oðerne befegedne, and ymbe
ðæne oþerne dæg hi ðæs scræfes locstan ut alynedon, þæt
hi eaðelice mihton ingan, and eaþelice utgan.
 427. Ða gelamp hit þæt God wolde þæt seo halige
geferræden aweht beon sceolde, þe on ðam scræfe tile hwile gereste
hæfdon.
 429. And he ða, ure Hælend, se þe unborenum cildum lif
sylð on heora modra innoðe, and se þe mid his anwealde ða forsearedon
ban wecð of deaðe, and se þe eac Lazarum to life gewende, and hine ymbe
þreo dagas ðæs þe he bebyrged wæs of deaðe awehte, he sylf
synderlice mid his agenre dæde þas seofon halgan þe on ðam scræfe
slepon he hi awehte ða of ðam slæpe; and hi sæton ealle upp gesunde
æfter heora agenum gewunan and heora sealmas sungon; forði him næs nan
deaðes mearc on gesewen, ne heora reaf næron nan þingc moðfretene, ac
ægðer ge þa ilcan reaf þe heom on uppan lagon wæron ealle gesunde,
and heora halgan lichaman hi gesawon eall blowende.
 439. And ealle hi leton swilce hi on æfen slepon, and sona
ðæs on morgen of ðam slæpe awacedon; and þæt ilce geþanc and
seo sylfe carfulnyss þe heom amang þam nihtslæpe wæs on heora
heortan, eall þa hi awacodon hi þæt sylfe geþohton, and hi nan oþer
ðing nyston buton þæt Decius se casere hete heora gecepan, and ða hi
ðus dreorigende þohton and mid heora modes unrotnysse tearas aleton.
 446. Þa besawon hi ealle to Malche þe wæs heora geferena an,
and wæs he eac heora ðeningmann, and hi hine þa axodon hwæt he on
æfen gehyrde þæt man be heom spræce on porte.
 448. He andwyrde þa Malchus and cwæð to his geferum,
þæt ic eow to æfen ær sæde þæt ilce ic eow nu segce,
þæt mann us toniht ofer eall sohte, and us man georne gehwar axode,
þæt we deofulgyldum sceoldon offrian; and Decius se casere is nu gyt
smeagende hwæt we gefaran habban, oððe hwær he us mæge ofaxian.
 453. Nu wat ure Drihten þæt we ðæs nane þearfe nagon,
þæt we him æfre fram abugan.
 455. Þa andwyrde Maximianus and cwæð to his gebroðrum, gif
hit swa sceal gewurðan þæt mann us her finde and mann us for Godes naman
to ðam casere læde, we eac sona ðider faran ealle swiðe gearwe, and we
ðær ætforan him standon us gearwe, and behate swilc wite swilc he us
behate.
 459. We nan þingc ne beon ofdrædde, ne we uran ærran life
ne wiþsacan næfre, þæt we habban clænlice Godes lof mid us
gehealden oð ðis, þurh þone halgan geleafan þæs lifigendan Godes
suna/.
 462. And hi ða gebroðru clypedon to Malche and him to
cwædon, nim nu broþor sumne dæl feos mid þe and far to porte mid, and
us sumne dæl hlafes bige, and ofaxa georne ðæs ðe þu mæge,
hwæt se casere be us geboden hæbbe, and do us eft ealle gewisse þæs
þe þu ofaxie.
 467. And bige us swa ðeah rumlicor todæg be hlafe þonne ðu
gebohtest gyrstan dæg, and bring us bet be hlafe þonne ðu ær
brohtest forþon þe þa hlafas wæron swiðe eaðelice þe us gyrstan
æfen comon.
 470. Swa hi leton þa halgan, and nan oþer ne wendon buton
þæt hi on æfen slepon, and þæs on morgen awocon.
 471. And he þa sona on ærnemergen aras, Malchus heora
þeningman, and dyde eall swa his gewuna wæs, nam þa mid him sumne dæl
feos swa micel swa hit mihte beon.
 474. Ðeah swilce hit wære sum twa and sixtig penega, and
wæs þæs feos ofergewrit ðæs ylcan mynetsleges þe man þæt
feoh onsloh, sona þæs forman geares þa Decius feng to rice.
 477. Feower siðon man awende mynetisena on his dagum, þe ðas
halgan ðagyt wunodon onmang oþrum mannum, and on þam frummynetslæge
wæron twa and sixtig penega gewihte seolfres on anum penege, and on þæm
æftran em sixtig, and on þæm þryddan feower and feowertig, and on
þam feorþan git læsse swa hi hit þær heoldon.
 482. Ða wæs þæt feoh þæt Malchus hæfde þæs
forman mynetslæges on Decies naman.
 483. Ðonne betweonan Decies frummynetslæges dagum þa þas
halgan into þam scræfe eodon, and betweonan Theodosius timan þe ða
wæs casere, þa Malchus þæt feoh bær to porte, be ealdum getele
wæron þa agane ðreo hund geara, and twa and hundseofontig wintra of
ðam dæge þe ða halgan slepon to ðam dæge þe hi eft awocon.
 488. And he ða Malchus sona mid ðam dæge eode him ut of
ðam scræfe, and þa he þærute wæs, ða geseah he hwær þa
weorcstanas lagon ofer eall þær onbutan, and he healfunga þæs
wundrode, þeah na swiðe embe þæt ne smeade; ac he forht of þære
dune mid micclan ege nyðereode, and he þanon cleacode swiðe earhlice to
porte, and æfre he him wæs onsittende þæt hine sum man gecneowe, and
hine þam casere þærrihte gecyðde.
 495. And he nyste se halga þæt se oþer earma wæs dead, ne
furðon an ban næfde he mid oþrum, ac toscænede ofer eall lagon, and
toworpene geond ða widan eorþan.
 497. And he þa Malchus þa he ful gehende wæs wið ðæs
portes geate eode, þa beseah he þiderweard, and beseah to þære halgan
Cristes rodetacne hwær heo uppan þam portgeate stod mid arwurðnysse
afæstnod; and hine þær gelæhte syllic wundrung, and on þære
gesihðe hine gestod wundorlic wafung, and he stod and beheold, and him
wundorlic þuhte, and he æghwider beseah on æghwilce healfe, and he
hawode on þa rode, and hit him eall wundorlic ðuhte, and he þohte on his
mode hwæt hit beon sceolde.
 505. And he ða þanon to oþran portgeate eode, and he þa eft
sona geseah þa halgan rode, and he þæs wundrode þearle, and he þa
portgeatv ealle beeode, and he geseah uppan ælcon þa halgan rode standan,
and eall he wæs ful wundrunge and wafunge; and eac þa byrig he geseah eall
on oþre wisan gewend, on oþre heo ær wæs, and þa gebotla geond þa
byrig eall getimbrode on oþre wisan on oþre hi ær wæron, and he nan
þincg þære byrig ne cuþe gecnawan þe ma þe se man þe hi næfre
ne geseah mid his eagan.
 513. And þa he wundrigende þohte swilce hine on niht mætte,
þa gecyrde he eft to ðam ylcan portgeate þe he ærest tocom, and he
þohte on his heortan, and cwæð to him sylfum, hwæt þis æfre beon
sceole færlices, þæt ic her geseo swa wunderlices, þæt gyrstan
æfen on ealre ðisre byrig þære halgan rodetacna nahwær næs
gesyne, and heo nu eall is geswutelod, and on ælcon portgeate is nu todæg
gefæstnod?
 520. And he eft sona þohte on his mode, and his hand up ahof and
senode hine sylfne and þus cwæð, God ælmihtig gebletsige me,
hwæþer/ hit furþon soð sy oððe hwæðer me on swefne
mæte eall þæt ic her geseo færlices wundres?
 523. And he æfter þysum geþance, teah him elnunge to be
dæle, and bewand his heafod mid anum claðe, and earhlice eode into porte,
and bearh him sylfum swiðe georne and þa he com ful neah into cypinge
þær gehwilce men heora ceap bean.
 528. Þa gehyrde he hu þa menn him betwynan spræcon and
oft and gelome Cristes helda sworon, and hi nane spræce þær ne drifon
butan æfre embe Cristes naman.
 530. Þa he swilce spræce gehyrde, ða ondræd Malchus him
þearle, and he ðæs eall forhtode and cwæð on his mode, La hwæt
þis æfre beon scyle þæt ic her wundres gehyre?
 533. Ær ic geseah micel wunder, nu ic gehyre miccle mare;
gyrstan æfen nan man ne mihte Cristes naman nemnian mid hihte, and nu
todæg on ælces mannes tungan Cristes naman is æfre on foreweardan.
 536. Ða cwæð he eft to him sylfum, to soðan ne þincð
me næfre þæt hit soð sy þæt þis sy Efesa byrig, forðy eall
heo is on oþre wisan gestaðelod, and eall mid oþrum botlum getimbred, ne
her nan man ne spricð on hæðenra manna wisan, ac ealle æfter
Cristenra manna gewunan.
 541. Þa wiðgynde he eft his geðance, and him þus andwyrde,
ac ic nat eftsona, ne ic næfre git nyste þæt ænig oþer byrig us
wære gehende buton Ephese anre her on em Celian dune; and he stod þær
stille ane lytle hwile, and þohte on him sylfum hwæt his soðes wære.
 545. Ða ofseah he ænne geongne man, and eode him to þæm
ylcan, and ongan hine axian and cwæð, la wel gedo ðe goda man; ic wolde
georne æt ðe gewitan þissere byrig riht naman, gif þu me woldest
gewissigan.
 548. Ða cwæð se geonga mann to him, ic þe wille full
hraðe secgan, Ephese hatte þeos burh, and heo wel gefyrn swa gehaten
wæs.
 550. Ða þohte he on his mode and cwæð to him sylfum, nu ic
wæs of þam rihtan wege mines ingeþances, ac betere hit bið þæt ic
eft fare ut of þysum porte ðylæs þe ic to swiðe dwelige, and forþy
þonne ne cume to minum geferum þe me ær hyder sendon; gewislice ic her
ongyten hæbbe þæt me hæfð gelæht fæste mines modes
oferstige, þæt ic nat na forgeare hu ic hit þus macige.
 556. Eall he Malchus rehte eft his geferum hu him gelamp on eallum
þisum þingum þa he eft heom to com on þam scræfe þe we ær
foresædon, and þa heora seo wundorlice ærist eallum mannum wæs
geopened and heora þæt halige lif eall geswutelod.
 560. And he Malchus þa him swa wundorlice þuhte eall þæt
he geseah and gehyrde, ða mid ðy þe he wolde gan ut of ðam porte, he
ða on ælmesmannes hiwe eode þyder full wel gehende þær man hlaf
sealde to ceape, and ða he þyder com, he sona teah penegas of his bosme,
and hi wið hlafe þam cepemen sealde, and hi þa cypemen swiþe georne
þa penegas sceawodon, and hi swilces feos fregnðearle wundredon, and hi
þa penegas þær to wæfersyne beheoldon, and fram bence to bence heom
betweonan ræhton and to sceawigenne eowodon, and heom betweonan cwædon,
butan tweon hit is soð þæt we ealle her geseoð, þæt þæs
uncuþa geonga cniht swiðe ealdne goldhord wel gefyrn funde, and hine nu
manega gear dearnunga behydde.
 571. Ða þa Malchus geseah þæt man his penegas swa georne
sceawode, he ondred him þa swiðe hearde, and eall þær he stod he
cwacode and bifode, and for an wende þæt ælc þara manna hine gecneowe
and cwæð þa on his geðance, Wella min Drihten, hwæt ic her nu
hreowlice hæbbe gefaren, ne mæg ic me nanes oþres wenan, buton þæt
hi nu me to Decie gelædon, þonne ne mæg ic nan gewis bringan to minum
geferum.
 578. And þa beheoldon swiðe georne þa cypemen hine, and be
him on geþance smeadon hwæt manna he beon sceolde.
 579. Ða cwæð he to heom eallum earhlicon wordum, La leof ic
bidde eow swa georne tyðiað me þæs ðe ic gyrne; þær ge habbað
þa penegas on handa, ateoþ hi swa swa ge willað.
 582. Ne gyrne ic æt eow nanes hlafes, ac ealra manna bruce ge
betst ægþres ge penega ge hlafa.
 584. Ða he þus wæs to heom sprecende, and swa hreowlice his
ceap gedrifan hæfde, hi sona ealle up stodon, and hine on heora handa
heoldon and him to cwædon, Sege us hwæt manna þu sy oþþe hwanon
þu cumen sy, þe þu þus eald feoh gemettest, and þus ealde penegas
hider brohtest, þe on gefyrndagum geslægene wæron on yldrena timan.
 589. Sege us nu þæt soðe buton ælcon lease, and we beoð
þine geholan, and ealne wæg þine midsprecan; ne we nellað þe
ameldian, ac hi eall stille lætan, þæt hit nan man ne þearf geaxian
buton us sylfum.
 592. Þa wæs Malchus ofwundrod heora spræce, and þohte
sarig on his mode, and cwæð be him sylfum to þam cypemannum, syllice is
me anum gelumpen, and earmlice hæbbe ic ana gefaren toforan eallum mannum
geond þas widan eorðan.
 596. Ælcon oþran men is alyfed þe on þysan life byð
gestreoned þæt he of his yldrena gestreone hine sylfne fercian mote, ac me
anon wreccan þæs nan þincg ne mæg gehelpan.
 598. Nu me is min agen ætwiten swilce ic hit hæbbe forstolen,
and man mid witum ofgan willað æt me, þæt ic mid rihtan þingon
begyten hæfde.
 601. Ða andwyrdon þa cypemen and him tocwædon, nese nese,
leofa man, ne miht þu us na swa bepæcean mid þinan smeðan wordan, se
goldhord þe þu gemettest and hine lange bedyrndest, he ne mæg beon
forholen, nu hit swa upp is aboren.
 604. He nyste hwylc andwyrde he heom syllan sceolde for þam
micclan ogan þe him on mode wæs.
 606. Ða hi gesawon þæt he stod þær stille, and him nan
þincg ne geandwyrde, hi fengon him sona on, and becnytton anne wriþan eall
onbutan his swuran, and hine þanon ealle atugan tomiddes þære cypinge,
and hine man heold on middan þære byrig swa gebundenne, and hit sprang
þa geond eall, and wæs sona wide cuð, and ealle men geond þa byrig
urnon þyder sona, and mid gehylde ælc cwæð to oþran, þæt
þær gelæht wære binnan þære byrig an uncuð geong man þe
yldrena goldhord sceolde findan, and swiðe eald feoh þyder gebringan, þe
man on fyrndagum sloh, and on ðæra yldrena casera timan notodon; and
þær wearð þa gegaderod wundorlice micel folc, and ealle men wafedon
his anes, þær he gebunden stod him tomiddes, and ofer eall hlydende ælc
man cwæð to oþrum, ðys is sum ælþeodig man of suman oþran
earde; ne gecnawe we his nan þincg, ne hine ure nan ne geseah næfre mid
his eagan ær.
 620. And he Malchus ealle þa word gehyrde, and æfre wæs his
uneaðnys wexende, and he þam folce æfre swa georne huru mid his
eadmodnysse cweman wolde, þæt he þurh his fullan eadmodnysse hreowan
sceolde; forþy he nu cuðe ne ne mihte nane tale findan, ne he nyste to hwam
he word sceolde cweðan.
 625. Þa hine synderlice ælc man beheold, and hine nan man ne
cuðe gecnawan.
 626. And þa þa he on þære micclan his modes wundrunge
þær gestod dreorig and swigende, þa arn him færunga to geþance
þæt he swiðe micelne truwan hæfde þæt his magas þagit on
þære byrig leofodon, and his þæt mære cynn þe wæs swiþe
namcuð eallum folce þe he þær binnan hæfde, and him þa for an
þuhte þæt he þæs gewiss wære þæt he þæs on æfen
ælcne man gecneowe and ælc gecneowe hine, and he þæs on morgen
nænne ne gecneowe ne nan hine; oþþe nan þridde be him sylfum ne let he
buton swilce he of his gemynde wære.
 634. And he þa mid þam geþance on þæt folc beseah on
ælce healfe, wolde georne sumne man gecnawan, oþþe broðor oððe
mæg oþþe sumne þara þe him ær cuð wæs geond þa byrig.
 637. Næs him ealles na þe sel þæs þe he georne hedde,
ne mihte he þær nænne geseon þe he gecnawan cuþe, ac þa he stod
þær swa hreowlice ana tomiddes eallum þam folce, hit æfre be him
micele swiðor ælc man spræc geond þa byrig, oþþæt hit wearð
cuð on þære halgan cyrcan æt þam bisceopstole, and man cyðde
þam bisceope Marine and þam portgerefan þæt sylfe.
 643. And hi budon begen þæt man Malchum swiðe wærlice
heolde, þæt he ne ætburste, ac man hine mid micclan ofste to heom
gelædde, and his penegas forð mid him þe he þyder brohte mid him, and
þa men þe Malchum on cypincge heoldon hine sona þanon abrudon and to
cyrcan læddon.
 648. And he þagit nan oþer ne wende buton þæt hi woldon
hine gelædan to Decie þam casere.
 649. And he þa com to cyrcean, and he beseah on ælce healfe
hwider he sceolde, and þæt folc wafigende him sah eall onbutan, and he
beseah on ælce healfe geornlice hwider he sceolde, and þæt folc hine
hæfde swa yfele swilce he sumes þinges scyldig wære, and ealle men hine
fram stowe to stowe brudon, and to wundre tawedon; and him wæs swa uneaðe
amang þam, and him eall þa eagan floterodon and bitere teares aleton.
 655. And se bisceop and se portgerefa namon þa his peningas, and
hi beforan þam folce sceawodon and heora þearle wundrodon, forþi hi
næfre ær ne gesawon swilc feoh mid heora eagan þe wæs on ealdum
dagum geslagen on Decius caseres timan, and wæs his anlicnys on agrafen, and
his nama þær eall onbutan awriten.
 660. Ða cwæð se portgerefa to Malche, Sege us nu hwær se
ealda hord sy þe þu digellice fundest, and hine eall oþ nu bedyrndest.
 662. Þylæs þe þu his ætsace, her is se man full gehende
þe sum þæt feoh hæfð on handa þe þu hider brohtest, and þu
hit him of þinum handum sealdest.
 665. Ða andwyrde Malchus and cwæð to heom eallum, eall ic
secge her beforan eow eallum folc soð, and gif hit eower willa is ge magon me
gelyfan, þæt ic næfre git ne gemette goldhord swa swa ge me onsecgað;
ac ic wat angewis soð, þæt of minra yldrena gestreone me becom þis
feoh on handa, and of þyssere ylcan byrig mangunge ic me þæt feoh
geræhte, and hit elles nahwær ne funde, ac ic þurh nan þincg ongytan
ne mæg hu me sy þus gelumpen þæt ic hit þus macige.
 672. Ða cwæð se portgerefa him to, Sege me nu her openlice
on hwilcere byrig þu geboren wære, oþþe to hwilcere byrig þe to
gebyrige.
 674. Ða cwæð he him to andwyrde, Leof swa ic læte on
minum geþance þæt me to nanre byrig swa rihte ne gebyrige, swa to
þissere byrig þæs ðe me þincð.
 677. Leof þis is Ephesa byrig þe ic on geboren wæs and
afeded.
 678. Ða cwæð eft se portgerefa to Malche, Gif þu her on
porte geboren wære and afeded, hwær synt þonne þine magas ðe þe
afeddon, and þe gecnawan cunnon?
 680. Lætan hi gelangigan hider to þam bisceope, and lætan
hi her beforan us forð gan, þæt hi for þe sprecon, and gif hi on
ænige wisan magon þe betellan.
 682. And he Malchus andwyrde, and his yldrena naman nemde, hwæt
þæs anes nama wæs, and hwæt þæs oþres næmnincg wæs.
 684. Ða ne gecneow se portgerefa þara namena nan ðing þe he
þær namode, ac he sona gelignode hine, and cwæð him to edwite, Nu
þurh þinre leasan tale ic her ongyten hæbbe þæt þu eart an
forswiðe leas man, and wel canst gif ðu nede scealt lease tale findan.
 688. He þa Malchus nyste hwæt he cweðan sceolde, ac stod
þær and hnipode, and wæs swa lange stille þæt sume menn cwædon
þe þær stodon, Nis his talu nan þincg soþ, ne drifð he butan
folcwoh, and hine to oþrum men hiwað, and his gebyrda mid þam bediglað,
þæt he huru on sume wisan heonan mæg ætberstan.
 693. And se portgerefa mid þysum wordum nam to Malche fulne
graman, and him mid eallum hete cidde, and hine þus axode, þu stunta and se
mæsta dwæs þe æfre on þissere byrig mæst wæs, on hwilce
wisan sceole we þe gelyfan and þinum ungewissum wordum, þæt we gecnawe
beon magon þæt þu ðys feoh begeate of þinre yldrena gestreone?
 699. Her mæg geseon ælc man þe telcræftas ænig
gescead can, and þisra peninga ofergewrit her eallum mannum openlice þæt
geswutelað, þæt hit mare is for an þonne þreo hund geara and twa and
hundseofontig wintra syððan ðyllic feoh wæs farende on eorðan, and
ealle men heom mid tiledon, and þæt wæs sona on þam fyrmestan dagan
þe Decius se casere to rixianne begann; and swilces feos nu nan dæl
nahwær nis amang þam feo þe we on þysum dagum notiað, and ure neode
mide bicgað.
 706. And be þam þe þu ær tealdest þa ðu þine magas
nemdest, hi wæron swa ær geo on ealdum dagum, swa ðæt nis nan swa
eald man þe hi nu on þisne timan mage geþencan, oððe ær for fela
gearan mihte gemunan swa gefyrn swa hi þine yldran wæron.
 710. Nu stentst þu her an geong man, and wylt þysre byrig ealde
witan mid þinan lote bepæcan.
 711. Ac man sceall þe oþer gecyþan þæt þu us na lencg
ne þearft mid þinre leasunge fercian.
 713. Ic gedo þæt man sceall þe wel fæste gewriðan,
ægðer ge handa ge fet, and þe eallswa seo domboc be swilcum mannum
tæcð, oft and gelome swingan, and to ealre sorge tucigan.
 716. Þonne scealt þu þines unþances þone hord ameldian
þe þu sylfwilles ær noldest cyðan.
 717. Ða Malchus þas word gehyrde þe se portgerefa him swa
hetelice wæs tospræcende, he ofdræd sloh adun þærrihte, and hine
sylfne astræhte ætforan eallum þam folce, and þa cwæð to heom
eallum mid wependre stefne, La leof, ic bidde eow þæt ælmyssan þæt
ic mote anes þinges axian, and ic eow sona eall wille cyðan hwæt ic
þence on minum geþance.
 722. Þæs ic wolde leof axian gif ge me secgan woldon, hwær
Decius se casere sy, seþe her wæs on þissere byrig.
 724. Ða andwyrde se bisceop him, Marinus, and cwæð to
Malche, Min leofe cild, nis nu todæg se casere on eorþan lifigende þe
Decius sy genemned.
 726. Se casere þe ðu embe axast, he wæs gefyrn worulde, and
swiðe fela geara synd nu agane syððan he gewat of þysan life.
 728. Ða cwæð Malchus to þam biscope to andwyrde, þæt
is þæt an, leof hlaford, ðæs ic eallan dæg me onsitte, and
þæt is se an ege þe me swa swiðe drecð on minum mode, and nan man
nele minon wordon gelyfan.
 732. Ac ic bidde eow nu eadmodlice þæt ge after me ane lytle
hwile willan gan.
 733. Ic hæbbe ful gehende ane feawa geferena, hi synd her geond
on þam scræfe æt Celian dune.
 734. Ealles þyses gescead ge magon buton tweon gelyfan, Ic
þeahhwæðere þæt wat to soþan þingon þæt we fram Decie
þam casere ealle ætgædere flugon, and we his ehtnysse lange þolodon,
and nu toniht ic geseah mid minum eagum þæt se ylca Decius into Ephesa
byrig ferde, and ic and mine geferan on Ephesa byrig hamfæste wæron.
 739. Ac for his micclan ehtnysse þanon ealle we flugon geond to
þære dune, and on þam scræfe lagon ealle þas niht fram Decie
behydde.
 741. Ac me todæg swa wundorlice is gelumpen, þæt ic þurh
nan þincg ne mæg gecnawan hwæðer þys sy Ephesa byrig, þe elles
ænig oþer.
 743. Ða Malchus eall þus gesprecan hæfde, þa þohte se
bisceop Marinus wundrigende on his mode, and cwæð to eallum þam folce,
ðis is to soþan sum wundorlic gesihð þe God ælmihtig þysan geongan
menn onwreogan hæfð; ac uton nu ealle swiðe gearwe arisan, and mid him
þyder geond gan.
 748. And se bisceop Marinus sona aras, and mid him se portgerefa
and þa yldostan portmen, and forð mid micel menio ealre þære
burhware.
 750. And þyder ealle mid micelre arwurðnysse eodon, and to
þam scræfe genealæhton.
 751. And Malchus eode þa on foreweardan into his þam halgan
geferan, and se bisceop Marinus æfter him inn eode, and syððan æfter
him sume þa yldestan arwurðe men into þam scræfe eodon.
 754. And mid þy þe hi in becomen, þa gemetton hi on þa
swiðran hand ane teage, seo wæs geinsæglod mid twam sylfrenan
insæglan, þe þa twægen getreowfæste menn ðærinne ledon, þa
Decius se casere het þæt scræf forwyrcan swa we ær beforan rehton,
þæt þa insægla wæron eft to swutelunge hwæt man þærinne
funde þonne se tima gewurðe eallswa God wolde þæt þa gewurðan
sceolde.
 760. And man bær þa ut þa teage and man ealle þa burhware
het gelangian, and hi eallan folce eowde, and hi nan man ne uninsæglode
ær hi ealle þyder comon.
 763. Syððan hi ealle þær ætforan þam bisceope
gegaderode wæron, þa feng se portgerefa to þære tege, and he on
gewitnysse ealles folces hi uninsæglode and hi sona unhlidode, and
þærinne funde ane leadene tabulan eall awritene, and þa hi openlice
rædde.
 767. Þa com he to þære stæfræwe þær he þæt
word funde awriten, and he hit þa rædde eallswa, þæt hi fram Decie
þam casere flugon, and his ehtnysse þoledon.
 769. Maximianus wæs þære burhgerefan sunu, Malchus,
Martinianus, Dionisius, Iohannes, Seraphion, Constantinus, ðys synt þa
halgan þe æfter Decies þæs caseres bebode on þyson scræfe
wæron mid weorcstane beworhte, and wytt, Theodorus and Rufinus, heora
martyrrace awriton and hi herinne mid þyson halgan uppon anum stane ledon.
 775. And þa þa hi þæt gewrit ræddon, hi ealle
wundrigende wæron, and God ælmihtigne anon mode wuldredon and
mærsodon, for þam micclum wundrum þe he þær geswutolode and geuþe
eallum mannum.
 778. And hi ealle anre stefne Godes þa halgan martyras heredon
þær hi on þam scræfe ealle on geræwe sæton, and eall heora
nebwlite wæron swilce rose and lilie bleowon.
 780. And se bisceop and eall seo mænio feollan adune on þa
eorðan, and hi to þam halgan hi gebædon, and eall þæt folc God
ælmihtigne bletsodon and wurðodon for his micelan mildheortnysse, þæt
he swilce wundra heom geopenian wolde.
 784. And hi þa halgan martyras on þam scræfe sæton, and
þam bisceope Marine, and þam yldestan mannum be endebyrdnysse rehton hu hi
hit macedon on Decius caseres timan, and hu manega earfoðnyssa hi under
him/ gebidon, and fela oðre þing hi heom þær geopenode þe on
his dagum gewurdon, and hu oþre martyras under his ehtnysse þrowedon, eall
swa we ær on foreweardan þysre race rehton.
 791. And se bisceop Marinus sona æfter þam godan casere sende
Theodosie ærendgewrit þe on þyson andgite wæs gediht; Ic grete þe
leof eadmodlice, and ic bidde þinne þrymfullan cynescype, þæt þu to
us cume swa þu raþost mæge, þæt þu þa micclan mærða mage
geseon þe God ælmihtig eallum mancynne geuþe, and he hi on þines
anwealdes timan hæfð geswutelod.
 797. Vs is cumen, leof, leoht ofer eorðan, and we habbað mid us
þone leoman rihtes geleafan, and us seo towearde ærist ealra manna is nu
gecyðed þurh opene tacna, and Godes halige martyras syndon arisene, and
embe þæt spæce habbað to mancynne.
 800. Þa se goda casere Theodosius þæt gewrit geræd
hæfde, he aras þa of þære flora, and of þam wacan sæcce þe he
lange onuppan dreorig wæs sittende, and he þancode Gode ælmihtigum, and
ofer eall clypode, we þanciað þe, mæra scyppend, þu ðe on heofonum
and on eorþan eart cynincg and wealdend; we andettað þe leofa Hælend,
þu þe ænlic eart þæs lyfigendan Godes bearn; we wuldriað þe
inweardre heortan þæt þu us woldest on eorðan þinre rihtwisnysse
sunnan/ oneowan and us on wræcsiðe onlihtan þinre micelan
mildheortnysse leoman æteowan.
 809. Ne ðu leof ne mihtest getemian þæt mire andetnysse
leohtfæt sceolde acwyncan, þe began of mire yldrena leohtfæte scinan,
Constantinus þæs æðelan, and þæs we gelyfað leof þines
gecorenan.
 812. And he sona mid micclan ofste fram Constantinopolim þære
byrig swiðe mid his crætum to Ephese ferde, and eall seo burhwaru sah ut
ætgædere ongean þæs caseres tocyme, and se bisceop swiðe
eadmodlice eode ongean hine, and mid þam yldestan mannum hine to þam
scræfe læddon.
 817. And hi stigon þa mid ðam casere up to Cælian dune, and
genealæhton þam halgan þe on þam scræfe wæron, and hi þa
halgan martyras eodon þa ongean þone casere, and sona swa hi him on besawon
eall heora nebwlite ongann to scinenne swilce seo þurhbeorhte sunne.
 821. And he þa eode inn se casere, and hine sylfne ætforan
þam halgan þær adune astræhte.
 822. And hi arærdan hine of þære flora, and he þa
beclypte hi ealle, and for þære micelan blysse synderlice he weop ofer
ælcne, and his heorte wæs fægnigende, and mid þam mæstan gefean
he cwæð to þam halgan, Eall me þincð þæt ic eow geseo her swa
beforan me swilce ic ful gehende wære þam Hælende urum Drihtne, and
hine mid minan eagan eahsynes beheolde þa he Lazarum of byrgenne awehte, and
nu me þincð eac swilce ic stande gesewenlice æt his wuldorfullan
mægenþrymme foran, and his agene stefne gehyre swa swa hit toweardlic is
to gehyranne, þonne on his micclan tocyme ealle menn gemænelice
þurhwuniað.
 832. Ða cwædon hi, Nu nu, God ælmihtig þe eac geunne
þæt þu on myrhðe libban mote, and we willað beon for ðe inne
gelome þæs God biddende, þæt he ðe on þære halgan
geleaffulnysse, and on þines geleafan strengþe, and þin rice on sibbe
gehealde, and þæt ure Hælend þæs lyfigendan Godes sunu, þe on
his naman wið ealle fynd gescylde, ge on þyson life ge on þæm
toweardan, him to wuldre ðe on ecnysse leofað and rixað mid fæder and
mid suna and mid ðam halgan gaste on ealra worlda woruld a buton ende.
 840. Amen.

LS 35 (VitPatr)
B3.3.35.
Vitae Patrum: Assmann 1889, 195-207.



 1. We willað nu ærest writan be sumum westænsetlan, swa swa
Ieronimus hit of Ebrea on Greca gereorde awænde and Pelagius syððan on
ure geþeode, þæt is on Læden, to bysne and to lare þam ðe
anrædlice deofles costnungum and his lotwræncum wiðstandan willað.
 5. Deofol is swyðe swicol and fandiende, hu he mage þa earman
saule lytelicost mid mænigfealdum costnungum beswicon.
 7. Nu age we micle þearfe, þæt we us on gehwilce wisan wið
his luþernessa warnian and gescildan and bysne niman æfter ðam, þe hi
sylfe oft and gelome for heora drihtnes lufan ongean costnunga swyðlice
swæncton, þelæs us se lytiga belæde on his sylfes wite ðurh his
lotwræncas on helle grundas, þær he a sceal yrmðe adreogan in worlda
world, swa him heardost bið.
 13. <foreign>Solitarius quidam erat in inferioribus partibus Aegypti. Et
hic erat nominatissimus.</foreign> Sum wer wæs on Egypta lande swyðe namcuð and
hlisful þurh his drohtnunga, þe he his drihtne dæghwamlice to lofe and
to wuldre adreah on anum westene.
 17. Þa genam deofol him andan wið, swa he eal is mid andan
afylled, and hine oft rædlice mid mænigfealdum costnungum costnode, swa
þæt sum myltestre þurh deofles tyhtince þohte on hyre geþance,
þæt heo his hlisan amyrran wolde, þe heo oft fore gehyrde.
 21. Began þa faran to hire gegadan and heom ðus to cwæþ:
Hwæt wille ge me syllan, gyf ic amyrre þisne eowerne westensetlan and
alecge his miclan drohtnunga?
 23. Hi sædon and on wedde sealdon, hwæt hy hyre syllan
woldon.
 24. Heo þa anes æfenes began faran to ðæs foresædan
cytan, swilce heo dweliende þyder come, and fæstlice on þære cytan
duru cnocode.
 26. Sona swa he þæt gehyrde and on hy beseah, swa wearð he
swyðlice gedrefed on his mode and hy acsode, hu heo þyder come.
 28. Heo cwæð mid woplicre stefne: Dweliende, leof, ic com
hyder.
 29. Him ða earmode þær ungesæligan angin and hy lædde
into þam infærlde þære cytan, and he sylf into þære inran eode
and ða duru him to beclysde.
 32. Þa cleopode eft seo ungesælige woperiende him to and
cwæð: Eala leof ealdor, help min, wildeor me habbað her fornean
toslyten.
 34. He þa eft sona wearð swyðlice gedrefed and him eac godes
domes adred, gif heo þær tosliten wurðe fram þa reðan wildeoran.
 35. Cwæð þa to his agenum geþance ðus: <foreign>Unde venit mihi
ira hæc?</foreign> þæt is on ure geþeode: Hwanon com ne æfre þes grama?
 37. And ðære cytan duru oponode and hy in let to him sylfum.
 38. Began þa se saula swicend his heortan mid fyrenum luste
ongean þa ungesæligan swyðlice dreccan.
 40. Þa ðurh godes mildheortnesse undergeat he deofles swicdom
and his costnunga.
 41. Cwæð þa eft to him sylfum: <foreign>Viæ inimici tenebræ
sunt, filius autem Dei lux.</foreign> þæt is on Englisc: Feondes wegas syndon
þysðru, godes agen bearn is soðlice leoht.
 44. Onælde þa his blacern onmang þære þearlan hætan
þæs lustes and cwæð: þa ðe heora lustum folgiað and ðyllice
adreogað, forað to ecum tintregum.
 46. Heold þa his finger ofer þæt byrnende leoht and ðus
cwæþ: Fanda þines sylfes, hwaðer ðu þone ecan bryne forberan
mage.
 48. Þa ne gefredde he naþinc þæs brynes for þam miclan
luste, ac swa þa niht adreah and his fingras ealle ontende.
 49. Heo wearð þa seo ungesælige oð deað afyrht and hyre
heorte ahyrd on stanes gelicnesse, swa heo þæt geseah.
 51. Comon þa a morgen iunge men on bysmor to ðam foresædon
munece and him to cwædon: Com þis wif to æfen to ðe?
 53. He cwæð, þæt heo come, and heom tæhte, hwær heo
læg.
 54. Hy ða inn eodon þære forwyrhtan to hospe and wið hi
specan woldon.
 55. Þa læg heo þær dead.
 55. Hy cleopodon þa ealle: Leof fæder, heo is dead.
 56. And he þa his wrigels geopenode and his fingras him eowede
þus cweðende: Geseoh nu ða, hwæt þeos deofles dohtor hæfð gedon
þurh hyre lyðran lust, þæt ic habbe mine fingras amyrd.
 59. And heom rehte, swa swa hit gefaran wæs.
 59. Hy ða hine swæncton and cwædon: Nu nis hit awriten on
eowrum bocum: Ne sceal nan man gyldan yfel mid yfele?
 61. He clypode þa to his drihtne and hy of deaðe arærde, and
heo þa þanon forð hyre lif on clænnesse geheold.
 63. Eala, hu micel þing se godes wer dyde, þæt he þære
saule geheolp, þe heora begra ær þurh deofles lare amyrran wolde.
 66. <foreign>Finit prima sententia. Incipit secunda. Frater quidam
impugnabatur a fornicatione. Contigit eum venire in vicum quendam Aegypti et
videns filiam sacerdotis paganorum adamavit eam.</foreign> Hit wæs geara geo,
þæs ðe Ieronimus awrat us to bysne and to lare, hu se swicola feond
sumne munuc mid lyðrum lustum lange drehte, swa he eal is luðre afylled and
yfele, swa þæt se foresæda munuc þurh ðone swyðlican lust his
drohtnunge forlæt and to sumes Egiptiscan tune gewende.
 73. Ða gelicode him sona ðurh deofles tihtince þæs
hæþenan sacerdos dohtor.
 74. Began þa niman swyðe micle lufe to hyre and to hyre
fæder gewænde and hy him to gemæccan gyrnde.
 76. He him þa forwyrnde and cwæð, þæt he na mihte him
na þæs tyðian, buton he his godes rædes befrune.
 77. For ða to þam deofle, þe he weorðede, and him to
cwæð: An munuc com and gyrnde mire dehter; sylle ic hi him oððe na?
 79. Him andswarede he awyrgda gast þus cweþende: Acsege me,
hwæðer he his gode wiðsace and his fulluhte and his munucbehate.
 81. Þa gewende se sacerd ongean and ðone munuc acsode, hwaðer
he ealles þæs wiðsacan wolde, gif he him his dohtor sealde.
 83. He þa þæs geanwerde he þæt eal wiðsacan wolde.
 84. Geseah ða sona fleon ut of his muþe swilce hit an culfre
wære and an an up wið þæs lyftes weard.
 85. For ða eft se sacerd to þam deofle and him cydde, þæt
se munuc þa ðreo þing wiðsacan wolde.
 87. He ða se saula swicend him ðus to cwæð: Na syle ðu
him na þine dohtor, forþon ðe his god ne gewende na fram him, ac he him
gyt fultumað.
 89. He þa se sacerd þæt ðam munece sæde: Ne mæg ic
na ðe mine syllan, forðon þin god ne gewende na fram ðe, ac he ðe
gyt/.
 91. Sona swa he þæt gehyrde, swa cwæð he to his agenum
geþance: Gif god is min god, þe swa yfelum nu gyt fultumað and on me
ypð swa micle godnesse, þonne ic yrminc him wiðsoc and minum fulluhte and
minum munucbehate, for hwy gewænde ic æfre fram swa godan and swa
mildheortan?
 96. Began þa his geþanc to syfernysse gehwyrfan and for ða to
anum ealdum witan, þe wæs þeowiende his drihtne on anum westene mid
micelre drohtnunge, and him eall rehte, swa swa hit gefaran wæs.
 99. He ða se ealda godes þegn hine his þearfe lærde and
hine mid him on þam scræfe het sittan and ðreo wucan him fæsten
bebead and for hine wæs dæges and nihtes swyðe swincende on his
gebedum, biddende his drihten, þæt he him þa saule forgeafe and his
dædbote underfenge.
 103. God þa his bene gehyrde and ðam forworhtan gemiltsode.
 104. Þa ða he þæt are wucan fæsten gefyld hæfde,
þa com se ealda him to, þe hit him ær bebead and hine acsode, hwaðer
he ænig þinc geseage.
 107. He cwæð, þæt he geseage up on heahnesse þære
heofonan ane culfran flyceriende ofer his heafod.
 108. Him ða andswarede se ealda þus cweþende: Eala ðu leofa
broðor, begym þines sylfes and bide god georne, þæt he þin gyme.
 110. Hine þa eft se godes þegen on þære oðre wucan
acsode, hwæþer he ða gyt aht gesege?
 111. He cwæð, þæt an culfre him fluge wið þæt
heafod oft and gelome, swilce heo þær on ufenan settan wolde.
 113. He him þa bebead, þæt he hine sylfne gladode and to
gode georne cleopode.
 114. Acsode hine þa on þære þriddan wucan, hwaðer he
ða gyt aht gesege?
 115. He þa sæde, þæt an culfre come and gesette up on his
heafde, ac þa ða he hy niman wolde, þa aras heo of his heafde and innan
his muð gewænde.
 118. He þa se ealda, sona swa he þæt gehyrde, blissode and
god herode and to þam geedstaþoledan cwæð: Blissa nu, god underfeng
ðine dædbote.
 120. Beo ðu heonanforð geornful ymbe þine agene þearfe.
 121. And se munuc him ða woplicre stefne georne þæs fultumes
þancode and him behet, he a mid him wunian wolde þa hwile, þe his lif
wære and his lare geornlice hlystan.
 124. <foreign>Qui navali proelio dimicatur sunt, ante in portu et
tranquillo mari (125) inflectant gubernacula.</foreign> Sagað her on þissum bocum,
hu Malchus spræc, se godes munuc.
 127. He cwæð: þa men, þa þe beoð winnende in sciplicum
gewinne, hig þonne begað ærost þa gereðru in þære hyðe and in
þære sæ smiltnesse and hig teoð þa gereðru and hig fæstniað
þone stepe þurh þa þilinge and hiora gewuna bið, þæt hig
fæstlice stonden, þæt hig geleornigen in þæs gewinnes onlicnesse,
þæt hig hiom eft nan wiht ondrædan in þæs soðan gewinnes
gefiohte.
 132. Swa me þonne dyde swiðe, cwæð Sanctus Malchus,
forþon ic wende, þæt min word wæren bismer.
 134. And he cwæð: ærest ic wille beon gefremed in littlum
weorce, þæt ic mæge sum rust on weg adrifan of minre tungan, þæt
ic mæge becuman to bræddran gewyrde, gif me min drihten þæt lif
syllan wille, þæt ic minre ehtera tælnysse befleo, swa manige Cristes
cyrcan mid ehtnesse weoxen and þurh martiras hig wæron gewuldrode and
þonne æfter þan becom sio miht to þam Cristenum, þæt wæron ure
yldran, and nu syndon godes cirican þam weolum maran and þam mægnum hig
syndon læssan gewordene, and þyllicu þing syndon gereht on þissum
bocum and oðre manega, þa þe nu togenelæcað.
 144. Sagað heron, þæt Maronius wære gehaten sum tun; se
wæs, swilce he wære on þrittigum mila fram Antiochia byrig, and þonne
wæs þær to eastdæle nowiht micel tun.
 146. And þæs gebad æfter gearum swiðe manigne hlaford and
swiðe manigne mundboran, Hieronimus þa wæs forð sprecende, þe þis
ærest awrat be Malchum.
 148. He cwæð, þæt he wære swiðe geong man, þa he
wunode in Siria dælum, and he wæs to þæs papan æhte bifealden
Evagrius his neodfreondes, and þone ic nu nemde, forþon ic wolde
ætywian, hwanon ic þis ærest writan ongan.
 152. Sum eald man wæs in þam nehtune, þær ic wæs.
 153. Þæs nama wæs Malchus, þæt is on Latinum gereorde
cyning genemned, and þæt word is on Syrisc æþelung gecweden.
 154. And sum swiðe eald wifman wæs in his gesiðscipe;
þæra wæs þa iu deaðe swiðe neah, þæs þe mannum þuhte.
 156. And hig wæron butu swiðe geornfulle, þæt hig
gehiolden godes æ, and hit wæs onlice bi hig geworden gewearð and bi
Elisabeth his wife, swa hit on þam godspelle in hiora midnesse geworden.
 159. And þa ongan ic acsian þa geornlice bi þisum mannum, hu
gerad hiora gegaderung wæs hæmedes, þe þæs gastes, and þa
sæde hi eall se þeodscipe geswegsu swiðe halige and gode swiðe
gecorene, and nat ic, hwilc wundorlic þing bi þære gitsunge
onworpennesse and þa wæs ic gespecende þone man þinges cuðnesse
æt him.
 166. Þa cwæð he to me: Ic wæs gebur on þam lande, þe
Nisibim/, and wæs minra yldrena anuga bearn.
 167. And hig me þa bædon swa wæstma and hiora cynnes and
hiora hordes yrfeweard, and þa geornde ic, þæt ic munuc.
 169. Eala, mid hu monigum medum min fæder and min moder me
biddende/, þæt ic forlete mine geþungenesse, and me wæs be þis on
micclum tweon, þæt sceolde forlætan þa hus and þæt ic sceolde
fleon mine yldran and hus.
 173. Ne mihte ic gangan to eastdælum for Romwarena cempena
neahhergunge and for ra gehældum and ic þa hwyrfde lythwon mine fet to
westdæle and ic ht hwæt lytel ic hæfde wægnyste.
 176. To hwan spece ic nu þus mænigfealdlice.
 177. Ic þa becom nat ic on hu micclum f to Calcidus þam
westene, þæt wæs betwux Barsan and Immas, and hit is wið suðdæl
geseted.
 179. Þa gemette ic þær munucas and ic þa girnde, þæt
ic moste wesan in hiora þiowdome, and þis ic dyde, forþan þe ic ongeat,
þæt þa munucas lifdon on hiora agenum handgewinne.
 181. And he geseah, þæt hig niorwedon mid fæstenum and mid
gebedum hiora lichaman unstilnesse.
 183. Þa æfter nowiht manigum wintrum becom me on se geþoht,
þæt ic sohte eft mine yldran and minne eþel, forþan ic hyrde, þæt
min fæder wæs dead and min moder lifde þa git.
 186. Þa wæs ic gemyndig hire widuwhades and þa þohte, ic,
þæt ic bebohte ænne dæl þæs landes and þæra æhta and
þærfum gedælde and þæt ic of oþrum dæle getimbrode mynster,
and ic nu forsceamige to secganne mine ungeleaffulnesse, forþon ic þohte
þone þriddan dæl me gehealden to big lifene.
 190. Þa cegde me se min fæder se abbud to him and he sæde,
þæt he gesege, þæt ic wære gemearcod mid deofles mearciserne, and
he sæde, þæt þæt wære cuðlice þæs ealdan feondes
geswifornis, þæt þing, þæt me getengce wære, and he sæde,
þæt hit wære þan gelicost, þe hund eft hwyrfde to his spiwðan,
and he sæde, þæt manige munucas wæron beswicene in þa ilcan wisan,
and sæde, þæt þis wære eall deofles weorc, þeah þe he me ne
ætywde opene andwlitan.
 197. And he þa e beforan me, hu se deofol beswac Adam and Evan
middaneardes.
 199. And þa æt nyxtan, cwæð Malchus, leat se abbud,
þæt ic hine ne forlete, ne þæt ic me sylfne ne forlete sul in minre
handa, forþan þe ic under bæc besege Malchus, forþan me oferswiðde
se wyrresta sigor, forþan na spræce na for minre þearfe.
 203. And he me þa wæs fyligende de ut of þam mynstre, efne
þam geliccost, þe he þa iu bære min ic ut eode of þam mynstre.
 205. Þa grette he me and he wæs cweþende: eart gemearcod
mid deofles mearciserne, and ne sece is þæt þing, ne unge ic ne after,
forþan ic wat þæt sceap, þæt þe bið gongende ut of þam e,
þonne bið him sona on geopenad wulfes bite.
 210. And þa wæron þefersce siðfæt donde to Edissum and
hig wæron farende þurh an westen on hiora fulcuðne weg.
 211. Þa wæron þær Sarocine gesamnode, þæt hig
sætnodan manna.
 212. And þa hit genealæcte, þæt hig sceoldon feran in
þone fræcnan weg, þa gesamnodan hio micel wered tosamne, þæt hig
mihton þa fræcnesse genesan.
 215. And in minum geferscipe wæron weras and wif, and þær
wæs ealdra manna and iungra and lytelra cilda, swa þær wære
hundsiofontig.
 217. And þa þiccodan þider semninga þa Ismaheli on horsum
and on olfendum, and hig hæfdon geþwinglode loccas and scearp fex on hiora
hiafde and healf nacode on hiora lichaman, buton þæt hig wæron mid
ænlypigum riftum ymbhangene, and wide sceos hangodan on hira fotum and bogan
hangodan on hiora eaxlum, and hig bæron lange sceaftas and ne coman hig na
to fiohtanne, ac þæt hig woldan mid hloðe geniman.
 223. And þa wæron we gegripene and todælde.
 224. And þa ymb þrage, cwæð Malchus, and æfter longre
yldo, þa ongan ic don hreowe mines siðfætes, and ic wæs gehloten mid
anum wife in anes ceorles þeowdome.
 226. Þa wæron wit twegen on anum olfende þurh þæt rume
westen and wit unc simble ondredon, hwonne wit sceoldon feallan of þam
olfende and of ahreosan, and miccle ma wit hangodan be þam olfende, þonne
wit þæron sæton, and uncer mete wæs healf soden flæsc and uncer
wæta wæs olfenda miolc.
 232. And nat ic, on hu micclum fæce se siðfætt wearð
geendod, þa become wit to þam inneran dæle þæs westenes, þær
uncer hlæfdige wæs and hire bearn.
 234. Þa wæron wit bædde bi hæþenra þeawe, þæt
wit sceolden hig wurþian, and wit wæron belocene in carcerne.
 236. Þa wit þis dydon, þa ne forlet þære lyfte smyltnes
ane wesan gegerede, buton þæt an, þæt wit uncre sceome mihton
bewreon.
 238. Þa sealde man me sceap to healdenne and þis an wæs
minra yfela eaðnys þæs þeowdomes, þe ic on wæs, þæt ic mine
hlaford and mine efenþeowas swiðe seldan geseah.
 240. Þa þuhte me, þæt ic hæfde hwæthwugu gelices
þam eadigan Iobe, and ic wæs Moyses gemyndig, hu he fedde his nytenu in
westenne.
 242. And þa wæron wit þær fedde mid niowe cyse and mid
meolca, and ic þa sang mine sealmas, þa þe ic iu, nat hwonne, in mynstre
geleornade.
 244. And ic wæs gelustfullod minre hæftnyde and ic dyde gode
þancas, forþan ic funde þone munuchad in þam westene, þe ic ær on
mynstre forlet.
 247. Eala hwæt, ne bið æfre owiht gesundfullices in þam
deofle.
 248. Eala hwæt, þæs diofles geswipornys syndon swiðe
unasecgendlice.
 249. And me þa geeode, þæt ic gemette þæs diofles
æfste, þær ic wæs dyrne in þam westene.
 250. Þa geseah min hlaford, þæt his eowde wæs weaxende
and na waniende, and næs ænig facen, þæt he funde in me, ac wæs
gemyndig þæs apostoles gespræces Sancte Paules, forþon he cwæð,
þæt man sceolde þeowian his hlaforde swa his drihtne.
 254. And þa wolde he gedon, þæt ic him wære borhfæst
and þæt ic him wære getreowra, þonne ic ær wæs.
 255. And þa ætfæste he me mine efenþeowene, seo þe
wæs ær oðres gemæcca, ic nat hwanne.
 257. And þa wiðsoc ic hire and ic sæde, þæt ic wære
Cristen, and ic sæde, þæt me nære alyfed oðres mannes wifes to
onfonne, and ic sæde, þæt hire wer lifde, þeah þe heo gehæftedu
wære.
 259. And he wæs alæded on weg fram hire þurh oðerne
hlaford.
 260. And þa wæs se min hlaford in micle hatheortnysse and he
wæs swiðe unlioðewac geworden wið me and he gebrægd his swurd and
wolde me ofslean.
 263. Þær ic him ne æt onette, þæt ic þæt wif
gegripe be hire earme and me toforan abræd, and þær þis nære,
þonne wære min blod instæpe agoten.
 265. And þa com þær swiðe hraðe þære nihte
þysternys, þæt wit sceoldan bion tosamne geþydde.
 266. And þa lædde ic min þæt niowe wif in min þæt
healf clæmede hus, and wit þa wæron butu swiðe unrote geworden for
þy hæmede, þe wit wendon, þæt wit hæman sceoldan, and uncer
laþette ægþer oþer, þeah þe he hit oþrum ne sæde.
 270. And þa ongeat ic soðlice, cwæð Malchus, mine
hæftnede and ic me astrehte on þa moldan and ic ongan wepan minne
munuchad, þone þe ic ær forleas, and ic cwæð, þæt ic wære
to þære yrmðe gehealden and þæt me mine mandæda to þan
gelæddon, þæt ic þa sceolde wesan ceorl on hariendum heafde.
 274. And þus he wæs specende wið hine sylfne: Hu nyt is me
nu, þæt ic ær mine yldran forhogode and mine eþel and minne hired,
and þis ic dyde for drihtne, þæt ic þis eall forhogode.
 277. Ac hit w, þæt ic þis eall forþan þrowige, forþan
ic eft gyrnde, þæt ic sohte minne eþel.
 279. And ic þa wæs specende to minre sawle, cwæð Malchus,
and ic cwæð: Hwæt do wit la sawul?
 280. Wit willað forweorðan, þonne wit beoð oferswiðde.
 281. Hweþer onbidað wit nu on drihtnes handa, þe wit þonne
unc acwellan mid uncer agene swurde.
 282. Hwerf þu nu þin swurd in þe, forþan þære sawle
deað is ma to ondrædenne, þonne þæs lichaman.
 284. Þonne hafað sio geþungennys gehealden hire martirhad and
þonne ligð min lichama in þissum westene unbebyriged, and me is Crist to
gewitan, þæt ic þonne bio min ehtere geworden and ic bio martir.
 287. And þa ic on þis wæs specende Malchus, þa genam ic
min þæt scinende swurd and ic gehwyrfde þone ord ongean me and ic
cwæð to minum þam ungesæligan wife: Hafa þu me ma to martire,
þonne to were.
 290. And þa astrehte hio hig to minum fotum and cwæð: Ic
þe bidde þurh hælend and þurh þisse tide nydþearfe, þæt þu
ne ageote þin blod.
 292. Gif þe þonne licige to sweltenne, asend þonne þin
sweord in me, þonne bioð wit swa ma tosamne geþeodad; þeah þe min wer
eft hwyrfe to me, þonne gehealde ic þeah hweþere þa clænnyss, þa
þe me sio hæftnyd gelærde.
 295. Ac for hwann sweltest þu, ær þu sig to me geþioded?
 296. Ic þe þonne andette, þæt ic swelte, ær ic wille
beon to þe geþeodad, ac hafa þu me to þan geþungennestan wife, and
wit syn ma þurh þa sawle tosamne geþiodad, þonne wit syn þurh þone
lichaman.
 299. Þonne wenað uncre hlafordas, þæt wit syn swa swa
gesinhina.
 300. Crist þonne wat uncre clænnyss, midþy þe he gesihð,
hu wit doð.
 301. Ic þonne andette, cwæð Malchus, þæt ic aforhtade
and ic wæs wundrigende on þæs wifes word, and ic hig þa lufode
swiðor þonne ænig riht wif.
 303. And ic næfre ne geseah hire nacode lichama, ne ic næfre
ne æthran hire nacodum leomum.
 305. Ic þa ondred, þæt ic in þære sibbe forlure,
þæt ic ær in þam gefiohte gehiold.
 306. And þa æfterþon þe manige dagas wæron
forðgewitene, þa gesegon uncre hlafordas, þæt wit lufedan unc
betweonan.
 308. Þa ne wendon hig nanes fleames to unc, ac hio unc bæddan
to gemangum.
 310. And þa æfter micelre tide sæt ic ana in þam westenne
and ic ne geseah nowiht buton eorðan.
 311. Þa ongann ic swigiendlice þencan be manegra munuca life
and ic þohte ealra swiðost ymb þone abbud, þe me getydde, and ic his
wæs gemyndigost, hu he me genam and he me forleas.
 314. And þa ic þis wæs þencende, cwæð Malchus, þa
geseah ic micelne æmettena heap up astigendne, and hio bæran maran
byrðene, þonne hiora agene lichaman wæron, and sume hio twiccedan þa
grasu mid hiora muðe, sume hio wurpon þa moldan up, and hio wæron
forsettende þara wætera rynas, and hig wæron gemyndige þæs
toweardan hungres, þylæs þa ofþinenan corn in brord gehwyrfden, and
hig forcur ohtan sæd, and sume hig ongunnon, swa hio mid heafde bæren
deadra manna lichaman, and hig dydon, þæt gyt mare to wundrienne is,
þæt wæs, þæt in swa micclum heape þære amettena, þe
þær wæron ut gongende, þæt hiora nænig þam in gangendum
æmettum ne wiðstod; eac þonne gif hiora hwilc geseah, þæt hiora
hwilc gefeoll under þam byrðenum, þonne wæron þa oðre sona in
hiora fultume and gesetton þa byrþene eft on hiora eaxle.
 327. To hwan spece ic nu þus fela, cwæð Malchus.
 328. Se dæg me ætywde swiðe micele wæfersyne, and ic
þa wæs gemyndig þæs snottran Salomones, forþan he sæde, þæt
þa latan mod wæron gereht in æmettena onlicnysse.
 330. Þa ongan me langian for minre hæftnyde and ic ongan
gyrnan, þæt ic sohte eft min mynster, and ic wilnode, þæt ic become
to þære æmettena onlicnysse, forþon þær bið gewinn in midnesse
þæs mynstres and in godum mynstre ne bið owiht syndriges, ac eall hit
bið gemæne.
 335. And þa hwyrfde ic eft to minum huse.
 335. Þa gearn me ongean min þæt ungesælige wif and hio me
gegrette.
 336. Þa ne mihte ic hire bedyrnan mines modes unrotness, forþan
hit wæs on minum andwlitan gesyne.
 338. Þa gehyrde hio fram me, þæt ic hig hwette to fleame,
and þa sette hio swigunge butwuh hire geleafan hiht and wit þa wæron on
midnesse miccles eges.
 340. Þa genamon wit on midnyss þæs eowdes twegen buccan;
þa wæron on wundorlicre micelnesse, and wit hig acwealdon and wit
geworhton þa hyde to twam kyllum gehioldan hiora flæsc unc to
wægnyste.
 343. And þa on æfenne wende uncer hlaford, þæt wit
wæron in uncres cofan digolnesse, þa ongunnon wit feran and wit dydon
þæs flæsces hwylcne hwugudæl in þa kylla.
 346. And þa coman wit to anre ea, seo wæs þanon on tyn
milum, and þa bleowan wit þa kylla and astigon þæron and scufon hig
þa ut on þa ea, and wit reowan sticcmælum mid uncrum fotum, oð
þæt hig unc asetton swiðe feor on oðre healfe þære ea, þæt
þa ne mihton uncre swaðe findon, þa þe unc æfter ferdon.
 351. And þa in gemang þissum wearð uncer wegnyst afulod and
hit feoll of þam kyllum, buton þæt wit mihton þry dagas big lifian,
and þa æton wit þeh hweþere swyðe þæt wæter æfter and wit
wæron gemyndige þæs toweardan hungres n wit swiðe on weg and wit
locodon swiðe oft under bæc and miccle oftor wit urnon nihtes þonne
dæges for Sarcina hergunge and for þære sunnan bryne.
 357. And ic earma nu aforhtige to secgenne, hwæt me becom,
cwæð Malchus, and ic eom nu ealle mode orsorh and þeah hweþere me nu
forhtað eall se lichama.
 360. And þa locodon wit þy þriddan dæge under bæc; þa
þuhte unc, þæt wit gesegon sittan twegen men on twam olfendum and þa
efstan mid þære mæstan hrædnesse.
 362. Þa sona aforhtade uncer mod, forþan hit bið ælces
yfeles forewis, forþan wit wendan, þæt þæt wæren uncre
hlafordas, and wit unc þa ondræddon oð deað.
 364. Efne, þæt me þuhte, þæt sio sunne swearte scine,
and wit wendon, þæt þæt sand uncre swaðe geypte.
 366. Þa gesegon wit on þa swiðran healfe nowiht feor unc an
eorðscræf and wit unc ondredon, þæt þær wæron næddran cyn
in þam eorðscræfe, and wit eoden hweþere þider in and wit unc
gestaðelodon sona on þa wynstran healfe þæs scræfes and ofer þis
wit ne dorston bion ut gangende, forþon wit unc ondredon, gif wit ut eoden
and flugon þæra næddrena deað, þæt wit þonne bicoman to
deaðe.
 372. And þa cwædon wit: Her wit habbað hælo, gif drihten
unc wile fultmian, and gif he forhigeð uncet fyrenfulle, þonne habbað wit
her byrgene in þissum eorðscræfe.
 375. Tellað ge nu la, hwilc modes fyrhtu unc þa wæron and
hwilc ege, þa wit gesegon uncerne hlaford swiðe yrne standan biforan þam
eorðscræfe.
 377. Eala, hu miccle hefigra bið se wenenda deað, þonne se in
brohta.
 378. And þis ic spece nu gyt mid swa miccle ege and mid swa
miccle fyrhtu, þæt me þinceð, þæt me sio tunge stomrige.
 380. And me wæs efne þan gelicost, þe ic þa eft gehyrde
minne hlaford cegan, nis hit gyt forðun, þæt ic þwastrian durre.
 382. And þa sende he uncerne efenþeowa mid unc, þæt he
uncet sceolde ut alædan of þam eorðscræfe, and uncer hlaford hiold
hiora olfendu biforan þam scræfe and þær abad mid atogenum swurde
uncres tocymes.
 385. Þa midþy þe se þeow hæfde gegan þreora fæðma
oððe feowra in þæt eorðscræf, þa ne mihte he unc gesion,
forþan eagena gewuna bið, þæt hio bioð æfter sunnan beorhtnesse
swilce hio blinde syn.
 388. And þa cegde he hluddre stefne and cwæð: Gangað ut,
git godwrecan, and gongað ut, git rode wyrðan, forþan inc cegð incer
hlaford.
 390. And þa hig swa cigdon, þa ahleop þær an leo
eorðscræfes þystrum and hio swengde on hine and forbat him þone
sweoran cwæð Malchus: Hwilc ege unc þa wæs and eac hu micel modes
bliss, forþan wit gesegon, þæt uncer efenþeow wæs forworden biforan
unc.
 394. And se uncer hlaford hlydde þærute and cidde and abad mid
getogene sweorde uncres tocymes.
 395. And he þa þrowade þæs þeowes sleacnysse and he þa
æt nextan wende, þæt wit twu hine hæfdon ofercumene, and þa he
þæs þeowes yldinge geseah, þa eode he sylf in þæt scræf.
 398. Þa swengde sio lio sona forð and forswealh uncerne hlaford
biforan unc and gedranc hire þæt blod.
 400. Ac hwæt la talast þu, hu micel ege unc þa wære and
hu micel modes bliss, forþan wit geseagon uncre feond biforan unc
forwordene.
 402. Hwilc man mihte æfre gelyfan, þæt þæt deor fuhte
for unc.
 403. And þa midþy se ege wæs anumen fram unc, oðer mare
ege unc wæs þa ætywed, forþan wit gesegon þa leon in þam
eorðscræfe mid hire hwelpum.
 405. And þa gewat sio lio on uhtan ut of þam scræfe and hio
bær hire hwelpas ut mid hio and hio unc forgeaf þæt gestern, and þa
gyt hweþere ne dorstan wit gan of þam scræfe, forþan wit unc ondredon,
þæt sio leo unc come to.
 409. And wit wæron ealne þone dæg on þære mæstan
modes fyrhto.
 410. And þa se dæg wæs forðgewiten, þa gewiton wit on
æfenne ut of þam eorðscræfe, and wit astigon on þa olfendan, þe
uncer hlaford þider on com, and wit unc gefyldan niowes ceses and wit bicoman
þy teoðan dæge to Rome byrig and wit gerehton æfter endebyrdnesse
þam ealdormen bi ealre uncer fore.
 414. And þanon wit þa wæron ferende to Mesopotamiam
þære mægðe and þær wit bibohtan uncre olfendan, and þa
æfter þyssum ic com to þam mynstre, þe ic ær fram com.
 417. And þa wæs min abbud forðfered, and þa gewat to
þam munucum, þa þe þær wæron, and ic hig simble lufode, swa swa
swustor.
 419. And ic wæs swiðe iung, cwæð Hieronimus, þa Malchus
me þis wæs secgende, and þis nu secge eow ealdum, þæt ic wolde,
þæt þa clænan and þa unwemman hira clænnysse and hiora
unwemnysse forð gehioldan.
 422. And þæt hig witon, þæt bitweoh sweord and betwux
westenne and betwux wildeor, þæt sio geþungennes ne mæg næfre
wesan besmitan.
